naa, Abrahaame naa gidida Yesus Kirstoosa yeletetha zarkey hayssafe kaallizayssa;
Abrahaamey Yisaaqa yelides; Yisaaqi Yaqoobe yelides; Yaqoobey Yuhudanne iza ishata yelides;
Yuhuday Timaarippe Faareesanne Zaara yelides; Faareesay Esroome yelides; Esroomey Araame yelides;
Araamey Aminadabe yelides; Aminadabey Ne7asoone yelides; Ne7asooney Salomoone yelides;
Salomoonka Bo7eeze Era7aabippe yelides; Bo7eezey Urutippe Iyoobeede yelides; Iyoobeedey Isseye yelides;
Isseyey kawo Dawute yelides; Dawutey Ooriyo macheyfe Solomoone yelides.
Solomoonka Robi7aame yelides; Robi7amey Abbiya yelides; Abbiyayka Aasafe yelides;
Aasafey Yoosapixe yelides; Yoosapixey Iyooraame yelides; Iyooraamey Ooziya yelides;
Ooziyaney Iyoo7aatame yelides; Iyoo7aatamey Akaze yelides; Akazey Hiziqaase yelides;
Hiziqaasi Minaase yelides; Minaasey Amoxe yelides; Amoxeykka Yoosiyaasa yelides;
Yoosiyaasi Babiloone di7o layth Ikonyaanenne iza ishata yelides.
Babiloone di7oppe guye Ikonyaaney Salatiyaale yelides; Salatiyaaleyka Zerubaabele yelides;
Zerubaabeley Abiyoode yelides; Abiyoodey Eliyaqeeme yelides; Eliyaqeemey Azaare yelides;
Azaarey Saadooqe yelides; Saadooqey Akime yelides; Akimeykka Eliyoode yelides;
Eliyoodey Alazaare yelides; Alazaarey Maataane yelides; Maataaney Yaqoobe yelides;
Yaqoobeyka Kirstoosa geetettidayssa Yesusa yelida Maaramo ekkana giigissida Yoosefe yelides.
Hessa gish Abrahaameppe yiidi Dawute gakkanaas tammanne oyddu yeleteth; qasse Dawuteppe Babiloone di7o wode gakkanaas tammanne oyddu yeleteth; Babiloone di7oppe Kirstoosa yeleteth gakkanaas tammanne oyddu yeleteth gidees.
Yesus Kirstoosa yeletetha taarikey hayssafe kaalli dizayssa; iza aaya Maarama Yoosefes giigetta dishin izi izira gayttonta Xillo Ayanan qanthatada beettadus.
Izo giigissida Yoosefey xillo as gidida gish Maaramo asaa sinthan qonce kessonta qotara agganas ba woznara qachchides.
Hayssa izi qoppishin Xoossa kiitanchay agumora izas qoncidi “Dawute naa Yoosefe! Ne giigissida Maarama qanthatiday Xillo Ayanan gidida gish izo neso efanaas babbofa.
Iza attuma naa yelana; izi asa nagarappe ashshanadde gidida gish iza sunth ne ‘Yesusa’ ga sunthana” gides.
Goday nabe Isayaasa duunan “Hekko! Gela7oy qanthatana; attuma naakka yelana; naaza sunthayka Amanu7eela geetettana; hessa birsheththika ‘Xoossi nunara dees’ geetettidi xaafettidayssi polettana mala hayssi wurikka hanides” gides.
<range>
Yoosefeykka dhiskofe beeggidi Goda kiitanchay iza azazida mala Maaramo baso efides.
Gido attin baada iza koyro naaza yelana gakkanaas izo ekibenna. Yeletida guutha naaza suntha “Yesusa” gides.
Kawo Herdoosa wode Yesusi Beeteleme Yuhudan yeletidappe guye awa arshey mokkiza baggafe eranchati Yerusalame yiidi
“Yeletida Ayhuda kawoy awan dizee? Awa arshey mokkiza baggara iza xoolinteza beyidi izas goynnana yidos” giidi oychida.
Kawo Herdoosi hessa siydi daggammides; Yerusalamen diza asay wuri izara daggammides.
Izikka Qeeseta halaqatanne woga tamarsizayta ubba shiishshidi “Kirstoosi awan yelettanee?” giidi oychides.
Istika izas “Nabey ‘Yuhuda biittan dizaare hanne Beeteleme! Ta dere Isra7eele naagizadey neeppe kezana gish hanko Yuhuda haarizaytappe aazanka guuxakka’ giidi xaafida gish izi Beeteleme Yuhudan yelettana” giidi yootida.
<range>
Hessafe guye Herdoosi he eranchata geemara xeygisidinne ista hasayssidi xoolintezi istas bettida wodeyo shaakki erides.
Eranchata Beeteleme yeddidi “Biidi guutha naaza koyite, takka baada izas goynnana mala demmida mala ha taakko simmidi izi awan dizaakkon taas yootite” gides.
Eranchatikka kawoy istas gidayssa siyidappe guye simmi bida; awa arshey mokkiza baggara istas bettida xoolintey ista kaaleththidi guutha naazi dizaso gaththides.
Isti xoolinteza beyida wode daro ufayetida.
Keeththe gelidi guutha naaza iza aayo Maaramira demmidinne gulbatidi izas goynnida; ba saaxine saaxine dooydi worqa, exaanenne karbe giza miish izas immida.
Isti Herdoosakko simmonta mala agumon keehi naagettana mala geetettida gish hara ogera ba dere simmida.
Eranchati bidappe guye Goda kiitanchay Yoosefes agumora beettidi “Herdoosi guutha naaza wodhana koyiza gish ne simmana wode ta nena erissana gakkanaas dendada guutha naaza aayeyra ekkada duge Gibxe biitta baqatada heen daashsha” gides.
Hessa gish Yoosefey dendidi aayiyo naazara ekkidi gidoththara duge Gibxe biitta bides.
Herdoosi hayqqana gakkanaas heen de7ides. Hessanka “Ta naaza ta Gibxe biittafe xeeygadis” giidi Goday kase nabe duunan haasayidayssi polettides.
Eranchati iza baleththidayssa erida wode Herdoosi keehi hanqettides. Eranchati izas kase yootida mala ba as kiittidi nam7u laythanne nam7u layth kumontayta Beetelemeninne Beetaleme yuushon diza guutha attuma nayta ubba wodhisides.
Hessan “Yeehoynne gita waaso giirisay Eraaman siyettides; Ira7eela ba naytas yeekkadus; nayti wuri wurida gish minnanas dandayonta ixadus” geetettidi nabe Ermaasan yootettidays polettides.
<range>
Herdoosi hayqqidappe guye Goda kiitanchay agumora Yoosefes Gibxe biittan beettidi,
“Dendada guutha Naazanne iza aayiyo ekkada Isra7eele biitta simma; Naaza wodhana koyizayti hayqqida” gides.
Yoosefey dendidi naaza aayiyra ekkidi Isra7eel biitta simmides.
Gido attin Arkalawosi ba aawa Herdoosa soon Yuhudan kawotidayssa siydinne he baanas babbides; Goday agumora izi he boonta mala yootida gish Galila awurajja bides.
Naazirete geetettiza katamayo biidi heen duus oykkides. Hessanka kase nabetan “Naazirete as geetettana” geetettidi kasetidi sinthafes hasayettidayssi kumides.
He wode xammaqiza Yohannisi asaas “Salo kawotethi matida gish inte nagarappe simmite” gi sabakishe Yuhuda bazzora yides.
<range>
“Goda oge ooththite, wogga ogezakka lo7ethite gishe bazzo biittan waassiza qaala” geetettidi kase nabe Isayaasan yootetidayssi Yohannisa gishassa.
Yohannisi gaamella isikefe oosettida may7o may7ees. Ba xeessan dafo gixxees; izi miza qumay degera essanne boole.
Yerusalameppe, kumeththa Yuhudappenne Yordanoose shaafa matan diza dere asay wuri Yohannisakko wodhdhidi,
ba nagarakka izas paaxishe Yordaanoose Shaafan iza kushen xammaqettides.
Daro Farsaaweetinne Saduqaaweti izi xammaqizaso yishin beyidi Yohannisi “Inteno shooshato! Inte sinthara diza hanqofe attana mala intena ooni bessidee?
Inte inte nagarappe simmidayssa bessiza ooso ooththite.
‘Nu aaway Abrahaamey nuus dees’ gizayssan interka intena baleththofte; ta intes Xoossi hayta shuchchatappe Abrahaames naa ooththi denthanas dandayees gays.
Hekko kaltay qanxanaas mithata garsan giigeti uttides; hessa gish lo7o ayfe ayfonta mithi wuri qanxettananne taman yeggettana.
Tani maarotethas haaththan xammaqays; haray atto shin ta iza caamma tookkanas bessontadey taappe aadhdhiza minoy guyera yaana; izikka Xillo Ayananinne taman intena xammaqana.
Kath suragiza pithay iza kushen dees; izikka ba kaththa baleza pitti geeshshana; ba gistezakka kaththa di7en qolana; happa gidikko to7onta taman xuugana” gides.
He wode Yesusi Yohannisan xammaqettanas Galilappe Yordanoose shaafa bides.
Gido attin Yohannisi “Hayssi hanenna; tani nenan xammaqettana bessishin neni waanada taakko yay?” giidi izara marshettides.
Yesusikka “Aykkoy baawa, ero garkii? Hayssa ooththidi nuni xilloteth ubba polanas nuus bessees” gides. Yohansikka iza qofa ero gi ekides.
Yesusi xammaqetidi haaththafe kezida mala heerakka saloy doyettin Xoossa Ayanay haraphe kafo misatidi iza bolla wodhdhishin beyides.
Saloppekka “Tani izan ufayetiza Naazinne ta siiqiza ta Naazi hayssa” giza qaalay siyettides.
Hessafe guye Xillo Ayanay Xala7en paacettana mala Yesusa duge bazzo biitta efides.
Oyddu tammu gallassinne oyddu tammu qamma xoomidappe guye Yesusi gafides.
Paacizayssi Yesusakko shiiqidi “Ne Xoossa Naa gidikko ane hayta shuchchata uketh gidana mala azaza” gides.
Yesusikka “ ‘Asi Xoossa duunappe keziza qaalanpe attin kaththan xalla deenna’ geetetti xaafettides” giidi izas zaarides.
Qasseka Xala7ey Yesusa geeshsha katamayo efi Xoossa Keeththa quste bolla kessidi,
“Ne Xoossa Naa gidikko ane hayssafe duge guppa; ayssi giikko ‘Ne tohoy shuchchan dhuphetonta mala kiitanchati ba kushera nena oykki denthana mala ne gish Xoossi ba kiitancha kiittana’ geetetti xaafettides” gides.
Yesusikka “Geeshsha Maxaafan ‘Ne Goda Xoossa paacofa’ geetetti xaafettides” giidi zaarides.
Qasseka Xala7ey Yesusa keehi dhoqa zuma bolla kessidi salo gupanthon diza kawoteththa bonchozara ubba ehi bessidi,
“Ne kundada taas goynnikko hayssa ubba ta nees immana” gides.
Yesusi “Haysso Xala7e! Ta sinthafe haakka! ‘Neni ne Godas Xoossas goynna; izas xalala azazeta’ geetetti Geeshsha maxaafan xaafettides” gides.
Hessafe Xala7ey iza aggidi bides; kiitanchatikka yiidi iza maaddida.
Yesusi, Yohannisi qashetidayssa siydi gede Galila simmides.
Naazirete katama aggidi Zaabiloone Niftaaleme heeran abba matan diza Qifirnahoome kataman duus oykkides.
“Hessan Zaabilooneninne Niftaaleme biittan, Yordanooseppe he pinthan abba lanqera efiza oge matan diza Ayzaabe gidida Galila dere asay, dhuman diza derey wolqama poo7o beyides. Hayqo kuwa giddon diza deres poo7oy poo7ides” geetettidi nabe Isayaasa duunan kasetidi hasayettidayssi polettides.
<range>
<range>
Yesusi he wodeppe ha simmin “Salo kawotethi matides, maarota gelite” giidi sabbako oykkides.
Yesusi Galila Abba lanqera aadhdhishe nam7u ishanta; heytikka Phexroosa geetettiza Simoonanne iza isha Indiraasa beyides. Istika mole oykkizayta gidida gish mole oykkiza gite abban yeggishe deettes.
Yesusi ista “Haa yiite! Tana kaallite! Ta intena as oykkiza as kessana” gides.
Isti heerakka mole oykkiza giteza yeggi aggidi Yesusa kaallida.
Guuth sinthe bishe hara nam7u ishanta Zabidoosa naa nam7ata Yaqoobenne Yohannisa beyides; istika ba aawa Zabidoosara wogolo giddon mole gite lo7ethettes. Yesusikka ista xeygin;
isti heerakka wogolozanne ba aawa aggidi kaallida.
Yesusi Ayhudata ista Woosa Keeththan tamarsishenne kawoteththa Mishiraachcho qaala sabbakishe qasse dere giddon ay hargeyka sakizayta pathishe kumeththa Galilan yuuyides.
Hessa geedon lo7o nashoy kumeththa Sooriya biittan siyettides; dereyka dumma dumma sakon daro waayetizayta, daydanthi istan gelidayta, bollafe biittan yeggiza hargey dizaytanne silidayta izakko ehin ubbaakka pathides.
Hessafe dendidayssan Galilappe, tammu katamatappe, Yerusalameppenne Yuhudappe, Yordanoose shaafa pinthafe yida daro asay iza kaallides.
Daro derey shiiqidayssa beyidi Yesusi pude zuma bolla kezi uttides; iza kaallizaytikka izakko yida.
Izikka ista hizgi tamarso oykkides;
“Ayanan bana kawushshizayti anjettidayta; ayssi giikko Salo Kawoteth istassa.
Qadhetizayti anjettidayta, ayssi giikko isti minettana.
Ashketi anjettidayta; ayssi giikko isti biitta laattana.
Xilloteth gafetizaytinne saamotizayti anjettidayta; ayssi giikko isti kallana.
Asas lo7o ooththizayti anjettidayta; ayssi giikko istaska lo7oy oosettana.
Wozina xilloti anjettidayta; ayssi giikko isti Xoossa beyana.
Saroteth ooththizayti anjettidayta; ayssi giikko isti Xoossa nayta geetetti xeeygettana.
Xillotetha gish goodettizayti anjettidayta; ayssi giikko salo kawotethi istassa.
“Ta geedon asay intena cayikko, goodikkonne iita yo7o wordora inte bolla haasayikko inte anjettidayta.

“Inte ha biitta asas maxine mala. Maxiney ba mal7otetha yeddiza gidikko gede kare yegettidi yedhetethafe attin, zaaridi demmanas dandayizee?
Inte deres poo7o. Zuma bolla diza katamaya qotetanas danda7ukku.
Asi xompe oythidi keeththan diza asaa kumeththas poo7ana mala dhoqason woththes attin geema soon woththi erenna.
Hessathoka asay inte lo7o ooso beyidi salon diza inte Aawa bonchana mala inte poo7oy asa sinthan poo7o.
“Tani Muse woganne nabeta qaala shaarana yida intes misatoppo; polanas yadis attin shaaranas yabeekke.
Ta intes tumu gays; saloynne sa7ay aadhdhana gakkanaas Muse wogay wuri polettana attin wogappe issi pidaleykka woykko qeerinyakka shaaretukku.
Hessa gish oonikka ha azazotappe guuxizaro gidikkoka ooththonta yeggi aadhdhikko, hankoytaka yedhi aadhdhana mala tamarsikko salo kawoteththan hessadey guuth geetetti xeeygettana; gido attin hayta azazota ooththi polishe hankoyta polana mala tamarsikko hessadey Salo Kawoteththan gita geetettana.
Ta intes gays, inte xillotethi Farsaaweetappenne Muse woga tamarsizayta xillotethappe aadhdhonta aggikko Salo Kawoteth gelana dandayekketa.
“Kase asatas ‘Wodhoppa; wodhidade bolla pirdettana’ geetettidayssa inte siyideta.
Ta qasse intes gizay ba isha bolla ogey baynda hanqettizade bolla pirdettana; oonikka ba isha ‘Nappay’ gizaddey duulata sinthan oyshettana. ‘Eeyay’ gizade Gaanname tama pirday naages.
Hessa gish neni yarsho shiishshizason Xoossas yarshana gishin ne ishay ne bolla mishetidazi nees qoppetikko,
ne yarshizayssa heen yarshoson aggagada koyro baada ne ishara giiga; hessafe guye simmada ne yarshoza Xoossas shiishsha.
“Nena mootida ne morkey ne bolla pirdisonta mala, pirdiza daannay qachizayssas nena aaththi immonta mala, qasho keeththan ne wodhdhonta mala buro oge bolla dashe ne morkera elela giigaycha.
Ta nees tumu gays; izi pirdisi wursida gidikko wursetha santiyo qanxana gakkanaas qashoppe birshetaka.
“ ‘Laymatoppa’ gizayssa inte siyideta.
Tani gidikko intena hizgays; macasa amo ayfera xeellidadey wuri ba woznan izira laymatides.
Nagara ooththanas ne ushacha ayfey nees gaaso gidikko neeppe kessa wora yegga; ne asatethay kumeth gede Gaanname taman yegetanappe ne asatethafe issina paccikko lo7o.
Ne ushachcha kushey nagara oosos gaaso gidikko neeppe qanxa digga; ne asatethay kumeth Gaannamen yegetanayssafe ne asatethafe issi billitey nees pacce gidikko lo7o.
“ ‘Macho anji yeddizadey pirma waraqata izis immana bessees’ geetettides.
Tani qasse intena hizgays, hara asara laymatishin beyonta dishe ba macho anjizadey wuri iza laymatana mala ooththes. Hessathoka anjettidaro ekizadeyka laymatida mala qoodetes.
“Kase asatas ‘Wordo caaqofa; Xoossa sinthan ne caaqidayssa naaga’ geetettidayssa inte siyideta.
Ta qas intena aykkokka caaqofte gays; saloy Xoossas uttiza alga gidida gish salon caaqofte.
Biittay Xoossa tohoy yedhizaso gidida gish biittanka caaqofte. Wogga kawo katama gidida gish Yerusalamenka caaqofte.
Inte hu7enka caaqofte; inte hu7e binanappe issineyokka booth woykko kareth histanas dandayekketa.
Hessa gish inte inte giddon haasayettishin inte haasayay “Ee” gaanaz gidikko “Ee” giite “Akay” gaanaz gidikko “Akay” giite; hessafe kare gididay wuri iita asappe yizaza.
“ ‘Ayfe gishas ayfe achcha gishas achcha’ geetettidayssa inte siyideta.
Ta qasse intes gizay iita ooththidadera eqetoppite; gido attin nees ushachcha shagala baqqizades hankoyssakka yuusha bessa.
Issi asi ne giddora may7idayssa neeppe ekkanas nena mootikko bollara may7idayssakka gujada izas imma.
Issi asi nena issi saate oge ne baana mala wolqathikko issife nam7u dakko gidana oge izara ba.
Nena woossizades imma; neeppe tal7e ekkanas koyizades zokko zaaroppa.
“ ‘Ne lagge siiqa; ne morke ixxa’ geetettidayssa siyideta.
Ta qas intena inte morketa dosite; intena goodizaytas woossite gays.
Inte hessatho ooththikko inte salo Aawas nayta gidana. Izi awa arshe iitatassinne lo7otas issi bolla gaththi imees. Irakka xillotassinne nagaranchatas issi bolla bukises.
Intena dosizayta xalala inte dosikko intes aaza go7ay dizee? Qaraxa qanxisizyti hessatho ooththetennee?
Inte ishata xalla inte sarotikko hankoytappe aazan lo7etii? Ammanontaytikka hessatho ooththetes.
Hessa gish inte salo Aaway wosoy bayndayta gidida mala inteka wosoy bayndade gidite.
“Asi intena beyana mala asa sinthan lo7o ooththonta mala naagettite; hessatho ooththikko inte salo Aawappe go7a demmeketa.
Inte manqotas maado immiza wode asi tana beyo giidi asa sinthan bonchetanas ogeninne Ayhuda Woosa Keeththan xurumba punisiza qoodheppe qommon hanizaytatho ooththofte. Ta intes tumu gays; isti ba waaga ubba haan ekkichida.
Inte manqotas immishin ushachcha kushey ooththiza hadirisa kushey eroppo.
Inte imoy geeman gido; qotan oosettidayssa beyiza inte Aawayka inte waaga intes immana.
“Inte woossishe qoodheppe qommon hanizayta mala hanoppite; isti asi beyana mala Ayhuda woosa keeththataninne oyddu oge bolla eqqidi woossanas dossettes. Ta intes tumu gays; isti kumeththa waaga ekichida.
Ne woossana geliza ne kifile gela; karekka ne bolla gordada geeman diza ne Aawakko woossa. Geeman oosettidayssa beyiza ne Aaway ne ooso mala nees immana.
“Ammanonta asay issi qaala zaari zaari woossikko istas siyetiza misatin isti zaari zaari gizayssatho inteka woossishe issi qaala zaari zaari gooppite.
Gido attin inte Aaway inte woossanappe kasetidi intes aazi koshshizakkone eriza gish inte ista misatoppite.
Inte woossishe ‘Salon diza nu Aawawu! Ne sunthi anjeto.
Ne kawotethi haayo; ne sheney salon gidida mala sa7anka hano.
Hachchis gidiza kath nuus hachchi imma.
Nu nuna qohidaytas atto giza mala nekka nu qoho nuus atto ga.
Iitappe nuna ashsha attin nuna paacen gelthofa; bonchoy merpe merna gakkanaas neyssa. Amiin’ gi woossite.
“Inte intena qohidaytas atto giikko inte salo Aaway intes atto gaana.
Qasse inte asa nagara atto gonta ixikko inte Aawayka inte nagara atto geenna.
“Inte xooma xoomishe qoodheppe qommora xoomizaytatho shullofte. Isti ba xoomizayssa asi erana mala ba ayfeso iissetes. Ta tumu gays; hessatho ooththizayti ba waaga kumeth ekkichida.
Neni xooma xoomashe ne ayfeso meeceta, ne hu7e tiyetta.
Hessatho ne xoomikko geeman diza ne Aaway xalala erizazinne asi oonikka eronta qotan gidana. Qotan oosettidayssa beyiza ne Aawayka ne waaga nees immana.
“Bilay mizason buuqidinne shiydi mooretizason kaysoy bookkidi kaysanas dandayizason, ha biitta bolla intes miishe shiishofte.
Gido attin bilay maanas, buuqidi woykko shiydi mooretontason, kaysoy bookki ekkana dandayontason heen salon intes miishi shiishshite.
Ne miishay dizason ne woznay heen dees.
“Ayfey asatethas poo7o; hessa gish ne ayfey paxa gidikko, ne kumeththa asatethayka poo7o gidana.
Ne ayfey hargancha gidikko, ne kumeththa asatethayka dhuma xalla gidana. Histikko nenan diza poo7oy dhuma gidikko, qasse dhumay waanida gird gida dhuma gidandee?
“Issi asi nam7u godas ooththana dandayenna. Issa ixidi nam7anthoza dosana; woykko issa bonchidi nam7antha leqqana; Xoossassinne miishas nam7atas gaththi ooththanas dandayettenna.
“Hessa gish ta intena inte duussa gish ay miinoo? Ay uyinoo? Ay may7inoo? giidi hirgofte gays. Shempoy qumappe, ashoy may7oppe aadhdhenee?
Ane salo kafota xeellite! Zerettenna, maxettenna, di7en qoletenna shin inte salo Aaway ista mizees. Inte istafe keehi aadhdheketii?
Ane intefe daro waayettidi baas imettida laytha bolla hara issi gallas gujana dandayiza asi dizee?
“Qasse may7o gish aazas hirgetii? Ane coo denban diza ciishshata xeellite; daaburetenna woykko suqetenna.
Hessa gish ta intena gizay haray atto shin kawo Solomoonikka ba bonchora ha ciishshatappe issiney mala lo7o may7ibenna.
Inteno pace ammanoy dizayto! Hachchi asa ayfen beettidi wonto taman wodhdhana maata hayssatho mayziza Xoossi intena hessafe lo7ethi aaththi mayzanas dandayenee?
Hessa gish nu ay maanee? Ay uyanee? Ay may7anee? giidi hirgofte.
Hanko ammanonta asay hayssa demmanas daro qoppees. Hayssi wuri intes koshshizayssa inte salo Aaway erees.
Harappe sinthatidi Xoossa Kawoteththa xilloteth koyite; hayti wuri intes gujettana.
Hessa gish wontos keehi qoppofte; wonto metoy wontos aqo; issi issi gallassay baassi gidiza metora dees.
“Inte bolla pirdetonta mala hara asa bolla pirdofte.
Inte pirdida mala inte bollakka pirdettana. Inte makkida miishara intes makettana.
Ne ayfen diza gita mitha beyonta dashe ne isha ayfen diza qeeri buura aazas xeellay?
Ne ayfen gita mithi dishin ne isha ‘Ane ta ne ayfeppe qeeri buurayo kessays’ gaanas waana dandayay?
Neno qoodheppe qommon hanizaysso kasetada ne ayfen diza gita mitha kessaycha. Hessafe kaallada ne isha ayfen diza buura kessanas lo7etha xeellandasa.
Ba tohon yedhonta malanne simmidi intena saxi daakerethonta mala anjettidayssa kanata sinthan yeggofte; qasse inte worqakka guddunthata sinthan yeggofte.
“Woossite intes imettana; koyite inte demmana; kare qoxite intes doyettana.
Woossida ubbas imettana; koyiza asi demmana; qoxizades karey doyettana.
Inte giddofe issades nay uketh woossikko shuch immiza aaway dandee?
Woykko mole woossikko shoosh immizadey dandee?
Histin inte iitata gidi uttidi inte naytas lo7o miish imo erizayta gidikko inte salo Aaway iza woossizaytas waanidi aadhdhiza lo7o miish imenee?
Hessa gish hara asi intes ooththana mala inte koyizayssa, inteka haratas ooththite. Muse wogaynne nabeti hayssan kuuyettes.
“Xuuntha pengera gelite; dhayoso efiza ogey gita; pengeykka aaho; daro asay he pengezara gelees.
De7os gaththiza ogey gidikko xuuntha; pengeykka xuuntha; gelanaytikka guuthata xalala.
“Istas giddo baggay Kana suyte mala gidi uttidinne dorsa ite may7idi inte giddo gelidi giddora ooththiza wordo nabetappe naagettite.
Inte ista, ista ooson erandeta. Aguntha worappe woyney, kindicho agunthafe balase ayfey maxetizee?
Hessathoka lo7o mithi wuri lo7o ayfees; iita mithika iita ayfe ayfees.
Lo7o mithi iita ayfe ayfanas dandayontayssa mala iita mithi lo7o ayfe ayfanas dandayenna.
Lo7o ayfe ayfonta mithi wurikka qanxetananne taman yegettana.
Hessa gish inte ista isti ayfiza ayfen shaakki erana.
“Salon diza ta Aawa shene polonta dishe tana ‘Godo! Godo!’ gizay wuri Salo Kawoteth gelenna.
He gallas daroti ‘Godo! Godo! Nuni ne sunthan tinbite yootibekonii? Ne sunthan daydanthi kessibekonii? Ne sunthan daro malata ooththibekonii?’ gaana.
He wode ta istas ‘Ta intena mulekka erikke! Inte iitati taappe haakkite’ gaada qoncera ta istas yootana.
“Histikko hayssa ta qaala siydi ooson peyshizadey ba keeththe zaalla bolla keexizade misatees.
Deexo iray bukkin; haroyka harottides; carkoyka carkides; keeththaka sugides shin zaalla bolla keexettida gish kundibenna.
“Hayssa ta qaala siydi ooththontadey gidikko ba keeththe ace bolla keexida eeya asa mala.
Deexo iray bukkin haroyka harottides; carkoyka carkides; he keeththaka sugides; keeththayka iita kundeth kundides” gides.
Yesusi tamarsi wursin asay iza timirtezan malalettides.
Gaasoyka Muse woga tamarsizayta mala gidonta izi godateththi diza asa mala tamarsides.
Yesusi zuma bollafe wodhdhin daro derey iza kaallides.
Issi inchiracha hargey dizaddey Yesusakko shiiqidi iza sinthan gulbatidi “Godo! Ne koykko tana pathanas dandayassa” gides
Yesusi ba kushe yeddidi “Ta dosadis; paxa!” giin addezi he hargezappe heerakka paxides.
Qasseka Yesusi addeza “Ne paxidayssa oonaska yootoppa; gido attin baada nena Qeeses bessa. Isti azazida yarshoza gaththa; hessika istas marka gidana” gides.
Yesusi Qifirnahoome gakkida mala mato halaqay izakko shiiqidi iza hizgi woossides.
“Godo! Ta ashkaray keehi sakettidi keeththan ichchidi dees” gides.
Yesusikka izas “Ta baada pathana” gides.
Mato halaqay izas zaaridi “Ta nena ta keeththe gelthanas bessizadde gidikke; gido attin ne haan daada issi qaala xalla giikko ta ashkaray paxana.
Taaska tana azaziza halaqati taappe bollara deettes; qasseka taas azazettiza wotadarati taappe garsara deettes; istafe issa ‘Ba!’ giikko bees; qasse issa ‘Haaya!’ giikko yees; ta ashkara ‘Hessa ooththa!’ giikko ooththes” gides.
Yesusi iza zaarozan malaletidi bana kaallizaytas “Ta intes tumu gays; haray attoshin Isra7eeleta giddon hayssa mala ammanoy dizadde issadeka demmabekke.
Ta intes yootays; daroti awa arshey mokkiza baggafenne wulliza baggafe yaana. Salo Kawoteththa maaddan Abrahaamentara Yisaaqantaranne Yaqoobentara issife uttana.
Salo Kawotethi istas gidana bessiza asati heen kare dhuman yegettana. Heenka yeehoynne achcha garcech gidana” gides.
Yesusikka mato halaqas “Ne ba ne ammano mala nees hano” gides; ashkarazi heerakka paxides.
Yesusikka buro Phexroosa keeththe gelshin Phexroosa bolloteya misho harge saketada ichchidaaro beyides.
Izi kushe Yesusi bochchin misho hargey aggides. Izakka dendada Yesusa mokkadus.
He gallasa omaris daydanthi oykkida daro asata Yesusakko ehida. Izikka tuna ayanata ba qaalara istafe kessides; harganchataka ubba pathides.
Isayaasi “Izi nu harge ekkides; nu sakokka tookkides” gida qaalay hayssan polettides.
Daro asay iza giddoththidayssa biyidi Yesusi asaa abbafe he pinth pinana mala azazides.
Hessa wode issi Ayhuda ammano tamarsizadey izakko shiiqidi “Astamaare! Ne bizaso awakka ta nena kaallana” gides.
Yesusikka izas zaaridi “Workanatas ollay dees; salo kafotas keeththi dees; taas Asa Naas gidikko hu7e gelthizasoy baawa” gides.
Iza kaalliza issi hara asi qasse “Godo! Koyro baada ta aawa moogoo?” gides.
Izi qasse “Hayqidayti ba hayqeth moogeto; neni gidikko tana kaalla” gides.
Hessafe guye Yesusikka wogolon gelin iza kaallizaytikka izara issife bida.
Qopponta abba giddon dambalay dendidi wogoloyo mittana gakkanaas ista waayssides. Hessi wuri hanishin Yesusi dhiskides.
Iza kaallizayti iza beegoththidi “Godo! Nu dhayoos; nuna ashsha!” gida.
Yesusikka ista “Inteno ammanoy paccidayto! Aazas hayssa mala babbetii?” gides. Hessafe dendidi carkozanne abba dambala izi hanqin heerakka sirph gides.
Istika “Hayssi abbaynne carkoyka izas azazettizaddey izi waanidadee?” giidi malaletida.
Izi abba pinnidi Gergesenoone geetettiza dere gakkida mala daydanthi oykkida nam7u as dayti ba diza dufoppe kezidi izara gaaggida. Asi he ogezara aadhdhanas dandayetonta mala asas daro keehi meto gidi deettes.
Istika “Xoossa Nawu! Nees nunara aaza issifeteth dizee? Nu wodey gakkonta dishin nuna xuugana yadii?” giidi waassida.
Heen istafe guuth haakkidi daro gudduntha wudey issi bolla heemetes.
Daydanthati Yesusa “Ne nuna kessana gidikko haytan daro guddunthatan nu gelana mala nuus piqaade imma” giidi woossida.
Yesusikka ista “Biite!” gides. Daydanthatikka istafe kezidi guddunthatan gelida. Guddunthati wurikka ba dizaso aafora bicharshe abban gelidi haaththan mitettidi hayqqida.
Gudduntha heemmizayti elelidi katamay dizaso biidi guddunthay hanoyssanne daydanthi ista oykkida asata bolla hanidayssa ubba asas yootida.
Katama asay wuri Yesusara gagganas kezides. Yesusa beyidinne ista dere yeddi baana mala iza woossida.
Hessafe guye Yesusi abba bolla wogolora pinnidi kase ba diza katama yides.
Heen issi gunda addeza, asay halara tookkidi Yesusakko ehides. Yesusikka ista ammano beyidi gunda addeza “Aykkoy ba; haysso naazo! Ne nagaray atto geetettides” gides.
He wode Muse woga tamarsizayti “Hayssi Xoossa cashsha” giidi ba woznan qoppida.
Yesusi ista qofa eridi “Inte woznan iita yo7o aazas qoppetii?
‘Ne nagaray atto geetettides’ guussafenne ‘Dendada ba!’ guussafe awayssi kawushshee?
Gido attin Asa Naas biitta bolla ase nagarappe maaranas sheney dizayssa erana malassa” giidi gunda addeza “Denda! Ne hala ekkada gede neso ba” gides.
Gunda addezikka dendidi baso bides.
Dereyka hessa beyidi malaletethaninne babon kumidi hayssa sire godateththi asas immida Xoossa galatides.
Yesusi heeppe dendidi bishe issi Matoosa geetettizadey qaraxa qanxisizason uttidayssa beyidi “Tana kaalla!” giin, dendidi iza kaallides.
Yesusi Matoosason maadda bolla dishin daro qaraxa qaraxizytinne nagaranchati izakko yiidi izaranne iza kaallizaytara issife maanas uttida.
Farsaaweeti hessa biyidi Yesusa kaallizayta “Intena tamarsizayssi qaraxa qanxisizaytaranne nagaranchatara wosti istara issife kath mizee?” gi oychida.
Yesusikka isti gizayssa siydi ista “Aakkimey koshshizay saketidaytas attin saketonta paxatas gidenna.
Hessa gish ‘Inte biidi yarsho gidonta maaroteth dosays’ giza qaala birsheth tamarite. Nagaranchata xeeygana yadis attin xillota xeeyganas yabekke” gides.
Xammaqiza Yohannisa kaallizayti Yesusakko yiidi “Nuninne Farsaaweeti xoomishin nena kaallizayti aazas xoometenee?” gi oychida.
Yesusi istas “Mishiraa laggeti mishirazi istara dishin muuzotana bessizee? Mishiray istafe ekettana wodey yaana; isti he wode xoomana.
“Gal7a may7o bolla ooratha woso woththi sikkiza asi deenna. Gal7a bolla oorath woththi sikkikko oorathazi gala7aza peedherethidi ha daassi darissanna.
Oonikka ooratha woyne cajje gal7a lukkamon gujenna. Gujiza gidikko lukkamozi dhuuqana; woyne cajjezikka gukkana; lukkamozikka go7ay bayndazi gidana. Gido attin ooratha woyne cajjey ooratha lukkamozan gujjetees. Hessa malara woyne cajjezinne lukkamozi lo7o naagettidi gam7ana” gides.
Yesusi asaa haasaysson dishin issi shuumey iza sinthan kundidi “Taas naa daara hayqqana gawus. Iza paxa daana mala yaada ne kushe izi bolla wotharkii?” giin,
Yesusi dendidi izara bides; Yesusa kaallizaytikka izara bida.
Tammanne nam7u layth kumeth izippe suuthi gukkiza issi macassi Yesusappe guyera yaada iza afala macara bochchadus.
Iza hessa ooththiday “Ta izas afaala macara bochidakko paxana” giza ammanoy izi woznan diza gish bochadus.
Yesusikka guye simmi xeelidi macasayo “Aykkoy ba, ta naye; nena ne ammanoy pathides” giin macasaya heerakka paxaagadus.
Yesusikka shuumeza so mata gakkishin derey zayeranne dinkera waassishe yeekkizayssa be7idi,
“Kichchite! Naya dhiskadus attin hayqqabeekku” giin isti iza bolla miicida.
Derey wuri keeththafe kezin izi keeththe gelidi nay kushe oykkides; nayakka denda eqadus.
Iza goobatethi he dere ubban seetettides.
Yesusikka heeppe bishin nam7u qooqeti “Dawute Nawu! Nuna maarariki!” giidi waassishe iza geedo kaallida.
Qooqetikka Yesusi gelida keeththa iza kaallidi gelida. Yesusikka ista “Ta inte ayfe pathana danda7izayssa ammanetii?” giidi oychides. Istika “Ee, Godo!” gida.
Hessafe guye Yesusi ista ayfe bochidi “Inte ammano mala intes hano!” gides.
Ista ayfeykka xeellides. Yesusikka “Hayssa oonikka eronta mala” giidi minthi yootides.
Gido attin isti biidi, heera ubbason Yesusa gish woresida.
Isti heeppe kezishin daydanthi oykkida issi duuna duude as Yesusakko ehida.
Daydanthazi kezidappe guye he duuna duude addezi haasaya oykkides; derezikka malaletidi “Hayssa mala hanoy Isra7eele biittan hanin nu beyi erokko” gida.
Gido attin Farsaaweeti zaaridi iza “Daydanthi kessizay daydanthata halaqanna” gida.
Yesusi Ayhudata Woosa Keeththan Ayhudata tamarsishenne Xoossa Kawoteththa Mishiraachcho qaala yootishe qasseka harge ubbaafe asa paathishe gutatan gutatan yuuyides.
Asay wuri heemizadey baynda dorsa mala keehi metotettidi xeellizay bayndade gididayssa beyida wode istas daro mishettides.
Bana kaallizaytaska “Maxa gakkida kaththay daro shin maxi shiishshizayti guuthata.
Hessa gish kaththa Goday kaththako oosanchata yeddana mala woossite!” gides.
Yesusi bana kaalliza tammanne nam7ata baako xeygidi, isti tuna ayanata kessana mala qasseka sakoppenne hargefe pathana mala istas godateth immides.
Tammanne nam7u Hawaareta sunthay hayssafe kaallizayssa; koyro Phexroosa geetettiza Simoona, iza isha Indiraasa, Zabidoosa naa Yaqoobenne iza isha Yohannisa,
Piliphoosanne Bartelemoosa, Toomaasanne qaraxa shiishshiza Matoosa, Ilfiyoosa naa Yaqoobenne Tadoosa,
ba baggas mishetiza Simoonanne guyeppe Yesusa hayqos aaththi immida Asqoroonto Yuhuda.
Hayta tammanne nam7ata ubba “Gede Ayzaabeta gaath booppite; Samaariya asaa katama geloppite.
Gido attin Isra7eele deraa garsafe dhayida dorsatakko biite.
Biidinne ‘Salo kawoteth matides!’ giidi sabakite.
Harganchata paathite, hayqqidayta hayqoppe denthite, inchiracha hargizayta geeshshite; daydanthata kessite; inte mela ekidayssa mela immite;
worqa, bira woykko xarqimala gidin inte kiisen oykkofte.
Oosanchas hachchis hachchis gidizazi koshshiza gish inte oges giidi shinqe, koshshonta may7o, caamma woykko guufe eki booppite.
“Issi katama woykko issi guta inte geliza wode intena mokkanade koyi demmidi iza keeththan shempite; heeppe kezana gakkanaas heen diishshite.
Inte oona keeththika gelishe ‘Saro’ giite.
He keeththay sarotay bessiza keeththe gidikko inte sarotay he keeththas gido; sorotay bessonta keeththe gidikko inte sarotay aggidi intes simmo.
Ay asikka intena mokki ekkanasinne inte giza siyanas koyontade gidikko hessade keeththafe woykko he katamappe kezishe ista bolla yiza gomeppe inte attidayssas marka gidana mala inte toho bolla diza gudula pittidi kezite.
Ta intes tumu gays; pirda gallas he katamay bolla gakkana pirday Soddome bollan Gamoora bolla gakkida pirdafe deexo gidana.
“Ta intena dorsa mala kana suyteta giddora kiittays. Hessa gish shoosha mala cincatanne haraphe mala ashketa gidite.
Asay intena oykkidi pirdiza duulatas shiishana; Ayhudati ba Woosa Keeththan intena garafana; hessa gish istafe naagettite.
Ta geedon dere haarizaytakkonne kawotakko intena efana; ista sintheninne ammanonta asata sinthan inte marka gidana.
Intena isti oykkiza wode ‘Nu ay gi haasayinoo? Wozgi zaaro imminoo?’ gi hirgofte. He wode inte gaanazi intes imettana.
Intenan haasayanay inte Aawa Ayanappe attin intena gidekketa.
“Ishay ba isha hayqos aaththi immana; aaway ba naa bolla, nayti bana yelidayta bolla makalatethan dendidi hara asan wodhisana.
Ta gish asi wurikka intena ixana. Gido attin wurseth gakkanaas miqnni eqiday izi attana.
Asay intena inte diza heerappe gooddikko haraso kichchite! Ta intes tumu gays; inte Isra7eele katama ubba gakkonta dishin ta Asa Nay yaana.
“Ashkaray godappe woykko kaallizadey kaalethizadefe aadhdhenna.
Tamarey bana tamarsizayssa mala woykko ashkaray goda mala gidikko hessi izas gidana. Keeththa aawa ‘Bi7elizeebula’ giikko so asaa ayssi hessafe iita geetenne!
“Hessa gish istas babbofte; geemetiday qonconta qotetiday geesh kezonta attenna.
Ta intes dhumara yootidayssa poo7on haasayite; haythan siyidayssa qoncen haasayite.
Asho wodhikkofe attin shempo wodhanas dandayontaytas babbofte; hessafe ashonne shempo gathi Gaanname taman dhayssanas dandayizayssas babbite.
Issi santen bayzettiza nam7u siine kafotappe issiniyakka inte salo Aawa sheney baynda coo kunda attuku.
Haray atto shin inte hu7e binanaykka tayibon dees.
Hessa gish babbofte. Daro siine kafotappe inte waagay aadhdhi bonchettidaza.
“Asa sinthan taas markattizades takka salon diza ta Aawa sinthan izades markatana.
Qasse asa sinthan tana kadidade takka salon diza ta Aawa sinthan iza kadana.
“Ta biitta bolla saroteth ehanas yida intes misatoppo; mashsha ehanas attin saroteth ehanas yabeekke.
Tani yiday naa aawappe, maca naa aayippe, naa macho bollotippe shaakanassa.
Asas morkey so asa gidana.
“Taappe aaththidi ba aawa woykko ba aayo siiqizadey taas gidanas bessenna. Taappe aaththidi ba attuma naa woykko, maca naa siiqizadey taas gidanas bessenna.
Ba masqale tookkidi tana kaallonta asi taas gidanas bessenna.
Ba shempo aashshanas koyizadey dhaysses; ba shempo ta gish aaththi immizadey ashshees.
“Intena mokki ekizadey tanakka mokki ekkees. Tana mokki ekkizadey tana kiittidadekka mokki ekkees.
Issi nabe nabetethan mokki ekkizadey he nabeza waaga demmana. Xillo as iza xillotetha gish mokki ekkikko he xilloza waaga ekkana.
Hessa gish ta intes tumu gays; oonikka hayta guuthatappe tana kaallizade gidida gish issi xu7a irxa haath ushshikko hinniska waagay dhayenna” gides.
Yesusikka bana kaalliza tammanne nam7u asatas azazo immi wursidappe guye tamarsanassinne sabakanas Galilan diza katamata bides.
Yohannisi qasho keeththan dishe Kirstoosas ooththiza hanota siydi bana kaallizayta izakko yeddidi “Asi ashshizaddey yaana geetettiday neneyee? Hara naaginoo?” giidi oychides.
<range>
Yesusikka zaaridi “Biidi inte sidayssanne inte beyidayssa Yohannisas yootite.
Qooqeti xeellettes; wobeti hammutettes; inchracha hargizayti paxettes; tulleti siyettes; hayqidayti hayqoppe paxi dendettes; manqotas Mishiraachcho qaalay yootettes.
Tanan dhuphetontadey anjettidade” gides.
Yohannisa kaallizayti bidappe guye Yesusikka asas Yohannisa gish “Ay beyanas duge bazzo bidetii? Carkoy qaathiza shomboqo beyanas yidetii?
Woykko ay beyanas kezidetii? Lo7o may7o may7idi lo7i uttidade beyana yidetii? Lo7o may7o may7idi lo7izayti kawota keeththan deettes.
Histin ay beyana kezidetii? Nabe beyana kezidetii? Ee, ta intes gays nabeppe aadhdhizayssa beyanassa.
“ ‘Ne bana oge nees giigissanadde neeppe kaseta ta nees kiittana geetettidi iza gish kase xaafettidadey izakko!’ gides.
Ta intes tumu gays; macasape yeletida asappe xammaqiza Yohannisa misatiza asi biitta bolla dendibenna. Gidikkoka Xoossa Kawoteththan as ubbafe laafa asi Yohannisappe aadhdhana.
“Xammaqiza Yohannisa wodeppe ha simmin ha7i gakkanaas Salo Kawoteththaya daro baaxeta bolla dawus. Mino asati xalla izo demmana.
Nabetikka Muse wogaykka wuri Yohannisa wode gakkanaas buroppe hananayssa yootida.
Histikko inte ekkana koykko izi yaana geetettida Elaasi izakko!
Siyiza haythi diza as siyo!
“Hayssa ha wode asaa aazan leemisoo? Giyan uttidi ba laggeta ‘Nu intes diiththi diixxin inte durbeekketa! Yeeho zilalth zilalin yeekkibeekketa!’ giza nayta misatetes.
<range>
Yohannisi muussafenne ushshafe naagetidi yida gish ‘Izi daydanthara dees’ gida.
Ta Asa Nay mashenne uyashe yiin ‘Hayssi miidi kallonta asa, ushshancha, qaraxa shiishshizaytassinne nagaranchatas laggekko!’ gida. Gido attin Xoossa eratethi ba ooson xilladus” gides.
Hessafe guye Yesusi izi malatata ooththida katama asay maarotethan gelonta aggida gish “Kuraziinenne Betesayda! Intena aayye ana! Inte bolla oosettida malatay Xiroose bollanne Sidoona bolla oosettidakko isti maaqa may7idinne bidinthan uttidi beni beni maarotethan gelanakoshin.
<range>
Hessa gish tani intes gizay pirda gallas intefe aadhdhi Xiroosessinne Sidoonas qixaatey kawuyana.
“Hanne Qifirnahoome pude salo dhoqu dhoqu gaanas koyadii? Gido attin neni duge Si7oole wodhandassa; ne bolla oosettida malatay Soddomen oosettidakko Soddomey hachchi gakkanaas daanakkoshin.
Hessa gish ta nena gizay pirda gallas qixaatey neeppe Soddomes kawuyana” gides.
He wode Yesusi “Salonne sa7a Godo! Ta Aawawu! Hayssa daro eranchataappene cincatappe qotada qeeri naytas ne qoncisida gish ta nena galatays.
Ta Aawawu! Ee hayssi ne sinthan lo7o ne shene gididi beettides.
“Wurikka ta Aawappe taas imettides; Aawappe attin Naaza gish eriza as baawa; qasse Naazappenne Naazi ba shenen qoncisida asappe haray aawa eriza as baawa.
“Toohoy deexxidayto, daaburidayto inte wurikka taakko ha yiite; takka intes shempo immana.
Ta qambara tookkite; taappekka tamarite; tani ta woznan aadanne ashke; inte shempos inte shempo demmana.
Ta qambaray shaykonne ta toohoy kawushsha” gides.
Hessafe guye Yesusi Sambata gallas kaththa giddora aadhdhi bides. Iza kaallizaytikka gafida gish tiya duuththidi shigechi muus oykkida.
Farsaaweeti hessa beyidi Yesusa “Hekko nena kaallizayti Sambata gallas ooththetanas bessontayssa ooththetes” gida.
Izikka istas zaaridi “Dawuteynne izara diza asati gafida wode izi ay ooththidakkone nababibeekketii?
Xoossa Keeththe gelidi Qeesetappe attin Dawuteynne izara dizayti bochchanas bessonta dummatida uketh mides.
Qasse Qeeseti Sambata shaaridi Xoossa Keeththa giddon ooso ooththikko mooro gidontayssa Muse wogappe nababibeekketii?
Gidikkoka ta intes gizay Xoossa Keeththafe aadhdhizadey haan dees.
‘Tani yarsho gidonta maaroteth dosays’ giza qaalay ay guussikkone inte erizakko xillota bolla pirdeketakkoshin.
Asa Nay Sambatas Goda” gides.
Heeppe izi gede aadhdhishe Ayhudata Woosa Keeththan gelides.
Henka issi kushe silidadey dees. Yesusa mootanas gaaso koydi “Sambata gallas pathanas bessizee?” giidi iza oychides.
Izikka ista “Intefe issade dorsi Sambata gallas ollan gelikko ba dorsa izi gelidi ollafe goochchi kessi erenee?
Histikko asi dorsafe keehi aadhdhenee? Hessa gish Sambata gallas lo7o oosoy digettenna” gides.
Qasseka addeza “Ne kushe piddisa!” gides; addezikka ba kushe piddisin hinko kusheza mala paxa gidides.
Gido attin Farsaaweeti heeppe kezidi, Yesusa wosti oykki wodhanakonne ba giddon zoretida.
Yesusi ista qofa eridi heeppe haraso sher7i gides. Daro derey iza kaallides; harganchatakka ubba pathides.
Izi oonakkone asas yootonta mala ista azazides.
Hessika haniday nabe Isayaasan “Ta dooridaynne ta izan ufayettiza ta nay hayssakko! Ta Ayanappe ta iza bolla wothana; izikka ammanonta deretas tumu pirda awajjana; marshettenna; woykko waassenna. Izas qaalaykka karen siyettenna; tuma pirda xoonos gaththana gakkanaas dincetti uttida shomboqokka menthenanne cuwattiza muqadakka toyssenna; Ayzaabeti iza ufayssan naagana” geetetti yootettida tinbite qaalay polettana.
<range>
<range>
<range>
<range>
Hessafe guye daydanthi oykkin xeellanassinne haasayanas dandayonta issi as Yesusakko ekki yida. Yesusikka iza pathin addezi xeellanassinne haasayanas dandayides.
Asay wurikka malaletidi “Hayssi addezi Dawute naashaa?” gides.
Gido attin Farsaaweeti hessa siyida wode “Hayssi addezi daydanth kessizay daydantha halaqa Bi7elizeebula wolqan xalla gidanas bessees” gida.
Yesusikka ista qofa eridi “Ba giddon issoy issafe shaakettiza kawotethi wurikka kundana; ba giddon shaakettiza katamay woykko keeththa asi minnenna.
Xala7ey Xala7e kessiza gidikko Xala7ey ba giddon shaakettides guussa. Hessatho hanikko iza kawotethi waani minnana dandayizee?
Tani Bi7elizeebula wolqan kessiza gidikko inte nayti aaza wolqan kessanee? Hessa gish inte nayti inte bolla pirdana.
Gido attin tani daydanth kessizay Xoossa Ayanan gidikko Xoossa Kawotethi inteko yides guussa.
“Woykko issi as wolqara dizadde keeththe gelidi miishe bonqana koyko kasetidi he wolqara diza addeza oykki qachonta wosti bonqanee? Qachidappe guye bonqana dandayees.
“Tanara gidontadey tanara eqettees; tanara issife shiishonta asi wurikka laalles.
Hessa gish ta intes tumu gays; nagara oosoynne cashshi wuri asas atto getettana shin Xillo Ayana cayidadey maarettenna.
Ay asikka asaa naa bolla haasayiza iita qaala gish maarettana shin, Xillo Ayana bolla haasayiza iita qaalay gidikko hayssa ha woden gidin woykko buro yaana woden gidin maaroy deenna.
“Mithi wuri ayfen eretizayssa mala inte lo7o ayfe demmanas intes lo7o mithi do; intes iita mithi diza gidikko inte iita ayfe ekkana.
Inteno mardzera diza shooshato! Inte iitata gidi uttidi wosti lo7o haasayanas dandayetii? Ulo giddon kumidazi duunara hasayettes.
“Lo7o asi ba woznan kunthi woththida lo7o qofappe lo7o haasayees; iita asikka ba woznan kunthi woththida iitatethafe iita yo7o kessees.
Gido attin ta intes gizay asay ba haasayida hada qaala ubba gish pirda gallas wurikka oyshettana.
Gaasoyka ne qaalappe dendidayssan ne xillada attananne ne qaalappe dendidayssan ne bolla pirdettana” gides.
Hessafe guye issi issi Muse woga tamarsizaytinne Farsaaweeti Yesusa “Astamaare! Nu neeppe malalisiza malata beyanas koyoos” gida.
Izi istas zaaridi “Ha iitanne layma yelettay malata oychees; gido attin nabe Yoonaasa malatappe attin hara malatay immetenna.
Yoonaasi gita mole ulo giddon heedzdzu qammanne heedzdzu gallas gam7ida mala Asa Naykka heedzdzu gallassinne heedzdzu qamma biitta garsan gam7ana.
Nanawe asay pirda gallas hayssa ha yelettara dendidi ha yeletta bolla pirdana; gaasoyka Nanawe asay Yoonaasa markatethan maaroteth gelida gishassa. Hekko Yoonaasappe aadhdhizadey haan dees.
Dugeha dere kawoya Solomoone erateth siyanas biitta gaxappe dendada yida gish pirda gallas iza hayssa yeletethara dendada ha yeletetha bolla pirdana. Hekko Solomooneppe aadhdhizadey hayssan dees.
“Tuna ayanay asappe kezidi shempo demmanas haaththi baynda mela biittan daaburees. Gido attin ba koyiza shempo demmenna.
Hessafe qasse kase ta dizaso simma baana giidi beeniso izi simmishin kase izi dizasoy aykkoynne baynda mela keeththe gididi geeyedayssanne giigeti dizayssa demmees.
Hessafe biidi hara baappe iitiza laapun iita ayanata banara ekkidi yees. Istika he addezan gelidi de7ana. He addezas kase duussafe guye duussay iita gidana. Hayssa iita yeletethaska hessa mala hanana” gides.
Yesusi asaas yootishin iza aayeyanne ishati iza yoochana koydi karen eqqida.
Issi asi “Hekko ne aayanne ne ishati nena haasayissanas karen eqqidi nena koyeettes” gides.
Yesusikka “Ta aaya oonee? Ta ishatich, isti oonantee?” gides.
Ba kushera bana kaallizaytakko malatidi “Ta aayanne ta ishati haytanta.
Salon diza ta Aawa shene ooththizayti wurikka taas isha, michonne aayo” gides.
He gallassi Yesusi keeththafe kare kezidi abba lanqen uttides.
Daro derey iza yuuyi aadhdhi giddoththida gish asaa abba gaxan aggidi wogolo gido geli uttidi,
daro yo7o leemisora “Issi goshshanchay zereth zeranas kezides.
Izi zerishin issi issi zerethi oge duunan wodhdhin kafoti yiidi maxi mida.
Issi issi zerethi melanne shuchchatiza biitta bolla wodhdhin biittay mela biitta gidida gish elle caarides.
Gido attin away awattin shullidinne xapho yeddonta aggida gish melides.
Issi issi zerethay aguntha giddon wodhdhides; agunthayka diccidi caarechcha cuullides.
Hara zerethikka lo7o orde biittan wodhdhidi ayfeka ayfides; issoy xeetu, issoy usuppun tammu issoy heedzdzu tammu ayfe immides.
Siyiza haythi dizadey siyo!” gi yootides.
Hessafe iza kaallizayti izakko shiiqidi “Aazas leemisora yootay?” gida.
Izikka istas “Salo Kawoteththa xuura eroy intes imettides; istas gidikko imettibenna.
Dizaddes dizayssa bolla gujettananne darana shin bayndadefe hinna dizaarakka eketaychana.
Ta hayssatho leemisora yootizay isti siyishe ezgonta gishshinne xeellishe demmoonta gishassa.
“Isayaasi ‘Inte sisa siyanashin yuushi qoppeketa; xeelo xeellana shin woznan wotheketa; dereza woznay muumides; ista haythayka siyenna; xeellonta mala ba ayfe qilm7ida; hessi bayndakko isti ba ayfera beyidinne ba haythara siydi ba woznan yuushi qoppidi taakko ha simmin ta ista pathana shin’ gida tinbite qaalay istan polettides.
<range>
“Inte ayfey xeelliza gishshinne inte haythati siyiza gish inte anjettidayta.
Ta intes tumu gays; daro nabetinne daro xillo asati ha7i inte beyizayssa beyanassinne ha7i inte siyizayssa siyanas amottida shin istas hanibenna.
“Histikko ha7i zeretha leemisoza birsheth siyite:
Kawoteththa qaala siydi yuushi qopponta ay asa woznappekka Xala7ey yiidi zerettida zeretha eeson maxichana. Hessika oge bolla wodhdhida zeretha.
Shuchcha bolla zerettidayssi qaala siyida mala ufayssan siydi heerakka ufayssan ekizade misatees.
Gido attin xapho yeddanas dandayonta aggida gish daro gam7onta qaala geedon metoynne goodeteththi yiza wode eleli dhuphetes.
Aguntha giddon zerettida zerethay qaala siydi hayssa ha alamezas daro metotethanne duretetha qofan balettidinne cuulettidi ayfe immoonta asa mala.
Lo7o biittan zeretida zerethay qasse qaala siydi yuushi qoppizade misatees; tummu ayfe ayfees; issoy xeetu, issoy usuppun tammu, issoy heedzdzu tammu ayfe immides” gides.
Yesusi qasseka hara leemiso istas “Salo Kawotethi ba goshsha gaden lo7o zereth zeridade misatees.
Gido attin asi wuri ichchida wode morkey yiidi gisteza giddon leeshsho zeridi bides.
Gistezi diccidi ayfe ayfiza wode leeshshoyka izara issife beettides.
“Katha goda ashkarati godazakko shiiqidi ‘Godo! Neni ne goshshan lo7o zereth zerabeekii? Hayssi leeshshoy awappe yidee?’ gida.
“Izikka istas ‘Hessa morkey ooththides’ gides. Ashkaratikka ‘Nu biidi leeshshoza shoddana mala koyay?’ gi oychida.
“Izikka istas, ‘Akay hanenna; gaasoyka inte leeshshoza shoddishe gistezara gaththi shoddana;
aggite! Maxa wodey gakkanaas issife dicco; he wode maxizayti leeshshoza kasetidi qori maxidi taman xuuganas mirqen mirqen qachite; gisteza qasse shiishshidi gootaran gelthite’ gaada ta intes yootana” gi yootides.
Hara leemiso istas “Salo Kawotethi issi asi ba gade giddon zerida barzaafe mitha ayfe mala.
Barzaafe mitha ayfey hara mitha ayfe ubbaafe daro laafa gidikkoka diccada mitha ubbaafe gita gidawus. Salo kafotikka izi hagga bolla keexxidi daana gakkanaas gita mithi gidawus” gides.
Ha7ikka hara leemiso istas “Salo Kawotethi macassi liixey dendana mala liixe giddon gujida guutha irsho misatawus” gides.
Yesusi hayssa ubba asas leemisora yootides. Leemisoy baynda issinokka yootibenna.
Hessanka kase nabe duunan “Ta duuna ta leemison doyana; alamey medhetosappe ha simmin qotetidayssa ta haasayana” geetetti yootettidays polettides.
Hessafe Yesusi asaa aggidi so gelides. Iza kaallizayti izakko shiiqidi “Katha giddon diza leeshshoza gish ne yootida leemisoza birsheth nuus yoota” gida.
Izikka istas zaaridi “Lo7o zereth zeriday Asa Naa.
Goshshay hayssa alameza; lo7o zerethay Kawoteththa nayta gididayssa bessees; leeshshoy qasse Xala7e nayta.
Leeshshoza zeridi bida morkey Daabuloosa. Maxa wodey alame wursethi gidishin maxizayti Xoossa kiitanchata.
“Leeshshoy qoretidi taman xuugetizayssa mala alame wursethan hessatho hanana.
Asa Nay ba kiitanchata kiittana; istika nagaras gaaso gididaytanne iita ooththizayta iza Kawoteththa giddofe ubba qori kessana.
Yeehoy dizasonne ach garcizason daro wolqama taman ista yeggana.
Hessa wode xilloti ba Aawa Kawoteththan awa arshe mala poo7ana. Siyiza haythi dizadey siyo!
“Salo Kawotethi gade giddon qotetida miishe misatees. Issi as he miishayo demmidi zaari qottides. Ufayssafe dendidayssan biidi baas dizazi ubba bayzidi he miishiya diza biitta shamides.
“Hessathoka Salo Kawotethi al7o worqa koyiza zal7ancha misatees.
Daro al7o gidida inqo giza shuchcha demmida mala biidi baas dizazi ubba bayzidi shamides.
“Qasseka Salo Kawotethi abba giddon yegettidi dumma dumma mole oykkida mole gite misatees.
Mole oykkizayti gitey kumin goochchidi abba lanqe kessida. Heen uttidi lo7o lo7o mole qoridi keeshen gujida. Iita moleta wora yeggida.
Alame wursethan hessatho hanana. Kiitanchati yiidi nagaranchata xillotappe shaakkidi yeekkizasonne ach garcizaso gede to7onta taman yeggana.
<range>
“Yesusi ista hayssi wuri intes gelidee?” gides. Istika “Ee” gida.
Izikka zaaridi “Hessa gish Salo Kawoteththa xuuray gelida Muse woga tamarsizadey oonikka izas minji woththida al7o miishafe oorathanne kase gal7a miish kessizade misatees” gides.
Yesusikka hayta leemisota yooti wursidi heeppe haraso bides.
Gede ba dere biidi Ayhudata Woosa Keeththan asa tamarso oykkides. Istika malalettidi “Hayssi addezi hayssa eratethanne hayta malatata ooththana wolqa awappe demmidee?
Hayssi anaxeza naa dennee? Iza aayey sunthi Maaramo gidenee? Iza ishati Yaqoobe, Yoosefe, Simoonanne Yuhuda gidettennee?
Micheti nunara dizayta gidettennee? Histin hayssi addezi hayssa ubba awappe ekidee?” gida.
Hessa gish isti izi gizayssa ekkibeetenna. Yesusikka istas “Nabey ba dereninne ba keeththan bonchettenna attin harason bonchettes” gides.
Isti ammanonta aggida gish daro malatata heen ooththibenna.
He wode Galila dere haariza Herdoosi asay Yesusa nashizayssa siydes.
Herdoosi ba ashkaratas “Hessa gidikko, Xammaqiza Yohannisi hayqoppe dendidi yides guussakka! Hayssi wuri gita malatay iza kushen oosettizay hessassa” gides.
Herdoosi ba isha Piliphoosa macho Herodiyadi gaason Yohannisa oythidi qasho keeththan yeggides.
Gaasoyka Yohannisi Herdoosa “Ne izo ekkana mala woga gidenna gida gishassa” gides.
Herdoosikka Yohannisa wodhanas koyishin asay Yohannisa nabe mala xeelliza gish babbides.
Herdoosi ba yeletetha gallas Herodiyadi naya yethan iza ufayssida gish naya iza oychidaz ubba immanas izis caaqides.
<range>
Nayakka aayey zoren “Xammaqiza Yohannisa hu7e keren wothada ha7i hannin taas imma” gadus.
He wode kawozi izas mishettides. Gido attin caaqida gishshinne izara diza imathata gish giidi nay oyshoy polettana mala azazides.
Kiittidinne Yohannisa woyne keeththan dishin qoodhe qanxisides.
Qanxetida hu7eza keren woththidi nays immida. Nayakka ekkada ba aayeys immadus.
Yohannisa kaallizayti iza aha ekkidi moogidinne hanidayssa ubba Yesusas yootida.
Hessa siyida mala Yesusi kase ba dizaso aggidinne wogolon gelidi barka hara asi bayndaso bides. Dereyka hessa siydi katamay dizasoppe tohora iza kaallides.
Yesusikka wogolozappe wodhdhishe daro asa beyidi asas mishettides. Saketizaytaka pathides.
Gadey qammi qammi bizayssa beyidi iza kaallizayti izakko shiiqidi “Hayssi nu dizasoy bazzo; gadeyka qammi qammi biza gish gede gutatan gutatan biidi baasi maanaz shammana mala asaa yedda” gida.
Gido attin Yesusikka ista “Inte asas maanaz immite attin asay baanas koshshenna” gides.
Istika izas zaaridi “Hayssan nuus ichashu ukethinne nam7u moleppe attin haray baawa” gida.
Izikka ista “Ane heyta dizayta haa taas ekki yiite” gides.
Qasseka asay maata bolla uttana mala azazides. Ichashu ukethanne nam7u moleta ba kushen oykkidi ba ayfe pude salo dhoqu histi galatidi, uketha menthi bana kaallizaytas immides. Istika asaas immida.
Asay wurikka miidi kallides. Hessafe guye iza kaallizayti asaappe mishin attidayssa tammanne nam7u leemate kumeth shiishida.
Mida asay macasattinne guutha nayti gujettonta attumasay xalala ichashu shi gidana.
Heerakka iza kaallizayti wogolon gelidi gede pinth izappe kasetidi pinana mala azazidi asa moyzanas baassi guye attides.
Dereza moyzidappe guye woossa woossanas barka zuma bolla kezides. Gadey dhuminka yaan zuma bolla barka dees.
Hessa wode wogoloya abba kantha bishin dambalay dendidi daro metotho oykkides.
Qamappe koyro kuttoy baqqishin Yesusi abba bollara hamutidi iza kaallizayti dizaso yides.
Yesusa kaallizaytikka izi abba bollara hamuti yishin beyi babbida gish iza moytile giidinne waassida.
Yesusi heerakka “Aykkoy ba! Tanakko; babbofte!” gides.
Phexroosi “Godo! Nena gidikko ta abba bollara hamutada neekko baana mala tana azaza” gides.
Yesusi iza “Haaya!” gides. Phexroosikka wogolozappe wodhdhidi haaththa bollara hamutidi Yesusakko yides.
Gido attin carkoza wolqa biyidi babbida gish haaththan miteteth oykkidi “Godo! Tana ashsha!” gi waassides.
Yesusi heerakka ba kushe yeddi oykkidi “Neno, ammanoy paccidaysso! Aazas sidhadii?” gides.
Yesusinne Phexroosi wogolozan gelida mala carkoy sirph gides.
Hessafe guye wogolon dizayti “Neni tumu Xoossa Naa!” giidi izas goynnida.
Yesusinne iza kaallizayti abba pinnidi Gensereexe geetettizaso gakkida.
Heen dizayti Yesusa gididayssa eridi, he heeran yuuyi aadhdhanas diza asaas kiita yeddida. Asaykka harganchata ubba Yesusakko ehides.
Harganchati iza afala xeera xalala bochchana mala Yesusa woossida. Bochchidayti wurikka paxida.
Qasseka Yerusalameppe yida Farsaaweetinne Muse woga tamarsizayti Yesusakko shiiqidi
“Nena kaallizayti kase nu aawata woga aazas dhayssizoo? Quma maanas kushe mecetetenna” gida.
Yesusikka istas “Inte inte wogas giidi Xoossa azazo ays shaaretii?
Xoossi ‘Ne aayiyonne ne aawa boncha; ba aawa bolla woykko ba aayi bolla iita qaala haasayidaddey hayqo!’ gi azazides.
inte gidikko ay asikka ba aawa woykko ba aayo ‘Ta intes ooththanas bessizaz ay miishekka Xoossas yarsho ooththa shiishadis’ giikko,
‘He addezi ba aawa woykko ba aayo bonchides’ geeta; hessa gish inte woga gish Xoossa qaala shaareta.
Inteno, qoodheppe qommon hanizayto! Isayaasi inte gish yootishe ‘Hayssi derey tana duunan xalala bonchees; woznay gidikko taappe haakkides; mela hada tana goynnees; ista timirteykka asi woththida woga’ gididi sinthafe hananayssa yootidayssi tumakko” gides.
<range>
<range>
Yesusi asaa baako xeygidi “Siyite woznan woththite.
As tunisizay izaade duunara ha kezizayssafe attin duunara duge gelizay tunisenna” gides.
Qasse iza kaallizayti izakko shiiqidi “Farsaaweeti ne gidayssa siydi hanqettidayssa eradii?” gida.
Izi istas “Ta Aawa saloyssi tokkonta mithi wurikka dhoqallettana.
Ista aggagite isti qooqeti kaalethiza qooqeta gidida gish, qooqeti qooqe kaalethikko nam7ay issoy issara oyketidi aafon wullana” gides.
Phexroosi Yesusa “Ne yootida leemisoza nuus birsha” gides.
Izikka “Inte ha7i gakkanaska eribeekketa guussee?
Duunara gelizay wuri duge qanthe kanthidi gede kare kezizayssa ereketii?
Duunara kezizay gidikko woznappe pultees. As tunisizay hessa.
Iita qofay, shempo wodhoy, laymay, laymatanas qaaqatoy, kaysoy, wordo markatethinne asa sunth mooroy wuri woznappe pultees.
As tunisizay haytantafe attin kushe mecetonta muusi as tunisenna” gides.
Yesusi heeppe kezidi gede Xiroosenne Sidoona geetettiza dere bides.
Issi Kanaane macassi dizaara he heerappe kezada Yesusakko yaada “Godo, Dawute nawu! Taas miisheta! Ta naya tuna ayanay oykkin keeha waayawus” gaada waassadus.
Gido attin izi issi qaalakka izis zaaribenna. Histin he wode iza kaallizayti izakko shiiqidi “Nuna kaalla kaalla waayssiza gish ne izo moyzikkochii?” giidi iza oychida.
Izikka istas “Tani Isra7eele keeththafe dhayida dorsatakko xalala kiitetadis” gides.
Macasayakka Yesusa toho bolla kundada “Godo! Tana maaddarki!” gadus.
Izikka izis zaaridi “Nayta kath ekkidi kana butulatas yegganas bessenna” gides.
Izakka “Ee Godo; butalatikka ba goda maaddappe gaden wodhdhida kath maxi meettes” gadus.
Hizgin Yesusikka macasayo “Hanne macasaye, ne ammanoy gita! Ne koyda mala nees hano” gides. Macasay nayakka heerakka paxadus.
Yesusi heeppe dendidi Galila Abba lanqe biidi heen diza issi zuma bolla kezi uttides.
Qoodan daro derey wobeta, qooqeta, silata, haasayonta duudeta harataka daro harganchata ehidi iza sinthan woththides; izikka ista pathides.
Duudey haasayishin, toho silay paxishin, wobey siti giidi hamutishin, qooqey xeellishin beyidi asay malalettides; Isra7eele Godakka galatides.
Yesusi bana kaallizayta xeygidi “Asay tanara heedzdzu gallas gam7ida gishshinne maana kaththi baynda gish asay tana michees. Oge bollan gafan daaburidi kundonta mala mela ulora yeddanas koyikke” gides.
Iza kaallizayti “Hayssan aykkoykka baynda bazzo biittan hayssa keena dere mizanas gidiza quma nu awappe demmanee?” gida.
Yesusi ista “Intes aappun ukethi dizee?” gi oychin istika “Laapun ukethinne qii guutha moleti deettes” gida.
Izikka derezi gaden uttana mala azazides.
Laapun ukethanne moleza ba kushen oykkidi galatidappe guye menthidi bana kaallizaytas immides; istika deraas gishida.
Asay wurikka miidi kallides; Yesusa kaallizayti asaappe attidayssa laapun leemate kumeth shiishida.
Midaytikka naytinne macasay baynda addeti xalala oyddu shi gidida.
Yesusi dereza moyzidappe guye wogolon gelidi Megidoone geetettizaso bides.
Farsaaweetinne Saduqaawe geetettizayti Yesusakko shiiqidi iza paacanas “Saloppe malata bessa” giidi oychida.
Izikka istas “Omarsa wode saloy zo7ikko ‘Gadey awattana’ geeta.
Wonta bolla ‘Saloy deexikko deexides; hachchi iray bukkana’ geeta; salo medha xeelidi shaakki ereeta shin ta yaana wode malata shaakki eranas dandayekketa.
Hayssi iitanne layma yelettay malata koyees; gido attin Yoonaasa malatappe attin hara malatay izas imettenna” gides. Yesusi ista heen aggagidi haraso bides.
Abba pinnida mala Yesusa kaallizayti quma oykkanayssa balettida.
Yesusikka “Qoppite; Farsaaweeta irshofenne Saduqaaweta irshofe naagettite” gides.
Isti qasse ba giddon “Nuni kath oykkonta gish hessa gides” giidi issoy issara haasayettida
Yesusikka ista qofa eridi “Inteno ammanoy paccidayto! Kath oykkonta gish aazas issoy issara haasayetetii?
Ichashu ukethi ichashu shi asas gididi aapun leematey tirpin inte denthidakkonne yuushi qoppeketii?
Hessathoka laapun ukethi oyddu shi asas gididi aapun leematey tirpin inte denthidakkonne woznan woththibeekketa guussee?
Histin ta intes yootiday kaththa gish gidontayssa waandi yuushi qoppeketii? Ha7ikka Farsaaweeta irshofenne Saduqaaweta irshofe naagettite” gides.
Ha7i izi ista qofisizay bukeeso denthanas gujiza irsho gish gidonta Farsaaweetanne Saduqaaweta timirtefe naagettana mala gididayssi istas gelides.
Yesusi Qisaariya Piliphisiyoose geetettiza biitta gakkida wode bana kaallizayta “Asay tana Asa Naa oona gizee?” giidi oychides.
Istika “Issi issi asay ‘Xammaqiza Yohannisa’ gees; bagga asay ‘Elaasa’ gees; baggay ‘Ermaasa woykko nabetappe issade gidonta aggenna’ gees” gida.
Izikka ista “Inte tana oona geetii?” gides.
Simoona geetettiza Phexroosi “Neni Kirstoosa de7o Xoossa Naa gidikkii?” giidi zaarides.
Yesusi “Yoona naa Simoona neni anjettidade! Nees hayssa qoncisiday salon diza ta Aawappe attin ashonne suuthi gidenna.
Neni zaalla; hayssa zaalla bolla tani ta Woosa Keeththe keexxana; Gaanname pengetikka izo xoonetenna.
Salo Kawoteththa qulpeta ta nees immana; neni biitta bolla hano gizay wuri salonikka hanana. Biitta bolla ne hanoppo gidayssi wurikka salonikka hanenna” gides.
Qasseka izi Kirstoosa gididayssa isti oonaska yootonta mala bana kaallizaytas lo7ethi yootides.
Hessafe ha simmin Yesusi Yerusalame baanayssa, heen dere cimatan, Qeeseta halaqataninne Muse woga tamarsizayta kushen waaye ekkanayssa, hayqqanayssanne heedzdzantho gallas hayqoppe dendanayssa bana kaallizaytas qoncisidi yootides.
Phexroosi Yesusa gede issi bagga zaaridi “Godo! Hayssi ne bolla gakkofo!” giidi hanqides.
Yesusi Phexroosakko shiiqidi “Haysso Xala7e! Hayssafe kichcha! Neni asazappe attin Xoossa yo7oy ne wozna giddon baynda gish ne taas dhuphe gidadasa” gides.
Qasseka Yesusi bana kaallizaytas “Tana kaallanas dosiza asi bana kado; ba masqale tookkidi tana kaallo.
Ba shempo ashshana koyiza asi wuri dhayssana; gido attin ba shempo ta gish dhayssizadey ashshana.
Asi alamen dizaz kumeth haarid ba shempo dhayssikko iza ay maaddanee? Woykko asi ba shempo gish qanxana dandayizazi aazee?
Asa Nay ba Aawa bonchoranne salo kiitanchatara yaana; issas issas iza ooso mala izaade waaga immana.
Ta intes tumu gays; hayssan eqqida asata giddofe Asa Nay ba kawoteththara yishin beyana gakkanaas hayqoy ista bochonta asati deettes” gides.
Usuppun gallassafe guye Yesusi Phexroosanne Yaqoobe qasseka Yaqoobe isha Yohannisa banara ekkidi istara xalala issi dhoqa zuma bolla kezides.
Isti heen dishin Yesusa medhay laamettides; iza ayfesoy Awa arshe mala poo7ides; iza may7oykka poo7o mala xolqides.
Heerakka Museynne Elaasi Yesusara haasayishe istas beettides.
Phexroosi Yesusa “Godo! Nu hannin dizaakko nuus lo7okko! Ne shene gidikko issi daase nees, issi daase Muses, issi daase Elaasas heedzdzu daase ooththoo?” gides.
Izi buro haasayan dishin poo7iza shaaray ista kammides; shaara gaaththara “Tani izan ufayettiza ta dosiza ta nay hayssa; izi gizaz siyite” giza qaala giiris siyettides.
Iza kaallizaytikka hessa siyida wode dagammidi biitta bolla gufannida.
Yesusi istako shiiqi ista ba kushen bochidi “Dendite; babbofte!” gides.
Isti dhoqu gi xeellishin Yesusappe attin izara hara as oonakka be7ibeetenna.
Isti zuma bollafe wodhdhishin Yesusi “Asa Nay hayqoppe dendana gakkanaas inte beyoyssa oonaska yootonta mala” gi azazides.
Yesusa kaallizayti “Histin Muse woga tamarsizayti, Elaasi kasetidi yaana bessees aazas gizoo?” giidi oychida.
Izikka istas “Tumakko; Elaasi yiidi wursikka giigissana giidi zaarides.
Ta intes gizay Elaasi yides; gido attin asay ba koyda mala iza bolla ooththides attin iza erbeenna; hessathoka Asa Nay ista kushen waaye beyana” gides.
He wode Yesusa kaallizayti Yesusi istas yootizays Xammaqiza Yohannisa gish gididayssa erida.
Yesusinne iza kaallizayti asaakko simmida mala issi asi Yesusakko shiiqidi iza sinthan gulbatidi “Godo! Ta naa dayssa bollafe yeggiza hargey daro waayssiza gish taas maarariki! Daro wode taman kundees; haaththanka gellees.
<range>
Tani naaza nena kaallizaytakko ehadis shin isti iza pathana dandayibeetenna” gides.
Yesusi “Neno ammanonta geella yelettazo! Ayde gakkanaas ta intenara daanee? Qasse ayde gakkanaas ta intena dandayanee? Ane naaza ha taakko ehite” gides.
Hessafe guye Yesusi daydantha seeridi naazappe kessides; naazikka he saateppe simmidi paxides.
Yesusa kaallizayti xalala izakko shiiqidi “Nuni daydantha kessanas aazas dandaybeykkonii?” giidi oychida.
Izikka istas “Intes ammanoy pace gidida gish dandaybekketa; ta intes tumu gays; qeeri gaashe ayfe mala ammanoy inte bolla dizaakko hayssa zuma ‘Hayssafe dendada gede ba!’ inte gidakko izi intes baana. Intena xoonanay deenna.
Hayssa malay gidikko xoomaninne woossan attin haran kezenna” gides.
Isti Galilan issife dishin Yesusi ista “Tana Asa Naa asas aaththi immana.
Istika iza wodhana; izikka heedzdzantho gallas dendana” giin iza kaallizayti keehi mishettida.
Yesusinne iza kaallizayti Qifirnahoome geetettizaso gakkidappe guye Xoossa Keeththa giira ekkizayti Phexroosakko shiiqidi “Inte astamarey Xoossa Keeththa giira nam7u dinareza ays qanxenee?” gida.
Izikka istas “Qanxees” gides. Phexroosi so gelida mala Yesusi kasetidi “Simoona dere kawoti giira gidin woykko qaraxa gidin ba naytappe ekkizoyee? Haratappe ekkiza misatizee?” gides.
Phexroosikka “Haratappe ekkettes” gides. Yesusi “Histikko nayta bolla accoy ba guussaka!
Histikkokka ista nu dhuphethonta mala ne mole oykkiza gite ekka baada abban yegga; koyro oykkida moleza duuna ne pooqada demmiza miisha ekkada ta suntharanne ne sunthara giira qanxa” gides.
He wode Yesusa kaallizayti izakko shiiqidi “Salo Kawoteththan nu garasan ubbafe aadhdhanadey oonee?” gi oychida.
Yesusi issi naa xeygi ehidi ista giddon essidi “Ta intes tumu gays; inte simmonta ixikkonne guutha nayta mala hanonta ixikko mulekka Salo Kawoteth gelekketa.
<range>
Hessa gish ha naaza mala bana ziqqisizadey Salo Kawoteththan ubbafe aadhdhana.
Hayssa mala guutha naa ta sunthan ekkizadey tana ekkees.
“Gido attin tana ammaniza guuthatappe issade dhuphethizay deexo woxa shuch ba qoodhen qashettidi abba ciimman yegettidi mitettikko izas lo7o gidana” gides.
Hanna alameya asi dhuphana gaaso gidida gish izis aayye-ana! Dhuphey yuus aggenna shin dhuphezas gaaso gidizaddes aayye-ana!
Ne kushey woykko ne tohoy nena dhuphanas gaaso gidikko neeppe qanxa digga! Ne nam7u kushera woykko nam7u tohora gede merna taman yegettanappe wobe woykko toho sila gidada he gede de7oy dizaso geloy nees lo7ana.
Hessathoka ne ayfey nees dhuphe gidikko neeppe kessa yegga! Nam7u ayfera gede Gaanname taman ne yegetanappe issi ayfera de7oy dizaso ne gelizaysi nees lo7o.
“Hayta guuthata giddofe issiniyoka inte kadhonta mala naagettite! Ta intes tumu gays; salon diza ista kiitanchati salon ta Aawa ayfeso ubba gallas xeelletes.
Asa Nay dhayidayta ashshanas yides.
“Ane taas yootite issades xeetu dorsi diikko qasse istafe issina dhaykko, hanko uddufun tammanne uddufunata zuma bolla yeggidi dhayidaro koyana bi erennee?
Ta intes tumu gays; hanko dhayonta attida uddufun tammanne uddufun dorsatappe aaththidi beettida dorsayn ufayetees.
Hessathoka ha guuthata giddofe issoy dhayana mala salon diza inte aawa shene gidenna.
“Ne ishay nena qohikko izakko baada iza xalala nenara ekkada iza mooro izas yoota; izi ne giza siyikko ne isha ne as ooththassa.
Izi ne gizayssa siyonta ixikko yo7oy wuri nam7u markan woykko heedzdzu markan ladhdhiza gish issade woykko nam7u as nenara ekka baada iza hasayssa.
Izi istaka siyonta ixikko Woosa Keeththas yoota; Woosa Keeththayokka siyonta ixikko izaade ne ammanontade malanne yootin simmonta iita asa mala qooda.
“Ta intes tumu gays; inte biitta bolla qachiday wurikka salonikka qashettida gidana; inte biitta bolla birshidazi salonikka birshettidayssa gidana.
Qasseka ta intes tumu gays; inte biitta bolla nam7u gididi ay miishikka ero ero giidi inte oychikko salon diza ta Aaway intes immana.
Nam7u woykko heedzdzu gididi ta sunthan inte shiiqizason heen inte giddon ta daana” gides.
Hessa wode Phexroosi Yesusakko shiiqidi “Godo! Ta ishay tana qohikko ta izas aapunto atto goo? Laapunto atto goo?” gides.
Yesusikka izas zaaridi “Laapun tammuto laapun attin laapunto xalala ga, giikke;
“Hessa gish Salo Kawotethi ashkara bolla diza miishe shiishana koyda kawo misatawus.
Miisha qooda oykkida mala iza ashkaratappe daro milone bira accoy iza bolla dizadde ekki yida.
Ashkaraykka iza bolla diza accoza qanxoy xoonda gish izikka iza machiyakka iza naytinne izas dizazi wuri bayzettidi miishay qanxettana mala iza goday azazides.
He wode ashkarazi godaza toho bolla kundidi ‘Tani ta bolla diza accoza wursi nees qanxana gakkanaas taas guutha wode immarki!’ giidi woossides.
Iza godayka izas mishettidi iza accoza wursi maaridi yeddides.
“He ashkaraykka ba goda achchafe kezida mala guutha accoy iza bolla diza ba lagge demmidinne ‘Ne bolla diza ta miishayo ha7i hannin qanxa’ giidi cuulli oykkides.
He iza lagge ashkaray ‘Taas guutha wode immarki! Ta nees qanxana’ giidi iza toho bolla kundidi woossides.
“Gido attin izas guutha wode immanas koyonta ixidi iza laggezi ba bolla diza accoza qanxana gakkanaas qasho keeththan yeggides.
Hessa izi ooththishin beyida asaynne hanko iza lagge ashkarati daro mishettida. Biidikka hanidayssa wursi ba godas yootida.
“He wode godazi he ashkara xeygisi ehidi, haysso neno! Iitazo, ne tana woossin ne bolla diza accoza ta nees aggadisishin ta nena maarida mala nekka ne laggeza maaranas bessenee?
<range>
Giidi iza bolla diza accoza izi wursi qanxana gakkanaas qachana mala qachizaytas aaththi immides.
Hessa gish inte issoy issa woznappe maaronta aggikko salon diza ta Aawayka intena maarenna” gides.
Yesusi yooti wursidappe guye Galila aggidi Yordanoose pinthan diza Yuhuda awurajja bides.
Daro derey iza heen kaallin izikka harganchata pathides.
Farsaaweeti iza paccanaas izakko shiiqidi ay gaasonka “Asi ba macho anji yeddana bessizee?” giidi oychida.
Izikka istas “Xoossi koyroppe macanne adde medhdhidayssa nababibeykketii? gides.
Qasseka ‘Asi aawanne aayo aggidi ba machira issife gides. Nam7aykka issi asho gidettes’ geetettidayssi hayssa geedon gidenee? gides.
Nam7ay issi asho attin sinthafe nam7u gidettenna. Hessa gish Xoossi gaththi waaxidayssa asi shaakkofo” gides.
Istika izas “Histin Musey ‘Asi ba macho anji yeddida anjo waraqata izis immi yeddo’ giidi aazas azazidee?” gida.
Yesusikka istas “Musey inte wozna muumeteth beyidi macheta inte anjana mala piqaade intes immides attin koyroppe hessa mala gidenna.
“Ta intes tumu gays; ba azinappe harara laymatonta dishin ba macho anjidi hara macho ekizadey wuri laymatees. Anjettidarokka ekkizadey izira laymatees” gides.
Yesusa kaallizayti izas “Machi wogaynne azina wogay hayssa mala gidikko macho ekkonta agoy lo7o” gida.
Gido attin Yesusi istas “Issi issi imettida asatappe attin hayssa timirteza oonikka ekkanas dandayenna.
Gaasoyka issi issi asay ba aayi uloppe yelettishe shuufa gididi yelettees; issi issi asay asa kushen qaaratettidi gundulees; issi issi asay Salo Kawoteththas giidi bana barka gundula ooththiza asikka dees. Hayssa ekkanas dandayizaddey ekko” gides.
He wode Yesusi ista bolla ba kushe woththidi woossana mala guutha nayta izakko ekki ehida; gido attin iza kaallizayti nayta ehida asata bolla hanqettida.
Yesusi “Nayti haa taakko yeeto; diggofte; Salo Kawotethi haytanta malassa!” gides.
Ba kushe nayta bolla woththidi anjidappe guye heeppe dendi bides.
Hessafe guye issadey Yesusakko shiiqidi “Astamaare! Merna de7o demmanas tani lo7o ooso ay ooththoo?” giidi oychides.
Yesusikka “Tana aazas lo7o gish oychay? Lo7oy issi Xoossa xalala; gede de7oy dizaso ne gelana koykko azazota naaga” gides.
Addezi “Azazoti awaytee?” giidi oychides. Yesusikka zaaridi “As wodhoppa; laymatoppa; kaysotoppa; wordo markatofa; ne aawanne ne aayo boncha; ne shooro ne mala siiqa” gides.
<range>
Naatethazi zaaridi “Hayssa wursa ta naagadis; haray aazi taas paccidee?” gides.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Ne mule xillana koykko baada ne haaridaz wursa bayzada miisha wursa manqotas imma; neni salon miish demmandasa; hessafe guye simma yaada tana kaalla” gides.
Addezi hessa siydi izas daro miishi diza gish keehippe mishetishe bides.
Yesusi bana kaallizayta “Ta intes tumu gays; dureti Salo Kawoteth gelanayssi daro meto.
Qasseka tani intes gizay durey Salo Kawoteth gelanayssafe gaamellay narpe lukkora aadhdhethi kawuyana” gides.
Hessa siyida iza kaallizayti daro qoppidi “Histin ooni attanas dandayizee?” giidi Yesusa oychida.
Yesusikka ista xeelidi “Hayssi asa achchan dandayettenna; Xoossa achchan gidikko wurikka dandayettes” gides.
Phexroosi izas zaaridi “Nu wursikka aggidi nena kaallidos; histin ha7i nu ay demmaneshaa?” gides.
Yesusikka istas “Ta intes tumu gays; Asa Nay buro yaana ooratha alamen ba boncho alga bolla uttiza wode inte tana kaallidayti tammanne nam7u alga bolla uttidi tammanne nam7u Isra7eele nayta bolla pirdana.
Ta suntha gish giidi ba keeththe, ba ishata, ba micheta, ba aawa, ba aayonne ba nayta, woykko ba biitta aggiza asi wuri xeetu kushe dakko ekkana; medhina de7okka laattana.
Gido attin daro sinthe gidida asati guye gidana; daro guyen diza asati sinthatana.
“Salo Kawotethi ba woyne atakilte giddon ooththiza oosanchata qaxaranas maaladora kezida issi atakiltey diza gadadde misatawus.
Issi gallasa damoza gidizaz hasayettidi giigidappe guye oosanchata woyne atakilte ooso oythides.
“Maalado heedzdzu saaten kezidi oosoy baynda mela giyay eqqizason eqqida hara asata demmides.
‘Inte biidi ta woyne giddon ooththite; ta intes bessiza miishe immana’ gides.
Istika bida. Qasseka gallassafe usuppun saateninne uddufun saate bolla kezidi hara oosanchata ooson gelthides.
Omarsa wode tammanne issi saate gidiza wode kezidi coo eqqidayta harata demmidi ‘Inte kumeththa gallas oosoy baynda aazas hayssan eqqetii?’ giidi oychides.
“Istika ‘Nuna ooththisiza asi dhayida gish eqqidos’ gida. Izikka ista ‘Inteka biidi ta woyne atakilte giddon ooththite’ gides.
“Gadey qammishin woyne atakilteza goday oosanchata alafezas ‘Guyeppe yidaytappe oykkada koyro yidayta gakkanaas diza oosanchata wursi xeeygada ista ooso waaga qanxa’ gides.
Tammanne issintha saate bolla ooson gelidayti yiidi issoy issoy kumeththa gallasa waaga ekkida.
“Koyro ooson gelidayti yishe ba woznara hinkoytappe bollara daro demmana gi qoppishin istaska hinkoytara gina immides.
Miisha ekkishe qanxizade bolla ‘Hayti wursethan ooson gelidi issi saate xalala ooththidayti kumeththa gallas ooson duuridinne awan xuugetidi pe7ida nuussara wosta istas issi gina qanxay?’ gida.
<range>
“Izikka istafe issades ‘Ta jalawu! Nena qohabeekke; issi gallassas gidiza damozan ooththanas tanara giigabeykii? Ha7i hehi ne gisha ekkada ba; nees immidayssa mala wursethan yidayssaska ta immana koyays.
<range>
Histin ta miishan ta dosidazi ooththanas danda7ikkinaa? Woykko ta kiya gididayssi nena qanatisizee?’
“Guyen dizayti sinthe, sinthen dizayti guye aadhdhana” gides.
Yesusi Yerusalame bishe bana kaalliza tammanne nam7ata dumma shaakki ekkidi
“Hiya nuni Yerusalame baana goos; Asa Nay Qeeseta halaqasinne Muse woga tamarsizaytas aadhdhi imettana; istika izi hayqqana mala iza bolla pirdana.
Iza bolla qidhi ka7anassinne garafana mala, wodhana malakka deretas aaththi immana; heedzdzantho gallas izikka hayqoppe dendana” gides.
Hessafekka Zabidoosa nayta aaya ba naytara Yesusakko shiiqada iza sinthan gulbatada Yesusi izis issi miish ooththana mala woossadus.
Izikka izo “Ay koyay?” gides; izakka “Hayti ta naa nam7ati ne kawoteththan issoy ne ushachara, issoy ne hadirsara uttana mala ooththarki!” gadus.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Inte woossizaz erekketa; tani uyiza xu7a inte uyana dandayanee?” gides. Istika “Ee dandayoos” gida.
Izikka “Ta xu7appe tumu inte uyanashin ta ushachaninne ta hadirsan utethi ta Aaway giigissidadentas attin tani immizaz deenna” gides.
Tammati hessa siydi nam7u ishata bolla hanqettida.
Yesusi ista issi bolla xeygidi “Ayzaabe halaqati ba haariza dere bolla godatizayssa mala godateththi dizayti wolqara haarizayssa inte ereeta.
Inte giddon hessa mala hananas bessenna; intefe gita gidana koyizadey intes ooththizade gido.
Intefe bolla gidanas koyizadey intefe gars gido.
Asa Nay asay izas ooththana mala gidonta asas ooththanassinne ba shempo darota gish aaththi immanas yides” gides.
Yesusi bana kaallizaytara Iyarkofe kezidi bishin daro derey iza kaallides.
Heen ayfey qooqida nam7u asati oge duunan utti deettes. Yesusi aadhdhi bizayssa siydi “Godo! Dawute nawu nuna maara!” giidi waassida.
Derezi “Hayzite!” giidi hanqides; gido attin isti darsi waassishe “Godo! Dawute nawu nuna maara!” gida.
Yesusikka eqqidi ista xeygidi “Ta intes ay ooththana mala koyetii?” gides.
Istika “Nu ayfey xeellana mala koyoos” gida.
Yesusi istas mishettidi ista ayfetakka ba kushera boshechin heerakka xeelidi iza kaallida.
Isti Yerusalame matan Dabrazayte zuma bolla diza Betefaage geetettizaso gakkida mala Yesusi bana kaallizaytappe nam7ata kiittides.
“Hanno inte matan diza gutayo biidi inte he gakkida mala issi hare dizaara ba gutteyra qasheta dishin inte demmana. Birshidi ha taakko ekki yiite.
Oonikka intena ‘Ays hayssatho ooththetii?’ giikko ‘Goday ista koyees’ giite; intena oychizadey heerakka yeddana.
“Hayssika hanizay kase naben Xiyoonis hizgite ‘Hekko! Ne kawoy ashke gididi hareyonne harey gutteyo togidi neekko yaana’ geetettidayssi poletanassa” gides.
<range>
Iza kaallizayti Yesusi istas yootida mala ooththida.
Hareyo izi gutteyra ehidi ba may7o ista bolla woththin izikka hareta toggides.
Deraappe dariza baggay ba may7o oge bolla micides; bagga asay mitha bonco duuththi duuththi oge bolla aaththi aaththi yeggides.
Izappe sinthara biza dereynne guyera kaalliza dereyka ba qaala dhoqu histidi “Hoosana! Dawute nay galattetto! Goda sunthan yiday anjettidade! Xoossi galattetto!” gida.
Izi Yerusalame gelida wode katama asay wuri “Hayssi oonee?” giidi yark yarkides.
Iza kaallidi yida dereyka “Hayssi Galila giddon diza Naazireteppe yida Nabe Yesusa gidenee?” gides.
Hessafe Yesusi Xoossa Keeththa gelidi Xoossa Keeththa kare giddon gaaththan bayzizaytanne shamizayta goodides. Miish laammizayta xaraphezatanne haraphe bayizizayta oyde shiri shiri yeggidi “ ‘Ta Keeththay Woosa Keeththe geetettes’ geetettidi xaafettides; inte qasse bonqizayta gongolo histideta” gides.
<range>
Ayfe qooqetanne tohoy silida asata Yesusakko Xoossa Keeththe ehida. Izikka ista pathides.
Gido attin Qeeseta halaqatinne Muse woga tamarsizayti izi ooththida malatata beyidayssaninne guutha nayti “Woze kawo, galatay Dawute naas gido!” giidi waassizayssa siyida gish daro hanqettida.
Istika Yesusa “Hayti nayti gizayssa siyay?” gida; Yesusikka istas “Ee siyadis; nayta duunappenne dhammiza qeeri nayta duunan tani galata giigissadis gizaso mulerakka nababi ereketii?” gides.
Ista yeggi aggidi he katamappe kezidi Bitaaniya geetettizaso biidi heen aqides.
Yesusi wontetha gallas maalado guye katama simmishin iza gafisides.
Oge matan issi balase geetettiza mithi beyidi gede izikko shiiqishin hayth xalalappe attin ayfey bayndayssa beyidi “Hiyappe guye ne bolla ayfey dooppo!” giin balase mithaya heerakka meladus.
Yesusa kaallizayti hessa beyidinne malaletidi “Hanna balaseya waanada heerakka meladee?” gida.
Yesusikka ista “Ta intes tumu gays; intes ammanoy diikkonne inte sidhonta aggikko balase mithay bolla hanidayssa mala xalala gidonta hayssa zuma ‘Hayssafe dhoqalletada duge abban gela’ inte gidakkokka izi gelana” gides.
Intes ammanoy diikko inte woossan oychida miish wursikka ekkana.
Yesusi Xoossa Keeththe gelidi tamarsishin Qeeseta halaqatinne dere cimati izakko shiiqidi “Hayssa wursa oona shenen ooththay? Hayssa ooththanas shene nees ooni immidee?” giidi iza oychida.
Yesusikka istas zaaridi “Takka intena issino oychays; inte taas zaarikko takka hayta ooththizayta oona shenen ooththizakkonne intes yootana.
Yohannisa xinqatey awappe yidee? Saloppe yideyee? Asappee?” gides. Istika “Nu ‘Saloppe yides’ giikko ‘Histin aazas ammanibekketii?’ gaana giidi ba giddon issoy issoy issara zorettida.
Qasse nu ‘Asappe’ giikko, asay wurikka Yohannisa nabe giidi ammaniza gish nu babboos” gida.
Hessa gish Yesusas “Nu erokko” giidi zaarida. Izikka istas “Hayta ta ooththizayta oona shenen ooththizakkonne takka intes yootikke” gides.
Yesusi ista “Intes ay misatizee? Nam7u attuma nay diza issadey dees; izikka koyro naazakko biidi ‘Ta naazo! Hachchi gede woyne mithaso baada ooththa’ gides.
Naazi qasse ‘Biikke!’ giidinne guyeppe muuzottidi bides.
“Nam7antho naazakka kaseyssathoka ‘Ba!’ giin naazi ‘Ero!’ giidi boonta aggagides.
Hayta nam7atappe aawa shene poliday awayssee?” giidi oychida. Istika “Koyro naaza!” gida. Yesusikka istas, “Ta intes tumu gays; qaraxa qanxisizaytinne laymatizayti Salo Kawotethi intefe sinthan gelana.
“Xammaqiza Yohannisi intena xillotetha oge bessanas inteko yides shin inte izi gizayssa ammanibekketa; gido attin qaraxa qanxisizaytinne laymatizayti gidikko ammanida; izi hanidayssa inte beyi simmidikka maarotethan gelidi ammanibekketa” gides.
“Hara leemisokka siyite; woyne mithi tokkizasoy dizaddey he woynezas birda yuushi aaththidi woyneza ayfe gum7anas olla bokkides. Woyneza naaganas mitha bolla shako giigissides. Hessafe guye gadeza woyne mithara goyzaytas kira immidi hara dere bides.
Boney gakkishin woyne mithaza ayfe ekkanas ba ashkarata gadeza goyzaytakko yeddides.
Gadeza goyzayti ashkarata oykkidi issa wodhida; issa qasse shuchchan caddida.
Gadaa goday kaseytappe aadhdhiza hara ashkarata yeddides. Goyzayti ha7ikka kaseyta bolla ooththidayssa malakka ista bollakka polida.
Wursethan ooni erize ‘Isti iza bonchanakkonne’ giidi ba naa aaththi yeddides.
Gido attin gadaa goyzayti naaza beyida mala ‘Hayssi iza laattanayssakko! Ane haa yiite, iza wodhidi gadaa laattoos’ gida.
Naaza oykkidi woyney tokkettidasoppe gede kare kessidi wodhida.
“Ero! Woyneza goday yiza wode he gadaa goyiza asata wostana intes misatizee?” gides.
Istika “Heytanta iitata daro waayssi wodhidi woyney tokkettiza gadappe bessiza woyne ayfe wodera izas immiza hara gade goyzaytas kirasana” giidi izas zaarida.
Yesusikka istas “Geeshsha Maxaafan ‘Gimbe keexxizayti iita giidi wora yeggida shuchchay keeththas maazanne bolla wodhdhiza shuch gidides; Xoossi hayssa ooththides; iza oosoykka nu ayfes malalisizaz’ geetetti xaafetidayssa nababibekketii?
“Hessa gish ta intes Xoossa Kawotethi intefe eketada ayfe ayfiza deretas imettana.
