Hayssa shuchcha bolla kundizay meqana; shuchchay iza bolla wodhizadeykka liiqana” gides.
Qeeseta halaqatinne Farsaaweeti iza leemisoy ista gish gididayssa erida.
Gido attin isti iza oykki qachonta mala asay Yesusa nabe mala xeelliza gish babbida.
Qasseka Yesusi hara leemiso
“Salo Kawotethi ba naas sarge giigissida issi kawo misatawus.
Kawoykka diggissas yootidayta xeeyganas ba ashkarata yeddides; xeeygettidaytikka ‘Nu bookko’ gida.
“Qasseka hara ashkarata ‘Kase istas yootidayta hekko ta sanga booratanne modhida meheta shukada diggisa giigissadis; wurikka giigettida gish sargeso haa yiite!’ giidi yootite.
Xeeygettidayti gidikko iza xeeyssa wudan yeggonta aggidi issoy ba goshshaso, issoy ba zal7eso bides.
Hanko attidayta, ashkarati oykkidi daro waayssidi wodhida.
“Kawoykka hanqettidi wotadarata yeddidi ashkara wodhidayta dhayssides; ista katama xuugides.
Ba ashkarataka ‘Sargeza diggisey giigides; gido attin sargezaso xeeygettidayti sarges bessizayta gidibeetenna.
Gede oge bolla kezidi inte demmida as wursi ha sarge diggisses xeygite’ gides.
Ashkaratikka oge bolla kezidi ba demmidayta lo7otaka iitataka wursi shiishshidi sargezaso imath kunthida.
“Kawoykka xeeygettida imatha beyanas so geliza wode sarge may7o may7onta as demmides.
‘Haysso! Sarge may7o may7onta waanada hayssa gelanas dandayadii?’ gi oychin addezas zaarana qaalay dhayides.
Kawoykka ba ashkarata ‘Hayssa addeza tohonne kushe shiishshi qachidi heen karen diza dhuman kessi olite; heen yeehonne achcha garcech gidana.’
“Xeeygettidayti darota; doorettidayti gidikko guuthata” gi yootides.
Hessafe guye Farsaaweeti kezi bishe “Iza duunappe bala qaala wosti demmi oykkinoo?” giidi zorettida.
Bana kaallizayta Herdoosa asatara izakko kiittidi “Astamare! Neni tumanchanne Xoossa oge tumappe tamarsizade gididayssanne oonaska dumma maado ooththonta wursaka issi mala ne xeellizayssa nu eroos.
Nees ay misatizakkone ane nuus yootaa? Qeesares giira qanxanas bessizee? Bessenee?” gida.
Yesusikka ista gene qofa eridi “Inteno qoodheppe qommon hanizayto tana yo7on baleththi oykkanas aazas koyetii?
Inte giira qanxiza miisha ane tana bessite” giin istika issi dinare geetettiza miish izas ehida.
Izikka “Hayssa miisha bolla diza misileynne xaafettida sunthay oonayssee?” gides.
Istika izas “Qeesareyssa” gida. Izikka istas zaaridi “Qeesareyssa Qeesares, Xoossayssa Xoossas immite” gides.
Hessa siyida wode malaletidinne iza aggi bida.
“Hayqqidaytas dendoy baawa” giidi ammaniza Saduqaaweti he gallas Yesusakko shiiqidi,
“Astamaare! Musey ‘Issadey macho ekkidi naa yelonta hayqqikko iza ishay hayqqidayssa macho ekkidi ba isha laattiza naa izas yelo’ gides.
Nu achchan laapun ishati deettes shin koyro ishay macho ekkidi naa yelonta hayqqida gish kaalo ishay iza macheyo ekides.
Nam7antho ishayka hayqqida ishaatho naa yelonta hayqqides; hessathoka hanishin macasaya laapuntha isha geladus.
Wursethan macasaya hayqqadus.
Hessa gish laapunati wurikka izo ekkida shin hayqoppe dentha gallas macasaya laapuntappe awayssa macho gidanee?” gida.
Yesusikka istas zaaridi “Geeshsha Maxaafatanne Xoossa wolqa inte eronta gish baletteta.
Hayqoppe dendidappe guye asay salo kiitanchata mala gidana attin eketettenanne geletenna.
Hayqqidayta dentha gish gidikko Xoossi ‘Tani Abrahaame Xoossa, Yisaaqa Xoossa, Yaqoobe Xoossa’ giidi intes yootoyssa nababibekketii? Xoossi paxata Xoossa attin hayqethata Xoosse gidenna” gides.
<range>
Dereyka hessa siydi iza timirtezan malalettides.
Yesusi Saduqaaweta co7u histidayssa siydi Farsaaweeti issi bolla shiiqettida.
Ista giddofe issi Muse woga lo7ethi erizadey Yesusa paaccanaas koydi “Aastamare! Muse wogata giddon ubbafe aadhdhizay awayssee?” giidi oychides.
<range>
Izikka zaaridi “ ‘Ne Goda Xoossa ne kumeththa woznappe, ne kumeththa shempofe, ne kumeththa qofappe dosa.’
Hayssi koyronne ubbafe aadhdhiza azazo.
Nam7anthoykka iza misatees, hessika ‘Ne shooro ne hu7e mala dosa’ gizayssa.
Muse wogaynne nabeta timirtey wurikka hayta nam7u azazotan qashettes” gides.
Farsaaweeti issi bolla shiiqeti dishin Yesusi ista,
“Kirstoosa gish inte ay geetii? Izi oona naa?” gi oychides; Istika izas zaaridi “Izi Dawute naa” gida.
Izikka istas “Histin Dawutey Xillo Ayana wolqan ‘Xoossay ta Goda’ giidi waani xeygidee? ‘Ta ne morketa ne toho giddon gulbatissana gakkanaas ne ta ushachan utta!’ gides.
<range>
Hessa gish Dawutey iza ‘Ta Goda’ giidi xeygikko waanidi izas naa gidana dandayizee?” gides.
Izas issi qaala zaarana dandayida asi woykko he gallassafe simmin iza oysho oychana xalida asi oonikka bettibenna.
Qasseka Yesusi derezassinne bana kaallizaytas,
“Muse woga tamarsizaytinne Farsaaweeti Muse wombara bolla uttida.
Hessa gish isti intes yootizayssa wursi ooththitenne naagite; gido attin isti duunan haasayizayssa mala ooson bessonta gish inte ista ooso kaallofte.
“Hessathoka asi tookkanas dandayonta deexo tooho qachidi asa hashe bolla wothettes shin baassi gidikko biradhdhe xeeranka bochettenna.
Ista ooso wursi asi beyana mala ooththetes; ba ashenkitabe Geeshsha Maxaafa giddofa xaafi ekkida issi issi xiqiseta kitabe sikidi liiphe bolla woykko kushen qachizaz ooththetes. Ba may7o macara adussettes.
Diggisay dizason boncho so Ayhuda Woosa Keeththanka sinthara uttana doossettes.
Hessathoka giya giddon saro geetettanassinne asay ista ‘Astamaare!’ gaana mala koyettes.
“Inte gidikko ‘Astamaare’ geetetti xeeygetofte. Inte Astamarey issa xalala gidishin inte wurikka issoy issas ishanta.
Salon intes issi Aaway xalala diza gish biitta bolla oonakka ‘Aawawu!’ giidi xeeygoppite.
Inte astamarey issi Kirstoosa xalla gidida gish inte ‘Astamareto!’ geetetofte.
Inte giddon ubbafe aadhdhizaddey intes ooththizade gidana.
Bana dhoqisizadey kawuyana; bana kawushshizadey bonchettana.
“Inteno qoodheppe qommon hanizayto, Muse woga tamarsizayto, inteno Farsaaweeto! Asay Xoossa kawoteth gelonta mala asa bolla inte penge gordiza gish intena aayye-ana! Inte intes geleketanne gelanas koyizaytaka geltheketa.
Inteno qoodheppe qommon hanizayto, Muse woga tamarsizayto, qasseka Farsaaweeto! Intes aayye-ana! Azinay baynda macasata keeththa kallosishe asa ayfe sinthan adussa woossa inte woossiza gish inte iita pirda pirdettana.
“Inteno qoodheppe qommon hanizayto, Muse woga tamarsizayto, qasseka Farsaaweeto! Issi as Ayhuda ammanon gelthanas abba bollaranne biitta bollara yuuyi daburdinne ammanthida asa intefe nam7u kushe aaththidi Gaanname naa inte kessiza gish intena aayye-ana!
“Inteno! Intes qooqi uttidi harata kaalethizayto! Intes aayye-ana! ‘Oonikka Xoossa Keeththan caaqikko aykkoy ba’ gido attin ‘Xoossa Keeththa giddon diza worqan caaqikko caaqo gomey gakkana’ geeta.
Inteno qooqidayto! Balettidayto, worqafenne worqa dummasida Xoossa Keeththafe awayssi aadhdhizee?
Hessathoka ‘Oonikka yarsho yarshizaso bolla caaqikko aykkoy baawa; shin yarshizason diza yarsho bolla caaqikko caaqoy gomees’ geeta.
Inteno qooqeto! Yarshoppenne yarsho shiishshizasoppe awaysse aadhdhizay?
Hessa gish yarsho shiishshizaso bolla caaqizadey yarshosoza bollanne yarshizaso bolla diza ubba miishan caaqees.
Hessathoka Xoossa Keeththaza bolla caaqiday Xoossa Keeththaninne iza giddon aqizaysan caaqees.
Salon caaqizadeykka Xoossa alganinne alga bolla uttidayssan caaqqees.
“Inteno qoodheppe qommon hanizayto, Muse woga tamarsizayto, Farsaaweeto! Intena aayye ana! Aasutappe, aanugappenne katkal7afe tammafe issino immeeta shin wogatappe waannatizayta heytikka tuma pirda, maarotethinne ammanetteth gidikko kadhideta. Heyta aggonta dishe haytanta inte ooththanas intes bessees shin aggideta.
Inteno qooqi uttidi kaalethizayto! Uu7e gaccidi uyeeta shin gaamella muume mitteeta!
“Inteno qoodheppe qommon hanizayto, Muse woga tamarsizaytonne Farsaaweeto! Intes aayye-ana! Xu7assinne keres bolla bagga qucceeta shin iza giddon dizayssa inte bonqaninne uuzetethan shiishshideta.
Neno qooqe Farsaawezo! Koyrottada xu7assinne keres giddo bagga geeshsha! Hessafe guye kare baggay geesh gidana.
“Inteno qoodheppe qommon hanizayto, Muse woga tamarsizayto, qasse Farsaaweeto! Bolla baggay noorara meeshettidi lo7izayti giddoy gidikko hayqqidayta meqethinne daro tunanetethan kumida duufota misatiza gish intena aayye-ana!
Inteka bolla baggara asas xillo asata misateta; inte giddoy gidikko cimoninne iitatethan kumides.
“Inteno duunan cimmizayto! Muse woga astamareto, qasseka Farsaaweeto! Intes aayye-ana! Nabeta duufo lo7ethizayto, xillo asata duufo hawultera giigissizayto!
Nu aawati nabeta wodhiza wode nu dizakko istara zuppetokkokko shin,
inte nabeta wodhida asata nayta gididayssa inte duunara interka inte inte bolla markattetta.
Histikko oosettidi poletonta oge bolla diza inte aawata ooso polite.
“Inteno dukkiza iita shoosha nayto! Gaanname tama pirdafe inte waani attanee?
Hessa gish nabetanne eranchata astamaretaka ta intes yeddana. Inte ista giddofe issi issi asata wodhana. Baggayta inte kaqqana; baggayta inte Ayhuda Woosa Keeththan garafananne ha katamappe hara inte gooddana.
Hessa gish xillo Aabeele suuthafe ha simmin Xoossa Keeththaninne yarsho yarshizaso giddon inte wodhida Barakiyo naa Zakaraasa sutha gakkanaas biitta bolla gukkida xillota sutha ubbas inte oyshettana.
Ta intes tumu gays; kase aadhdhidaa yo7o ubbas hayssi ha yelettay oyshettana.
“Hanne Yerusalame! Nabeta wodhizare! Neekko kiitettidayta shuchchara caddizare! Hanne Yerusaleme kutto aaya ba ciyeta ba qefe giddo shiishshiza mala ta ne nayta shiishshanaas aapun wode koyadinashin ne gidikko koyabakka.
Hekko inte keeththi kays gidi attana.
Ta intes tumu gays; inte Goda sunthan yizadey anjettidade gaana wodey gakkanaas nam7antho tana beyekketa” gides.
Yesusi Xoossa Keeththafe kezi bishin iza kaallizayti Xoossa Keeththazi shuchchan keexxettidayssa bessana koydi Yesusakko shiiqida.
Izikka istas “Hayssa wursi xeelletii? Ta intes tumu gays; hayssi inte beyiza issoy issa bolla diza shuchchay laalettonta issi shuchchikka hayssatho deenna” gides.
Izi Dabrazayte geetettiza zuma bolla utti dishin iza kaallizayti xalala izakko shiiqidi “Ane nuus yoota; hayssi ne gizayssi ayde hananee? Ne yussassinne wode wursethas malatay aazee?” gi oychida.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Oonikka intena baleththonta mala naagettite.
Buro daroti ‘Ta Kirstoosa’ gishe ta sunthan yaana; darotaka baleththana.
Olanne ola gish haasayettiza wore inte siyana. Ha yo7oti wurikka wolqara polettana shin wursethi buro gidida gish inte hayssan daggamonta mala naagettite.
Derey dere bolla, kawoy kawo bolla dendana; dumma dumma deren koshaynne biitta qaathi hanana.
Hessi wurikka miixas leesso mala.
He wode intena waayes aaththi immana; intena wodhana; ta suntha geedon dere ubban inte ixettidayta gidana.
“He wode daro asay dhuphettana; issoy issa aaththi aaththi immananne ba giddon ixettana.
Daro wordo nabeti dendananne darota baleththana.
Iitatethi dariza gish darotappe siiqoy irxana.
Wurseth gakkanaas minnidadey attana.
Dere ubbas marka gidana mala hayssi kawoteththa Mishiraachcho qaalay kumeththa alamen yootettana; hessafe guye wursethi yaana.
“Hessa gish nabe Daanelan yootettidayssa mala ‘Harassiza tunatethi’ anjettidason eqqidayssa inte beyiza wode nababizadey woznan wotho.
He wode Yuhudan dizayti pude zuma bolla gangetto.
Keeththa kaara bolla dizaddey oonikka ba miish keeththafe kessana giidi duge wodhdhofo.
Gade giddon dizaddey oonikka ba may7o ekkana giidi so simmofo.
He gallasatan qanthara diza macasatassinne naa dhanthiza aayetas aayye-ana!
Hessa gish inte gangoy balgo woykko Sambata gallas gidonta mala woossite.
He wode alamey medhetosappe hachchi gakkanaas hani eronta miishi sinthafekka iza misatizay baynda wolqama metoy hanana.
He gallassati qaammontakko asho may7ida asi wuri attenna shin doorettidayta gish he gallassati qaammana.
“He wode oonikka ‘Hekko Kirstoosi hayssan dees!’ Woykko ‘Hessan dees’ gizade ammanoppite.
Wordo Kirstoosanne wordo nabeti buro dendidi istas dandayettikko doorettidayta baleththanas giidi wolqama malatatanne kase oosetti eronta miish ooththana.
“Hekko hayssa ta intes kaseta yootays.
Hessa gish ‘Hekko hirki bazzon dees’ giidi intes yootikko he kezoppite; ‘Hekko ilpinen dees’ giikko ammanoppite.
Wolqanthi awa arshey mokizasora wolqamidi awa arshey wullizaso gakkanaas poo7izayssa mala Asa Naa yuussaykka hessatho hanana.
Ahay dizaso anko kafoy shiiqqees.
“Heerakka he iita meto gallassatappe guye awa arshey dhumana; aginay ba poo7o diggana; xoolinteti saloppe qoqofettana; salo wolqamatikka qaaxana.
“He wode asa naa malatay salo bolla bettanna. Biitta bolla diza derey wuri yeekkana; Asa Naykka salo shaara bolla daro wolqaranne gita bonchora yishin asay beyana.
Kiitanchataka daro wolqama xurumba giirissara yeddana. Istika doorettidayta oyddu ma7izeneppe salos ha bagga gaxappe he gaxa bagga gaxa gakkanaas wursi issi so shiishana.
“Balase geetettiza mithafe hayssa tamarite; balase mithays unquloy cililiza wode iza hayth kessishin boney matidayssa inte ereeta.
Hessatho hayta inte beyiza wode izi penge matidayssa inte erana.
Ta tumu gays; hayssi wuri polettana gakkanaas ha yelettay aadhdhenna.
Saloynne sa7ay aadhdhana shin ta qaalay gidikko mulekka aadhdhenna.
“He gallassayonne he saateyo Aawappe attin salo kiitanchata gidinka Naaza gidinka oonikka erenna.
Nohe wode hanidayssa mala Asa Naa yuussi hessa mala gidana.
Dhayssiza haaththafe kase Nohey markaben geliza gallas gakkanaas asay mishenne uyishe, ekkishenne gelishe gam7ides.
He wodey gakkanaas aazi hananakkonne asay erontanne qopponta bashsha haaththay yiidi mitidayssa mala ta Asa Nay yiza wodeykka hessatho hanana.
“He wode nam7u asati issife goshshan pe7ana shin istafe issadey ekettana; issadey attana.
Nam7u macasati woxan issife gaaccana shin istafe issineya ekettana issineya attana.
“Histikko inte Goday yaana gallasa inte eronta gish beeggidi naagite.
Hayssa woznan woththite; kaysoy qammafe aafuntha saate bolla yaanakkonne erizakko iza miish kaysoy ekkonta mala keeththa aaway beeggidi naagana.
Asa Naykka inte qopponta saate bolla yaana; inteka hessatho giigettidayta gidite.
“Wodera so asa quma mizana mala goday ba keeththa asa bolla shuumida ammanettiza cinca oosanchay oonee?
Keeththa aaway simmidi yiza wode izas immida hadara ooththi polishe beettida oosanchay anjettidayssa.
Ta intes tumu gays; goday iza ba haarida ubba bolla shuumees.
Gido attin he oosanchay iita gididi ‘Ta goday gam7idi yaana’ gi qoppidi,
dendi hanko oosanchata wadha oykikko mathottizaytara miikkonne uyikko,
izi qopponta gallassaninne saaten iza goday yiidi,
iza qanxethi kaa7ana; iza exxa qoodheppe qommon hanizaytara ooththana. Henka yeehoynne achcha garcechi hanana.
“He wode Salo Kawotethi mishira mokkanas xompe oykkidi kezida tammu gela7ota misatawus.
He tammatappe ichashu gela7oti eeyata, hanko ichashati qasse cincata.
Eeyati kuraze xompe oykkida shin wurikko gujana hara naage lamba oykkibetenna.
Cincati gidikko ba kurazezara wurikko gujana lamba hara xarmusen oykkida.
Machiyo ekkana mishiray yoonta gam7in dhiskoy deexxin asay wurikka dhiskides.
“Leela gidoth gidishin ‘Mishirazi yees! Kezidi mokki ekkite!’ giza xeeyssa qaalay siyettides.
Hessa wode gela7oti wurikka dendidi ba xompe xompe oysethonne giigeteth oykkida.
Eeyati cincata ‘Nu xompey to7ana giza gish inte lambappe nuus immite’ gida.
“Cinca gela7oti istas zaaridi ‘Nuus diza lambay nuussaranne intessara gidonta gish biidi lamba bayzizaytappe intes shammite’ gida.
Isti lamba shammana bi kichchin mishirazi gakki wodhdhides. Kase giigeti uttida gela7oti bulachaso izara gelida; kareykka gordettides.
“Guuth gam7ishe hanko gela7oti yiidi ‘Godo! Godo! Kare nuus doya!’ gida.
Izikka zaaridi ‘Ta intes tumu gays; ta intena erikke!’ gides.
Hessa gish yaana gallasa woykko saateza inte eronta gish giigettidi naagite.
“Xoossa Kawotethi baassi dizazi wursi ba ashkaratas hadara immidi hara dere baana dendida issi as misatees.
Ashkaratas issas issas ista wolqa mala giigissidi issas ichashu shi bira, issas nam7u shi bira, hankoyssas qasse issi shi bira immidi bides.
Ichashu shi bira ekkida addezi heerakka miishan zal7e oykkidi hara ichashu shi bira wodhisides.
Qasseka nam7u shi bira ekkidayssi hara nam7u shi bira wodhisides.
Issi shi bira ekkidayssi ba goda bira biittan moogidi qottides.
“Ashkarata goday ba bidason daro wode gam7i simmidi miisha istara sala7ettides.
Ichashu shi bira ekkida ashkaray hara ichashu shi bira wodhisidayssa ekki yiidi ‘Godo! Ne taas ichashu shi bira immadasa shin hekko hayssa ta hara ichashu shi bira wodhisadis’ gides.
Iza godayka ‘Lo7o ooththadasa; neno lo7o ammanettida ashkarazo! Ne guutha miishan ammanettida as gidida gish ta nena daro miisha bolla shuumana; gede ne goda ufayssaso gela’ gides.
“Hessathoka nam7u shi bira ekkidayssi godazakko shiiqidi ‘Godo! Ne taas nam7u shi bira immadasa shin hekko hara nam7u shi bira wodhisadis’ gides.
Godazikka ‘Lo7ethadassa; haysso lo7onne taas ammanettida ashkarazo! Neni guuthan ammanettidade gidida gish ta nena daro miisha bolla shuumays; gede ne Goda ufayssaso gela’ gides.
“Issi shi bira ekkida ashkaray shiiqidi ‘Godo! Neni zerontasoppe maxizadenne laallontasoppe shiishshiza menxe iita as gididayssa ta erays.
Hessa gish ta babbada biitta bokkada ne bira bookkida ollan moogada qottadis; ne miish hessa beya!’ gides.
“Iza goday zaaridi ‘Haysso iita azalla ashkarazo! Tani zerontasoppe maxizade laallontasoppe shiishshizade gididayssa ne eray?
Histin ta simma yiza wode ta miisha yelora ta ekkana mala tirpisi zal7iza asas ne immanas besseeseshin’ gides.
“ ‘Ane ha7i izappe shi bira ekkidi tammu shi biray dizaddes immite.
Dizaddes gujettananne dari dari baana; bayndadefe he diza guuththayakka izappe eketaychana.
Hayssa go7ay baynda ashkara gede yeekkizasonne achchey garcettizaso hen karen diza dhuman kessi yeggite’ gides.
“Asa Nay ba kiitanchata ubbara bonchon yiza wode ba boncho alga bolla uttana.
Derey wuri iza sinthi shiiqana; izikka mehe heemmizadey deyshi dorsafe qori shaakkiza mala asa issa issafe qori shaakana.
Dorsata izas ushacha baggara, deyshata hadirsa baggara essana.
He wode kawoy ushacha baggara dizayta ‘Inteno! Ta Aaway intena anjidayti haa yiite! Alamey medhetosappe intes giigetida kawoteththa laattite! gaana.
Gaasoyka tani gafin tana mizideta; ta saametin tana ushshideta; ta imatha gidada yiin tana mokki ekkideta.
Ta kallottin tana mayzideta; ta sakettin tana hargisideta; ta qashetin tana oychideta’ gaana.
“Xillotikka zaaridi ‘Godo! Ne gafin nu nena ayde mizidonii? Woykko ne saamotin ayde beyidi nu nena ushshidonii?
Nu ayde nena beyidi imathateth mokkidonii? Woykko ayde ne kallottin beyidi nena mayzidonii?
Hessathoka ne saketin woykko qashetin ayde beyidi nena oychidonii?’ gaana.
Kawoykka zaaridi ‘Ta intes tumu gays; hayta laafa gidida ta ishatappe issades ooththidayssi inte taas ooththida mala’ gaana.
“Qasseka hadirsa baggara dizaytas; ‘Inteno qangetidayto! Taappe shaaketidi Dabulossassinne iza kiitanchatas giigetida merna taman biite gaana.
Gaasoyka ta gafin tana mizibeekketa; ta saamotin tana ushshibeekketa;
tana imathateth mokibeekketa; ta kallottin tana mayzibeeketa; ta sakettininne qashettin tana oychibeekketa’ gaana.
“Istika zaaridi ‘Godo, ne gafin woykko ne saamotin woykko ne imath gidin woykko ne kallottininne ne saketin woykko ne qashetin nu nena beyidi ayde nees gakkibekkonii?’ gaana.
“He wode izikka istas zaaridi ‘Ta intes tumu gays; hanta laafa ta ishatappe issades inte ooththonta aggidayssi taas inte ooththonta aggida mala’ gaana.
Heyti gede merna pirdan baana; xilloti gidikko merna de7okko baana” gides.
Yesusi hessa haasayi wursidappe guye bana kaallizaytas “Nam7u gallassafe guye Paaziga gididayssa ereetii? Asa Nay kaqettanas aadhdhi imettana” gides.
<range>
Hessafe guye Qeeseta halaqatinne dere cimati Qayaafa geetettiza Qeeseta halaqa gibben shiiqidi hiillara Yesusa oythidi wodhisanas maqettida.
<range>
Gido attin “Asa giddon ooshi dendonta mala ba7aale gallas gidoppo” giidi qachida.
Yesusi Bitaaniyan inchiracha hargera diza Simoona geetettizade soon dishin,
issi macassi dizaara waagay keehi al7o gidida albasxiroose geetettiza shitto bilqaaxe kumeth oykkada Yesusakko shiiqada izi maaddan uttidishin iza hu7e bolla shittoza guussadus.
Iza kaallizayti “Hessa beyidi hayssi aazas mela morettizee?
Shittozi daro waagas bayzettidi miishay manqotas imettizakkochii?” gida.
Yesusi hessa eridi “Hanno macasayo aazas waayssetii? Iza taas lo7o ooththadus.
Manqoti ubba wode intenara deettes; ta gidikko ubba wode intenara diikke gides.
Iza shittoza ta bolla gussidayssi tana moogos giigissanassa.
Ta intes tumu gays; hayssi Mishiraachcho qaalay sabakettiza alame yuushon awanka iza ooththidayssi izo qofisizaz gididi hasayettana” gides.
Hessafe guye tammanne nam7atappe issoy Asqoroonto Yuhuda geetettizayssi Qeeseta halaqatakko biidi,
“Ta intes iza aaththa immikko inte taas ay immanee?” gides. Istika izas heedzdzu tammu bira iza kushen tayibi immida.
He gallassafe simmidi Yuhuday Yesusa istas aaththi immanas inje wode naagishe gam7ides.
Uketha ba7aale geetettiza ba7aale gallas iza kaallizayti Yesusakko shiiqidi “Ne Paaziga maanaso awan giigissana mala koyay?” gida.
Izikka istas zaaridi gede katama biidi ebelo geetettiza as “Astamarey ‘Ta wodey matida gish tana kaallizaytara Paaziga ta ne keeththan bonchana gides’ giidi yootite” gides.
Iza kaallizaytikka Yesusi ista azazida mala Paaziga kawo giigissida.
Gadey omarsishin Yesusi tammanne nam7atara maaddan uttides.
Isti muussan dishin izi istas “Ta tumu gays; intefe issoy aaththi immana” gides.
Istika keehi muuzottidi taran taran “Godo taneshaa?” gida.
Izikka zaaridi “Tana aaththi immanaddey keren tanara kushe yeddizade.
Iza gish kase xaafettidayssa mala Asa Nay baana; gido attin Asa Naa aaththi immizades aayye-ana! Hessadey yeletonta attidakko izas lo7okkoshin” gides.
Iza aaththi immana Yuhuday “Astamaare! Taneshaa?” gides. Izikka “Ee, ne gida mala” gides.
Isti muussan dishin Yesusi miza qumappe ekkidi anjides. Menthidinne bana kaallizaytas immidi “Heyite miite; hayssi ta ashokko” gides.
Qasseka ushsha denthidi galatidinne bana kaallizaytas immidi “Wurikka hayssafe uyite;
daro asa nagarappe maarana gukkiza ta ooratha caaqo suuthay hayssa.
Ta intes gizay ta Aawa Kawoteththan ta intenara ooratha woynen ushshaza uyana gakkanaas hayssafe sinthan hayssa woyne ushsha intenara uyikke” gides.
Mazamure yexidappe guye pude Dabrazayte geetettiza zuma bolla kezida.
Yesusi istas “Inte wuri hachchi omarsi tanan dhuphettidi tana yeggi baana; ‘Heemmizayssa ta shocana; mehetinne laalettana’ geetettidi kase xaafettides.
Gido attin tani dendidappe guye intefe sinthatada gede Galila baana” gides.
Phexroosi zaaridi “Hankoyti wuri ne geedon dhuphetikkokka tani mulekka dhuphetikke!” gides.
Yesusikka izas zaaridi “Tumu gays; hachchi qamma kuttoy waassonta kasetada heedzdzuto ne tana kadana” gides.
Phexroosi qasse “Nenara ta hayqqana koshikkokka mulekka ta nena kadikke!” gides. Yesusa kaalliza hankoytikka kumeth izayssathoka gida.
Hessafe guye Yesusi bana kaallizaytara gede Getesemaane geetettizaso bides. Istaka “He baada ta woossishin inte hayssan uttishiite” gides.
Phexroosara Zabidoosa nayta nam7ata banara ekki biidi muuzotethinne daro qofo oykkides.
Hessafekka “Ta shempoya hayqqana gakkanaas daro muuzotadus; tanara minnidi hannin takkite” gides.
Istafe guuth gede haakki bi gupandi “Ta Aawawu! Nees dandayettikko hayssi metoy taappe aadhdho; gido attin tani koyda mala gidonta neni koyda mala hano” gi woossides.
Hessafe simmidi bana kaallizaytakko yiidi isti dhiskishin demmides. Phexroosakka “Hayto asato! Inte tanara issi saatekkone minnanas xoonidee?
Paacen inte gelonta mala minnidi woossite; ayanay giigettides shin ashoy gidikko daburancha” gides.
Qasseka nam7antho biidi “Ta Aawawu! Hayssa uyanasi taas attonta miish gidikko ne sheney poletto” giidi woossides.
Qasseka izi yishin ista ayfen dhiskoy deexida gish ichchidayta beyides.
Ista aggidi qasseka biidi heedzdzantho kase woossida qaala zaari woossides.
Hessafe bana kaallizaytakko simmidi “Ha7ikka shempidi dhiskidetii? Hekko ha7i saatey matides; Asa Nay nagaranchata kushen aadhdhi imettana.
Dendite ane boos! Tana aaththi immizadey yuussa bolla dees” gides.
Izi haasayishin tammanne nam7atappe issoy Yuhuday yides. Qeeseta halaqatinne dere cimati yeddida daro asay tooranne durqa oykkidi Yuhudara issife dees.
Yuhudaykka “Ta yeerizadey iza gidida gish oykkite” giidi kase yooti woththides.
Siti gi Yesusakko biidi “Astamaare! Saro” gishe Yesusa yeerides.
Yesusikka “Ta lagge! Ne yida qofa pola” gides. Heerakka asay shiiqetidi Yesusa oykkidi qachides.
Yesusara dizaytappe issoy giththa mashsha shoddidi Qeeseta halaqaza ashkara hayth qanxides.
Yesusikka “Ane ne mashsha koohon zaara geltha; mashsha shoddizayti mashshan dhayana.
Koshshikko tani ta Aawa oychizakko daro shiyen qoodettiza oliza kiitancha taas yeddonta aggana misatizee?
Hessatho ooththikko qasse Geeshsha Maxaafatan hanana geetettidayssi waani poletanee?” gides.
He wode Yesusi asa “Panga oykkiza asatho mashshanne durqa ekkidi tana oykkana yidetii? Wontin wontin Xoossa Keeththan uttada ta tamarsishin kase oykkibeekketa shin.
Gido attin hayssi wurikka hanidayssi kase nabeti Geeshsha Maxaafatan yootidayssi poletanassa” gides. He wode Yesusa kaallizayti iza yeggidi dhayida.
He wode Yesusa oykkidi asati Muse woga astamaretinne dere cimati issife shiiqidason Qeeseta halaqa Qayaafakko efida.
Gido attin Phexroosi Qeeseta halaqa gibbe gakkanaas hahora Yesusa kaallides. Gibbe giddo gelidi hanizayssa wurseth beyanas, gibbe naagizaytara uttides.
He wode Qeeseta halaqatinne Ayhudata duulatay kumeth Yesusa wodhisanas wordo marka koyides.
Wordo markati daroti shiiqikkokka bessiza markateth demmibeetenna; gido attin guyeppe nam7u as dayti shiiqidi “Hayssi addezi ‘Ta Xoossa Keeththa laallada heedzdzu gallassara zaarada keexana dandayays’ gides” giidi markattida.
<range>
Hessa siyida Qeeseta halaqay utethafe dendi eqqidi “Hayti asati ne bolla markattizayssas aykkokka zaarikii?” gides.
Yesusikka co7u gides. Qeeseta halaqay “Ta nena de7o Xoossa sunthan oychays! Neni Kirstoosa, Xoossa naa gidikko taas yoota!” gides.
Yesusikka “Ne goyssakka mala; gido attin intes ubbas ta yootizay sinthafe Asa Nay Wolqamaza ushachan uttidi salo shaarara yiza wode inte beyana” gides.
He wode Qeeseta halaqay ba may7o daakkidi “Xoossa bolla cashsha qaala haasayides; nuus hayssafe aadhdhiza hara aaza marka koshshize! Xoossa bolla cashsha qaala izi haasayishin inte inte haythara siyideta.
Intes ay misatizee?” gides. Istika zaaridi izas “Hayqoy bessees” gida.
He wode Yesusa ayfeson cuttishe iccida; baggayti baqqishe,
“Kirstoosa! Ne nena nabe gaasashin nena baqqiday oonakkonne ane nuus yoota” gida.
Hessafe guye Phexroosi Qeeseta halaqa gibben utti dishin issi keeththa giddon ooththiza macas dizaara izakko shiiqada “Nenikka Galila Yesusara dizadde!” gadus.
Izi qasse “Ne ay gizakkonne ta erikke!” giidi ubba asa sinthan kadides.
Gibbezappe keziza penge izi bishin issi hara oosanchaya iza xeellada heen gadaan dizaytas “Hayssi addezi Naazirete Yesusara dizaddekko!” gadus.
Izikka “Ta iza erikke!” giidi nam7antho kadides.
Guuth gam7ishin heen eqqida asati shiiqidi Phexroosa “Ne haasayay ne haytara dizayssa qoncisees; tumappe ne ista bagga asa” gida.
Izikka caaqishenne amatishe hessa addeza “Ta erikke!” gides. Heerakka kuttoy waassides.
Hessa wode Yesusi kase Phexroosas “Kuttoy waassanas ne tana heedzdzuto kadana” giidi yootida qaalay qofetin, Phexroosi kare kezidi camo yeeho yeekkides.
Maalado wontara Qeeseta halaqatinne dere cimati wurikka Yesusa wodhana oge zorettida.
Yesusa qachi efidi gazhe Philaxoosas aaththi immida.
Iza aaththi immida Yuhudaykka Yesusa bolla pirdettidayssa beyidi “Aaththa immoonta aggarkina” giidi ba ekkida heedzdzu tammu bira Qeeseta halaqatassinne dere cimatas zaari immidi “Xillo as aaththa immida gish ta mooradis” gides. Istika “Histin nuus ay meto! Ne era ekka!” gida.
<range>
Hessa gish Yuhuday bira efidi Xoossa Keeththa giddon yeggidi kezi biidi cuuletti hayqqides.
Qeeseta halaqati bira denthidi “Suutha waaga gidida gish Xoossa Keeththa miishan gujanas bessenna” gida.
Ba giddon zorettidi imath gidida asatas duufo gidana mala issi urqa miish medhiza hiillaza gade shammida.
Hessa gish he gadey hachchi gakkanaas suutha gade geetettes.
Izas waaga gidana mala “Isra7eele nayti heregida heedzdzu tammu bira qoodi ekkida. Xoossi tana azazida mala urqa medhiza hiillaza gades immida” geetettidi nabe Ermaasa duunan yootettidayssi polettides.
<range>
He wode Yesusi dere haarizayssa sinth shiiqides. Dere haarizayssika “Neni Ayhuda kawoo?” giidi oychides. Yesusikka “Ne gida mala gido” gides.
Qeeseta halaqatinne dere cimati iza mootishin Yesusi istas aynne zaaribenna.
He wode Philaxoosi Yesusa “Aapun yo7on nena mootizakkonne siyikkii?” gides.
Dere haarizayssi keehi malalettana gakkanaas Yesusi issi qaalakka zaaribenna.
Dere haarizayssas ba7aale gallas derey qasho asappe “Ebeloy nuus birshetto!” gi oychikko issade birshiza wogay dees.
He wode gene ooson erettida Barbaane geetettiza issi qasho asi dees.
Derey shiiqida mala Philaxoosi “Barbaaneppenne Kirstoosa geetettiza Yesusappe ta intes oona birshana mala koyetii?” gides.
Philaxoosi isti coo qanates aaththi immidayssa erishe oychides.
Izi pirda alga bolla utti dishin iza macheya “Iza geedon hachchi tani agumora daro metotadis; hessa xillo addeza bolla ne aykkokka ooththonta mala” giza kiita Philaxoosas yeddadus.
Gido attin Qeeseta halaqatinne cimati istas Barbaaney birshettana malanne qasse Yesusa wodhana mala woossanas dereza qaalay gaaggana mala ooththida.
Dere haarizayssi “Nam7atappe oona birshana mala koyetii?” gi oychin, isti “Barbaane birsha!” gida.
Philaxoosikka “Histikko Kirstoosa geetettiza Yesusa wostoo?” gides. Wurikka “Kaqetto!” gida.
Philaxoosikka ayssii? “Ay iita ooththidee?” giidi ista oychides. Istika qasse keehi waassidi “Kaqetto!” gida.
Philaxoosi hanizayssi wurikka asay ba giddon bul7aketethafe attin hara ay go7ay bayndayssa yuushi xeelidi “Hayssa addeza suutha gomeppe ta geeshsha; hayssafe guye inte shene” giidi haaththi ehisidi dereza sinthan ba kushe mecettides.
Derey wuri “Iza suuthi nu bollanne nu nayta bolla gakko” giidi zaarides.
He wode Barbaane istas birshidi Yesusa garafissidappe guye kaqqana mala aaththi immides.
Hessafe wotadarati Yesusa gede dere haarizayssa gibbe ekki biidi wuri shiiqidi Yesusa giddo aaththida.
Iza may7o qaaridi hara zo7o may7o mayzida.
Aguntha aklile xaaxidi giigissida; iza hu7e bolla woothida; shomboqo guufe ushacha kushen oythidinne iza sinthan gulbatidi “Ayhuda kawo! Intes too!” giidi iza qidhida.
Iza bolla cuttida, shomboqo guufeza iza kusheppe ekkidi Yesusa hu7en zaari zaaridi shocida.
Iza bolla qidhi ka7idayssafe guye qasseka zo7o may7oza qaari ekkidinne kase iza may7oza zaari mayzidi kaqqanaso ekki bida.
Isti ekki bishin Qareena geetettizasoppe yida Simoona geetettizayssa demmidi masqaleza iza wolqara toossida.
Birshechay “Hu7e guuge” geetettiza Golgota gakkishin ciyera walakettida woyne cajje “Uya” giidi immida; gido attin izi gaanxi ekkidi uyana koybenna.
<range>
Iza kaqidappe guyen iza may7oza bolla saama yeggidi gishettida.
Heen uttidi iza naagida.
“Hayssi Ayhuda kawo Yesusa” giza mooto qaala iza hu7eppe bollara woththida.
Nam7u wombadetappe issoy Yesusappe ushacha baggara, issoy hadirsa baggara izara issife kaqettida.
Ogera aadhdhi biza asay cayishenne hu7e qaathishe “Xoossa Keeththa laallada heedzdzu gallassan hara keexana gizayso! Ane nena ashsha, ne Xoossa Naa gidikko ane masqale bollafe wodhdha” gida.
<range>
Qeeseta halaqati dere cimatara gididi iza bolla qidhishe;
“Hara asa ashshides shin bana ashshanas dandaybenna; izi Isra7eele kawo gidikko ane ha7i masqale bollafe wodhdho; nukka iza ammanana.
Xoossan ammanettides; bana Xoossa Naa gida mala Xoossi iza dosiza gidikko ane ha7i iza asho” gida.
Izara issife kaqettida pangatikka hessatho cashsha qaala iza bolla qoqofida.
Gallassafe usuppun saateppe biidi uddufun saate gakkanaas kumeththa biittay dhumides.
Uddufun saate gidishin Yesusi qaala dhoqu histidi “Eelohe! Eelohe! Lama sabaqitan” giidi waassides. Hessa guussas birsheththay “Ta Xoosso! Ta Xoosso! Tana ayssi aggadii?” guussa.
Heen gadaan eqqida asatappe issi issi asati iza waasoza siydi “Elaasa xeeygesko!” gida.
Istafe issadey woxxi biidi zandza misatiza sefinege geetettiza miish ekkidi caalida woyne cajjen yeggi caphisidinne shomboqo geetettiza mitha xeeran qaaphidi uyana mala Yesusa duunakko shiishshides.
Hanko asay qasse “Aggagite ane, Elaassi yiidi iza ashshin beyana” gida.
Yesusi qasseka dhoqa qaalan waassidi shempo kezides.
He wode Xoossa Keeththa magalashay bolla hu7era duge simmi daakkettidi nam7u kezides; biittay qaaxides; zaallati za77ida.
Duufoti doyettida; kase hayqqida Xoossa asappe daro baggay dendides.
Duufoppe kezidi Yesusa denthafe guye gede geeshsha katama gelidi darota ayfen bettida.
Mato halaqaynne izara issife Yesusa naagizayti biitta qaathanne hanidayssa wursi beyidi daro babbida. Qasse “Hayssi tumappe Xoossa Naakko!” gida.
Galilappe yiidi Yesusa koshshizazan ooththi maadanas kaalliza daro macasati hanizayssa wursikka hahora xeellishe heen deettes.
Ista giddon Magdaleppe yida Maaramiranne, Yaqoobenne Yoosefe aayo Maaramira, qasseka Zabidoosa nayta aayeyira issife deettes.
Gadey omarsishin Yoosefe geetettiza issi dure adde dayssi Armatiyasa geetettizasoppe yides. Izikka ba baggara Yesusa kaallizade.
Izi Philaxoosa sinthi shiiqidi Yesusa aha izas immana mala woossin Philaxoosikka izas immana mala azazides.
Yoosefey aha ekkidi geeshshiza moogo afalan xaaxides.
Shuch woocidi baassi giigissida duufon efi woththidi gita shuch gendersidi duufoza gordides.
Hessa wode Magdale Maaramiranne hara Maaramira duufoza ginan uttida.
Sambatas giigettiza wontetha gallas Qeeseta halaqatinne Farsaaweeti Philaxoosa sinth shiiqidi,
“Godo! He wordoy kase paxa dishe ‘Heedzdzu gallassafe guye ta dendana’ gida qaalay nu woznan turchu gides.
Hessa gish iza kaallizayti iza aha kaysoti ekkidi deres ‘Izi hayqoppe dendides’ giidi woresonta mala heedzdzantho gallas gakkanaas duufoy naagettana mala azaza; akay giikko kaseyssafe guye balay aadhdheth gidana” gida.
Philaxoosi “Intes naagizayti deettes; biidinne intes erettida mala naagisite” gides.
Istika biidi duufoza dunna maatamen gordidi naagana zabe essida.
Sambatay aadhdhidappe guye saamintappe koyro gallas buro saloy zo7ishin Magdale Maaramanne hara Maarama duufoza beyana bida.
Qopponta dishin gita biitta qaathi hanides; Goda kiitanchaykka saloppe wodhdhi duufakko biidi shuchcha gendersidi iza bolla uttides.
Kiitanchas medhay wolqantha poo7o mala; may7oykka shachcha mala bootha.
Duufo naagizayti kiitanchazas babbidi kokkoridinne hayqeth misatida.
Kiitanachay macasata “Babbofte; inte kaqettida Yesusa koyizayssa ta erays; izi ha7i haan baawa; izi kase yootida mala hayqoppe dendides; ha yiidi izi ichidaso beyte.
<range>
Ha7ikka eleli biidi iza kaallizaytas ‘Hayqoppe dendides. Intefe kasetidi Galila bees; inte iza heen demmana’ giidi yootite. Hi7a ta intes yootadis” gides.
Macasatikka baboninne ufayssan kumidi iza kaallizaytas yootanas elelidi wothan duufoy dizaso yeggi aggidi bida.
Heerakka Yesusi ista demmidi “Hayto saro” gides. Istika Yesusakko shiiqidinne iza toho oykkidi izas goynnida.
Yesusi ista “Babbofte! Biidinne isti Galila baana mala ta ishatas yootite. Isti tana heen beyana” gides.
Macasati buro oge bolla dishin naagizaytappe guutha baggati katama biidi hanidayssa wursi Qeeseta halaqatas yootida.
Qeeseta halaqatikka dere cimatara shiiqettidi zorettida; wotadaratas gidiza miish immidi “ ‘Nuni dhisikidaashin iza kaallizayti qammara yiidi kaysoti efida’ gite gida.
<range>
Hayssi worey dere haarizayssa matan siyetikkokka nuni izas lo7ethi yootana; aykko iitayka inte bolla gakkonta mala nu ooththana” gida.
Wotadaratikka miisha ekkidi isti gida mala ooththida; hayssi yo7ozi hachchi gakkanaas Ayhudata achchan daroson yootettishe dees.
Hessafekka Yesusa kaalliza tammanne issineti Yesusi ista bessida Galilan diza zuma bolla kezida.
Yesusa beyida mala izas goynnida, ista garasafe guuxiza baggati sidhida.
Yesusikka bana kaallizaytakko shiiqidi “Saloninne sa7an godateththi taas imettides. Hessa gish biidi dere ubba Aawa, Naazanne Xillo Ayana sunthan xammaqishe; tana kaallizayta ooththite; ta intena azazidayssa wursi naagana mala tamarsite. Takka alame wurseth gakkanaas ta intenara days” gides.
<range>
<range>
Xoossa Naa Yesus Kirstoosa koyro Mishiraachchoy hayssa;
nabe Isayaasa baggara “Hekko nees oge lo7ethanade ta kiittanade neeppe sinthara yeddana.
‘Godas oge giigissite; izi baana oge suurisidi ooththite’ gishe bazzo biittan waassiza giiris” geetetti xaafettides.
Hessathoka Xammaqiza Yohannisi asa xamaqishenne “Inte nagarappe simmidi xammaqettite, Xoossi inte nagara atto gaana” gi awajjishe bazzora kezi wodhdhides.
Yuhuda derey kumeth Yerusalame asay wuri Yohannisakko bi biidi ba nagara nagara paaxi paaxi Yordaanoose Shaafan Yohannisa kushen xammaqettides.
He wode Yohannisi may7izay gaamella isikeppe oosettida may7o; qasse ba xeessan dafo gixxees. Izi miza qumay boolenne degera eessa.
Izi “Tani hokkada iza caamma qasho birshanas bessontadey, taappe aadhdhizadey taappe guyera yaana.
Tani intena haaththan xammaqays izi gidikko intena Xillo Ayanan xammaqana” giidi sabakides.
He wode Yesusi Galila giddon diza Naazirete geetettiza katamaype Yordanoose Shaafa yiidi Yohannisa kushen xammaqettides.
Yesusi xammaqettidi haaththafe kezida mala saloy doyettin Xillo Ayanay iza bolla haraphe kafo misatidi wodhdhishin beyides.
Qasseka “Ta dosiza Nay nena, nenan ta ufayetays” giza qaala giirisi pude saloppe seetettides.
Heerakka Xillo Ayanay iza duge bazzo kaalethi efides.
Heen bazzonka oyddu tammu gallas gakkanaas Xala7era paacettishe gam7ides. Do7atara issife de7ides. Kiitanchatikka iza maaddida.
Yohannisi qasho keeth gelidayssafe guye Yesusi Xoossa Mishiraachcho qaala sabakishe gede Galila biidi “Wodey gakkides; Xoossa Kawotethi matides; nagarappe simmite, Mishiraachcho qaalan ammante” giidi sabakides.
<range>
Yesusi Galila Abba achchara aadhdhin Simoonaynne iza isha Indiraassi mole oykkizayta gidida gish isti mole oykiza gite abban yeggishin beyides.
Yesusi ista “Haa yite! Tana kaallite; inte mole oykki shiishshiza mala ta intena as oykkizayta ooththana” gides.
Isti heerakka mole giteza yeggi aggidi Yesusa kaallida.
Guuth gede sinthe aadhdhidi Zabidoosa naa Yaqoobeynne iza isha Yohannisi wogolon uttidi mole gite giigissishin beyidinne heerakka ista xeygides.
Istika ba aawa Zabidoosas qaxarettidi ooththiza asatara issife wogoloza giddon aggidi Yesusa kaalli bida.
Heeppeka Qifirnahoome bida. Heerakka Yesusi Ayhudata Sambata gallas Ayhudata Woosa Keeththe gelidi tamarso oykkides.
Xaafeta mala gidonta godateththara diza asa mala izi tamarsin asay wuri iza timirtezan malalettides.
He wode Ayhudata Woosa Keeththan diza tuna ayanay iza bolla diza issi addey
“Naazirete Yesusa ne nuuppe aazi koyay? Nuna dhayssana yadii? Ne oonakkonne ta nena erays; neni Xoossa geeshshaza” giidi waassides.
Yesuasikka tuna ayanaza “Co7u gaada izappe keza!” giidi hanqides.
Tuna ayanay addeza gendersidi izi qaketishin izappe waassishe kezides.
Derey wuri “Aso hayssi aaza palaa? Hayssi godateththara diza ooratha timirte; tuna ayanatakka azaazees; istika izas azazettetes” gi malalettishe asay ba giddon issoy issa oyshecho oykkides.
Heerakka iza ooso worey kumeth Galila yuushon diza dere ubban siyettides.
Ayhudata Woosa Keeththafe kezida mala Yaqooberanne Yohannisara issife gede Simoonasonne Indiraasaso gelida.
He gelida mala Simoona bolloteya misha harge sakettada ichchidayssa izas yootida.
Hessa gish Yesusi iziikko shiiqidi izi kushe oykidi denthides. Mishay aggin iza dendada ista mokkadus.
Awa arshey wullidappe guye gadey dhumishin asay harganchatanne daydanthi oykkida asaa wursi Yesusakko ekki yides.
He katamayin diza asay wuri keeththa karen shiiqides.
Izikka dumma dumma hargen sakettidayta darota pathides. Daro daydanthataka kessides. Gido attin daydanthati Yesusi oonakkonne eriza gish daydanthati haasayana mala Yesusi koybeenna.
Bazzoy zo7onta malado wontara Yesusi dendidi issi asi bayndaso biidi heen woossa oykkides.
Simooninne izara dizayti Yesusa koyana kezi bida.
Isti iza demmidi asi wuri nena koshshan dees gida.
Yesusikka “Ta yiday tamarsanas gidida gish ane Mishiraachcho qaala yootanas matan diza gutata boos” gides.
Hessa gish Ayhudata Woosa Keeththan geli geli sabakishenne daydanthi kessishe Galila kumeththan yuuyides.
Issi inchiracha hargizadey Yesusakko shiiqidinne iza sinthan gulbatidi “Ne shene gidikko ne tana paththana dandayassa” gi woossides.
Yesusikka addezas mishettidi ba kushe yeddi iza bochidinne “Ta ne paxana mala koyays; paxa!” gides.
Heerakka addeza inchiracha hargey aggin, addezi paxides.
Yesusikka addezas “Oonaska hayssa ne haasayonta mala naageta; gido attin baada Qeeses nena bessa. Derezas marka gidana mala ne paxxidayssas Musey azazida yarshoza shiisha” giidi keehi minth yootides.
<range>
Gido attin addezi kezi biidi ba bida ubbason wore darsi dharcides. Hessa geedon Yesusi ay katamanka qoncera gelanas dandaybenna. Hessafe dendidayssan katamappe karera asi bayndason duus oykkides. Asay gidikko dumma dummasoppekka izakko yides.
Guutha gallassafe guye “Yesusi Qifirnahoome simmidi soon dees” giza wore asay siyides.
Hessa gish keeththara karera uttizasoy dhayana gakkanaas daro derey shiiqides. Izikka Xoossa qaala asas sabakides.
Oyddu as dayti issi tohoy silida as tookkidi izakko ehida.
Asa daroteththafe dendidayssan Yesusi dizaso gaththanas dandayonta gish Yesusi diza ginara kaara qaaridi harganchaza izi ichida halara Yesusa sinth duge woththida.
Yesusi asata ammano beyidi tohoy silida addeza “Ta naazo! Ne nagaray atto geetettides” gides.
Heen gadaan uttida issi issi Muse woga xaafeti ba woznara hayssi addezi wosti hayssatho gizee? “Xoossa bolla cashsha qaala haasayees. Issi Xoossafe attin nagara maarana dandayizay oonee?” giidi qoppida.
<range>
Yesusi heerakka isti ba woznan qoppidayssa ba Ayanan eridi “Inte wosti hayssatho qoppetii?
Tohoy silida addeza, ‘Ne nagaray atto geetettides’ guussafenne ‘Dendada ne hala tookkada ba guussafe awayssi matizee?’
Gido attin Asa Naas biitta bollan nagara maarana godateththi dizayssa inte erana mala” giidi toho sila addeza;
“Dendada ne tookketta yida hala tookkada neso ba” gides.
Izikka dendidi asay wuri beyishin hala tookkidi bides. Heen gadaan diza asay wuri hanozan malaletidi “Kase hayssa malay hanin beybookko” giidi Xoosse galatides.
Qasseka Yesusi Galila Abba lanqe bides. Daro derey izakko yiin izikka yida asa tamarsides.
Izi ogera aadhdhi bishin Ilfiyoosa naa Lewey qaraxa shiishshizason uttidayssa beyidi “Haaya tana kaalla” gides. Izikka dendidi Yesusa kaallides.
Hessafe guye Leewe soon kaththa maaddan utti dishin qaraxa shiishshiza daro asatinne nagaranchati izara kaalli yida gish isti Yesusaranne iza kaallizaytara issife maaddan uttida.
Farsaaweeta baggafe gidida Muse woga tamarsizayti Yesusi nagaranchataranne qaraxa shiishshizaytara mishin beyidi iza kaallizayta “Qaraxa qanxissizaytaranne nagaranchatara aazas mizee?” giidi oychida.
Yesusikka isti gizayssa siydi “Aakimey harganchatas koshshes attin hargontaytas gidenna. Takka nagaranchata xeeyganas yadis attin xillota xeeyganas yabeekke” gides.
Yohannisa kaallizaytinne Farsaaweeti xooma xoomettes. Issi issi asati Yesusakko yiidi “Yohannisa kaallizaytinne Farsaaweeta kaallizayti xoomettes shin nena kaallizayti aazas xoomettenee?” gi oychida.
Yesusikka istas “Mishiray istara dishin mishira laggeti xoomi erizoo? Mishiray istara dishin xoomi eretenna.
Mishiray istafe ekettana wodey yaana. He wode isti xoomana.
“Gal7a may7o bolla ooratha woso woththi sikkizadey oonikka deenna; hessatho ooththikko oorathazi gal7a daakki daakki yeggees; daakkeththaykka kaseppe gede aadhdhi iitees.
Hessathoka ooratha woyne cajje gal7a lukkamon woththizadey deenna. Wothiza gidikko woyne cajjezi gal7a lukkamoza dhuussees; woyne cajjezinne lukkamozi nam7ay morettetes. Hessa gish ooratha woyne cajjey daanas bessizay ooratha lukkamonna” gides.
Yesusi Ayhudata Sambata gallas giste tiya giddora aadhdhishin iza kaallizayti izara issife bishe tiya xupho oykkida.
Farsaaweeti “Nena kaallizayti Sambata gallas diggettida miish aazas ooththizoo?” giidi Yesusa oychida.
Izikka istas “Dawutey gafidi miza miish koyda wode izara issife dizaytara izi ooththidayssa nabebibeekketii?
Abiyatarey Qeeseta halaqatethan dishin izi Xoossa Keeththe gelidi Qeeseti xalala maanas bessiza dumma kaththa baassi miidinne banara dizaytas immides” gides.
Qasseka Yesusi istas “Sambatay asas medhettides attin asi Sambatas medhetibenna.
Hessa gish ta Asa Nay Sambata goda” gides.
Hara gallas Yesusi Ayhuda Woosa Keeththe gelides. Henka kushey silidadey dees.
Yesusa mootanas gaaso koyiza asati izi Ayhudata Sambata gallas pathanakkonne giidi pathishin beyana koyda.
Izikka kushey silida addeza “Heen shiiqi uttida asa sinthan denda eqqa” gides.
Hessafe guye Yesusi asa “Sambata gallas bessizay lo7o oosoyee? Iita oosoo? Asa shempo ashoyee? Woykko shempo wodhoo?” giidi oychides. Istika co7u gida.
Ista wozna shuchchatethan mishetidi iza giddoththidi yuuyi aadhdhi eqqida asa hanqora xeelidi addeza “Ne kusheza piddisa!” gides. Addezikka ba kushe piddisin kushezi mulera pathides.
Farsaaweeti kezi biidi iza wosti dhayssanakkonne Herdoosa bagga gidida asatara zoretida.
Yesusi bana kaallizaytara abbako bides. Galilappenne Yuhudappe yida daro derey iza kaallides.
Izi ooththizayssa siydi asay Yuhudappe, Yerusalameppe, Edoomeppe, Yordanoose pinthan diza deretappe qasse Xirooseppenne Sidoona heerappe izakko yides.
Asay darida gish iza un7ethonta mala guutha wogolo isti giigisana mala bana kaallizayta azazides.
Izi daro harganchata pathida gish sakoy waayssizayti wuri iza ba kushera bochchanas dafettida.
Tuna ayanatikka Yesusa beyida mala iza sinthan kundidi “Neni Xoossa Naa” giidi waassida.
Gido attin izi oonakkonne tuna ayanati qoncisonta mala keehippe hanqides.
Yesusi pude zuma bolla kezidi ba koyizayta baako yaana mala xeygides, istika izakko yida.
Izara issife gidana malanne sabakanas yeddana mala tammanne nam7ata “Hawaareta” gi sunthides.
Asaappe daydanthata kessana mala istas godateththi immides.
Izi sunthida tammanne nam7ata sunthi hayssafe kaallizayssa; Phexroosa geetettida Simoona,
Bi7orinegeese woykko daada nayta geetettida Zabidoosa nayta Yaqoobenne Yohannisa,
Indiraasa, Piliphoosa, Bartelemoosa, Matoosa, Toomaasa, Ilfiyoosa naa Yaqoobe, Tadoosa, ba baggas mishettiza Simoona,
Yesusa aaththi immida Asqoroonto Yuhuda.
Hessafe guye Yesusi issi so gelides. Izinne iza kaallizayti kath maana wodey istas dhayana gakkanaas derey qasseka dari shiiqides.
Iza hanota siyida iza dabboti “Gooyonta aggenna” giidi banara ekki baanas izi dizaso gakkida.
Yerusalameppe yida xaafetikka “Bi7elizeebula geetettiza daydanthata halaqay iza bolla dees. Izi daydanthata kessizay daydanthata halaqa wolqanko!” gida.
Izikka ista xeygidi leemisora “Xala7ey asappe Xala7e wosti kessanee?
Ba giddon shaakoy diza kawotethi minnanas dandayenna.
Issi keeththa asikka ba giddon shaaketikko eqqanaas dandayenna.
Hessathoka Xala7ey ba garasan issoy issara shaakettikkonne ixettikko minni eqqanaas dandayenna. Hessika izas wurseth gidana.
“Hessa geedon issadey koyrottidi wolqama as qachonta dishe wolqamazaso gelanassinne iza miishe bonqanas dandayenna; iza aqo bonqanas dandayettizay wolqamaza qachikko xalala.
“Ta intes tumu gays; asa naytas nagaraynne cashshi wuri maarettana.
Gido attin Xillo Ayana bolla cashsha qaala haasayiza asa ubbas mernaas nagara acco gidana attin maarettenna” gides.
Hessa izi giday isti iza “Ne bolla tuna ayanay dees” gida gishasa.
Hessafe guye iza aayeyanne iza ishati kare yi eqqidinne ase izakko kiitti xeygisida.
Iza yuuyi aadhdhi uttida daro asay “Hekko ne aayeyanne ne ishati karen eqqidi nena koyeettes” gida.
Izikka zaaridi “Ta aaya oonee? Ta ishati oonantee?” gides.
Iza yuuyi uttida asaako xeelidi “Ta aayeyanne ta ishati haytantakko!
Xoossa shene ooththizay wuri izi ta isha, ta michonne ta aayo” gides.
Qasse Yesusi hara wode abba achchan tamarso oykkides. Izakko keehi daro derey shiiqida gish abba giddon diza wogolo dizaarin gelidi uttides; asayka wuri abba achchan shiiqides.
Izikka daro yo7ota leemiso hizgi tamarsides.
“Siyite! Issadey zereth zeranas kezides.
Izi zerishin issi issi zerethi oge bolla wodhdhides. Oge bolla wodhdhida zeretha kafoti maxi mida.
Baggay mela biittan wodhdhides. He biittay mela gidida gish heerakka caarides.
Gido attin awa arshey kezida mala shullidi xapho yeddonta gish melides.
Qasse issi zerethi aguntha giddon wodhdhides; agunthayka diccidi cuullida gish ayfibenna.
Hara zerethi qasse lo7o orde biitta bolla wodhdhida gish caaridi diccides; ayfeka ayfides; Issoy heedzdzu tammu, issoy qasse usuppun tammu, issoy qasse xeetu ayfides.”
Yesusi qasseka “Siyiza haythi dizadey siyo!” gides.
Yesusi barka dishin tammanne nam7atinne kase izara diza asay izi yootida leemisoza gish iza zaari oychida.
Izikka istas “Intes Xoossa Kawoteththa xuura eroy gelides shin karen dizaytas gidikko yo7oy wuri leemisora yootettes.
Hessika kase ‘Isti beyidi beyidayssa akeekonta malanne simonta mala, qasseka ista nagaray maaretonta malakko’ ” gides.
Qasseka Yesusi “Hayssi leemisoy intes gelibenee? Histin hara leemiso inte wosti erannee?
Zerizadey qaala zerees.
Issi issi asati oge bolla wodhdhida zeretha misatettes; isti qaala siyiza wode Xala7ey yiidi heerakka isti siyida qaala ista woznappe ekkichees.
Hessathoka harati mela biitta bolla wodhdhida zeretha misatetes. Isti qaala siydi ufayssan ekketes.
Gido attin isti xapho yeddonta gish guutha wode gam7ishin qaala geedon metoy woykko goodetay asata bolla yiza wode heerakka dhuphetetes.
Harati qasse aguntha giddon wodhdhida zeretha misatettes; isti qaala sisi siyeetes.
Gido attin ha biitta metoy, miisha siiqoynne hara amoy isti siyida qaala cuullidi ayfe ayfonta mala diggees.
Hankoyti lo7o biittan zeretida zeretha misatettes; heytikka qaala siydi ekkizadenne heedzdzu tammu ayfe, usuppun tammu ayfenne xeetu ayfe ayfizayta” gides.
Qasseka Yesusi “Xompe oythidi geemason woykko arsa giddon woththi eretii? Poo7ana mala qonceson wotheeta gidenee?
Hessa gish qotettidi qonce kezontay, poo7on kezonta geeman attanay baawa.
Hessa gish siyiza haythi dizaddey siyo!” gides.
Gujidikka “Inte siyizayssa woznan woththite; inte makkiza miishara intes makettana; hessafekka daroy gujettana.
Dizaddes gujettana shin bayndadefe izas dizaarakka ekketichana” gides.
Qasseka Yesusi “Xoossa kawotethi zereth zeriza issi as misatawus.
Zeridadey omars dhisikees. Wontishin dendees; gido attin izi eronta dishin zerettida kaththay mokkidi diccees.
Gadeyaka koyro caarech, kaalethada pudhe, qsseka pudheza bolla lo7o ayfe immawus.
Kathay kaxxidappe guye boney gakkin keeththa aaway heerakka maxa oykkes” gides.
Yesusi “Xoossa Kawoteth nu aazara ginisanee? Aazara leemisanee?
Biitta bolla ubbafe laafa gidida sanafice ayfe misatawus.
Zeretada diccidappe guye qas atakilteta ubbafe aadhdhiza gish kafoti yiidi he atakiltey haggata kuwa giddon shempeetes” gides.
Yesusikka asay ekkanas dandayizayssa keena hayta misatiza hara daro leemisora istas yootides.
Ay miish gidikkokka asas leemisoy baynda yooti erenna. Izinne iza kaallizayti xalla diza wode gidikko wursi birsh yootees.
He gallas gadey qammishin bana kaallizayta “Ane gede he pinth pinnoos” gides.
Isti asa heen aggagidi izi utti diza wogolozara Yesusa ekki bida. Hara wogolotikka istara issife deettes.
He wode wolqama dambalay abba bolla dendidi wogoloza haaththi kumana gakkanaas dambalay shocechides.
Gido attin Yesusi borkoth borkottidi wogolozas guye baggan ichides. Istika iza denthidi “Astamare! Nuni dhayishin nena metenee?” gida.
Izikka dendidi carkoza “Co7u ga!” abbaka “Woppu ga!” gides; carkoykka co7u gides; mulekka co7u gides.
Bana kaallizaytaka “Hayssatho aazas babbidetii? Hayssa gakkanaas intes ammanoy bawee?” gides.
Istika keehi babidi ba giddon issoy issara “Carkoynne abbay izas azazettizay hayssi oonee?” geetettida.
Abba pinnidi gede Gergesenoone geetettizaso bida.
Yesusi wogoloyippe wodhdhida mala tuna ayanay iza bolla dizaddey duufoppe kezidi Yesusara gaaggana izakko yides.
Hayssi addezi duufoson dizaddenne haray attoshin oonikka iza sansalatanka qachanas dandaybenna.
Daro wode toho birataranne sansalatara qashetees. Gido attin kushe sansalata duuththethi yegees; toho birataka mentherethi yeges; oonikka iza oykidi teqanas dandaybenna.
Gallassinne qamma duufota giddoninne zumata bolla yuuyi yuuyi waassishe ba bolla shuchchara qanxerethidi madunthees.
Izikka Yesusa hahon beyida mala wothan izakko yiidi iza sinthan gulbatidi goynnides.
Keehi waassidi “Haysso wogga Xoossa Naa Yesusa, nees tanara aazi dizee? Xoossa sunthan ta nena woossays tana waaysoppa” gides.
Izi hessa giday Yesusi kase “Neni tuna ayanay hayssafe keza” gida gishassa.
Hessafe qasse Yesusi iza “Ne sunthi oonee?” giidi oychides. Izikka “Nuni darota gidida gish ta sunthi Leegone geetettes” gides.
He dereppe kessi yeddonta mala Yesusa keehi woossides.
Heen matan zuma bolla daro guddunthi heemettes.
Tuna ayanati “Nu guddunthatan gelana mala nuus ero garkii?” giidi Yesusa woossida.
Izikka istas “Ero” gides. Tuna ayanatikka addezappe kezidi guddunthatan gelida. Nam7u shi gidida guddunthay wuri aafozara dugeththa genderetti wodhdhidi abban mitettida.
Gudduntha heemmizayti baqatidi hanidayssa katamaninne dere giddon yootida. Dereyka hanidayssa beyanas ba dizasoppe dizasoppe kezides.
Yesusakko yiidi daro daydanthi iza bolla diza addeza woznay izas simmin may7o may7idinne wogara uttidayssa yida asay beyidi babbides.
Hayssa beyida asay daydanthi iza bolla diza addeza gishshinne guddunthati hanoyssa derezas yootida.
Hessafe guye he dere asay Yesusi ista dere yeddidi baana mala woossides.
Yesusi wogolon gelishin daydanthati izappe kezida addezi Yesusara daanas woossides.
Yesusi qasse izi oychidayssa akay giidinne “Neni gede ne so ba, Goday nees ay mala gita miish ooththidakkonne izi nees ooththida maarotetha ne so asas yoota” gides.
Addezikka baso biidi Yesusi izas ooththida gita miish wursi tammu katama geetettiza deren yootin siyiday wurikka malalettides.
Qasseka Yesusi wogolon gelidi gede pinth pinnidi abba achchan dishin daro asay iza achchi shiiqidinne iza giddoththides.
Ayhudata Woosa Keeththa halaqatappe issoy Iya7iroosa geetettizayssi izi dizaso biidi Yesusa demmida mala iza toho bolla kundidi
“Taas guutha naa dizaara hayqqana gawus. Iza hayqqonta paxa daana mala ne ha yaada ne kushe izi bolla wotharkii?” giidi keehi woossides.
Yesusikka izara issife bides. Daro asay iza un7ethana gakkanaas kaallides.
Tammanne nam7u layth kumeth suuthi izi bollafe gukkiza macas dizaara heen asaara dawus.
Iza baassi diza miish wursa ongana gakkanaas akimeppe akime laamon daro daburadus. Gido attin sakoy izis gede darides attin aykkokka lo7ibenna.
Iza Yesusa gish siyida mala asa giddora Yesusa guyera kaallada iza may7o bochchadus.
Gaasoyka “Ta ay hanadakka iza may7o kushera bocho bochidakkoka ta paxana” gaada qoppida gishassa.
Gukkiza suuthay heerakka eqi aggides; izakka paxidayssa ba asatethan eradus.
Bappe wolqay kezidayssa Yesusi eridi gede asaakko simmidi “Ta may7o oone bochiday?” gides.
Iza kaallizayti qasse “Hayssi derey un7etidi sugetishin beyashe waanada ‘Tana bochiday oonee?’ gay” gida.
Yesusi hessa ooththiday oonakkonne beyanas yuushi xeellides.
Macasayakka baas aazi waanidakkone erada babbashenne kokkorashe yaada Yesusa sinthan gufannada hanida tuma wursa izas yootadus.
Izikka “Ta naye! Ne ammanoy nena ashshides. Saron ba! Ne waayeppe paxa!” gides.
Yesusi buro haasayan dishin Ayhudata Woosa Keeththe halaqa Iya7iroosa soppe yiidi Iya7iroosas “Ne naya hayqadus, Goda mela aazas daaburissay?” gida.
Gido attin Yesusi ista haasaya lepi histidi Ayhudata Woosa Keeththa halaqaza “Ne ammano xalla ammana attin babbofa!” gides.
Phexroosa Yaqooberanne Yaqoobe isha Yohannisappe attin haray oonikka iza kaallana mala koybenna.
Gede Ayhudata Woosa Keeththa halaqa so gakkida mala asay waassishe camo yeeho yeekkizayssa beyides.
So gelidi “Hayssi wuri aaza waasonne aaza yeehoo? Naya dhiskadus attin hayqqabeykku” gides.
Qasse asay wuri iza bolla miicides; asa wursikka keeththafe kessidi nay aawanne nay aayiyo qasseka izara issife yidayta iza kaallizayta xalla kaaleththidi naya diza so gelides.
Nay kushekka oykkidi “Xaabita kum!” gides. “Xaabita kum” guussas birsheththi “Hanne naye, denda” guussa.
Nayakka heerakka denda eqqadus; heenne haane hamutadus. Iziska laythay tammanne nam7u laytha; asaykka he hanozan daro malalettides.
Yesusi hayssa oonikka eronta mala keehi minthi yootides; “Nays maana quma immite” gides.
Hessafe guye Yesusi heeppe dendidi gede ba dere bides. Iza kaallizaytikka izara bida.
Ayhudata Sambatay gakkin Ayhudata Woosa Keeththe gelidi tamarsishin siyida asay “Hayssi addezi hayssa wursi aawappe ekkidee? Hayssi izas imettida eratethay aazee? Qasse hayti izi ooththiza malatati waani iza kushen hanizoo?” gishe malalettida.
“Hayssi anaxeza gidenee? Maarami naa Yaqoobenta Yoosanta, Yuhudantanne Simoonanta isha gidenee? Iza micheti nunara haan nu matan dizayta detenee?” giidi hessafe dendidayssani izan ufayettibetenna.
Yesusikka istas “Nabey bonchettontay ba deren ba dabbota giddoninne baso asa achchan xalla” gides.
Heen guutha harganchata bolla kushe woththi pathorippe attin hara aykko malataka ooththanas dandaybenna.
Istas ammanoy bayndayssa beyidi malalettides. Hessafekka Yesusi gutan gutan yuuyi yuuyi tamarsides.
Tammanne nam7ata baako xeygidi nam7u nam7u histi kiittishe tuna ayanata bolla istas godateththi immides.
Izi “Oges gidiza guufe attin oge shinqe woykko korojo woykko miishe oykkofte.
Caamma aaththite gido attin laammana may7o oykkofte.
Issi keeththe inte gelikko he katamappe inte kezana gakkanaas he keeththan diite.
Awanka oonikka intena mokki ekkonta ixikko heeppe kezishe he dereta bolla marka gidana mala inte toho bolla diza gudulla qoqofte” giidi azazides.
Istika heeppe kezidi derey maarotethan gelana mala sabakida.
Daro daydanthata kessida; daro harganchata zayte tiyi tiyidi pathida.
Yesusa sunthi kaseppe ereti ereti bishin kawo Herdoossi hessa siyides. Issi issi asati “Hayssa mala malatata ooththiza Xammaqiza Yohannisi hayqoppe dendinikko” gida.
Baggayti “Elaasa” geettes; bagga asay qasse “Kase nabetappe issa misatees” geettes.
Herdoossi yo7oza siydi “Ta iza qoodhe qanxisida Yohannisi hayqoppe paxi dendides” gides.
Herdoossi ba isha Piliphoosa macho Herodiyado ekkida geedon oyketidi qashettana mala azazidi Yohannisa qasho keeththe gelthides.
Yohannisi Herdoosa “Ne isha macho ne ekkonta mala wogay nena diggees” gida gish qachides.
Herodiyada hessa gish hoollotada iza wodhisanas koyadus shin dandayabekku.
Gaasoyka Yohannisi xillonne geeshsha as gididayssa Herdoossi eriza gish Yohannisas babbessinne iza naagees. Yohannisi yootizayssa Herdoossi siydi hirgiza gidikkokka izi yootizayssa woznappe siyees.
Herdoosa yeletta gallas bonchanas dhoqa shuumetas; olla wotadarata azaziza waannatassinne Galila biittan keehi erettiza gita asatas gibira kessides; hessika Herodiyadis giiga gallas gidides.
Herodiyadi maca naya gelada asa sinthan yeth yexin Herdoosanne izi xeygida asa izi yethay ufaysidees. Kawoykka nayo “Ne koyiza miish wursa tana oycha ta nees immana” gides.
Qasseka ta kawoteththa bagga gididakkokka ne oychikko wursa ta nees immana giidi izis caaqides.
Nayakka elela kezada ba aayeyo “Kawo ay oychoo?” gadus. Aayiyakka “Xammaqiza Yohannisa hu7e qanxada imma ga” gadus.
Nayakka elela kezada kawozakko gelada “Xammaqiza Yohannisa hu7e keren wothada ne taas immana mala koyays” ga oychadus.
Kawoy he yo7ozan daro modhettides; gido attin xeeygetida imatha gishinne caaqida qaala gish izis akay gaanas koybeenna.
Hessa gish wotadaratappe issa eeson kiittidi Yohannisa qoodhe qanxidi iza hu7e ekki yaana mala azazides; izikka biidi qasho keeththa giddon Yohannisa qoodhe qanxides.
Hu7eza kerera ehidi nays immides; nayakka ba aayeyssi immadus.
Yohannisa kaallizaytikka hessa siyida mala yiidi Yohannisa aha ekki efidi moogida.
Hessafe guye Hawaareti simmidi Yesusa achchan yuuyi aadhdhi ba ooththidayssanne ba tamarsidayssa wursi izas yootida.
Daro asay yishenne bishe giza gish quma miza wodeykka bettibenna; “Ane inte xalla tanara asi bayndaso biidi ane guuth shempi ekkite” gides.
Hessa gish isti barka wogolon gelidi issi asi bayndaaso bida.
Isti bishin daroti beyidi tohora wothan istafe sinthe aadhdhida.
Yesusi wogolozappe wodhdhiza wode daro derey shiiqi uttidayssa beyides. Heemmizadey baynda mehe mala gidida gish asas qadhettides. Daro yo7okka tamarso oykkides.
He wode gadey qammi qammi biza gish iza kaallizayti izakko shiiqidi “Hayssi nu dizasoy bazzokko, gadeykka qammides.
Hayssa heeran asi dizaso biidi asay baas miza kath shami maana mala asa yedda” gida.
Izi istas zaaridi “Asaas miza miish inte immite” gides. Istika malalettidi “Nuni biidi nam7u xeetu dinarera kath shamidi hayssa asas immizakko gidandee?” gida.
Izikka istas “Intes ay lagge ukethi dizakonne ane biidi xeellite” giin isti bi xeelidi “Ichashu ukethinne nam7u moley dees” gida.
Hessafe kaallidi asaa cilila maata bolla oyddan oyddan uttisana mala azazides.
Asaykka xeetu xeetunne ichashu tammu ichashu tammu gididi oyddan uttides.
Izikka ichashu ukethanne nam7u moleta ba kushen oykidi pude salo xeelidi anjidinne uketha menthi menthi asas gishana mala bana kaallizaytas immides; nam7u moletaka ubba asas shaakerethides.
Asay wurikka miidi kallides.
Yesusa kaallizayti asay kalli miin attidayssa tammanne nam7u pitha kumeth shiishida.
Kath mida asaappe attumasay xalla ichashu shi.
Heerakka izi asaa moyzishe iza kaallizayti sinthatidi gede pinth Betesayda geetettizso pinnana mala azazides.
Heeppeka ista aggagidi woossanas pude zuma bolla kezides.
Gadey qammin wogoloy abba giddon dishin izi barka biitta bolla dees.
Abba bolla carkoy keehi metida gish iza kaallizayti abba shiri shiri wogolo laaggiza miishara baaxetishin Yesusi beyides. Wonta bolla istako yides; yiidinne ista achchara aadhdhi baanatho hanides.
Gido attin aadhdhi bana hanishin iza beyida mala moytile beyida misatin wurikka waassida.
Wurikka iza beyidi daggammida; izikka heerakka ista yoochidinne “Aykkoy ba; tanakko dagammofte!” gides.
Izikka wogolon istako gelin carkoy co7u gides, istika daro malalettida.
Kase izi ukethan ooththida malata birsheth isti eronta gish ista woznay doccides.
Abba pinnidi Gensereexe geetettizaso gakkida; wogolappe wodhdhidi wogoloza heen qachidi aggi bida.
Isti wogoloppe wodhdhida mala asay Yesusa erides.
Wurikka ba dizaso dizaso woxerettidi harganchata halan tookki tookki ekkidi Yesusi dizaso ehida.
Izi gakkida gutan woykko katama giddon woykko dere giddon gidin harganchati izi aadhdhishin iza woossidinne iza may7o bochidi paxana mala shiishshi shiishshi dubbushshay dizaason woththida. Izi aadhdhi bishin iza may7o bochidayti wuri paxida.
Hessafe guye Farsaaweetinne Yerusalameppe yida issi issi xaafeti Yesusa lanqen yuuyi aadhdhida.
Yesusa kaallizaytappe baggayti mecetonta qita kushera kath mishin beyida.
Farsaaweetinne kase cima Ayhuda asati kase dere woga naaganas kushe lo7ethi meecetonta kath mi erettenna.
Giya bi simmikkokka bolla meeceti geeyonta dishe kath mi erettenna. Hessathoka wancakka, otokka, kerekka, ichchiza hiithekka meecha malata hara wogatakka naagettes.
Farsaaweetinne xaafeti Yesusa “Nena kaallizayti kase aawata woga mala duus aggidi aazas kushe meecetonta kath mizoo?” giidi oychida.
Izikka istas “Isayaassi qoodheppe qommon haniza inte gish ‘Hayssi derey ba metershan xalala tana bonches; woznay gidikko taappe haakkides.
Taas mela hada goynnetes; ista timirteykka asi woththida woga xalla’ giidi yootidays tuma” gides.
Xoossa woga aggidi asi woththida woga naagettes.
Qasseka “inte wogas giidi Xoossa woga inte aggagiza cincateththa ogey intes dees.
Ays giikko Musey ‘Ne aayonne ne aawa boncha; ba aayonne ba aawa cayizaddey mulekka hayqqo’ gides.
Gido attin inte qasse ‘Issi asi ba aawa woykko ba aayo inte taappe demmanas koshshiza maado ta Xoossas immadis’ giikko;
Inte qasse hayssadey ba aawaska ba aayeyssi hara aykkokka ooththana mala koyekketa.
Hessa gish inte woga naagana giidi Xoossa qaala laammeta. Heytanta misatiza darota ooththeta.” gides.
Qasseka Yesusi asa baako xeygidi “Wurikka ta giza siyitenne woznan woththite.
Kareppe ulo gido gelidi as tunisiza issi miishikka deenna. Harappeka ase tunisizay keeththa aawappe gede kare keziza miisha.
Siyiza haythi dizay siyo!” gides.
Izi asa karen aggidi keeththe gelin iza kaallizayti izi yootida leemisoza birsheth Yesusa oychida.
Izikka ista “Inteska yo7oy gellenee? Kareppe gelidi ase tunisiza miishi aazikka deenna.
Kareppe gelizay gede woznan gidonta; duge qantha gido gelees qasse heeppe izaade asatethafe gede kare kezees.” Yesusi hessa giday asi miza kaththi wurikka geesh gididayssa qoncisanassa.
Kaalethidikka “Asappe kezizazi ase tunises.
Asa wozna giddofe kezizay iita qofata, layma amonne kaysoteth, ase wodho, laymateth,
Yiiqeteth, iitateth, baleththo, layma kaas, qanatetteth, asa sunth mooro, otoretethinne azalla.
Hayti iita hanoti wuri asappe kezeetessinne ase tuniseetes” gides.
Yesusi heeppe kezidi Xiroose geetettiza dere bides. Heen issade keeththe gelidi izi heen dizayssa asi eronta mala koyides. Gido attin izi heen iza duussay qotettanas dandayettibenna.
Heerakka issi tuna ayanay oykkida guutha naa dizaari aaya Yesusi heen dizayssa siyada izakko yaada iza toho bolla kundadus.
Macasaya Ayhuda gidonta Girike qaala haasayiza macasashin iza yelettidasoy Sirofinqe geetettes. Izakka Yesusi naype tuna ayana kessana mala woossadus.
Yesusi zaaridi izis “Nayta quma ekki kanas yegganas bessonta gish koyro nayti mi kalletto” gides.
Izakka zaarada “Ee Godo! Kanatikka maadda matan de7idi nayta kusheppe gaden wodhdhidayssa meetesikko” gadus.
Izikka “Histikko neni hessa gida gish ba! Daydanthay ne naype kezides” gides.
Iza simmada so bishin naya daydanthay yeddin paxada hiixan ichchidaro demmadus.
Hessafe Yesusi Xiroose biittafe dendidi Sidoona gizasora aadhdhi tammu katama gizasora kanthidi gede Galila Abbako gakkides.
Asay issi haytha tullenne ayfe qooqe asi izakko he ekki yiidi Yesusi iza bolla ba kushe wothana mala woossida.
Yesusikka iza asappe shaakki ekki biidi ba kushe biradhdheta addeza haythan gelthides; qasseka cuchch cuttidi addeza inxarsa bochides.
Pude salo xeelidinne tookki shempidi “Efita” gides. Hessika “Pogeta” guussa.
Heerakka addeza haythati pogettida; inxarsaykka birshettin geeshshi haasayides.
Yesusi hayssa beyidayti oonaska yootonta mala azazides; gido attin asay izi azazizadayssafe bollara keehi gujidi yootida.
Derezikka wogappe aaththi malalettidi “Izi ooththidayssi wuri lo7o; tulleti siyana mala, duuna duudeti haasayana mala ooththides” gida.
He wode qasse daro asi shiiqides. Shiiqida asas miza kaththi baynda gish Yesusi bana kaallizayta xeygidi,
“Hayti asati tanara heedzdzu gallas gakkanaas gam7ida gishshinne qasseka istas miza kaththi baynda gish tana miichetes.
Istafe issi issi asati hahoppe yida gish hayssa gafara ta ista so yeddikko daaburidi oge bolla kundana” gides.
Iza kaallizaytikka zaaridi “Hayssa bazzon hayssa mala dere mizana quma awappe demmanee?” gida.
Izikka ista “Intekon aapun ukethi dizee?” gi oychides. Istika “Laapun ukethi dees” gida.
Izikka asay gaden uttana mala azazides; laapun uketha ba kushen oyki galatidinne menthidi asas gishechana mala bana kaallizaytas immin istika derezas gishida.
Qasseka heen diza qeeri guutha moleta gish Xoossa galatidi guutha moleta asaas gishechana mala bana kaallizayta azazides.
Dereyka miidi kallides. Hessafekka iza kaallizayti maaddafe palahida kath laapun pitha kumeth denthida.
Hessa mida asay oyddu shi gidana. He asa moyzidi bana kaallizaytara wogolon gelidi gede Dalmanuuta geetettizaso bides.
<range>
Farsaaweeti yiidi Yesusara palameteth oykkida. Iza paacanas koyiidi bana saloppe malata bessana mala oychida.
Izikka tookki shempidi “Hayssi yelettazi aazas malata koyizee? Ta intes tuma gays; hayssa yelettas issi malataykka imettenna” gides.
Ista heen aggidinne wogolon gelidi he pinth pinnides.
Iza kaallizayti kath oykkonta balettida gish issi uketh attin wogolo giddon hara ay kaththikka deenna.
Yesusi ista “Farsaaweeta irshofenne Herdoosa irshofe naagetite” giidi azazides.
Isti qasse ba giddon issoy issara “Izi nuna hayssa gizay nuus kath baynda gishassa” gi yootettida.
Qasse Yesusi ista qofa eridi “Nuus kaththi baynda gish gaasa giidi inte giddon aazas hasayettetii? Ha7ikka yuushi qoppeketii? Woznanka wotheketii? Woykko inte woznay shuchchatidee?
Intes ayfey dees shin xeelleketii? Haythi dees shin siyekketii? Akeekekketii?
Ichashu uketha ichashu shi asaas ta mentha immin aapun pitha kumeththa kath denthidetii?” gides. Istika zaaridi “Tammanne nam7u” gida.
Izikka “Laapun uketha oyddu shi asas ta mentha immin aapun pitha kumeththa kath denthidetii?” gi oychin istika “Laapun” gida.
Izikka ista “Histin ha7i gakkanaas yuushi qoppibeekketakka!” gides.
Hessafe gede Betesayda geetettizaso bida. Guutha asatikka issi ayfe qooqe asi Yesusakko ehidi Yesusi iza bochchana mala woossida.
Izikka he qooqeza kushe oykki goochchidi asi dizasoppe gede kare kessi addeza ayfen cuttidinne ba kushe iza bolla woththidi “Ha7i nees aazi bettizee?” gi oychides.
Izikka dhoqu gi xeelidi “Asay mith misatidi qaxettishe beettes” gides.
Qasseka Yesusi ba kusheta iza ayfeta bolla woththides; heerakka iza ayfeti xeellida; poo7oyka izas simmin wursikka geeshshi xeellides.
Qasse “Ha gutata giddo geloppanne oonaska yootoppa” giidi iza gede izaso yeddides.
Yesusi bana kaallizaytara Qisaariya Piliphisiyoose geetettiza dere achchan diza gutata bides; isti oge bolla dishin bana kaallizayta “Tana asay oona gizee?” giidi oychides.
Istika zaaridi nena “Xammaqiza Yohannisa gizaytikka deettes, baggati qasse Elaasa geettes, harati qas nabetappe issade geettes” giidi yootida.
Kaaleththidikka intech tana oona geetii? giidi oychides. Phexroosi “Neni Kirstoosa” gides.
Yesusikka ba gish oonaska isti yootonta mala minthi yootides.
Hessafe Yesusi bana kaallizayta, “Asa Nay daro waaye beyanayssanne dere cimatan, Qeeseta halaqaninne xaafetan kadhettanayssa asa kushen hayqqanayssa, hayqoppe heedzdzantho gallas dendanas bessees” giidi tamarso oykkides.
Izikka hessa istas qoncisi yootides, Phexroosikka iza dumma shaakki efidi “Hessatho gooppa!” giidi hanqides.
Yesusi qasse bana kaallizayta yuushi xeellishe Phexroosa “Haysso Xala7e ne taappe gede guye ba! Neni asazappe attin Xoossaz qoppakka!” giidi hanqides.
Hessafe guye asa bana kaallizaytara issife baako xeygidi “Tana kaallanas dosizadey diikko bana kaddo; ba masqale tookkidi tana kaallo.
Ba shempo ashshana dosizaddey dhayssana shin ta gishshinne ta Mishiraachcho qaala gish ba shempo dhayssizadey wurikka ashshana.
Asi alame kumeth haarikkonne ba shempofe dhayssiko iza ay go7anee?
Woykko asi ba shempo gish laame ekkanay aazi dizee?
“Hayssa laymanne nagarancha yeletta giddon dishe tananinne ta qaalan yellatiza asi wuri ta Asa Nay ta Aawa bonchoranne Geeshsha Kiitanchatara yiza wode izan yeellatana” gides.
Kaalethidikka Yesusi “Ta intes tuma gays; hayssan eqqida asappe Xoossa kawotethi wolqara yishin beyana gakkanaas hayqqonta gam7ana issi issi asati deettes” gides.
Usuppun gallassafe guye Yesusi Phexroosa Yaqoobenne Yohannisa banara kaalethi ekkidi issi gita zuma bolla kezides. Isti barka dishin ista sinthan iza medhay laameti wodhdhides.
Izi may7ida may7oy biitta bolla oonikka may7o meecidi hessa mala boothanas dandayonta booth boottides.
He wode Elaassinne Musey Yesusara hasayettishe istas beettida.
Phexroosi Yesusa “Astamare! Nuni haan hayssan dizaakko nuus lo7o; nees issi daase, Muses issi daase, qasse Elaasas issi daase, heedzdzu daaseta nu oothikkochii?” gides.
Daro babbida gish Phexroosi ba gizayssa eridi gibenna.
Heerakka shaaray ista kammin shaara giddora “Hayssi ta dosiza ta naazakko! Izi giza siyite” giza qaala giirisi yides.
Heerakka isti yuushi xeellin Yesusappe attin oonikka hara as istara deenna.
Isti zuma bollafe duge wodhdhishin Asa Nay hayqoppe dendana gakkanaas hayssa isti beyidayssa oonaska yootonta mala azazides.
Istika baas yootida qaala ba woznan oykkida shin “Hayqoppe dendo guussi ay guussakkonne” giidi ba giddon haasayettida
Qasse isti Muse woga tamarsizayti “Kasetidi Elaassi yaana koshshees aazas gizoo?” giidi iza oychida.
Yesusi istas “Tumukka Elaassi kaseti yiidi wursikka giigissana. Histinka Asa Nay daro waaye ekkanassinne kadhettanas bessees geetetti xaafettidayssi intes ay misatizee?
Gido attin ta intes gizay Elaassi gidikko yides shin asaykka iza gish xaafettida mala bana koshshida mala iza bolla ooththides” gides.
Duge giddon attida Yesusa kaallizaytakko isti simmi yishin daro asay ista giddoththin Muse woga tamarsizayti istara palamettizayssa beyida.
Derey iza demmida mala malalettidi sarokanas izakko woxxides.
Izikka ista “Inte istara aaza gish palametettii?” giidi oychides.
Asaa giddofe issadey “Astamare! Tuna ayanay izan gelin duuna duudida ta naa dayssa ta neekko ekka yadis.
Ayanazi dendiza wode bollafe yeggees; duunara gopponto kessi kessi yeggees; achchakka garcees; asatethakka zoodisses. Tuna ayana kessetto gaada nena kaallizayta ta oychin istika dandayibeetenna” gides.
Yesusikka istas zaaridi “Inteno ammanonta yelettato, ayde gakkanaas ta intenara daanee? Qasse ayde gakkanaas ta intena dandayanee? Ane naaza ha ehite” gides.
Asaykka naaza izakko ehides, tuna ayanay Yesusa beyida mala naaza heerakka gaden gendersidi kokkorsidinne duunara gopponto coppu histides.
Yesusi naaza aawa “Hayssi hargey iza ayidesappe oykkidee?” gides. Naaza aawaykka “Naatethafe doommidi” gides.
“Iza wodhanas koydi daro wode tamanka haaththanka yeggees. Nees dandayettikko nuus mishetanne nuna maadda” gides.
Yesusi qasse “ ‘Nees dandayettikko’ gay? Ammanizades wurikka dandayettes” gides.
Naaza aaway heerakka “Ta ammanays shin ta ammanoy laafa, tana maaddarikii?” giidi waassides.
Asay wocamishe buuretti ekkidi izakko yizayssa Yesusi beyidi “Haysso tullenne duude ayanazo! Hayssa naazappe keza, ne qasse simmada gelonta mala ta nena azazays” giidi tuna ayana seerides.
Tuna ayanazikka keehi waassides; naazikka keehi qaketidappe guye naazappe kezides. Daroti hayqqides gaana gakkanaas naazi aha misatides.
Gido attin Yesusi naaza kushe oykki denthides. Naazikka dendi eqqides.
Yesusi so gelidappe guye iza kaallizayti “Nu izappe tuna ayana kessanas aazas dandayibeykkonii?” giidi iza oychida.
Izikka istas “Hayssa malay kezana dandayizay woossaninne xooman xalla” gides.
Heeppe dendi Galila baggara aadhdhi bida. Yesusi ba dizaso oonikka erana mala koybenna.
Gaasoyka Yesusi bana kaallizaytas “Asa Nay asa kushen aadhdhi imettana istika iza wodhana, heedzdzantho gallassafe guye izi dendana” giidi ista tamarsiza gishassa.
Gido attin izi gizayssi istas gelibenna; iza oychanaska babbida.
Hessafe guye Qifirnahoome bida. Izi keeththe gelidi “Inte yishe oge bolla aaza gish palametidetii?” gi oychides.
Isti qas oge bolla “Nu giddon nuuppe ubbafe aadhdhizay oonee?” giidi palametida gish wurikka co7u gida.
Izi uttidappe guye tammanne nam7ata xeygidi “Koyro gidana koyizadey ubbafe wursethinne ubbatas ashkara gido” gides.
Qii guutha naa ehidi ista giddon essides. Idimmidinne
“Hayta guutha naytappe issade ta sunthan mokki ekkizadey tanakka mokki ekkees. Tana mokki ekkizadey wuri tana xalala gidonta tana kiittidayssakka mokki ekkees” gides.
Yohannisikka “Astamare! Issadey ne sunthan daydanthi kessishin nu beydos. Izi nuna kaallonta gish kessonta mala diggidos” gides.
Yesusi qasse “Diggofte; oonikka ta sunthan malata ooththidi eesotidi ta bolla iita haasayanas dandayenna.
Nunara eeqettontay wuri nunara dees.
Ta intes tumu gays; inte tiyettida Kirstoosas gidida gish ta sunthan issi wanca haath intena ushshidadey wuri ba oosoys waaga dhayenna.
“Hayta tana ammaniza ha guuthatappe issades dhuphe gidizay wuri deexxo woxa shuchchi iza qoodhen qashetin duge abba gido olettidakko izas lo7o gidana.
Hessa gish ne kushey nena baleththikko neeppe qanxa yegga; nam7u kushera daada gede Gaanname taman ne baanayssafe kushe duuxa gidada gede de7on geloy nees lo7o gidana.
Gaannamen guxuney hayqqenna, tamaynne to7enna.
Nena ne tohoy baleththikko neeppe qanxa digga; nam7u tohora daada gede Gaanname taman yegettanappe ne wobe gidada gede de7oso geloy nees lo7o.
Gaannamen guxuney hayqqenna, tamaynne to7enna.
Nena ne ayfey baleththikko wooca kessada neeppe digga; nam7u ayfera daada gede Gaannamen yegetanappe issi ayfera Xoossa Kawoteth geloy nees lo7o.
Gaannamen guxuney hayqqenna tamaynne to7enna.
“Buro asi wuri taman paacettana.
“Maxiney lo7o; gido attin maxiney ba maxinetetha yeddiko inte wosti iza mal7o eranee? Inte asatethan maxiney de7o. Inte inte giddon dosettite” gides.
Yesusi heeppe dendidi gede Yuhuda geetettiza derenne Yordanoose shaafappe pinthan diza dere bides. Dereyka qasse iza yuuyi aadhdhin izi kase ba ooththiza mala asa tamarsides.
Issi issi Farsaaweeti izakko yiidi “Asi ba macho anji yeddanas bessizee?” giidi iza paace oysho oychida.
Izikka istas “Musey intena ay gi azazidee?” giidi zaari oychides.
Istika izas “Musey ta izo anja yeddadis giza waraqata xaafi immidi anjo gides” gida.
Yesusikka zaaridi ista “Musey hayssa mala woga xaafidayssi inte woznay minnida gishassa.
Gido attin koyro Xoossi medhishe macanne adde ooththi medhides.
Hessa gish asi ba aawanne ba aayo aggidi ba machira waaxettes.
Nam7ay issi asho gideettes; hessa gish isti nam7ay issinoppe attin nam7u deettenna.
Hessa gish Xoossi gaththi waaxidayta asi shaakkofo.” gides.
Qasseka isti so gelin iza kaallizayti he yo7oza gish zaari iza oychida.
Izi istas “Oonikka ba macho anji yeddidi hara macas ekkiko he macasay bolla layma ooththes.
Macasayakka ba azina aggada hara adde gelikko izakka laymatawus” gides.
Yesusi ba kushe wothana mala asay nayta izakko ehides. Iza kaallizayti qasse ehida asa bolla hanqettida.
Yesusi hessa beyi hanqettidi “Nayti taakko yeto; diggofte; Xoossa Kawotethi haytanta malassa.
Ta intes tumu gays; Xoossa Kawoteth hayssa guutha nayta mala ekkontadey izin mulekka gelenna” gides.
Nayta idimmidi ista bolla ba kushe woththidi anjides.
Heeppe buro oge kezishin issadey wooxishe izakko gakkidinne iza sinthan gulbatidi “Kiya astamareento! Tani merna de7o demmana mala ay ooththana taas bessizee?” gi oychides.
Yesusikka “Aazas tana kiya gay? Issi Xoossafe attin kiyay ba” gides.
“Neni azazota eray? ‘Wodhoppa; laymatoppa; kaysotoppa; wordo markatofa; as baleththofa; ne aawanne ne aayo boncha’ gizayta” gides.
Addezikka zaaridi “Astamare! Ta hayta wursa naatethafe oykkada naagadis” gides.
Yesusi iza xeelidinne dosidi “Histikko ha7i nees issi miishi paccees. Baadanne nees diza wursa bayza, miisha manqotas imma; neni salon shiiqida miish demmandassa; histadanne haaya tana kaalla” gides.
Addezikka hessa siydi daro yiillottides. Izas daro haroy diza gish muuzottishe bides.
Yesusi yuushi aaththi xeelidi bana kaallizayta “Duretas Xoossa Kawoteth geloy ay mala deexo!” gides.
Iza kaallizaytikka iza haasayan malalettida. Yesusi qasse zaaridi “Nayto! Xoossa Kawoteth geloy ay mala deexo miishe!
Durey Xoossa kawoteth gelanayssafe gaamellay narpe lukkora aadhdhanayssi kawuyana!” gides.
Iza kaallizaytikka darsi malalettidi ba giddon issoy issa “Histin ooni attana dandayizee?” gida.
Yesusi ista xeelidinne “Hayssi asas dandayettenna; Xoossa matan gidikko hessa mala gidenna. Xoossas wurikka dandayettes” gides.
Phexroosi qasse “Hekko; nuni wursikka aggidi nena kaallidos” gides.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Ta intes tumu gays; ta gishshinne Mishiraachcho qaala gish giidi ba keeththe, woykko ba ishata, woykko ba micheta, woykko ba aayo, woykko ba aawa, ba nayta, woykko ba gade aggida as wuri,
hayssa ha wodezan ha7i goodeteththara keeththata, ishata, micheta, aayeta, naytanne gadekka xeetu kushe aaththi ekontaynne buro yaana alamezanka merna de7o laattontadey deenna.
Gido attin sinthatida daroti guyettana; guyetidayti sinthatana” gides.
Isti Yerusalame efiza oge bolla dishin Yesusi istafe sinthe sinthe bees. Iza kaallizayti iza buussan malalettida. Hanko iza geedon diza asay qas izas babbides. Qasseka tammanne nam7ata derezappe dumma shaakkidi ba bolla aazi gakkanakkonne istas hizgi yootides;
“Nuni Yerusalame kezana; Asa Nay Qeeseta halaqatassinne Muse woga tamarsizaytas aadhdhi imettana; istika iza bolla hayqo pirda pirdananne dere asas aaththi immana.
Iza bolla qidhi ka7ana; iza bolla cuttana; izakka garafananne wodhana shin izi heedzdzu gallassafe guyen hayqoppe dendana.”
