Qasse Zabidoosa nayti Yaqoobeynne Yohannisi izakko shiiqidi “Astamare! Nuni nena woossidayssa ne nuus wursa ooththana mala nu koyoos” gida.
Izikka istas “Ta intes ay ooththana mala koyetii?” gides.
Istika “Neni ne kawoteththa boncho wode nuuppe issadey ne ushachan issadey ne hadirsan uttana mala nuus ero garkii?” gida.
Yesusikka “Inte oychizayssa erekketa. Tani uyana ushsha uyanassinne tani xammaqettiza xinqata xammaqettanas dandayandetii?” gides.
Istika zaaridi “Ee, dandayoos” gida. Yesusikka “Ta uyiza ushsha inte uyananne ta xammaqettiza xinqata inte xammaqettana.
Gido attin ta ushachara woykko ta hadirisara utethi Xoossi istas giigissidaytas attin ta immana miish gidenna” gides.
Tammati hessa siydi Yaqoobenne Yohannisa bolla hanqettida.
Yesusikka issi bolla shiishshidi “Dere halaqa geetettizayti dere haarizayssa mala ista shuumeti ista bolla ba godateth bessizayssa inte ereeta.
Gido attin inte giddon gita gidana koyiza ubbay ashkara gido.
Sinthe aadhdhana koyizay wurikka ubbas aylle gido.
Asa Nay gidikko asas ooththanassinne ba shempo darota gish aaththi immanas yides attin ase oosisanaas yibenna.” gides.
Heeppe gede Yarko bida. Yesusinne iza kaallizayti hara daro asatara Iyarkofe kezishin Ximoosa naa Barxemoosa geetettiza ayfe qooqey oge bolla uttidi woosses.
Izikka yizay Naazirete Yesusa gididayssa siydi “Dawute naa Yesusa tana maara” giidi keehi waassides.
Daroti izi co7u gaana mala hanqida; gido attin izi “Dawuteno! Tana maara” giidi keehi waassides.
Yesusikka eqqidi “Iza ha xeygite” gides. Istika qooqeza “Aykkoy ba denda nena xeeyges” gida.
Izikka ba may7o qaari yeggidi pusukku gi dendi eqqidi Yesusakko yides.
Yesusikka “Ta nees ay ooththana mala koyay?” gides. Qooqezikka “Aastamareento! Ta xeellanawu koyays” gides.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Ba nena ne ammanoy pathides” gides. Heerakka iza ayfey xeellides. Izikka Yesusa kaalli bides.
Isti gede Yerusalamen Dabrazayte geetettiza zuma achchan diza Betefaagenne Bitaaniya geetettizaso matida wode Yesusi bana kaallizaytappe nam7ata hizgi kiittides,
“Gede inte sinthan diza gutayo biite. Inte he gelida mala heen asi togi eronta qashon diza hare gutte inte demmana; birshidi iza ha ekki yiite.
Oonikka intena ‘Hayssa ays ooththetii?’ giikko Godas koshshees giidi yootite; izikka intes eeson zaari yeddana” gides.
Istika biidi issi keeththa karen oge bolla qasheti diza hare gutte demmidi birshida.
Heen eqqida issi issi asati “Hare gutteza aazas birshetii?” gi oychida.
Yesusa kaallizayti Yesusi istas gida mala asatas yootin ero eki biite gida.
Guttezakka Yesusakko ehidi ba may7o iza zokko bolla yeggin Yesusi iza toggides.
Daro asay ba may7o kessi kessi oge bolla micides. Bagga asay cilila mitha hayth qanxi qanxidi oge bolla laallides.
Yesusappe sintharanne guyera diza asay qaala dhoqu histidi “Hoosana; Goda sunthan yizadey anjettidade.
Hanna yizara nu aawa Dawute kawoteththaya anjettidaro; hoosana! Bolla salon Xoossi bonchetto” gishe waassides.
Yesusi Yerusalame gakkidi hessafekka Xoossa Keeththe gelides. He heeran dizayssa wursi xeelidi gadey qammida gish tammanne nam7atara gede Bitaaniya kezides.
Wontetha gallas isti Bitaaniyappe kezi bishin Yesusi gafides.
Izi issi haythi cililida balase geetettiza mithi hahon beyidi ayfey daanakkonne giidi iziikko yides. Gido attin balase mithi ayfonta wode gidida gish haythafe attin issi ayfekka izippe demmibenna.
Hessa gish mithayo “Hannife guye mernas oonikka neeppe ayfe mooppo!” gides. Iza kaallizaytikka izi gizayssa siyida.
Gede Yerusalame bida; heeppeka gede Xoossa Keeththe gelidi heen bayzizaytanne shamizayta kessi goodo oykkides. Miishe laammizayta xaraphezanne haraphe bayzizayta oyde gufanthi gufanthi yeggides.
Oonikka ay miish tookkidi Xoossa Keeththe gibbe giddora aadhdhonta mala diggides.
Istaka tamarsishe “Ta keeththi dere ubbas Woosa Keeththe gidana geetetti xaafettibenee? Gido attin inte qasse kaysota gongolo kessideta” gides.
Qeeseta halaqatinne Muse woga tamarsizayti hessa siydi iza wosti dhayssanakkonne oge kosh oykkida. Gido attin dereyka iza timirtezan malalettida gish izas babbida.
Istika gadey qammin katamaype kezi bida.
Wontetha gallas maalado isti ogera aadhdhi bishin balase mithaya xaphoppe melidaro beyida.
Yo7ozi iza woznan akeeketin Phexroosi Yesusa “Astamare! Hekko, hanna ne qangida balaseya meladus” gides.
Izikka zaaridi “Xoossa ammante.
Ta intes tumu gays; ‘Oonikka hayssa zumaza ne dhoqalletada gede abban gela’ gizakkonne hessaka woznan sidhonta ammanidakko izaades hanana.
Hessa gish inte woossan oychidaz wursi ekkida mala ammanikko intes hanana.
Hessathoka inte woossas eqqiza wode inte Salo Aaway inte nagara atto gaana mala inteka intena qohidayta nagara wursi atto giite.
Inte atto goonta ixikko inte salo aawaykka inte nagara atto geenna.” gides.
Qasseka Yerusalame yida. Yesusi Xoossa Keeththe kare giddon gedene haane yuuyetishin Qeeseta halaqati, Muse woga tamarsizaytinne dere cimati izakko shiiqidi,
“Hayssa ne ooththizay ay godatetharaa? Hayta ne ooththana mala hayssa mala godateth nees ooni immidee?” gida.
Yesusikka istas zaaridi “Ane takka intena issi oysho oychays inteka taas zaarikko takka ha yo7ota ay godateththara ooththizakkonne intes yootana.
Yohannisa xinqatey Xoossafeyee? Asappee? Ane taas zaarite” gides.
Istika ba giddon issoy issara “Nu saloppe giikko izi nuna ‘Histin aazas iza ammanibeyketii?’ gaana;
‘Nu asappe’ giikko” Yohannisi tumu nabe gididayssa derey wuri ammaniza gish hessatho gaana babbida.
Hessa gish “Nu erokko” giidi Yesusas zaarida. Yesusikka “Histikko ta hayta aaza godateththara ooththizakkonne takka intes yootikke” gides.
Qasse istas leemisora yootishe “Issadey ba woyne mith tokkides. Keela yuushi aaththi keelides; woyne mitha ayfe gum7ana olla bokkides. Naage keeththekka keexides. Hessafe goshshanchatas kira immidi hara dere bides.
Mithay ayfiza wode woyne mitha ayfe ekkada ya giidi ashkaratappe issade goshshanchatakko yeddides.
Goshshanchati ashkaraza oykki shocidi coo mela kushe yeddida.
Nam7anthokka hara ashkara yeddides. Goshshanchati ha7ikka ashkara oykkidi izas hu7etara qoo7idinne kawushshidi zaari yeddida.
Ha7ikka zaaridi hara ashkara yeddides. He yeddoyssakka wodhida; hara darota giddofe issi issi asata qoxida; baggayta wodhida.
“Ha7ikka kiittonta attiza haray dees; izikka aaway dosiza iza naaza. ‘Ta naaza isti boossana’ gi qoppidi wursethan ba naaza yeddides.
Goshshanchati qas ba giddon ‘Hayssi waanna iza laattana naaza; ha yiite nu iza wodhikko biittay nuus gidana’ gida.
Hessa gish heen oykki wodhidi woyne mithaya dizasoppe haraso kessi yeggida.
“Histin woyne mitha goday intes ay ooththana misatizee? Izi yaana; goshshanchatakka wodhana; woyne mitha haratas immana.
Geeshsha Maxaafan ‘Shuchcha keeththe keexizayti hanenna giidi wora yeggida shuchchay keeththa maazanes bolla hu7e gidides; hessaka Goday ooththides. Hessika nu ayfes malalisizaz geetettidi xaafettidayssa nabebibeekketii?’ ” gides.
<range>
Izi istas leemisoza yootiday ista gish gididayssa Ayhuda halaqati erida gish iza oykkanas koyda. Gido attin asas babbida gish aggi bida.
Yesusa yo7on qaxana mala Farsaaweetappenne Herdoosa baggatappe guutha asata dooridi izakko yeddida.
Istika izakko yiidi “Astamare! Neni mooroy baynda as gididayssa nu eroos; ne oonaska babbada wordo maaddakka; Xoossa oge xalala tumu tamarsassa. Oroome kawo Qeesares giira qanxanas bessizeyee? Bessenee? Nu qanxinoyee? Qanxofinoo?”
Yesusi ista oyshoy qoodheppe qommo gididayssa eridi “Aazas tana qaxana koyetii? Ane issi dinare hammite ta beyays” gides.
Istika miisha ehin “Hayssi iza bolla diza misilezi oona misilee? Iza bolla xaafetidayssi oona gizee?” gides. Istika “Qeesareyssakko” gida.
Yesusikka “Qeesareyssa Qeesares, Xoossayssa Xoossas immite” gides. Istika iza zaaron malalettida.
Hessafe guye hayqqidaytas hayqoppe denthi baawa giza Saduqaaweti izakko yiidi iza hizgi oychida.
“Astamare! Issi asi macho ekkidi naa yelonta hayqqikko hayqqidayssa ishay iza macheyo ekkidi izas laata naa yelana mala kase Musey nuus xaafides.
Gido attin laapun ishanti deettes; istafe bayray macho ekkidi naa yelonta hayqqides.
Kaalozi he macasayo ekkidi ha7ikka naa yelonta hayqqides; heedzdzanthoyka yelonta hayqqides.
Laapunatikka he macasayo ekkidi laata yelibeetenna wursethan macasayakka hayqqadus.
Histin laapunatikka izo ekkidashin hayqoppe dendoy diza gidikko ha macasaya istafe oona macho gidanee?” gida.
Yesusikka istas “Inte balettizay Geeshsha Maxaafatanne Xoossa wolqa eronta gishassa.
Hayqqidayti dendiza wode Salo Kiitanchata mala gidana attin ekkettettenanne gelettettenna.
Hayqqidayta dentha gishas gidikko Muse maxaafan hessika qeeri wora giddon eexxiza tama giddofe Xoossi ‘Tani Aabrahaame Xoossa; Yisaaqa Xoossa; Yaqoobe Xoossa’ gizayssa nababibeekketii?
Xoossi paxata Xoossa attin hayqethata Xoossi gidenna. Hessa gish inte daro balettideta” gides.
Isti palaman dishin xaafetappe issadey ista palama siydinne Yesusi oyshetidayssas lo7eth zaaridayssa akeekidi “Ero! Azazotappe ubbafe aadhdhizay awayssee?” giidi oychides.
Yesusi izas hizgides “Ubbafe aadhdhizay hayssa ‘Isra7eele siya! Goda Xoossi issi Goda,
Nekka Goda ne Xoossa ne kumeththa woznappe, ne kumeththa shempofe, ne kumeththa qofappe, ne kumeththa wolqafe dosa.’
Nam7anthoykka ‘Ne lagge ne hu7e mala dosa’ ha nam7atappe aadhdhiza azazoy baawa.”
Xaafezikka “Aastamare, lo7o gadasa, ‘Xoossi issino gididayssanne izappe haray bayndayssa’ ne yootidayssi likke.
Iza ne kumeththa woznappe ne kumeththa qofappe ne kumeththa wolqafe dosoy qasseka ne lagge ne hu7e mala dosoy xuugetiza yarshofenne hara yarsho ubbafe aadhdhees” gides.
Yesusikka addezi yuushi qoppidi zaaridayssa beyidi “Neni Xoossa Kawoteththafe hahon daakka” gides. Hessafe guye iza oychanas xalidadey bettibenna.
Yesusi Xoossa Keeththe gaaththan tamarsishe “Muse woga tamarsizayti aazas ‘Kirstoosa Dawute naa’ gizoo?
Dawutey Xillo Ayanan haasayishe ‘Goday ta Goda ne morketa ta ne toho gars aaththana gakkanaas ta ushachchan utta gides’ gees.
Histin Dawutey ba duunara iza ‘Goda’ giikko waanidi simmi izas naa gidanee?” gides. Daro dereyka izi gizayssa ufayssara siyides.
Izi tamarsishe “Muse woga tamarsizaytappe naagettite, gadera gooshettiza aduussa may7o may7idi yuush yuuyana doosettes; awanka aadhdhi aadhdhi asi istas boncho sarota immana mala koyettes.
Ayhudata Woosa Keeththan dhoqaso, gibirasokka bonchoso koyeettes.
Isti azinay baynda macasa keeththa kallosettes; qasseka bana bessanas adussa woossa woossetes. Haytanti iita pirda pirdettana” gides.
Yesusikka asay muxuwata yeggizason uttidi daro asati immizayssa Xoossa Keeththa miisha shiishshiza saaxinen yeggizayssa xeellides. Daro dureti daro miish yeggida.
Issi azinay baynda am7e dizaara issi sikinafe daronta xarqimala biratappe oosettida nam7u miish yeggadus.
Yesusi bana kaallizayta xeygidi “Ta intes tumu gays; saaxinezan yeggida ubbafe hanna manqo am7eya aadhdheth yeggadus.
Hayti wuri baas diza tirpa miishafe yeggidashin hanna qasse ba manqotethafe baas dizayssa sinthafe izo koshizayssara wursa immadus” gides.
Izi Xoossa Keeththafe kezishin iza kaallizaytappe issoy “Astamare! Hayssi keeththaynne keeththay keexettida shuchchay ay mala lo7izakkonne hayssa beyay?” gides.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Hayta gita keeththata xeellay? Shuchchati issoy issa bolla diza mala deettenna; wurikka laalettana” gides.
Yesusi Xoossa Keeththa ginara Dabrazayte zuma bolla uttidishin Phexroosi, Yaqoobi, Yohannissinne Indiraassi xalla izakko shiiqidi,
“Hayssi ayde hananakkonne nuus yoota. Hayssi wursethan poletanas malatay aazee?” gi oychida.
Yesusikka istas “Oonikka intena baleththonta mala naagettite.
Buro daroti ‘Ta Kirstoosa’ gishe ta sunthan yaana; darotaka baleththana.
Inte olanne ola wore siyiza wode daggammofte. Hessi hananayssi attenna. Wursethi gidikko burona.
Derey dere bolla kawoy kawo bolla dendana, daroson biitta qaathinne koshay hanana; heyti wuri miixas leeso mala.
“Inte intes naagettite. Buro intena dere duulatan aaththi immana. Isti intena Ayhudata Woosa Keeththan garafana. Inte ta markata gidana mala ta gish dere daannata sinthaninne kawota sinthan eqqana.
Koyrottidi Mishiraachcho qaalay dere ubbas sabakettana bessees.
Inte oyketidi pirdas shiiqiza wode hinno he saateyin intes imettizaro haasayite attin biidi nu ay giinoo? giidi kaseti hirgofte. Haasayanay Xillo Ayanappe attin intena gidekketta.
“Ishay isha, aaway ba naa hayqos aaththi immana; nayti bana yelidayta bolla makalananne wodhana.
Ta geedon inte asa ubban ixettidayta gidana. Wurseth gakkanaas minni eqqidadey gidikko attana.
“Inte harassiza tunatethi izas bessontason eqqidashe beykko nababizadey woznan wotho; Yuhudan dizayti pude zuma bolla baqatetto.
Keeththa karen dizaddey so geloppo; ba miish kessana giidi keeththe geloppo.
Goshshason dizaddey ba may7o ekkanas guye simmofo.
He gallasatan shaara macasatassinne naa dhanthizaytas aayye-ana!
Hessika balgon gidonta mala Xoosse woossite.
Koyro Xoossi medhetetha wursi medhosoppe ha7i gakkanaas woykko hayssafe guye iza misatizay baynda gita metoy hanana.
Goday he gallassata qaanthontakko oonikka attenna shin baassi doorettidayta gish he gallassata qaanthides.
“He wode oonikka hekko Kirstoosi hayssan dees; giikko woykko hekko heen dees giikko ammanoppite.
Wordo Kirstoosatinne wordo nabeti buro dendidi malatatanne kase hani eronta pala miish ooththana. Istas dandayettikko haray atto shin doorettidaytakka baleththana.
Hessa gish naagettite; he wodey gakkonta dishin haara hayssa wursa ta intes yootadis.
“He wode he metozappe kaallidi awa arshey dhumana; aginaykka poo7usuku.
Xoolinteti saloppe qoqofettana, salon diza wolqamati qaaxana.
He wode Asa Nay gita wolqaranne bonchora salo shaarara yishin asay iza beyana.
Izikka kiitanchata yeddidi oyddu baggafe biitta gaxappe gaxa gakkanaas diza baas doorettidayta shiishana.
“Leemisoza balase mithafe tamarite. Unquloy cililiza wode haythi kessishin boney matidayssa inte ereeta.
Hessathoka hayti ta gidayti poletishin inte beykko wodey mati yiidi penge gakkidayssa erite.
Ta intes tumu gays; ha yo7oti polettana gakkanaas hayssi ha yelettay aadhdhenna.
Saloynne sa7ay aadhdhana shin ta qaalay gidikko aadhdhenna.
“Qasse he gallassay gish woykko he saatey gish ta Aawappe attin Salo Kiitanchata gidinka Naaza gidinka oonikka erenna.
Hessa gish wodey aydekkonne inte eronta gish nagettite, minnitenne woossite.
Hessika ba keeththe ashkaratas aggidi ashkarata issa issa ooso oythidi penge naagizayssi beggidi naagana mala azazidi bida asa misatees.
“Histikko keeththa aaway ayde yaanakkonne woykko qamma leela gidoth yaanakonne woykko koyro kuttoy baqishin yaanakkonne woykko wonta bolla bazzoy zo7ishin yaanakko inte eronta gish beggidi naagite.
Inte qopponta dishin izi yiidi inte dhiskidishin intena demmofo.
“Ta intes yootizayssa asa ubbas yootays; minnidi naagite! gays” gides.
Paaziganne uketha muussa ba7aale gallassay bonchetanas nam7u gallassi attishin Qeeseta halaqatinne Muse woga tamarsizayti Yesusa baleththi oykidi wodhana oge koyda.
Gido attin “Asay meto medhonta mala ba7aale gallasatan gidoppo” gida.
Izi Bitaaniya geetettiza soon issi inchiracha hargancha gidida Simoona soon quma bolla dishin waagay daro al7o gidida nardoose geetettiza shittoy kumi uttida albasxiroose bilqaaxe oykkida issi macasaya bilqaaxeza menthada shittoza Yesusa hu7e bolla gussadus.
Heen gadaan diza asatappe issi issi asati “Hayssi shittozi aazas wogay baynda gukkizee?” giidi ba giddon hanqettida.
“Shittozi bayzo bayzidakko heedzdzu xeetu dinareppe bollara bayzettidi manqotas imetteneshin” giidi macasayokka kadhida.
Gido attin Yesusi istas “Aggite! Hanno macasayo aazas waayssetii? Iza taas lo7o miish ooththadus.
Manqoti ay wodekka intenara deettes. Inte koyda wode aydekka ista maaddanaas dandayeta shin ta gidikko ubba wode intenara diikke.
Hanna ba ooththanas dandayizaari keena ooththadus. Taas moogos gidana mala ta asho kaseta tiyadus.
Ta intes tumu gays; hayssi Mishiraachcho qaalay alame kumeththan sabaketizason awanka iza ooththidayssi izo hassa7issizaz gididi hasayettana” gides.
Hessafe guye tammanne nam7atappe issoy Asqoroonto Yuhuday Yesusa aaththi immanas Qeeseta halaqatakko bides.
Istika hessa siydi ufayettida; izas miishe immanas izara giigida. Hessa gish Yesusa aaththi immanas inje wode naagishe gam7ides.
Paaziga dorsi shukettiza uketha muussa bonchiza koyro gallas Yesusa kaallizayti Yesusakko shiiqidi “Paaziga kawo maanaso awan giigisana mala koyay?” gi oychida.
Izikka bana kaallizaytappe nam7ata “Gede katama biite; inte bishin haaththe otora tookkida issadey intenara gaaggana.
Izi biidi gelizaso gakkanaas iza kaallite. Keeththadezas ‘Astamarey nena tana kaallizaytara Paaziga kawo maanas taas gidiza imatha shemposoy awayssee? gides’ giite.
Izikka bolla pooqe bolla diza giigi uttida aaho so intena bessana; heen izan giigissite” gi kiittides.
Iza kaallizaytikka kezidi gede katama bida. Wurikka Yesusi gida mala hani beettides; Paazigakka heen giigissida.
Gadey qammishin Yesusi bana kaalliza tammanne nam7atara gakkides.
Isti maaddan dishin “Ta intes tumu gays; inte giddofe issoy izikka tanara issife mizayssi tana aaththi immana” gides.
Istika muuzotidi “Taneshaa? Taneshaa?” giidi issoy issoy Yesusa oychida.
Izikka istas “Tammanne nam7atappe issoy tanara ba kushe keren yeddizade.
Kase xaafettida mala Asa Nay iza gish hayqqana shin asa naa aaththi immizades aayye-ana! Hessadey kase yeletonta aggidakko izas lo7okkoshin!” gides.
Isti mishin uketha ekki anjidinne menthidi bana kaallizaytas “Hayssa ta asho heyte” gi immides.
Ushshakka denthi galatidi istas immin isti wurikka uyida.
Qasse Yesusi “Hayssi darota gish gukkana ta ooratha caaqo suutha.
Ta intes tumu gays; ooratha woyneppe giigida ushsha Xoossa Kawoteththan ta uyana wode gakkanaas nam7antho hayssa uyikke” gides.
Hessafe guye mazamure issife yexidi pude Dabrazayte zuma bolla kezida.
Yesusi “ ‘Ta heemmizayssa shocana he wode iza dorsati laalettana’ geetetti xaafettidayssa mala inte wurikka tanan duphettana.
Ta dendidayssafe guye gidikko ta intefe kasetada Galila baana” gides.
Phexroosikka “Asay wuri dhuphetikkokka tani dhuphetikke!” gides.
Yesusikka “Ta nees tumu gays; hachchi qamma kuttoy nam7uto waassana gakkanaas neni tana heedzdzuto kadana” gides.
Phexroosi qas “Ta nenara hayqqizakkoka mulekka nena kadikke” giidi keehi minthi yootides. Hankoytikka wuri izayssatho gida.
Hessafe guye Getesemaane geetettizaso bida Yesusikka bana kaallizayta “Tani woossishin inte hayssan gam7ishshite” gides.
Phexroosa, Yaqoobenne Yohannisa banara ekki bides. Keehi qoppidessinne metottides.
Qasseka istas “Ta shempoya daro metottadus inte haan diishshite. Dhiskonta naagite” gides.
Ista achchafe guuth gede pooqidi biitta bolla gufannidi hanko he saateya izappe aadhdhana mala woossides.
“Ta Aawawu! Nees wuri dandayettes; hayssa waaye xu7a taappe haassa. Gidikkoka ne sheneppe attin ta sheney hanoppo” gides.
Izi heeppe simmi yishin iza kaallizayti dhisikkidayta beyides. Phexroosakka “Simoona dhiskadii? Haray atto shin issi saatekka minnada naagoy nena xoonidee?
Inte paacen gelonta mala beggidi woossitenne minnite. Ayanay giigeti uttides shin ashoy gidikko daburancha” gides.
Qasseka biidi koyroyssatho woossides.
Izi nam7antho simmi yishin ista ayfen dhiskoy deexxin dhiskidayta demmides shin isti izas ay zaaranakkonne eribetenna.
Heedzdzantho yiidi “Ha7ikka inte ichchidi shempetii? Ha7i gidana, saateyakka gakkadus; hekko Asa Nay nagaranchata kushen aadhdhi imettana.
Ane eqqite boos; tana aaththi immanaddey yides” gides.
Yesusi buro haasayan dishin tammanne nam7atappe issoy Yuhuday yides. Izara issife Qeese halaqatappenne Muse woga tamarsizaytappe kiitettida daro asay giththa mashshanne durqa oykidi yides.
Iza aaththi immana Yuhuday istas “Asa giddofe ta yeerizadey iza gidida gishas oykidi lo7ethi naagi efite” giidi kaseti malata immi woththides.
Gakkida mala Yuhuday Yesusakko shiiqidi “Astamare!” giidi yeerides.
Asatikka Yesusa oykkida.
Iza achchan eqqida issoy mashsha koohoppe shoddi Qeeseta halaqa ashkara hayth qanxides.
Yesusikka istas “Panga mala tana oykkana mashshanne durqa oykidi yeetii?
Wontin wontin Xoossa Keeththan tamarsashe ta intenara dishin oykibeekketa shin kase xaafetidayssi polettana mala hayssi hanides” gides.
Hessa wode iza kaallizayti wuri iza yeggi aggi bida.
Ba kalloteth qeeri naxalan kammida issi nay Yesusa kaallishin asay iza oykin,
Naazi naxala yeggidi kallo kichchides.
Yesusakka gede Qeeseta halaqakko efida. Qeeseta halaqati, dere cimatinne Muse woga tamarsizayti heen issife wuri shiiqida.
Phexroosikka Yesusa hahora kaallishe Qeeseta halaqa gibbe gakkanaas bides. Izi heen uttidi hara asatara tama ho7ishin,
Qeeseta halaqatinne dere cimati wuri Yesusa wodhanas markattana as koyda shin demmanas dandayibeetenna.
Daroti iza bolla wordora markattikkokka markata qaalay oykketibenna.
Issi issi markati dendidi wordora,
“Hayssi addezi ‘Ta asa kushen keexettida Xoossa Keeththa laallada asa kushey bochontaz hara Xoossa Keeththa heedzdzu gallassara ta keexxana’ gishin nu siyidos” gi markattida.
Gido attin ista markatethi issi bolla wodhdhibenna.
Qeeseta halaqayka ista sinthan eqqidi “Hayti ne bolla markattizaysi aazee? Ne aazas duuna zaarikii?” giidi Yesusa oychides.
Gido attin Yesusi istas aykkokka zaaronta co7u gides. Qeeseta halaqay qasseka “Anjettida Xoossa Nay Kirstoosi nenee?” gi oychides.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Ee; tanakko! Asa Nay wolqama Xoossa ushachchan uttishininne salo shaarara yishin inte iza beyana” gides.
Qeeseta halaqay ba may7o daakkidi “Nuus hara aaza marka koshshizee?
Izi cashsha qaala Xoossa bolla hasayshin inte siyideta; ha7ich intes ay misatizee?” gides. Istika “Izas hayqoy bessees” giidi wurikka issi qaalan pirdida.
Hessa wode issi issi asati iza bolla cuch cuttida; iza ayfe goozi oykidi iccishe “Ane tinbite yoota” gida. Baggayti qasse shagalan baqqishe efida.
Phexroosi duge baggara heen gibbe giddon dishin Qeeseta halaqa garadetappe issiniya yadus.
Phexroosi tama ho7ishin tishshi hista xeellada “Neni Naazirete Yesusara daassa gidikkii?” gadus.
Izi qas “Ne gizayssade ta erikke; ne gizyssi taas gelenna” giidi kadides. Hessafe gede penge pooqi eqqi dishin heerakka kuttoy waassides.
He garadeya iza beyida mala heen eqqida asatas “Hayssi addezi izara diza asatappe issadekko!” gaada qasseka haasayadus.
Izi qasseka kadides. Guutha wode gam7ishin heen eqqida asati Phexroosa “Neni Galila asa, hessa gish tumappe ne istafe issade” gida.
Gido attin izi qas “Inte gizadde ta erikke!” gishe caaqonne bana qangeth oykkides.
Heerakka kuttoy nam7antho waassides. Phexroosikka “Kuttoy nam7a waassanas ne tana heedzdza kadana” gida Yesusa qaalay izas qofetin hiqqimidi yeekkides.
Maalado wontara Qeeseta halaqati, dere cimatinne Muse woga tamarsizayti kumeththa shango alafetara issife zoretidi Yesusa qachi ekki efidi Philaxoosas aaththi immida.
Philaxoosikka Yesusa “Ne Ayhudata kawoo?” gi oychides. Yesusikka “Ee, ne gida mala” giidi izas zaarides.
Qeeseta halaqatikka daro yo7o iza bolla shiishshi mootida.
Philaxoosi qas “Ne aazas oysha zaarikii? Hekko nena daro yo7on mootetes” giidi qasseka oychides.
Gido attin Yesusi ha7ikka izas aykkokka zaaro immonta gish Philaxoosikka malalettides.
Paaziga ba7aale gallas Philaxoosi derey birshana mala oychidade birshi yeddiza wogay kase dees.
Iita ooson dere bolla dendidi shempo wodhida asatara issife qashettida Barbaane geetettiza issadey dees.
Dereyka yiidi kase lose gididayssa izi ooththana mala Philaxoosa woossides.
Philaxoosikka istas “Ta intes Ayhuda kawo birshana mala koyetii?” gi oychides.
Philaxoosi hessatho oychiday kase Qeeseta halaqati Yesusa qanaten aaththi immidayssa eriza gishassa.
Qeeseta halaqati qas “Iza exa Barbaaney birshetto!” gi oychana mala dereza dentheththida.
Philaxoosi “Histikko inte Ayhuda kawo giza addeza wostana mala koyeti” gides.
Isti qasseka “Kaqqa! Kaqqa!” gi waassida.
Philaxoosikka “Ay iita ooththidee?” gi ista oychides. Isti qas “Kaqqa! kaqqa!” giidi kaseppe aaththi waassida.
Philaxoosikka dereza ufayssana giidi Barbaane istas birshides. Yesusa garafidi kaqqanas aaththi immides.
Wotadarati Yesusa dere haarizayssa gibbe ekki biidi attida wotadarata wursi shiishida.
Yesusa zo7o may7o mayzida; aguntha aklile xaaxidi iza hu7en woththida.
Hessafekka “Ayhuda kawo saroy nees gido!” gishe iza sarothida.
Iza hu7e guufera shocida; iza bollakka cuttida gulbatidi izas goynnida.
Iza bolla qidhi ka7idappe guye kase mayzida zo7o may7oza qari ekkidi kase iza may7oza zaari mayzidi kaqqanaso eki bida.
Alakisandrosanne Ruufoosa aawa Simoona geetettiza issi Qareena dere asi dereppe katama yizayssa Yesusa masqale wolqara oykki toossida.
Hessafe guye Yesusa Golgota geetettizaso efida; izas birsheththay “Asa hu7e guuge” guussa.
Karbe geetettiza camora walaketida woyne cajje uyana mala izas immin izi ekkonta ixxides.
Hessafe guye iza kaqqida, iza may7o issade issade awayssi gakkanakkonne giidi saama yeggidi gishettida.
Isti iza kaqishin wontafe heedzdzu saate gidides.
Isti masqale bolla xaafi shiishida mooto qaalay “Ayhuda kawo” giza qaala.
Izara issife nam7u pangata issa izappe ushachara issa hadirsara kaqqida.
Hessanka kase maxaafay “Iitatara issife taybettides” gida tinbite qaalay polettides.
Ogera aadhdhi bizaytikka ba hu7e qaathishe “Oy! Oy! Xoossa Keeththa laallada heedzdzu gallassan keexxanay nenee?” giidi iita cashshe cayishe;
“Ane ha7i masqale bollafe wodhdhada nena ashsha” gida.
Hessathoka Qeeseta halaqatinne Muse woga tamarsizayti ba giddon issoy issas “Harata ashshides shin bana ashshana dandaybenna” giidi iza qidhida.
“Nu iza beyidi ammanana mala ane hayssi Kirstoosi Isra7eeleta kawoy ha7i masqaleppe wodhdho” gida. Izara kaqettidaytikka iza bolla cashshe korida.
Usuppun saateppe oykkidi uddufun saate gakkanaas biittay wuri dhumides.
Uddufun saate bolla Yesusi “Eelohe! Eelohe! Lama sabaqitane” giidi qaala dhoqu histidi waassides. Hessas birsheththay “Ta Xoosso! Ta Xoosso! Ne tana aazas aggadii?” guussa.
Heen gadaan eqqida asappe issi issi asati hessa siydi “Elaasa xeeygesko” gida.
Hessafe issi asi eleli biidi caalida woyne cajje isponje mala miishan gelthi kessidi mitha xeeran oythidi uyana mala Yesusas shiishshides. Hessafe qasse “Ane aggagite; Elaassi yiidi iza kaqqoppe woththishin nu beyana” gides.
Hessafe Yesusi qaala dhoqu histi waassidi shempo kezides.
Xoossa Keeththe magalashay hu7era duge nam7u kezi daakkettides.
Yesusa ginara eqqida issi mato halaqay Yesusi hessatho gita qaalara waassidi shempo kezishin beyidi “Hayssadey tumu Xoossa naakkoshin” gides.
Hessa wode macasati hanizayssa hahon diidi xeellida. Ista giddofe Magdaleppe yida Maaramanne kaalotiza Yaqoobenne Yoosa aayo Maaramira qasseka Saloomira issife deettes.
Heyti macasati Galilan Yesusa kaallishenne izas ooththishe gam7idayta. Istarakka issife hara daro macasati Yerusalame bida.
Gadey qammi qammi bishin Sambatas giigettiza gallassi gakkides.
Dere cimata giddon bonchettida issi Armatiyasa dere as Yoosefe geetettizayssi Xoossa Kawoteth naagishe dizaddey babbonta Philaxoosakko biidi Yesusa aha woossides.
Philaxoosikka izi hinni wode ellera hayqqidayssa siydi malalettides. Mato halaqa xeygisdi “Izi hayqqi gam7idee?” giidi oychides.
Izi hayqqidayssa mato halaqay geeshshi eridappe guye Yesusa aha Yoosefes immides.
Yoosefekka moogo may7o shamidi aha masqaleppe woththidi moogo may7on xaaxidi shuchchafe woocetida duufon moogides. Duufa duuna shuchchara gordides.
Magdaleppe yida Maaramiranne Yoosefe aayo Maaramira Yesusa aha awan moogidakkone beyida.
Sambatay aadhdhidappe guye Magdale Maarama, Yaqoobe aayo Maaramiranne Saloomira issife biidi Yesusa aha tiyanas shitto shammida.
Saamintafe koyro gallas maalado wontara buro awa arshey kezida mala Yesusa duufokko buro bishin,
“Duufoza duunappe shuchcha nuus ooni gendersanee?” giidi ba giddon haasayettida.
Isti dhoqu gi xeellishin daro gita shuchchay duufoza duunappe genderidayssa beyida.
Gede duufoza giddo gelida mala issi bootha may7o may7ida paanthi ushachcha baggara uttidayssa beyidi dagammida.
Izi qas istas “Dagammofte! Inte kaqettida Naazirete Yesusa koyeeta; izi dendides haan deenna, isti iza woththidaso hayssa beyte.
Gido attin inte biidi iza kaallizaytassinne Phexroosas kase intes yootida mala intefe kasetidi izi Galila baana. Inte iza heen demmana giidi istas yootite” gides.
Macasatikka malalettishenne kokkorshe duufappe kezi baqattida. Babbida gish oonaska aykkokka qaattibetenna.
Saamintafe koyro gallas Wogga wonta maaladora izi hayqoppe dendidappe guye Yesusi izippe laapun daydanthi kessida Magdale Maaramis koyro beettides.
Izakka baada kase izara dizayti kayotishenne yeekkishe dishin demmada yootadus.
Isti Yesusi paxa dizayssanne iza ta Yesusa beyadis gidayssa siydi ammanbeetenna.
Hessafe guye iza kaallizaytappe nam7ati gede dere gars bishin Yesusi istas hara as misati beettides.
Istika simmidi hessa iza kaallizaytappe attidaytas yootida. Gido attin iza kaallizayti siydi ammanbeetenna.
Hessafe guye tammanne issineti maadda bolla dishin Yesusi istas qoncides. Izi hayqoppe dendin iza beyida asati istas yootin siydi ammanonta aggida gish istas ammanoy bayndayssanne ista wozna muumetetha gish ista borides.
Istasika “Alame ubbaso biite, Mishiraachcho qaala medhetetha ubbas sabakite.
Ammandaynne xammaqettiday attana. Ammanontay gidikko pirdettana.
Tana ammanizayta hayti malatati kaallana. Isti ta sunthan daydanthata kessana, ooratha qaalanka haasayana.
Isti shooshata ba kushera oykkana; wodhiza marze uyikkokka ista qohenna. Ba kushe harganchata bolla woththi woossikko harganchati paxana” gides.
Goda Yesusi hessa yootidappe guye pude salo dendi biidi Xoossa ushachan uttides.
Iza kaallizayti hessafe kezidi ubbason aadhdhi aadhdhi sabakida. Godayka istara ooththides. Ista timirteza ekkidi ooththizaytas ba yootida qaalakka malata ooththi ooththi minthides.
Boncho Tofilosa nu achchan hanida yo7ota gish daro asati baassi hanida mala xaafida.
He taarikezikka koyroppe denthidi ba ayfera beyida markatinne Xoossa qaala yootidayti nuus aaththidayssa.
Takka ta baggara xaphoppe denthada keeha naagetadanne paaca xeellada taarikeza wursa sinthe xaafetanas bessizayssa sinthasada kaallidi xaafetanas bessizayssa kaalethada naagetada nees xaafana mala taas lo7o gidi beettides.
Hayssa wursisa ta ooththizay ne tamaridayssi tuma gididayssa nena ero guussassa.
Herdoossi Yuhuda biittan kawotida wode Aabiya geetettiza Qeeseta halaqa baggafe Qeesetetha ooso taray iza gakkida Zakaraasa geetettiza issi Qeesey dees. Iza macheyakka Elisabeexo geetetawus, izakka Aarone bagga asa. Nam7atikka Goda azazonne iza woga wosoy baynda naagidi dizaytanne Xoossa sinthan xillo asa.
<range>
Gido attin Elisabeexa naa yelonta makkara gidida gish istas nay baawa; nam7atikka wodey sugetida asa.
Zakaraassi Xoossa sinthan Qeesetetha ooso taray iza gakkin izi ooththishin
Qeesetas diza woga mala Xoossa Keeththan gelidi exane cuwassana mala exay iza gakkides.
Exaney cuwattishin asay wurikka karen diidi woosses.
Goda kiitanchay exaney cuwattiza soppe ushachcha baggara eqqidi Zakaraasas beettides.
Zakaraasikka iza beyidi keehi daggammidi babbides.
Kiitanchay Zakaraasas “Babbofa! Ne woossay seetettides, ne macheya Elisabeexa nees attuma naa yelana iza sunthaka ne Yohannisa gaada sunthana.
Iza yelettan neni daro ufayettana; Daro asaykka ufayettana.
Goda sinthan izi gita gidana. Woyneppe oosettida cajje gidinka hara mathosiza ushsha gidinka izi uyenna; izi buro ba aayey qanthan dishe Xillo Ayanan kumana.
Isra7eele asappe darota ista Xoossako zaarana.
Aawata wozna ista naytaakko, azazetontaytikka gede Xillota cincateththakko zaarana malanne Godas bessiza dere giigissana mala Elaasa Ayananne iza wolqan Godappe sinthara izi baana” gides.
Zakaraassi kiitanchas, “Tani cima; ta macheyakka cimmadus; tani hayssa aazan eranee?” giidi oychides.
Kiitanchaykka zaaridi “Tani Xoossa sinthan eqqiza Gabrelle. Tanikka ha Mishiraachchoza nees gaththanas kiitetada yadis.
Hekko neni ba woden polettana ta qaala ammanonta ixida gish ne duunay duudana, nenikka haasayana dandayakka” gides.
He wode derey Zakaraassi “Xoossa Keeththafe kezonta aazas gam7idakko” giidi modhetishe naagides.
Izi Xoossa Keeththafe kezidi asa haasayissanas dandaybenna. Malati malati besoppe attin haasayanas dandayonta aggin asay izi Xoossa Keeththan Xoossafe ooratha miish beyidayssa erides.
Zakaraasikka ba ooso taray poletidappe guyen baso simmides.
Hessafe kaallin iza macheya Elisabeexa naa qanthatadus, ichashantho aginay gakkanaas asi bana beyonta mala qotetadus.
Izakka Goday ba maarotan ta leqettidayssa asa giddofe digganas ha wodezan hayssa taas ooththides gadus.
Elsabeexa qanthatida usuppuntha aginan, Xoossi ba kiitancha Gabrelle, Galila biittan diza, Naazirete giza katama yeddides.
Izikka kawo Dawute zereth gidida Yoosefe geetettiza asas giiga uttida Maaramo geetettiza geela7oykko kiitettides.
Yiidinne iza dizaaso gelidi “Hanne Xoossi nena anjidare saro Xoossi Goday nenara dees nenka anjettidaaro” gides.
Maarama kiitancha haasayan keeha daggammada, “Hayssi ay giza sarotaa?” gaada yo7oza keeha qoppadus.
Kiitanchaykka Maaramo “Xoossi nenan ufayetiza gish babbofa!
Neni qanthatana; attuma naaka yelana, sunthaka Yesusa gaada sunthana;
Izikka gita gidana; ubbafe bolla Xoossa naa geetettana, Goda Xoossi iza aawa Dawute kawoteththa izas immana.
Izi Isra7eele nayta bollan mernas kawotana; iza Kawotethasikka wursethi deenna” gides.
Maaramakka kiitanchas “Tani adde gelabeekke, shin hayssi waani hananee?” gaada oychadus.
Kiitanchaykka Maaramisi “Xillo Ayanay ne bolla wodhana wursofe bolla Xoossa wolqay ne bolla kuwasana; Hessa gish yelettana naazi Geeshsha Xoossa naa geetettana.
Asi yeluku iza makkara giidi haasayiza ne dabboya Elisabeexa cimateththan attuma naa qanthatada yelanas usuppuntho agina oykkadus.
Xoossassi hanonta miishi baawa”
Maaramakka zaarada “Hekko tani Xoossa aylle diikkina; ne gida mala taas hano” giin kiitanchay izippe shaakatidi bides. Maarama Elisabeexo beyana badus.
Maaramakka he wode matara eesota dendada pude gezze deren diza issi Yuhuda katama badus.
Zakaraasa keeththe gelada Elisabeexo sarotadus.
Elisabeexa Maarami sarotha siyida mala qanthan diza naazi izi qanthan guppides, Elisabeexinka Xillo Ayanay kumides.
Izakka ba qaala dhoqu ooththada “Macasa ubbafe ne anjettidaaro; Ne qanthan diza naazikka anjettidayssa.
Ta Goda aaya taakko yaada tana oychanas tani oonee?
Ne saroka qaala ta siyida mala ta ulo giddon diza nay ufayssa guppides.
Polettana giidi Goday izis yootidayssa ammanidara iza anjettidaro” gadus
Maaramakka “Izi ba aylle kawushshatetha xeellida gish ta shempiya Goda dhoqu ooththada bonchawus. Ta Ayanaykka tana ashshiza ta Xoossan ufayetawus. Wolqama Goday taas gita miishe ooththida gish hachchife sinthan asi wuri tana anjettidaro gaana. Iza sunthaykka geeshsha.
<range>
<range>
<range>
Iza maaroy izas babbizaytas naa naa gakkanaas daana.
Ba wolqan daro mino ooso ooththides; ba wozna qofan otoretizayta laallides.
Kawota kawoteththafe woththides, ashketa qasse dhoqu dhoqu histides.
Gafidayta lo7o miishan kalthides; dureta gidikko mela kushe yeddides.
Kase nu aawatas Abrahaamessinne iza qommotas gida qaala naaganas ba maaretetha yuushi qoppidi ba aylle Isra7eele maaddides” gadus.
<range>
Maaramakka Elisabeexi achchan heedzdzu agina sire gam7ada baso simmadus.
Elisabeexis yelo gallassay gakkin attuma naa yeladus.
Izi gutatinne dabbottikka Goday izis gita maaretetha ooththidayssa siydi izira issife ufayetida.
Yeletida ospuntha gallas qaxxaras yida. Iza aawa sunthan Zakaraasa giidi sunthana koyda.
Gido attin aaya “Hanenna, iza sunthi Yohannisa geetetto” gadus.
Istika izis “Ne dabbotappe Yohannisa geetettidi xeeygetida asi oonikka baawa” gida.
Aaway Zakaraassi “Naaza oona giidi sunthana koyidakkonne” malatan oychida.
Zakaraaska xaafiza miishe izas immana mala oychi ekkidi sunthay “Yohannisa” giidi xaafin asay wurikka malalettides.
Heerakka Zakaraasa duunay pogetidi inxarsi birshettin Xoossa galata oykkides.
Iza gutati wuri daro babbida. Hayssi wurikka dhoqa gezze biittan Yuhuda deren, ubbason haasayettides.
Hayssaka siyida asi wurikka “Ha guutha nay ay hananeshshaa?” giidi hanoza wursikka ba woznan oykkides. Goda kushey tumappe izara issife dees.
Naaza aaway, Zakaraassi Xillo Ayanan kumidi tinbite haasayishe
“Yiidi ba asa ashshida gish Isra7eele Xoossi galattetto.
Beni wode ba geeshsha nabeta duunan haasayettidayssa mala ba aylle Dawute keeththan ashshiza wolqa nuus denthides.
<range>
Izi nuna nu morketappenne, nuna ixizayta kusheppe ashshees.
Hayssa izi ooththiday nu aawatas ba maaretetha bessanassa, ba geeshsha caaqqoza yuushi qoppanassa.
Kase nu aawa Abrahaames caaqidayssa qoppana malanne nu morketa kusheppe izi nuna kessin nuni izas babboy baynda ooththanassinne nu diza wode ubban ba sinthan nuna geeshshatethanne xillotethan essanassa.
<range>
<range>
Goda oge giigissanas ne izappe sinthara biza gish ta naazo neni woga Xoossa nabe geetettana.
Asay ba nagarappe maarettida gish deres atotetha erateth ne immana mala
nu Xoossa lo7o maaretethafe dendidayssan Saloppe nuus away kezides.
Hessika dhuman dizaytassinne hayqo kuwa giddon dizaytasikka poo7isana malanne nu tohotakka sarotetha oge kaalethanassa” gides.
Guutha naazikka diccides; Ayananikka minnides. Isra7eele asas qoncen beettana gakkanaas bazzo biittan de7ides.
He wode biitta bollan diza asi wurikka tayibettidi xaafettana mala Oroome kawo Awuggisxossappe awajjay kezides.
Hessika Qerenewoosa geetettizayssi Sooriya geetettiza dere haariza wode hanida koyro dere taybo.
Hessa gish asi wuri xaafettanas ba dere dere bides.
Yoosefeykka asho dabboteththan Dawute baggafe gidida gish Galila awurajja giddon diza Naazirete katamappe Yuhuda awurajja Beeteleme geetettiza Dawute katamappe yides.
Izi xaafettana bishin izas giigetta dashe yelana matida Maaramira bides.
Istika heen dishin izis yelo wodey gakkides.
Izakka koyro attuma naa yelidayssafe guye imaththi aqiza keeththan aqizasoy baynda gish naaza carqara xaaxada miiza sinthan ishissadus.
Beetaleme achchan dorsa heemiza asati dorsa naagishe qammara karen aqizayti deettes.
Goda kiitanchaykka istako yides; Goda boncho poo7oykka ista lanqen yuuyi aadhdhanas poo7ides. Istika keehi dagammida gish,
Kiitanchay ista “Babofte! Tani asa ubbas gidiza gita ufayssa mishiraachcho ekka yadis.
Hach kawo Dawute katama Beetalemen shempo dhaley yelettides. Izikka Goda Kirstoosa geetettes.
Carqara xaaxeti ichchida gacino naa demmandeta hessika intes malata gido” gides.
Izarakka hara daro salo kiitanchati beettida. Xoossa galatishe,
“Bolla salon Xoossas bonchoy gido sarotethika biitta bollan izi dosiza asa ubbas gido” gida.
Kiitanchati istafe shaaketidi salo simmin dorse heemizayti ba giddon issoy issa “Ane ha yiite Goday nuus qoncisidayssanne hanidayssa Beeteleme katama biidi beyoos” gida.
Istika elelli biidi Maaramira, Yooseferanne miiza sinthan ichchida naaza demmida.
Beydayssafe guyen Goda kiitanchay naaza gish istas yootidayssa wursi zaari yootida.
Heemizayti yootidayssa siyida asay wuri keehi malalettides.
Gido attin Maarama yo7oza wursa ba woznan wotha dentha qoppashe gam7adus.
Heemizaytikka handays wurikka kiitanchay istas yootida mala gididi beettida gish siydayssassinne beyidayssas ubbas Xoossa galatishenne bonchishe simmida.
Naazi yeletin ospuntha gallassan qaxxarettiza wodey gakkin aayeya iza qanthatanappe kase kiitanchay gida mala Yesusa geetettidi summides.
Muse woga mala isti geeyiza wodey wurin Yoosefeynne Maarama guutha naa Yesusa Goda Xoossa sinthe shiishshanaas ekkidi Yerusalame kezida. Hessika Goda wogan koyro yeletiza attuma nay wuri Godas dumma gidana geetettidi xaafettidayssa polanassinne
<range>
qasseka Goda wogan nam7u haraphphe kafotanne woykko nam7u haraphphe kafo ciyeta geetettiddayssa mala yarsho shiishshanaassa.
He wode Yerusalame kataman xillonne Xoossa babbiza issi Simoona geetettiza asi dees; izikka Isra7eele nayta atotetha naagiza asanne Xillo Ayanay iza bolla shempida asa.
Qasseka Kirstoosa beyonta dishe hayqqonta mala Xillo Ayanay izas qoncides.
Izikka he wode Xillo Ayanay kaalethin Xoossa Keeththe lasha gaath gelides. Naaza aayeyiranne aawara Muse wogan bessizayssa polanas guutha naa Yesusa ekkidi gelida wode,
Simooni naaza ekki idimmidi Xoossa galatishe,
“Godo! Ne caaqida qaala mala ha7i tani ne aylley ne ashshizayssa ta ayfera beyida gish hi7a tana saron ekka; asa ubba sinthan ne giigissida atotetha ha7i tani ta ayfera beyadis.
<range>
<range>
Hayssika ubba deres geemmettidayssa qoncisiza poo7o, ne dere Isra7eelesikka boncho” gides.
Iza aawaynne aaya iza gish haasayettida yo7ozan malalettida.
Simoonikka ista anjides; Maaramokka “Daro asa wozna qofay qoncana mala hayssi Isra7eelen diza darotas dhayossinne atotethassa; Iza ixizaytas qasse malata gidana mala doorettides.
Qasseka darota wozna qofay qoncana mala naaza mishay qara mashsha mala ne wozna phalqana” gides.
Qasseka Aasseere baggafe Fanu7eele naa Haana geetettiza cimmida nabey dawus; izakka ba koyro azinara laapun layth kumeth de7adus.
Laythay izis osupun tammanne oyddu layth gidana gakkanaas qammanne gallas xoomashenne woossashe Xoossa Keeththafe shaaketonta am7etethan gam7adus.
He wodekka shiiqada Xoossa galatadus. Yerusalame wozeteth naagishe dizaytas ubbas guutha naaza gish yootadus.
Yooseferanne Maaramira Goda wogan azazettidayssa polidi Galila awurajjan diza baso Naazirete katama simmida.
Guutha naazikka diccidi minni minni bides; aadhdho eratethan kumides; Xoossa aadhdho kiyatethayka iza bolla dees.
Iza aawaynne aaya laythan laythan Paaziga bonchanas Yerusalame beettes.
Naazas laythay tammanne nam7u layth kumida wode kase lose gididayssa mala Paaziga bonchana kezida.
Paaziga ba7aaleza bonchidi baso simmishin Yesusi Yerusalamen attides. Yelidaytikka izi attiddayssa eribeyttenna.
Banara issife biza oge asara dees gishe issi gallassa oge bida. Gido attin izi istara bayndayssa eridi ba dabbota achchaninne laggeta achchan dizaakkonne giidi koyda.
Koyi koydi beettonta ixin Yerusalame simmida.
Heedzdzu gallassafe guye Xoossa Keeththan tamarsizayta giddon uttidi siyishe, asata oychishenne ista oysha zaarishe Xoossa Keeththan dishin demmida.
Siyidayti wuri Yesusa akeekkaninne iza zaarozan daro malalettida.
Yoosefeynne Maarama iza beyida wode malalettida. Maaramakka “Ta naazo ays hayssa mala ooththadii? Ne aawaynne taninne nena koyishe keehi metottettidos” gadus.
Izikka zaaridi “Tana ays koyidetii? Tani ta aawa keeththan daanas bessizayssa eribeekketi” gides.
Gido attin istas izi yootidayssi gelibenna.
Heeppe simmin istara issife Naazirete wodhdhidi istas azazettishe de7ides. Iza aaya Maaramakka he hanida miisha wursa ba woznan naagashe gam7adus.
Yesusi aadhdho eratethan, geesaninne saban Xoossa sinthaninne asa sinthan diccides.
Xibiraadoose geetettizays Qeesarey kawotida tammanne ichashantho laythan Phanxoosa Philaxoosa gizayssi Yuhuda biitta haariza wode, Herdoossi Galila biitta haariza wode, iza ishay Piliphoosi, Ixuriyaasanne Xirakondoose biitta haariza wode, Lisanoosikka Abloone biitta haariza wode,
Haanaynne Qayaafay Qeeseta halaqa gidida wode Xoossa qaalay bazzo biittan diza Zakaraasa naa Yohannisakko yides.
Yohannisi Yordanoose shaafa achchan diza dereta “Inte nagara atto gaanas nagarappe simmidi xammaqetite” giidi yootides
Hessika qasse nabe Isayaassi “Bazzon hizgidi waassiza asa kooshinchi ‘Godas oge giigissite baasidikka lo7ethite.
Shoobba biittay wuri kumana; zumatinne zumbullati wuri ziqqi gaana; geella ogey sitti gaana; moorettida ogey lo7o gidana.
Asa zereth ubba ashshiza Xoossa wolqa beyana’ giidi bazzon waassiza asa qaala giiris” giidi ba maxaafan xaafida mala.
Yohannisikka iza kushen xammaqettana yiza asas “Inteno ha shoosha nayto! Yaana diza Xoossa hanqofe haakkana mala ooni intena zoridee?
Inte nagara oosoppe simmidayssa erisiza ooso ooththite ‘Nu aaway Abrahaamey nuus dees’ guus aggite gides. ‘Xoossi baas giikko ha shuchchatappe Abrahaames naa ooththi denthanas danda7izayssa erite’
Kaltay mith qanxanas mitha xaphon dees. Lo7o ayfe ayfonta iita mithi wuri qanxettidi taman yeggettana” gides.
Asaykka “Histin ay ooththonii?” giidi oychides.
Yohannisikka asas “Nam7u may7oy dizay issi may7oy baynda asas immo; qasseka qumay dizayka bayndades shaakkidi immo” gides.
Qaraxa shiishshizaytikka xammaqetanas yiidi “Astamaare! Nu ay ooththinoo?” gida.
Izikka “Inte azazettidayssafe bollara qaraxa shiishoppite” gides.
Wotadaratikka “Nuni qasse ay ooththinoo?” giidi oychida. Izikka “Oona miishekka gidin wolqan ekkofte; qasseka oonanne wordon mootoppite; inte damozay intes gidana” gides.
Asay Yohannisa beyidi “Hayssi Kirstoosee?” giidi ba woznan sidhides.
Yohannisikka ubbas “Tani intena haaththan xammaqays; gido attin ta iza caamma birshanas bessonta taappe aadhdhizaddey yaana. Izi intena Xillo Ayananinne taman xammaqana.
Balezan diza kathaa gafezappe geeshshaas kath suragiza pithay iza kushen dees. Baleza kumeththa geeshshana; gisteza qasse di7en qolana; gafezakka to7onta taman xuugana” gides.
Yohannisi asa hara dumma dumma zore qaalara minithethi zorishe Mishiraachcho qaala yootides.
Gido attin Galila biitta haariza Herdoossi ba isha macho Herodiyado ekkida gishshinne hara daro iita ooththida gish Yohannisi iza hanqida gish,
kase mooro bolla hara gujjidi Herdoossi Yohannisa qasho keeththan yeggides.
Asay xammaqettidappe guye Yesusikka xammaqettides; izi woossishin saloy doyettides.
Xillo Ayanaykka haraphe misatidi iza bolla wodhdhides. “Saloppe ta dosiza nay nena; Nenan tani ufayettays” giza qaalay yides.
Yesusi Xoossa ooso oykkishin laythay izas heedzdzu tammu laytha mala gidana. Asaykka izi Yoosefe naa, Eelle naa,
Maate naa, Lewe naa, Milka naa, Yuhuda naa, Yoosefe naa,
Matotiyo naa, Amoxe naa, Naahoome naa, Isilime naa, Naage naa,
Maate naa, Matotiyo naa, Semeye naa, Yoosefe naa, Yuhuda naa,
Yoonane naa, Reese naa, Zerubaabele naa, Selatiyaale naa, Neere naa,
Milka naa, Hade naa, Yoosa naa, Qoosaame naa, Elimodaame naa, Eera naa,
Iyaaso naa, Eli7azaare naa, Yoorame naa, Maate naa, Eele naa,
Simoona naa, Yuhuda naa, Yoosefe naa, Yoona naa, Eliyaqeeme naa,
Meeliya naa, Maynaane naa, Maxaate naa, Naatane naa, Dawute naa,
Iseeye naa, Iyoobeede naa, Bo7eeze naa, Solomoone naa, Naasoone naa,
Amnadaabe naa, Aarame naa, Aarone naa, Esroome naa, Faareese naa, Yuhuda naa,
Yaqoobe naa, Yisaaqa naa, Abrahaame naa, Taara naa, Naakoore naa,
Seerohe naa, Raaguwe naa, Faaleqe naa, Abeere naa, Saala naa,
Qayineme naa, Aarfakiside naa, Seeme naa, Nohe naa, Laamehe naa,
Matusaala naa, Henooke naa, Yaareede naa, Malali7eele naa, Qayiname naa,
Henoose naa Seete naa Addame naa, Xoossa naa, misatides.
Yesusi Xillo Ayanan kumidi Yordanoose shaafappe simmida mala Xillo Ayanay iza kaaleththidi bazzo biitta efides.
Heenka Xala7en oyddu tammu gallas paacettides. He paacettiza gallassatan aykkokka moonta gish wursethan gafides.
Xala7eykka Yesusa “Ne Xoossa naa gidikko ane hayssa shuchcha kath gidana mala azaza” gides.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Asi kaththan xalla deenna geetettidi xaafettides” giidi Xala7es zaarides.
Hessafe kaallidi Xala7ey Yesusa issi dhoqa zuma bolla kessidi salo gufanthon diza kawotetha qiphida ayfey xeellanas bessidinne,
“Hayssi ne beyiza biitta kawota godateththaynne bonchoy wurikka taas imettides; takka ta dosizaddes immanas dandayiza gish neeska immana.
“Hessa gish neni kundada taas goynnikko hayssi wurikka nees gidana” gides.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Ne Goda Xoossas kundada izas xalla goynna geetettidi xaafettides” gides.
Hessafekka Yesusa Yerusalamen Xoossa Keeththa xeera kessi essidi Xoossa Maxaafan “Nena naagana mala Xoossi ne gish ba kiitancha azazana; ‘Ne tohoy shuchchan dhuphetonta mala kiitanchati ba kushera nena dhoqu histi oykkana’ geetettidi xaafettida gish ane ne Xoossa Naa gidikko hayssafe duge kunda” gides.
<range>
<range>
Yesusikka “Ne Goda Xoossa paacofa” geetettides giidi zaarides.
Xala7eykka ba paacanayssa wursidappe guyen hara baas inje wodey bettanashshe Yesusappe shaakettides.
Yesusikka Xillo Ayana wolqan Galila simmides. Iza goobateththay Galila achchan diza deretan siyettides.
Izikka Ayhudata Woosa Keeththan tamarsishin iza timirtey lo7in asay wurikka iza galattides.
Heeppe ba yelettida katama Naazirete yiidi kase Sambata gallas Ayhuda Woosa Keeththe geliza mala gelidi Xoossa Maxaafa nababanas dendi eqqides.
Nabe Isayaasa Maxaafay izas imettin maxaafa doyida mala.
“Goda Ayanay ta bolla dees; manqotas Mishiraachcho qaala yootana mala tana tiyides; qashetidaytas birsheteth, qooqeti xeellana oge ta awajjana mala, metotettidayta aashshana mala, dossettida Goda laytha awajja ta yootana mala tana kiittides” giza so demmi nababidinne.
<range>
Maxaafakka gordidi Ayhuda Woosa Keeththe naagizayssas zaari immidi uttides. Ayhudata Woosa Keeththan dizayti wurikka iza tishshi ooththi xeellida.
Izikka istas “Hayssi inte inte haythara siyida maxaafa qaalay hachchi polettides” gides.
Asay wurikka iza gish lo7o xalala hasayeettes. Qasseka iza duunappe keziza lo7o qaalappe dendidayssan malalettidi “Hayssi Yoosefe naa gidennee?” gida.
Izikka “Dhale Godo nerka nena patha. Qifirnahoomen neni ooththishin nu siyidayssa hayssan ne katamanka ooththa giza leemiso inte ta bolla malatanayssas sidhey baawa” giidi istas yootides.
Qasseka “Ta intes tuma gays nabey ba yeletida deren bonchetti erenna.
“Gido attin ta intes tuma gays heedzdzu laythinne bagga gakkanaas saloy gordettin wolqama koshay biitta bolla hanida Elaasa wode he laythatan azinay baynda daro macasati Isra7eele biittan deettes shin Elaasay istafe issineykkoka kiitettibenna. Gido attin Sidoona geetettiza biittan Seraphita geetettiza kataman diza issi azinay baynda macaseykko kiitettides.
<range>
Nabe Elisa7e wode Isra7eele deren daro inchiracha hargizayti deettes shin Sooriya biitta asa gidida Ni7imaaneppe attin he darotappe oonikka inchiracha hargefe paxibenna” gides.
Ayhudata Woosa Keeththan dizayti wurikka hessa siydi daro hanqettida.
Ba uttidasoppe dendi eqqidi Yesusa katamappe kare kessidi duge zaari yeddanas ista katamaya oosettida zuma bolla aafotizason oosettidaso ekki efida.
Gido attin izi ista giddora shaakki yeggidi aadhdhi bides.
Heeppeka Galila awurajjan diza Qifirnahoome geetettiza katama wodhdhides. Heenka Sambata gallas daro asa tamarso oykkides.
Izi Godateththara haasayiza gish iza timirtezan malalettida.
Ayhudata Woosa Keeththan tuna ayanay oykkida addey dees. Izikka ba qaala dhoqu histidi
“Naazirete Yesusa ha7i ta waanoo? Nenara tana aazi gaththidee? Ne yiday nuna dhayssanasee? Ne oonakkonne ta erays ne Xoossa Xillo gidikii?” giidi waassides.
Yesusikka tuna ayanaza ha addezappe “Co7u gaada keza” giidi seerides. Tuna ayanayka daro asa sinthan addeza bollafe yeggidi issi qohokka gathonta yeddidi kezides.
Asay wurikka malalettidi ba giddon issoy issara “Aso hayssi ay giza timirtee? Godateththaranne wolqara iita ayanan azazes; istika kezeettes” giidi haasayettides.
Yesusa goobateththayka ubbas gakkides.
Hessafe guye Yesusi Ayhuda Woosa Keeththafe kezidi Simoona keeththe gelides. Simoona bolloteya wolqama misho hargey oykin saketada dishin Yesusa izo patharkii giidi woossida.
Yesusikka izikko shiiqidi misho hargeza seerides. Misha hargeykka yeddin heerakka denda eqqada imathata mokadus.
Awa arshey wullana gishin dumma dumma hargey oykkida asa wursi izakko ekki yida. Izikka hargiza asata ubba bolla ba kushe woththidi pathides.
Tuna ayananti qasseka Yesusa “Neni Xoossa naa” gishenne waassishe daro asatappe kezida; gido attin izi ista seerides; tuna ayananti izi Kirstoosa gididayssa eriza gish isti issinoka haasayana mala koybenna.
Gadey wonitishin Yesusi issi asi bayndaso bides. Daro asaykka iza koyishe izi diza so gakkides. Izi istafe shaakatidi boonta mala digganas koyda.
Gido attin istas “Gede hara katama baada Xoossa Kawoteththa Mishiraachcho qaala yootanas taas bessees; tani kiitettida gita qofay hessakko” gides.
Izikka Yuhudan Ayhuda Woosa Keeththan qaala gujji yootides.
Yesusi Gensereexe Abba lanqen eqqidi Xoossa qaala tamarsishin siyiza asay iza un7ethides.
He wode nam7u wogoloti abba achchan dishin Yesusi beyides. Mole oykkizayti wogolotappe wodhdhidi mole giteta meceettes.
Yesusi wogolotappe Simoona wogolon gelidi biittafe gede abba gido shiishana mala oychidinne wogolo giddon uttidi asaa tamarsides.
Tamarsi wursidappe guye Simoona “Abbay ciimmatizaso shiiqa mole oykkanas inte giteza abba gido yeggite” gides.
Simoonay Yesusas zaaridi “Godo! Qamma kumeth daaburi aqqidi issinokka oykkibookko; gido attin ne qaalan giteza yeggana” gides.
Yeggida wode daro mole oykkida. Giteyka daakkettides.
Hara wogolon dizayti yiidi ista maaddana mala kushera wutti xeygida. Istika yiidi nam7u wogolota mole kunthida. Wogolotikka duge mitetteth oykkida.
Simoona geetettiza Phexroosi hessa beyidi Yesusa toho bolla kundidi “Godo! Ta nagarancha gidida gish ta achchafe kichcha” gides.
Izi hessa giday izinne izara dizayti oykkida daro molezan malalettida gishassa.
Qasseka Simoona laggeti Zabidoosa nayti Yaqoobeynne Yohannisikka wuri malalettida. Yesusikka Simoona “Babbofa! Hayssafe guye ne as oykkizade gidana” gides.
Istika wogolota biittakko shiishshidi wursikka yeggi aggidi Yesusa kaallida.
Yesusi katamatappe issineyin dishin inchiracha hargey bolla wursi oykkida issi asi he kataman dees. He addezikka Yesusa beyidi iza sinthan kundidi “Godo! Ne koykko tana pathana dandayassa” giidi woossides.
Yesusi ba kushe yeddi bochchidi “Ta dosadis, paxa” gides. Inchiranchay heerakka dhayides.
Yesusi izas “Hayssa oonaska yootoppa; Gido attin baada nena Qeese halaqas bessa; istas marka gidana mala ne geeyidayssas Musey azazida yarshoza shiisha” giidi azazides.
Gido attin iza gish asay haasayiza worey kaseppe aakki aakki bides. Keehi daro asay iza haasaya siyanassinne bana sakiza hargefe paxanas izakko shiiqides.
Yesusi daro wode asi bayndaso biidi woossides.
Yesusi tamarsishin asay Galilappenne Yuhudappe qasseka Yerusalameppe yida Farsaaweetinne woga tamarsizayti heen uttida. Izi pathana mala Goda wolqay izara dees.
He wode asay issi kumeththa bollay silidi qaaxonta hargancha halara tookki ekki yiidi keeththe gelthidi Yesusa sinthan wothanas paacida.
Asa daroteththafe dendidayssani keeththe gelthanas xoonettida gish pude keeththa kaara bolla kezidinne kaara qaaridi hargancha halara tookki ehidi asa giddora Yesusa sinthan woththida.
Yesusi ista ammano beyidi “Haysso neni ne nagarappe maarettadasa” gides.
Muse woga xaafizaytinne Farsaaweeti “Hayssi Xoossa bolla xalatethan hayssatho haasayizay izi oonee? Issi Xoossafe attin nagara maaranas ooni dandayizee?” giidi qoppida.
Yesusi ista qofa erida gish “Inte inte woznan ays hessatho qooppetii?
‘Neni nagarappe maarettadasa’ guussafenne ‘Dendada ba’ guussafe awayssi kawushee?
Gido attin ta hayssa giday asa naas biitta bolla asa nagarappe maaranas godateththi dizayssa inte erana mala” gides. Qasseka he sila addeza “Nena gays! Denda eqqa! Ne hala tookkada ba!” gides.
Izi heerakka ista sinthan dendi eqqides. Kase ba ichida hala tookkidi Xoossa galatishe baso bides.
He wode asi wuri malalettides. Xoossa galatishe “Hach malalisizaz beydos” giidi daro babbida.
Hessafe guye Yesusi heeppe kezi bides. Lewe giza issi qaraxa qanxisizayssi qaraxa qanxizason uttidayssa beyidi “Tana kaalla” gides.
Izikka wursi aggidi iza kaallides.
Leweykka Yesusasi ba keeththan gita diggisa diggisides. Qaraxa qanxisiza daro asatinne hara asatikka istara issife maaddan uttida.
Farsaaweetinne ista Xaafeti “Qaraxa qanxisizaytaranne nagaranchatara issife aazas meetii?” giidi Yesusa kaallizayta bolla zuuzumetida.
Yesusikka istas “Harganchatas attin paxa asas aakkime koshshenna.
Takka nagaranchata maarotethakko zaaranas yadis attin xillota xeeyganas yabeekke” gides.
Istika zaaridi “Yohannisa kaallizayti daro wode xoomettessinne woossettes. Farsaaweeta kaallizaytikka izatho ooththettes. Nena kaallizayti gidikko ubba wode meettessinne uyeettes” gida.
Yesusikka istas zaaridi “Mishiray issife dishin diggissas xeeygettidayta xoomisanas bessizee?
Gido attin mishiray istafe shaakettana wodey yaana isti he wode xoomana” gides.
Istas “Oorath may7oppe qanxi ekkidi gal7a may7o bolla woththi sikkizadey deenna; woththi sikkikko oorathazi gal7ara gaaggonta gish gal7aza daakkanna.
Woyneppe oosettida ooratha cajje gal7a lukkamon kunthidi woththiza asi oonikka baawa; woththiza gidikko woyneppe oosettida ooratha cajjey gal7aza daakkana. Woyne cajjezikka biittan gukkana; gal7a lukkamoy sinthafe go7ontaz gidana.
Hessa gish ooratha woyne cajjey ooratha ogoron gujettanas bessees.
Histikko caala woyne cajje uyidappe guye caalontazi uyana koyizay ooninne deenna gaasoyka caalay lo7o giza gishassa” gides.
Issi Sambata gallas Yesusi kaththa giddora aadhdhi bishin iza kaallizayti tiya xuphi ekkidi ba kushen shigichi mishin,
Farsaaweetappe issi issi asati “Sambata gallas ooththanas bessontayssa ayssi ooththetii?” gida.
Yesusikka istas “Dawutey izara diza asati gafida wode izi ooththidayssa nababibeekketii?
Izi Xoossa Keeththe gelidi Qeeseti xalla maana mala azazettida dumma uketha baassi miidi banara dizaytas immides” giidi zaarides.
Qasseka Yesusi “Asa Nay Sambata Goda” giidi istas yootides.
Yesusikka hara Sambata gallas Ayhuda Woosa Keeththe gelidi tamarsishin ushacha kushey silida issi asi heen dees.
Muse woga tamarsizaytinne Farsaaweeti Yesusa mootanas gaaso koydi ane izi Sambata gallassan addeza pathiko beyana giidi naagishe gam7ida.
Yesusikka ista wozna qofa eridi kushey silida addeza ubba sinthan “Denda eqqa” gides. Addezikka dendi eqqides.
Yesusikka ista “Ta intena issi miish ane oychays; Sambata gallas ooththanas bessizay lo7o oosoyee? Iita oosoo? Shempo asho woykko dhayssoo?” giidi oychides.
Qasseka Yesusi ba yuushon diza wursi yuushi xeellidappe guyen addeza “Ne kushe piddisa” gides. Addezikka Yesusi gida mala ooththides. Iza kusheykka paxides.
Gido attin asati hanqettida; Yesusa bolla ay ooththanas koshshizakkonne ba giddon zoretida.
He gallassatappe issi gallas Yesusi woossanas zuma bolla kezidi qamma kumeth Xoossa woossishe aqides.
Gadey wontishin bana kaallizayta xeygidi istafe tammanne nam7ata doorides. Istaka “Hawaareta” giidi sunthides.
Istika Phexroosa giidi sunthida Simoonanne iza isha Indiraasa, Yaqoobe, Yohannisa, Piliphoosa, Bartelemoosa,
Matoosa, Toomaasa, Ilfiyoosa naa Yaqoobe, ba baggas mishettiza Simoona,
Yaqoobe naa Yuhudanne Yesusa aaththi immida Asqoroonto Yuhuda.
Yesusikka istara issife zuma bollafe duge wodhdhidi denbason eqqides. Iza kaallizaytappe daro asay heen dees, Yuhudappenne Yerusalameppe, qasseka Xirooseppenne Sidoona Abba achchafe yida keehi daro asaykka heen dees.
Istika yiday Yesusi gizayssa siyanassinne hargefe paxanassa. Tuna ayanaykka waayssizayti wuri paxida.
Wolqaykka izappe kezidi darota pathiza gish asay wuri iza bochchanas yides.
Yesusikka bana kaallizaytas “Xoossa Kawoteththay intes gidida gish inteno manqotoo! Inte anjettidayta;
Inte guyeppe kallana gish ha7i gafizayto! Inte anjettidayta; inte guyeppe miicana gish inteno ha7i yeekkizayto! Inte anjettidayta;
asay ta gish intena ixishin ba giddofe shaakkishin, borshininne intena iita sunthara xeygishin inte anjettidayta;
“Intes salon gita woytoy diza gish he wode ufayssan guppite; ays giikko ista Aawati nabeta bolla hessatho ooththida.
Gido attin inteno dureto inte ha7i ufayettida gish intena aayye-ana!
Inteno ha7i kallidayto intena aayye ana! Inte guyeppe gafana; inteno ha7i miicizayto! Intes aayye ana! Inte guyeppe mishetananne yeekkana.
“Asi wuri inte gish lo7o haasayiza wode intens aayye-ana! Ays giikko ista aawati wordo nabetas hessa mala ooththida.
“Gido attin ta yootizayssa siyizayto tani intes yootizay inte morketa siiqite; intena ixizaytas lo7o ooththite;
intena qangizayta anjite; intena qohizaytas woossite;
Issi shagalan baqqikko, nam7antho shagala gujja bessa; ooninne ne bollara may7idayssa qaari ekkikko gaaththara may7idayssakka diggofa.
“Nena woossiza ubbas imma; ne miisha ekkida asi zaari immana mala oychofa.
“Asi intes ooththana mala inte koyizayssatho inteka hara asas ooththite.
“Nagaranchatikka bana siiqizayta siiqiza gish inte intena siiqizayta xalla siiqikko intes ay dumma anjoy dizee?
Inte intes lo7o ooththizaytas xalala lo7o ooththikko intes ay dumma anjoy dizee? Ayssi giikko nagaranchatikka hessatho ooththiza.
Tal7e ekkidi zaarana dandayettes gizaytas xalla inte tal7ikko inte hara ay dumma anjo demmanee? Ayssi giikko nagaranchatikka isti tal7idayssa sire zaaridi ekkanas nagaranchatas tal7etes.
Gido attin Xoossi bana galatontaytassinne iitatas kiya gidida mala inte morketa siiqite; lo7o ooththite; guyeppe zaaridi ekkanas qopponta dishe tal7e immite; hessanka intes kushe zaaroy gita gidana; qasseka inte wogga Xoossa naa gidana.
Inte aaway kiya gidida mala inteka kiyata gidite.
“Inte harata bolla pirdofte inte bollakka pirdetenna; inte bolla pirday daronta mala harata bolla pirda darsofte; Asas atto gite inteska atto geetettana.
Immite! Inteska imettana; intes inte makida miishan simmidi makettana; harappeka naaqi baqqettidi yiggeti kumidi wora gukkanashe lo7o makiza miishan makettidi intes imettana” gides.
Qasseka Yesusi istas leemison “Qooqey qooqe kaalethanas dandayizee? Kaalethikkokka nam7ati issoy issara oyketidi ollan gelettennee?
Tamarey bana tamarsizadefe aadhdhenna, gido attin lo7ethi tamarida asi wuri ba astamare mala gides.
“Ne ayfe giddon diza tuussa xeellonta dashe ne isha ayfe giddon diza buura ays xeellay?
Ne ayfen diza tuussa beyonta ne isha ‘Tani ne ayfen diza buura ane kessays gaanas wosta dandayay?’ Neno qoodheppe qommon hanzaysso koyrottada ne ayfen diza tuussa kessa; hessafe guye ne isha ayfen diza buura kessanas lo7etha xeellandassa.
“Lo7o mithi iita ayfe ayfenna; qasseka iita mithi lo7o ayfe ayfenna.
Mithi wurikka ba ayfen ayfen erettes; Agunthafe Balase geetettiza mitha ayfey maxettenna; laadeppe woyne ayfey qanxetenna.
Lo7o asi ba wozna kumida lo7o miish kesses; iita asikka ba wozna kumida iita miishafe iita kesses; asi wurikka ba wozna kumi palahidayssa ba duunan haasayees.
“Tani gizayssa ooththeketa shin ays tana ‘Godo! Godo!’ geetii?
Taakko yiidinne ta qaala siydi polizay wuri oona misatizakkonne ta intena bessana; keeththe keexanas ziqqi ooththi bookkidi shuchcha bollan ba keeththa keexida asa misatees. Haro haaththi yiidi he keeththa sugides; gido attin minni keexettida gish qaathanas dandaybenna.
<range>
Gido attin ta qaala siydi polonta asi ba keeththe lo7ethi baasontanne giddon shuch yeggonta keexida asa misatees; haroyka keeththa sugin keeththay heerakka kundidi iita laaleth laalettides” gi yootides.
Yesusi hessa wursikka dere sinthan yooti wursidayssafe guye Qifirnahoome gizaso bi gelides.
Heen Qifrnahoomen mato halaqay dees; he addezas izi siiqiza ashkaray hargidi hayqos shempo bolla dees.
Izikka Yesusa gish siydi “Ba ashkara pathana mala Yesusa woosseriketii!” giidi issi issi Ayhuda bagga asatappe cimata Yesusakko yeddides.
Kiitettidi bida asati Yesusakko yiidi “Hayssa addeza gish ne ashkaraza pathana bessees.
Ays giikko hayssi addezi nu asa daro dosees; Nuuska Ayhuda Woosa Keeththe keexisiday iza” giidi minthi woossides.
Yesusikka istara bides. Yesusi addeza keeththakko matiza wode addezi ba laggeta Yesusakko yeddidi “Godo! Ne ta keeththe gelanaas bessenna; takka nena ta keeththe gelthanas bessiza asi gidonta gish haa yashe daaburoppa.
Tani ne sinthan beettanas bessonta asa gidida gish neekko babeykke; hessa gish neni heen daada qaala xalla giikko ta ashkaray paxana.
Taaska tana azaziza asi taappe bollara dees. Taappe garsara tani azaziza wotadarati deettes. Issa ‘Haaya!’ giikko yees; issa ‘He ba!’ giikko bees; ashkkaraykka ‘Hessa ooththa!’ giikko azazettidayssa ooththes” gides.
Yesusikka addezi gidayssa siydi addeza hanotethan malalettides. Guye simmidi bana kaalliza deraas “Ta intes gizay hayssa mala gita ammano haray atto shin Isra7eele nayta giddonka demmabekke” gides.
Yesusakko kiitettida asati guye kiittida halaqaso simmida wode ashkaraya paxidayssa beyida
Hessafe guyen Yesusi gam7onta dishe Nayne geetettiza katama bana kaallizaytaranne daro derera issife bides.
Izi biidi katama geliza miixa gakkishin he katamaype daro asay aha tookki ekkidi kezi wodhdhides. Hayqqidays ba aayeys izi mexi issino. Aayeyska azinay baawa; katamappe daro asay izira issife dees.
Godayka izo beyida wode izis michetidi “Aykkoy baawa; yeekkofa!” gides.
Shiiqidinne aha tookkida hala bochchin aha tookkidayti sitti gi eqqida. Yesusikka “Haysso naazo nena gays denda!” gides.
Hayqqida naazikka suuri uttidi haasaya oykkides. Yesusikka naaza aayeys efi immides.
Asay wurikka keehi babbidi Xoossa galatishe “Gita nabey nu giddofe dendides; Xoossikka hayssa dereza yiidi beydes” gides.
Hayssi Yesusa gish haasayettiza lo7o haasayay kumeththa Yuhudaninne Yuhuda yuushon diza deretan kezides.
Xammaqiza Yohannisa kaallizaytikka hayssa wursi Yohannisas yootida. Yohannisikka ista giddofe nam7ata xeygidi,
“Izi yaana geetettidi haasayettizays neneyee? Hara as naaginoo? gi oychite” giidi Godakko yeddides.
Bida asati Yesusakko gakkidi “Xammaqiza Yohannisi ‘Izi yaana geetettidi haasayettizayssi neneyee? Hara as naaginoo?’ giidi neekko nuna yeddides” gida.
He wode Yesusi daro asa waayeppe, hargefenne tuna ayanatappe pathides. Daro qooqeta ayfeykka xeellees.
Yohannisi kiittin izakko yidayta “Biidi inte inte ayfera beyidayssanne siyidayssa Yohannisas yootite. Ayfe qooqeti xeelletes; toho wobeti suure hamutettes; inchiracha hargizayti paxida; tulleti siyida; hayqqidayti hayqoppe dendida; manqotas Mishiraachcho qaalay yootettes.
Tanan dhuphetonta asi wurikka anjettidayssa” gides.
Yohannisi kiittida asati Yesusa achchafe bidayssafe guye Yesusi daro asas Yohannisa gish “Inte ay beyanas bazzo kezidetii? Carkoy heenne haane qathethiza shomboqo beyanassee?
Ay beyanas kezidetii? Lo7iza may7o may7ida as beyana kezidetii? Lo7o may7o may7idi warix gizayti ishalo duussa dizayti kawo keeththan deettes.
Histikko ay beyanas kezidetii? Nabe beyanassee? Ee ta intes tuma gays; inte keziday nabeppe aadhdhizadde beyanassa.
Xoossa qaalan ‘Ne baana oge nees baasi lo7ethana kiitettida as ta neeppe sinthara yeddana’ geetettidi iza gish xaafettidays izakko.
“Tani intes gizay macasappe yeletida asa giddon Yohannisappe aadhdhizadey oonikka deenna; Xoossa Kawoteththan gidikko asa ubbafe guuth geetettida asi Yohannisappe aadhdhana” gi yootides.
Qaraxa qanxisizaytikka attonta hayssa Yesusa qaala siyidayti wurikka Yohannisa kushen xammaqettidi Xoossas bessiza boncho immida.
Farsaaweetinne Muse woga eranchati Yohannisa kushen xammaqettonta gish Xoossi istas waanna qofa ooththidi shiishidayssa hiraayssida.
Qasseka Yesusi zaaridi “Histikko ha7i yeletta aazan leemiso? Isti ay misatizoo?
Giyan uttidi ba giddon issoy issara xeeygettidi ‘Intes nuni diith diixxidos shin duribeekketa; zilalis zilalidos shin yeekkibeekketa; giza nayta misateetes’ gides.
Ays giikko Xammaqiza Yohannisi kath moontanne woyneppe oosettida cajje uyonta yiin ‘Daydanthi iza bolla dees’ gideta.
Asa nay qasse mishenne uyishe yiin ‘Ganjamanne ushshancha; qaraxa shiishshizaytaranne nagaranchatara laggetees’ gideta.
Hessa gish eratetha tumatethay izi nayta ubbata achchan ammanettides” gides.
Hessafe guye Farsaaweetappe issi asi Yesusa quma maanas ba keeththe xeygin Yesusi xeygida Farsaawe keeththa biidi uttides.
He kataman diza issi nagarancha macas dizaara Yesusi Farsaawe keeththan quma maadda bollan dizayssa siyada issi albasxiroose bilqaaxe shitto ekka yadus.
Yaadanne Yesusappe guyera iza toho achchan eqqada yeekkashenne ba afunthan iza toho caphisada ba hu7e binanara quccashenne yeerashe shitto tiyadus.
Yesusa qumas xeeyssida Farsaaweykka hessa beyidi “Hayssi addezi nabe gididakko hanna iza bochchida macasaya iza oonakkonne ay ooththiza asakkone eranakko shin; iza nagaranchakko shin” giidi ba woznan qoppides.
Yesusi “Simoona! Nees ta yootanazi dees” gides. Simoonaykka “Astamaare! Ero yoota” gides.
Yesusi zaaridi “Issi miishe tal7e immizaddefe tal7e ekkida nam7u asati deettes; istafe issa bolla ichashu xeet dinarey dees; nam7anthoza bolla ichashu tammu dinarey dees.
Istas qanxiza miishi dhayin tal7e immidayssi nam7ata accoza wursikka maarides. Histikko ha nam7atappe ha tal7e immidayssa darsi dosanay awayssee?” gides.
Simoonaykka zaaridi “Daro acoy maarettidayssa gaada qoppays” gides. Yesusikka “Tumu pirdadassa” gides.
He macasaykko yuuyidi Simoona “Hanno macasayo xeellay? Ta ne keeththe gelin ne ta tohos haaththe shiishabeekka; iza gidikko ta toho ba afunthan caphisada ba hu7e binanara quccadus.
Neni ubbakka tana yeerabeekka; iza gdikko ta gelosoppe oykkada ta toho yeero aggabeekku.
Ne ta hu7e zayte tiyabeekka shin iza gidikko ta toho shitto tiyadus.
“Hessa gish ta nena gizay iza tana keeha dosida gish iza ba daro nagarappe maarettadus; guuthara maarettiza asa siiqoykka guutha” gides.
Yesusi macasayo “Ne nagarappe maarettadasa” gides.
Izara issife maaddan uttida imathatikka “Hayssi nagara maarizay izi oonee?” giidi ba woznara qoppida.
Yesusikka macasayo “Nena ne ammanoy ashshides; saron ba!” gides.
Hessafe guye Yesusi Xoossa Kawoteththa Mishiraachcho sabakishe dumma dumma katamata giddoranne gutata giddora aadhdhides. Aadhdhidi biza wode iza kaalliza tammanne nam7ati izara deettes.
Qasseka tuna ayanappenne iita hargefe paxida issi issi macasati izara deettes. Istika laapun tuna ayanay izippe kezida Magdale getettiza dereppe yida Maaramo,
Kawo Herdoosason ooththiza Kuza macho Yohaano qasseka Soosinonne hara daro macasati deettes. Istika baas diza miishara Yesusas ooththizayta.
Daro derey issife shiiqidi dishin qasseka asay dumma dumma katamappe izakko wodhdhiza wode Yesusi leemisora tamarsishe,
“Issi goshshanchay zerethi zeranas kezides; izi zerishin baggay ogen wodhdhidi asa tohon yedhettides; salo kafotikka yiidi maxi mida;
Issi zerethay shuchcha gaden wodhdhidi heerakka caarides; gadezikka mela gade gidida gish elle melichides.
Qasseka hara zerethi aguntha giddon wodhdhides; agunthayka izara issife diccidi caarechchaykka dicconta mala cuullides.
Qasseka hara zerethay lo7o aradda gaden wodhdhides; caarida wodekka xeetu kushe ayfides” gides. Yesusi haasaya wursidi qaala dhoqu histidi “Siyiza haythi diza asi siyo!” gides.
Yesusa kaallizayti “Zeretha leemisozas birsheth imma” giidi oychin,
Izikka istas “Xoossa Kawoteththa xuura eroy intes imettides; haratas gidikko leemisora yootays qasseka harati beyidi woznan woththonta malanne siydi yuushi qopponta mala hanides.
“Zeretha leemisoykka hayssa; zereth geetettidaysi Xoossa qaala.
Oge lanqen wodhdhidayssi qaala siyizayta; giddo attin isti ammanidi attonta mala Xala7ey yiidi qaala ista woznappe ekkichizayta.
Shuchcha bolla wodhdhidaytikka qaala siydi ufayssara ekkizayta; istika ha7is ammanettes attin metoy ista bolla gakkiza wode xapho yeddonta gish ellera ammano kaddizayta.
Aguntha giddon wodhdhidayti qaala siyizayta; heytikka hayssa ha alame qofaninne aqotan, hayssa biitta bolla duussa lo7etethan cuulettidi lo7ethi ayfe imettenna.
Aradda biittan wodhdhidayssi qaala suureninne lo7o woznan siydi naagizaytanne dandayan minnidi ayfe ayfizayta.
“Poo7o poo7isidi baatha giddon woykko arsa giddon woththiza asi baawa; gido attin keeththe geliza asas poo7ana mala qonceson wothettes.
Qotettidi qonce kezontay; poo7on kezidi eretontta geeman attana miishi deenna.
“Hessa gish inte siyizayssa naageti siyite; diza asas gujettana bayndades ubbafe izas diza misatizarakka ekettaychana” gi zarides.
Hessafe guye Yesusa aayanne iza ishati Yesusakko yida. Gido attin asa daroteththafe dendidayssan izakko shiiqanas dandayibeetenna.
He wode asay Yesusas “Ne aayeyanne ne ishati nena beyanas koydi karen eqqida” giidi yootida.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Ta aayanne ta ishati Xoossa qaala siydi naagizayta” gides.
Issi gallas Yesusi bana kaallizaytara wogolo giddo gelidi “Abbafe he pinth pinnoos” gides.
Istika pinnishin abba bolla dambalay dendidi waayssiza wode Yesusi dhiskides. Haaththayka wogoloza giddo gelin asay daro metotettides.
Yesusa kaallizayti izakko shiiqidi “Godo! Godo! Nu wurana hanoos” giidi Yesusa dhiskofe denthida. Izikka beeggidi carkozanne abba dambala seerin carkoynne abba dambalay co7u gides.
Izikka bana kaallizayta “Inte ammanoy awa bidee?” gides. Istika ba giddon babbishenne malalettishe “Carkonne haaththe azazizay; istika Izas azazettizay izi oonee?” gida.
Izappe guye Galilappe he pinthan diza Gergesenoone geetettiza dere wogolora pinnida.
Yesusi wogolozappe gaden wodhdhida wode daydanthi iza bolla diza issadey katamappe kezidi iza demmides. He addezi daro wode may7o may7onta kallo dizaddenne keeththan aqonta duufo baas aqoso ooththida asa.
Yesusa beyida wode waassishe Yesusa sinthan kundides; qaala dhoqu histidi “Boncho Xoossa Naa Yesusa! Taasinne nees ay gaytoteththi dizee? Ne tana waayssonta mala ta nena woossays” gides.
Tuna ayanay hessa gaanas dandayiday addezappe kezana mala Yesusi azazida gishassa. Tuna ayanazikka woden woden dendiza gish addezi sansalataninne biratan toho qachchi naaginka qashetida sansalata duuthereththidi iza bolla diza daydanthay iza duge bazzo zaari efees.
Yesusi “Ne sunthi oonee?” giidi oychides; izikka daro daydanthati izan gelidi diza gish ta sunthi “Leegone” gides.
Daydanthatikka bana wursethi baynda ciimma ollan yeggonta mala minthidi woossida.
Henka zuma bolla daro guddunthi heemettes; daydanthatti “Gudduntha wudezan gelite” giidi azazana mala woossin Yesusi “Ero gelite!” gides.
Daydunthati addezappe kezidi guddunthatan gelida. Guddunthati aafoza dugunthara bicharshe biidi abban gelidi abban mitettida.
Heemizayti hanidayssa beyida wode beerotti biidi katama asassinne dere asas yootida.
Handayssa beyana giidi asay ba dizasoppe Yesusakko yides. Daydanthay izappe kezida addezikka woznay kahay simmin afala ma7idi Yesusa toho giddon uttidayssa beyidi babbida.
Daydanthan oyketida addezi paxishin beyidayti izi waani paxidakkonne derezas yootida.
Gergesenoone matan diza asay keehi babbida gish Yesusa “Hayssafe kichcha!” giidi woossida; Izikka wogolozan gelidi simmi bides.
Daydanthay izappe kezida addezi Yesusara issife daana mala woossides.
Gido attin Yesusi iza “Neso simmada Xoossi nees ooththida gita miish yoota” giidi moyzides. Addezikka Yesusi izas ooththida gita miish ba kataman diza asas ubbas qoncen yootishe bides.
Asay wuri Yesusa yuussa naagishe gam7ida gish izi simmishin ufayssan mokki ekkida.
He wode Iya7iroosa geetettiza Ayhuda Woosa Keeththe halaqay yiidi Yesusa toho bolla kundidi baso baana mala woossides.
Izi hessatho oychiday izas tammanne nam7u layth kumida issi maca nay sakettada shempo bolla diza gishassa. Izi hee buussan dishin derey daridi ba giddon sugettidi iza keehi un7isides.
Tammanne nam7u layth suuthi izippe gukkishin diza issi macasaya baas diza miisha wursa dhale eriza asatas imma wursin izo pathanas dandayida asi issadeyka baawa.
Izakka guyera shiiqada Yesusa afala macarata bochchadus; izippe gukkiza suuthay heerakka eqqi aggides
Yesusikka “Tana bochchiday oonee?” gides. Wurikka nuni bochchibeekko gi kadida wode Phexroosi zaaridi “Godo! Asi wuri yuuyi aadhdhidi nena suggerethidi un7isees” gides.
Gido attin Yesusi “Asi tana bochchides; wolqay taappe kezidayssa ta erays” gides.
Macasaya eretonta qotettada baanas dandayontayssa erada kokkorashe yaada Yesusa sinthan kundadus. Izakka Yesusa waana bochchidakkonne qasseka ellera waana paxidakko ubba asa sinthan yootadus.
Izikka “Ta naye! Ne ammanoy nena pathides; saron ba!” gides.
Yesusi buro macasays haasaya bolla dishin Ayhuda Woosa Keeththe halaqa Iya7iroosa keeththafe issi asi Iya7iroosas “Ne naya hayqqadus; hessa gish hayssafe guye astamareza mela daabursofa!” gides.
Yesusi hessa siydi Iya7iroosa “Aykkoy ba; babbofa! Ammana attin ne naya paxana” gides.
Yesusi Iya7iroosa keeththe geliza wode Phexroosa, Yohannisanne Yaqoobe qasseka nay aawappenne aayeyippe attin haray oonikka izara gelana mala koybenna.
He wode asay wuri nays “Wuu wuy!” gi waassi yeekkishin Yesusi “Yeekkofte iza ichchadus attin hayqqabeekku” gides.
Asaykka naya hayqqidayssa eriza gish Yesusa bolla miicides.
Gido attin izi nay kushe oykkidi “Ta naye! Denda!” gides.
Nays shempoykka simmides. Heerakka denda eqqadus; Yesusikka izis miza miish immana mala azazides.
Nayo yelidaytikka malalettida. Gido attin izi hanidayssa oonaska yootonta mala azazides.
Yesusikka tammanne nam7u Hawaareta issife xeygidi daydanthata kessana malanne hargefe pathana mala istas wolqanne godateth immides:
Qasseka Xoossa Kawoteththa yootanassinne hargizayta pathanas ista kiittides.
Istas “Oge bishe guufe woykko, qaraxite woykko, quma woykko, miishe woykko nam7u may7o oykki baanas koshshenna.
Inteka he katamaype kezana gakkanaas koyro gelida oona keeththanka gidin heen gam7ite.
Katama asay intena mokki ekkonta ixikko he katamaype kezidi intena mokkontaytas marka gidana mala inte tohon diza gudulla pittidi kezite” gides.
Istika Goday gida mala kezidi Mishiraachcho qaala yootishenne harganchata pathishe gutan gutan yuuyida.
He wode issi issi asati “Yohannisi hayqoppe dendides” baggayti “Elaassi kezidi beettides.” Qasse baggayti “Beni nabetappe issoy hayqoppe dendides” giidi haasayettiza gish Yuhuda biitta haariza Herdoossi hessa siydi haniza miishan ba woznan metotettides.
<range>
Herdoosikka “Tani iza qoodhe qanxida Xammaqiza Yohannisi hayqides. Histin iza gish hayssa mala haasayettishin ta siyizays izi oonee?” giidi iza ba ayfera beyana koydes.
Hawaaretikka simmidi isti ooththidayssa wursi Yesusas yootida. Izikka ista xalla banara ekkidi Betesayda geetettiza pooqethan diza katama bides.
Gido attin daro asay hessa eridi ista kaallides. Izikka ista mokki ekkidi Xoossa Kawoteththa gish yootides. Qasseka hargefe pathanas bessizayta pathides.
Gadey lem7ishin tammanne nam7u Hawaareti izakko shiiqidi “Nuni dizay bazzo biittan gidida gish asay biidi baas aqanasonne miza miish koyana mala asa moyza” gida.
Gido attin izi istas zaaridi “Inte istas mizaz immite” gides. Istika “Nuus ichashu ukethafenne nam7u moleppe haray ba. Ha asas gidiza kath koshshikko shammanaas bessees” gida.
Yesusikka bana kaallizayta “Asa ichashu tammu, ichashu tammu histi shaakki shaakki utisite” gides. Heenka ichashu shi gidiza attumasay dees.
Yesusa kaallizaytikka Yesusi azazida mala asa wursi utisida.
Yesusikka ichashu ukethanne nam7u moleta oykidi pude salo xeelidi Xoossa galatides. Izikka uketha menthidi asa gaththana mala bana kaallizaytas immides.
Asay wurikka miidi kaallides. Yesusa kaallizaytikka asappe attida tammanne nam7u leemate kumeth maaddafe denthida.
Issi gallas Yesusi barka woossishin iza kaallizayti izakko yida. Izikka ista “Asay tana oona gizee?” giidi oychides.
Istika izas “Issi issi asay Xammaqiza Yohannisa; baggayti Elaasa; harati qasse beni nabetappe issoy hayqoppe dendides geetes” gida.
Izikka ista “Intech tana oona geetii?” giidi oychides. Phexroosikka “Neni Xoossafe kiitettida Kirstoosa” giidi zaarides.
Yesusikka ista “Hayssa oonaska yootoppite” giidi minthi yootidi
Qasseka “Asa Nay daro waaye ekkanas bessees; dere cimatan, Qeese halaqataninne Muse woga xaafizaytan ixettananne ista kushen hayqqanassinne heedzdzantho gallassan hayqoppe dendana” gides.
Qasseka ubbas “Ba shempo ashshana giza asi wuri dhayssana shin ba shempo ta gish giidi dhaysiza asi ashshana. Hessa gish tana kaallana koyiza asi diikko bana kaddo; ubba gallas ba masqale tookkidi tana kaallo.
<range>
Asi alame go7a mule demmidi ba shempo dhayssikko aaza go7ay dizee?
Oonikka tananinne ta qaalan yeelattikko Asa Nay ba bonchora, Aawa bonchoranne Geeshsha kiitanchata bonchora yiza wode tani izan yeelatana.
Ta intes tumu gays; hayssan eqqida asappe hayqqanappe sinthan Xoossa Kawoteth beyana issi issi asati deettes” gides.
Yesusi hessa gida osupun gallassa malappe guye woossanas zuma bolla kezides. Bishe banara Phexroosa, Yohannisanne Yaqoobe ekki bides.
Izi woossishin iza ayfesoy laamettides. Iza medhaykka wolqantha mala xoliqidi boottiides.
Nam7u asati Museynne Elaassi izara haasayettida
Istika bonchora qoncidi Yerusalamen polettana diza Yesusa hayqo gish haasa7ettida.
Phexroosanne izara dizayta deexo dhiskoy oykkides. Istika dhiskofe beeggidi Yesusa bonchonne nam7u asi izara eqqidayta beyida.
He nam7u asati Yesusappe shaaketi bishin Phexroosi Yesusa “Godo! Issi daase nees, issi daase Muses, issi daase Elaasas ooththidi haan dizaakko nuus lo7okko! Shin” gides. Gido attin Phexroosi ba gizayssa eronta gides.
Izi hessa haasayishin shaaray yiidi ista geenthides. Shaara giddo gelidi babbida.
Shaara giddofekka “Tani doorida ta nay hayssa; iza siyite” giza qaalay seetettides.
Qaalay seetettida wode Yesusi xalla beettides. Yesusa kaallizaytikka hanida miisha wursi ba woznan oykkida attin oonaska yootibeetenna.
