Wontetha gallas isti zuma bollafe wodhdhin daro asay yiidi Yesusara gaaggides.
He wode asa giddofe issadey qaala dhoqu histidi “Tamarisizaysso! Taas issi nay xalla diza gish iza ne xeellana mala ta nena woossays.
Iza iita ayanay oykkishin hassa7ay baynda waasses; qaketishe duunara gopponto kessees; qoho gaththidappe guye daro waayssidi aggees.
Nena kaallizayti naazappe kessana mala ista ta woossadis; gido attin kessana dandayibeetenna” gides.
Yesusikka istas zaaridi “Ammanonta ha wode wobe asato! Tani intenara ayde gakkanaas daanee? Intenaka ayde gakkanaas dandayanee? Naaza ane ha eha!” gides.
Naazi yishin iita ayanay iza bollafe yeggin qaketides. Yesusikka iita ayanaza seeridi naaza pathidi naaza aawas immides.
Asaykka wuri Xoossa gitateththan malalettides. Izi ooththidayssan asay wuri malaletishin Yesusi bana kaallizayta
“Asa nay asa kushen aadhdhidi imettana; inteka ha yo7oza baloppite” gides.
Gido attin izi gizayssi istas gelibeenna. Ays giikko isti akeekkonta mala yo7ozi istafe geemettides; zaaridikka oychonta mala babbida.
Iza kaallizayti “Ooni oonappe aadhdhizee?” giidi ba giddon palamettida.
Yesusikka ista wozna qofa eridi guutha naa ekki yiidi ba matan essidi
“Ha guutha naa ta sunthan ekkizaddey oonikka diikko tana ekkees; tana ekkizaddeyka tana kiittidayssa ekkees. Inte ubbafe guutha asi izi ubbaafe aadhdhees” gides.
Yohannisikka “Godo! Issi asi ne sunthan daydanth kessishin beydos. Gido attin izi nunara kaallonta gish digganas koydos” gides.
Yesusikka “Intena ixonta asi wuri inte bagga gidida gish diggofte” gides.
Yesusi salo biza wodey matida gish Yerusalame baanas dendides.
Izikka sinthathidi ase kiittides. Istika koshshiza miish giigissanappe kasetidi Samaariya biittan diza issi guta bida.
Gido attin derey izi Yerusalame bizayssa erida gish mokki ekkibeetenna.
Iza kaallizaytappe Yaqoobeynne Yohannisi hanizayssa beyidi “Godo! Elaassi ooththoyssatho ‘Tamay saloppe wodhdhidi ista dip histo!’ giidi azazana mala koyay?” gida.
Gido attin Yesusi Istako yuuyidi “Intes ay mala ayanay dizakkonne erekketii? Asa Nay yiday asa shempo ashshanas attin dhayssanas gidenna” giidi ista seerides.
Isti wurikka hara guta bida.
Istika birshin issi asi istako shiiqidi “Tani neni biza ubbaso nena ta kaallana” gides.
Yesusi “Workenatas aqiza ollay, kafotas qasse aqiza kafo keeththi dees; gido attin asa naas ba hu7e ayssizasoykka baawa” gides.
Yesusikka hinkoyssa “Tana kaalla” gides. He addezikka “Godo! Ta kaseta baada ta aawa moogoo?” gides.
Yesusikka “Aggaga, hayqqidayti hayqqidayta moogeto. Neni gidikko baada Xoossa Kawoteththa asas yoota” gides.
Qasseka hara asi “Godo! Ta nena kaallana shin koyro soo baada ta keeththa asa saro gaada yo7oo?” gides.
Gido attin Yesusi “Boora kaso oykkidi goyishe guye zaari xeellizadey oonikka Xoossa Kawoteththas bessenna” gides.
Hessafe guye Goday hara laapun tammanne nam7u as dooridi sunthides. Istaka nam7u nam7u histidi izi baana sohotanne katamata wursikka isti kasetidi baana mala kiittides.
“Maxa gakkida kaththay daro; kaththa maxi shiishshizayti guuthata hessa gish kaththa Goday kaththa maxidi shiishshizayta kaththay dizaso yeddana mala woossite.
Hessa gish biite dorsati kana suyte giddora biza mala ta intena yeddays.
Korojo woykko qaraxite woykko caamma ekkofte; oge bolla oonakka saro gooppite.
“Inte oona keeththika geliza gidikko koyrottidi ‘Keeththa aso saro!’ giite.
He keeththan saro dosiza asi diikko inte sarotay he keeththan shempana; saro dosiza asi doonta aggikko inte sarotay intes simmana.
Intes maana shiishida kath wursi miishenne uyishe he inte gelida keeththan uttite; ooththizades ba wolqa waaga ekkanas izas bessees. Ha keeththafe he keeththe yuuyoppite.
“Inte ay katamakka gakkiza wode asay intena mokki ekkikko isti intes aaththida quma miite.
He kataman diza harganchata pathidi Xoossa Kawotethi inteko matides giidi yootite.
Gido attin inte biidi issi katama gelishin he katama asay intena mokki ekkonta ixikko he katama asay shiiqiza dubbushsha kezidi;
‘Nu toho bolla diza inte katama gudulla intes marka gidana mala nu toho bollafe pittoos shin Xoossa Kawoteththay inteko matidayssa erite’ giite.
Ta intes yootays pirda gallas he katama pirdafe Soddome katama pirday kawushshe gidana.
“Kuraziine nena aayye-ana! Betesayda nena ayye ana! Intenan oosettida malatati Xirooseninne Sidoonan oosettidakko istika may7o may7idinne bidinth gorpettidi he wode beni maarettanashin.
Gido attin pirda wode intefe Xiroosessinne Sidoonas kawuyana.
Hanne Qifirnahoome pude salo dhoqu dhoqu gadii? Neni duge Si7oole wodhdhana,
“Inte gizayssa siyiza asi tana siyees; intena ekkonta asi tanakka ekkenna; tana ekkontaykka tana kiittidayssa ekkenna” gides.
Laapun tammanne nam7atikka ufayetishe simmidi “Godo! Haray atto shin daydanthatikka ne sunthan nuus haarettida” giidi yootida.
Izikka istas “Xala7ey wolqantha mala saloppe kundishin ta beyadis.
“Histikko shooshanne masimaso inte yedhana mala morke wolqa ubba bolla intes godateth immadis; intena qohiza issi miishika deenna.
Inte sunthay salon xaafettida gish ufayettite attin tuna ayanati intes haarettida gish ufayettofte” gides.
He wode Yesusi Xillo Ayanan ufayettidi “Salossinne sa7as Goda gidida abbo hayssa wursaka aadhdho eranchatappenne erachatappe qottada qeeri guutha naytas ne qoncisida gish tani nena galatays; ee, ta Aawawu! Hayssi ne lo7o sheney hanides.
“Wuri ta Aawa matappe taas imettides; qasseka iza nay oonakkonne Aawappe attin erizay baawa. Aaway oonakkonne Naazappe attin woykko Naazi izas qoncisanas dosidadeppe attin erizadey baawa” gides.
Bana kaallizaytakko simmidi istas dumma “Inte beyizayssa beyiza ayfeti anjettidayta.
Ta intes tuma gays daro nabetinne kawoti inte ha7i beyizayssa beyanas koydi beybeetenna; inte ha7i siyizayssakka siyanas koydi siybeetenna” gides.
Issi gallas Muse woga tamarsiza issi asi Yesusa paacanas koydi “Tamarisizaysso tani merna de7o laattanas ay ooththoo?” giidi oychides.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Woga maxaafan ay geetetti xaafettidee? Izappe nees geliday aazee?” giidi oychides.
Addezi zaaridi “Ne Goda Xoossa ne kumeththa woznappe, ne kumeththa shempofe, ne kumeththa wolqafenne, ne kumeththa qofappe siiqa; ne laggeka ne hu7e mala siiqa gees” giidi zaarides.
Yesusikka “Lo7o zaaradasa. Nenikka hessatho ooththikko merna de7o demmana” gides.
Addezi bana xillisanas koydi “Histin ta laggey oonee?” giidi Yesusa oychides
Yesusikka zaaridi “Issi addezi Yerusalameppe Iyarko wodhdhishin pangati demmidi iza may7o qaari ekkida; keehi qoxerethidi hayqoppenne paxappe giddon yeggi aggidi bida.
Issi Qeesey he ogera baassi duge wodhdhishe aamunsonta he qoxettida addeza demmidi pooqethara yeggi aadhdhides.
Qasseka issi Lewe bagga asappe issi addezi he ogera aadhdhishe qoxetida addeza beyidi ha7ikka pooqidi aadhdhides.
Issi Samaariya biitta asi he ogera aadhdhi bishe qoxettida addeza bolla gakki wodhdhides; Addeza beyidinne keehi mishettides.
Addezakko shiiqidinne maduntha dhallana mala wogara mitha zaytenne woyne caje maduntha bolla gussidi qachchides; Addeza ba Hare togisidi imaththi shempizaso efidi lo7ethi xeellides.
Wontetha gallas imaththi shempiza keeththa godas nam7u dinare immidinne ‘Nena hara miisha kessisikko ta simmashe nees immana; neeppe kessada lo7etha naaga’ gides.
“Histikko ha heedzdzu asatappe pangatan qoxettidi hayqoppenne paxappe giddon yegettidades keehi mata laggey nees awayssa misatizee?” gides.
Muse woga tamarsizaysikka “Heesi ne michetidayssanne maaddidayssa!” gides. Yesusikka izas “Nekka baada izayssatho ooththa” gides.
Yesusinne iza kaallizayti oge bishin Yesusi issi guta gelides; Marta geetettiza issi macasiya bason Yesusa mokka ekkadus.
Izis Maaramo geetettiza issi micheya dawus. Maaramakka izappe qaala siyashe Goda toho garsan uttadus.
Gido attin Martay ooso daroppe dendidayssan daaburada Yesusakko shiiqada “Godo! Ta michiya ooso wursa ta bolla aggada uttishin neni co7u gay? Iza tana maaddana mala izis yoota attin” gadus.
Gido attin Goday “Hanne Martane! Neni daro miisha gish qofa daraasa; dirbataasa; tuggataasa.
Koshshizay gidikko issi miish xalla; Maaramakka lo7o exa dooradus; hessika izippe ekettenna.”
Issi gallas Yesusi issison woossides; izi woossa wursishin iza kaallizaytappe issoy “Godo! Xammaqiza Yohannisi bana kaallizayta woossa tamarsidayssatho nekka nuna woossa tamarsa!” gides.
Izikka istas “Woossishe ‘Nu Aawawu! Ne sunthi anjetto; ne kawotethi haayo;
hachchis gidiza quma nuus imma;
nuna qohidayta nu maariza mala nuna maara; paacenka nuna gelthofa’ gi woossite” gides.
Qasseka “Intefe issaddes laggey diikko leela gidoth he laggezaso biidi ‘Taas issi imaththi ogeppe yiin mizana kath baynda gish heedzdzu solloy diikko taas tal7arikii?’
<range>
Laggezikka zaaridi ‘Tana waaysoppa; kareykka gordettides; tanikka naytara ichchadis. Ha7i dendada immanas dandaykke’ gaandee?
Takka intes yootays laggetetha gish dendidi immonta aggikkokka izi oychon salethida gish dendidi koyizayssa wursi immides.
“Hessa gish tani intes gizay; woossite intes imettana; koyite inte demmenna; kare qoxite intes doyettana.
Ays giikko woossizay wuri ekkana; koyizaykka demmenna kare qoxizadeska doyettana.
“Intefe aawa gidi uttidi izi yelida nay mole oychikko shoosh immizay daandee?
Woykko phuuphulle oychikko masimaso immizay daandee?
Inte iitata gidishe inte naytas lo7o imota imo erikko; salon diza inte Aaway bana woossizaytas Xillo Ayanan wosti darsi immenee?” gides.
Issi gallas Yesusi haasayssonta duude daydanth kessides. Daydanthazikka kezidappe guye duuna duude addezi haasaydes; beyida asatikka darsi malalettida.
Gido attin issi issi asati “Bi7elizeebula geetettiza daydanthata halaqan daydanthata kessees” gida.
Issi issi asay iza paacanas “Saloppe malata bessa” giidi oychida.
Gido attin Yesusi ista qofa eridi “Ba giddon shaakettiza kawotethi wuri dhayana; ba giddon sigay baynda keeththikka kundana.
Inte tana ‘Bi7elizebulan daydanthata kessees’ giidi haasayeta shin Xala7eykka ba giddon issoy issafe shaaketikko iza kawotethi waani minnanee?
Histikko tani daydanthata Bi7elizeebula kessikko inte nayti oonan kessandetoo? Hessa gish inte nayti inte bolla pirdizayta gidana.
Gido attin tani daydanthata kessizay Xoossa wolqan gakkides; Xoossa Kawoteththay inteko matidaro erite.
“Mino asi lo7ethi gixxettidi ba keeththe naagikko keeththan diza miishi lo7on naagettes.
Gido attin izappe hara mino asi yiidi xoonikko izi ammanettida ola miishata woththi ekkidi izas diza haarozakka wursi haras gishanna.
“Tanara gidontay tanara eqettes; tanarakka shiishontadey laalles,
“Tuna ayanay asappe kezida wode shemposo koyishe haaththi baynda mela soon waayetees; shemposoy dhaykko ‘Tani kase kezidaso guye simmana’ gees.
Izappe simmidi yishin kase izi aggi bida keeththay pitettidinne giigi uttidayssa demmees.
Hessafe simmi biidi baappe iitiza hara laapun daydanthata banara ekkidi yees; istika gelidi heen daana; Hessadeska koyroyssafe guyeyssi keehi iita gidana” gida.
Yesusi hessa haasayiza wode asa giddofe issi macas dizaara ba qaala dhoqu ooththada “Nena tookkida qanthinne ne dhammida dhanthati anjettidayta” gadus.
Gido attin izi “Anjettidayti Xoossa qaala siydi azazettizayta” gides.
Daro derey Yesusakko shiiqida wode Yesusi “Hayssi yelettay iita yeletta; gita malata beyanas koyees. Gido attin Yoonaasa malatappe hara dumma malatay imettenna.
Gaasoyka Yoonaassi Nanawe asas malata gidida mala asa nay tani ha yelettas malata gidana.
Dugeha dere maca kawoya Solomoone erateth beyanas biitta gaxappe dendada yida gish pirda wode iza ha yelettara dendada pirdana; hekko Solomooneppe aadhdhizaddey haan dees.
Yoonaassi sabakishin siydi Nanawe asay ba nagarappe maarottida gish ha yelettara issife dendidi pirdana. Gido attin Yonaasappe aadhdhizay haan dees.
“Xompe oythidi kareppe geliza asas poo7ana mala qonceson wothetes attin geemason woththiza asi deenna.
Ne asatethas poo7oy ne ayfe; ne ayfey paxa gidikko ne kumeththa asatethay po7o gidana. Ne ayfey saketikko ne kumeththa asatethay dhuma gidana.
Hessa gish nenan diza poo7oy dhumonta mala naagetta.
Histikko ne asatethay poo7o gidikko dhumida asatethi deenna aggikko ne kumeththa asatethay xompe lo7ethi poo7iza mala lo7i beettanna” gides.
Yesusi haasaya wursida mala issi Farsaawey banara quma maanas Yesusa xeygides.
Yesusi quma maana kushe mecetonta aggidayssa beyidi malalettida.
Goday izas “Ha7i inte Farsaaweeti xu7assinne keres bolla bagga meeci geeshsheta; inte gido baggazi uzetethaninne iitatethan kumides.
Inteno eeyato! Kare bagga medhdhiday gido bagga medhibenee?
Yo7on gidikko giddon dizayssa muxuwata immite; he wode wurikka intes geesh gidana.
“Inteno Farsaaweeto! Intes ayye ana! Anugappenne xalotappe qasseka dumma dumma kathafe tammafe issino kesseeta; gido attin tuma pirdanne Xoossa dosanayssa aggi aadhdheta. Yo7on gidikko inte aggi aadhdhanas bessenna. Hankoyssa aggonta inte ooththana bessizaytikka hayta.
“Inteno Farsaaweeto! Intes aayye-ana! Ayhuda Woosa Keeththan uttanas boncho oyde koyeeta; giya giddonka asay inte sinthan hokkana mala doseeta.
Asi eronta iza bollara biza qotetti diza duufo inte misattiza gish intena aayye-ana!” gida.
Muse woga erizaytappe issoy zaaridi “Astamaare! Ne hessatho haasayiza wode nunakka cayaassa” gides.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Inteno Muse woga erizaytto inteska aayye-ana! Asi tookkanas dandayonta deexo tooho asa toosseta. Inte gidikko intes biradhdhe xeeranikka bochchekketa.
“Inte Aawati wodhida nabeta duufo inte lo7ethiza gish intes ayye ana.
Histikko inte inte aawata ooso minthiza markata; isti nabeta wodhida; inteka ista duufo lo7etheeta.
“Hessa gish Xoossa erateth hizgadus ‘Nabetanne Hawaareta ta istas yeddana; istika istafe issa issa wodhana; haratakka gooddana.
Hessa gish ha yelettay biittay medhettosoppe ha7i gakkanaas gukkida nabeta ubba suutha gish oyshettana.
Aabeele suuthafe oykkidi yarshizasoppenne Xoossa Keeththa giddon gukkida Zakaraasa suutha gakkanaas koyeettes.’ Ee ta intes gizay ha yelettay hayssas oyshettana.
“Inteno woga erizayto! Intes aayye-ana! Eratetha penge qulfe wolqara woththi ekkidi inteska gelibeekketa; gelanaytaka diggeeta” gides.
Yesusi heeppe kezidappe guye Xaafetinne Farsaaweeti eqettishe oyshan shempo diggida.
Iza duunappe keziza qaalan iza qaxanas naagettida.
He wode daro derey ba giddon issoy issara yedhettana gakkanaas shiiqi uttidashe Yesusi bana kaallizayta “Farsaaweeta irshofe naagettite; hessika qoodheppe qommo hano.
Qonconta kamettidi attanaynne erettonta qotan attana miishi deenna.
Hessa gish inte geeman haasayidazi wuri qonce kezana; qasseka inte qol7an haythan sasuketi haasayidazi wuri dere sinthan yootettana.
“Ta laggeto! Ta intes gizay asho xalla wodhanappe attin hara aykkokka ooththanas dandayontaytas babbofte.
Gido attin inte babbanas bessizay oonakkonne ta intena bessana; asho wodhidappe guye ashonne shempo issife gaththi Gaanname taman yegganas dandayizayssas babbite. Ee izas babbite gays.
“Siine kafo ichashati nam7u santes bayzettetes; gido attin istafe issiniyoka Xoossi dogenna.
Inte hu7e binanay kumeth taybon dees. Hessa gish babbofte; daro Siine kafotappe inte aadhdheta.
“Ta intes yootays ta gish asa sinthan markattiza asa ubbas Asa Nay qasseka Xoossa kiitancha sinthan iza gish markattana.
Gido attin asa sinthan tana kaadidadey Xoossa Kiitancha sinthan kaadettana.
“Asa Naa bolla kawushsha qaala haasayizades nagaray wuri maarettana shin Xillo Ayana cayizadey maarettenna.
“Asay intena oykkidi dere haarizaytakkonne godattizaytakko, Ayhuda Woosa Keeththe oykki efikko ‘Ay gi zaarinoo? Ay giinoo?’ giidi hirgofte.
Ays giikko inte haasayanas bessizayssa Xillo Ayanay he wode intena tamarsana.”
Daro asa giddofe issadey “Astamaare! Ta ishay nu aawa laata miishafe tana gakkizayssa taas immana mala izas yoota” gides.
Yesusikka “Haysso! Tana inte bolla pirdiza daanna ooththiday oonee?” gides.
Qasseka istas “Asas daro miish diikkokka shempoy he duretethan doonta gish naagettite; yiiqetethafe intena keehi naagite” gides.
Zaarethidikka istas “Lo7ethi kath immiza gade goda gidida issi dure asi dees.
He addezikka ba woznan ‘Ta kaththa shiishada woththizassoy baynda gish ay ooththoo?’ giidi qoppides.
“Addezikka ‘Taas diza gootarata laallada hara aakkizaz keexana; histada taas diza kathaanne taas dizaz wursa izan shiishana.
Ta shempoyokka ta shempoye! Daro wodes gidiza kath shiishida gish shempa uttada ma; uya; ufayeta’ gaana gides.
“Gido attin ‘Xoossi haysso eeyazo! Ne shempoyo hachchi omars neeppe ekkana koyeettes; hessa gish ne nees shiishidays oonas gidanee?’ gides.
“Hessa gish Xoossa achchan dure gidonta baas miishe shiishshiza asa wursethikka hessa mala” gi leemison yootides.
Hessafe guye Yesusi bana kaallizaytas “Intes ta yootays inte duussas ‘Ay maanakkonne woykko inte bollas ay may7anakkonne’ giidi ceecoppite.
Ays giikko shempoy kathafe asatethi qasse may7oppe aadhdhees.
Quurota xeellite zeretenna; maxetenna; kath shiishshiza gootaray istas baawa shin Xoossi ista mizees. Histikko inte istafe keehi aadhdheketii?
Gido attin intefe darsi qoppidi ba laytha bolla issi gallas gujjana dandayizay oonee?
Histikko guutha miish oosoy intes dandayettontashe ays hara miishas keehi qoppetii?
“Ciishshati waanidi diccizaakkonne ane xeellite; waayettenna; suqetenna; gido attin ta intes yootays; Solomooneykka gita asa shin istafe issineytho may7ibenna.
Histikko Xoossi hachchi beettidi wonto taman wodhdhana maata hayssatho mayziza gidikko inteno ammanoy paccidayto! Intena wosti aaththi mayizenee?
“Hessa gish ‘Ay miinoo? Ay may7inoo?’ giidi inte woznay darsi qoppofo.
Biitta bollan diza asi wuri hayssa koyees; gido attin hayssi wuri intes koshshizayssa inte Salo Aaway erees.
Ubbafekka koyrothidi Xoossa kawoteth koyite; hayssi wuri intes gujeti imettana.
“Inteno guutha wude mehe mala gididayto! Kawoteth intes immanas inte Aawas lo7o qofa gidida gish babbofte.
Intes dizayssa bayzidi manqotas immite; kaysoy ekkontason, bilay moontason, cimmoonta korojon wuronta miish salon shiishshite.
Inte woznay inte miishi dizason daana” gides.
“Qanthan gixxidi giigetite, inte poo7oykka poo7o,
Ista goday bulacha diggisappe simmidi yaanashe naagetizaytanne izi yiidi penge qoxishin elle doyanas giigi uttida asata misatite.
Ista goday yiza wode dhiskonta naagidi uttida ashkarati isti anjettidayta; ta intes tumu gays; ista goday baas qanthan gixxi eqqidi ista maaddan uttissidi muzana.
Omars woykko leela gidoththan yiidi isti dhiskonta dishin demmikko he ashkarati anjettidayta.
Kaysoy ay wode yaanakkon eriza gididakko keeththa goday kaysoy bookkishin co7u giidi bessontayssa erite.
Asa Nay inte qopponta woden yaanayssa eridi inteka giigettidi naagite” gides.
Phexroosikka “Godo! Hayssa leemiso ne yootizay nuus xallayee? Ubba asassaraa?” gides.
Godayka “Histikko baso asas koshshiza woden quma immana mala keeththadey keeththa asa bolla woththiza ammanettida woznama asi oonee?
Goday simmishin hessatho ooththishe beettizaddey izi anjettidade.
Ta intes tumu gays; baas diza miish ubba bolla hessade godassana.
Gido attin ‘Izadey ta goday elle yeenna gam7ana’ giidi qoppidi adde ashkaratanne maca ashkarata bukkikko, qasseka koyda mala miidinne uyidi mathotikko,
hessade goday izi qopponta gallassan yaana giidi ezugonta saaten yaana. Yiidikka iza qanxerethi yeggidi iza exa ammanontaytara issife ooththana.
“Ba goda qofa eridi giigetontaynne goda shene ooththonta ashkaray iita shoch shocettana.
Gido attin eronta dishe shochas bessiza mooro ooththida ashkaray guuthara shocettana. Daro imettida asa ubbafe daroy koyeettes; daro hadara ekkidadefe daroy koyeettes.
“Tani yiday biitta bollan tama eethanassa. He tamay ha7i eexxi kezidakko tana daro ufayssana.
Gido attin tani xammaqettana xinqatay dees; he xinqatay polettanashe tani keeha metottettadis.
Intes tani biitta bolla saro ehana yida misatizee? Gidenna; ta intes yootays tani yiday issa issafe shaakanassa.
Hayssafe sinthan issi keeththan ba giddon shaaketida ichashu asati daana. Nam7ati heedzdzata bolla heedzdzati nam7ata bolla dendidi ba giddon shaakettana.
Aaway ba attuma naa bolla, attuma naykka ba aawa bolla, aaya ba maca nay bolla maca nayakka ba aayey bolla, bollota ba naa mach bolla, naa machaka ba bolloti bolla dendidi ba giddon shaakettana” gides.
Qasseka derezas “Inte awa arshey mokiza baggara shaaray kezishin beyidi ‘Elleraka iray yaana’ gees geeta; inte gida malaka hanees.
Dugeha baggara pudeha carkishin gallassay ho7o gidana geeta; inte gida malaka hanees.
Inteno! Lo7o misatiza iitato; saloyssanne sa7a medha beyidi hananayssa ereeta shin histin ha wodeza eroy intena waani xoonizee?” gides.
“Histikko inte ays tuma pirdeketii?
“Ne morkera daanna sinthan eqqana bishin buro oge bollan dashe izara giigana oge koya; ne histonta aggikko izi nena goochchidi daanna sinth efana; daannaykka nena aaththidi halaqas immana; halaqayka nena woynen yeggana.
Ta nees yootays; daannay pirdida wursetha santimeyo qanxa wursana gakkanaas heeppe kezakka.”
He wode issi issi asati Yesusakko yiidi “Philaxoosi ista suuthi ista yarshora gaththi walakkida Galila asata” gish Yesusas yootida.
Izikka zaaridi “Histin hessa mala metoy ista bolla gakkida asati hanko waayey gakkonta attida Galila asa ubbafe aadhdhida nagarancha gidida gish giidi qoppetii?
Gidenna! Ta intes yootays inte maaretonta ixikko inte wurikka he asata mala dhayana.
Woykko Salhoomen gimbey ista bolla kundin hayqqida tammanne osupun asati Yerusalamen diza asa ubbafe nagarancha gidida gish giidi qoppetii?
Gidenna! Ta intes yootays inte maaretonta ixikko inte wurikka he asata mala dhayana” gides.
Qasseka istas “Issi asi woyne tokkizason tokkettida issi Balase giza mithi dawus; he balase mithaykko ayfe koyana yiidi issi ayfeka demmibenna.
Woyine atakilte ooththizayssas ‘Hekko tani ayfe demmanna gaada hachchira heedzdzu layth ha Balaseykko simereta yaada issi ayfeka demmabeekke; hessa gish izo qanxa digga; aazas coo biitta xunxazee?’ giidi leemiso yootides.
Izikka zaaridi ‘Godo! Tani izi xaphon osha yeggada oosetha xeellana mala halaythas aggaggarkii?
Yiza laythas iza ayfikko lo7o; ayfonta ixikko qanxandassa’ ” gides.
Yesusi Sambata gallas issi Ayhuda Woosa Keeththan tamarsishin;
tammanne osupun layth kumeth iita ayanay oykkidi asateth paccisida issi macasaya heen dawus; izakka zokkoy quunnida gish mulekka dhoqu gaanas danda7ukku.
Yesusi izo beyidappe guye xeygidi “Hanne macasaye! Neni nena sakkiza hargezappe paxadasakko” gides.
Yesusi ba kushe izi bolla woththin iza heerakka siti gaada eqqadus; Xoossakka galatadus.
Ayhudata Woosa Keeththa halaqazikka Sambata gallas pathidayssas Yesusa bolla hanqettidi izakko yiza dereza “Oosos bessiza usuppun gallassati diza gish he ooso gallassatan yiidi paxite attin Sambata gallas yooppite” gides.
Godayka zaaridi “Inteno qoodheppe qommon haasayizayto! Inte giddofe issadey ba boora woykko ba hare Sambata gallas bason qashetidasoppe birshidi haaththe ushshanas efi erennee?
Histin hanna macasaya Abrahaame naa gidada tammanne osupun layth kumeth Xala7ey qachchin dizasoppe Sambata gallas birshettanas izis bessennee?” gides.
Yesusi hizgi oychida wode izara eqettizayti wurikka yeellatida; gido attin derey wurikka izi oychida malalisiza oyshan ufayettides.
Qasseka Yesusi zaaridi “Xoossa Kawotethi ay misatizee? Izo aazara leemisoo?
Issi asi Sanafice geetettiza mitha ayfe ba gaden tokkin mokka diccada gita gidin kafoti izi hagga giddon duussaso giigissana gakkanaas diccida sanafice mith misatawus” gides.
Qasseka “Xoossa Kawotethi aazara leemiso?
Issi macassi munuqa caalisanas daro dhiillera walakkida guutha irsho misatawus” gides.
Hessafe guye Yesusi Yerusalame bishe kanthi biza katamaninne gutatan asa tamarsishe aadhdhishin,
issadey izakko shiiqidi “Godo! Pirdafe guutha asati xalla attanee?” giidi oychides. Izikka zaaridi “Xuuntha pengeyra gelanas baaxetite; daroti gelanaas koyeettes shin istas hanenna.
<range>
Keeththa goday dendidi ba kare gordi gidin inte karen eqqidi ‘Godo! Kare doyarki!’ giidi penge qoxana shin izi zaaridi ‘Inte oonakkonne awappe yidakkonne ta intena erikke’ gaana gides.
“Intenikka izas zaaridi ‘Nuni nenara issife midossinne issife uyidos; nu dubbushshan nuna ne tamarsadassa’ gaana.
“Izikka zaaridi ‘Intena inte oonakkonne inte awappe yidakko ta intena erikke; inte makalati wurikka taappe haakkite’ gaana gides.
“Inte Abrahaame, Yisaaqa, Yaqoobenne nabeta ubbata Xoossa Kawoteththan beyiza wode inte karen yegeti attikko he wode intes yeehonne achcha garcech gidana.
Asay awa arshey mokkiza baggafenne wulliza baggafe pudehappenne dugehappe yiidi Xoossa Kawoteththa maaddan uttana.
Hekko guyen dizaytappe baggayti sinthe aadhdhana sinthan dizaytappe baggati guye aadhdhanayti deettes” gides.
He wode Farsaaweetappe issi issi asi yiidi “Herdoossi nena wodhanas koyiza gish hayssafe denda kichcha” gida.
Yesusi istas “Tani buro ‘Hachchinne wonto daydanthata asappe kessana; hargizaytaka pathana; heedzdzantho gallas ta qofaso ta gaththana’ gides giidi he workanas yootite.
Gido attin nabey Yerusalameppe karen hayqqanas bessonta gish hachchinne wonto wontoppeynka ta sinthe buus gujjana.
“Hanne Yerusalame nabeta wodhizare neekko kiitettidayta shuchchara caddizare! Kuttoy ba ciyeta ba qefe gars shiishshiza mala ne nayta shiishshanaas aappun wode koyadinashin ne gidikko akay gadasa.
Hekko inte keeththay kayzides; ta intes yootays, ‘Goda sunthan yizadey anjettides’ inte gaana wodey gakkanaashe nam7antho tana beyekketa” gides.
Issi gallas Yesusi quma maanas Farsaaweeta halaqatappe issa so gelida wode asay wuri Yesusa ay ooththanakkonne giidi ayfe iza bolla tokki xeellides.
Heenka asatethay izas puurin waayettiza issi asi iza sinthan dees.
Yesusikka Muse woga erizaytanne Farsaaweeta “Sakettizade Sambata gallas pathanas koshshizeyee? Koshshennee?” giidi oychides.
Istika co7u gida; izikka addeza bochchidi pathi yeddides.
Qasseka “Intefe issi asas Sambata gallas nay woykko booray kundidi ollan gelikko eeson heerakka kessontadey oonee?” gides.
Istika oyshas aykko zaaroka demmanas dandayibetenna
Xeeygettida asati uttanas boncho so koyishin Yesusi beyidi leemisora istas,
“Issi asi nena sarges xeeyssikko bonchoson uttofa; neeppe bollara bonchettizaddey xeeyssetikko;
intena nam7ataka xeygidadey yiidi ‘Ne uttidasoza hayssades yedda’ gaana; nenikka yeellatashe ziqaso baandasa.
Gido attin ne xeeyssettida wode ziqaso xeellada utta; nena xeygidadey yiidi ‘Ta laggezo! Haaya dhoqason utta’ gaandes; nenikka he wode nenara maaddan uttida asa ubba sinthan bonchettana.
Ays giikko bana dhoqu histizaddey wuri ziqqi gaana; bana ziqqi histizaddey wuri dhoqu gaana” gides.
Yesusikka xeygidadeza “Quma woykko kawo mizanas xeeyssikko neyssatho nena xeeyssidi mizonta mala ne laggeta woykko ne ishata, ne dabbota woykko dureta woykko dure gutata xeeygoppa.
Gido attin asa xeeyssada mizana koykko manqota, kushey, tohoy baynda wobettanne qooqeta xeeyssa; neni anjettana.
Xeeyssettidayti kushe zaaranas dandayonta gish xillota dentha wode nees kushey zaarettana” gides.
Maaddan Yesusara issife uttidaytappe issoy hayssa siydi “Xoossa Kawoteththan shiiqidi maaddafe miza asi anjettidade” gides.
Yesusikka “Issi asi wolqama diggise giigissidi daro as xeygides.
“Diggise maana wodeykka gakkin xeeygettida imathata, ‘Wurikka giigida gish haa yiite!’ giidi xeeygana mala ba ashkara yeddides.
Gido attin wurikka baasi hara gaaso shiishshidi issoy ‘Ha7i gade shamadis; ta baada beyanas bessees; hachchis tana lancofa’ gides.
“Hankoysikka ‘Tani ichashu waaxa boora shamadis. Ista paaca xeellana gish hachchi tana lancofa’ gides.
“Qasse hara issadeykka ‘Tani buro mishiratethan days; baanas dandaykke’ gides.
“Oosanchayka kiitettidasoppe simmidi heedzdzati gidayssa ba godas yootides. He wodekka diggisa giigissidayssi hanqettidi oosancha ‘Elella oyddu oge kezada manqota, kusheynne tohoy baynda wobeta qomaxatanne ayfey baynda qooqeta ha geltha’ gides.
“Oosanchazikka zaaridi ‘Ta Godo! Ne tana azazidayssa wursa poladis; ha7ikka hara utethasoy dees’ gides.
“Godazikka oosanchaza ‘Gede oyddu oge kezada ta keeththe kumana mala pudenne duge aadhdhizayta wolqara ha geltha.
Tani tuma gays; diggisa maana xeeyssetidaytappe issadeykka duunan gelthenna’ ” gides.
Daro derey izara issife bizayssa Yesusi beyidinne guye simmi
“Taakko yizay wuri ba aawa, ba machonne nayta, ba ishatanne micheta, ba shempo gidin ixonta aggikko tana kaallizade gidanas dandayenna.
Ba masqale tookkidi tana kaallontay tana kaallizade gidanas dandayenna.
“Intefe issi asi keeththe keexanas koykko polanas dandayanakkonne dandayontakko koyrottidi baas diza bira qoppontay oonee?
Keeththa keexana doommidi wursanas hanonta ixikko beyida asi wuri iza bolla miicana.
Istika ‘Hayssi addezi keeththe keexo oykkides shin polibenna’ gi miicana.
“Woykko issi kawoy hara kawora olas giigettidi nam7u tammu shi asi ekki yiza kawo zaaranas tammu shi ola asara zaaranakkonne uttidi qoppontay oonee?
Ola zaaranas dandayetonta misatidi beettikko buro hahon dishin maqaynanas gaana yeddees.
Hessathoka intefe oonakka gidin baas dizayssa aggontay tana kaallizade gidanas dandayenna.
“Maxiney lo7oshin ba maxinetetha mal7o yeddikko zaaridi waani mal7ana dandayizee?
Gaden yeggin aradisonta gish coo kare wora yegettes; siyiza haythi diza asi siyo!” gides.
Issi gallas qaraxa shiishshizaytinne nagaranchati wuri Yesusappe siyanas iza achchi shiiqida.
Farsaaweetinne Xaafeti “Hayssi addezi nagaranchata ixenna; istarakka mees” giidi ba giddon zuuzumetida.
Yesusikka istas leemiso hizgi yootides;
“Inte giddofe issades xeetu dorsi diikko he xeetu dorsatappe issina dhaykko attida uddufun tammanne uddufunata denban yeggidi dhayidayssa demmana gakkanaas koyana boontay oonee?
Demmidi ufayssara hashen tookki ekkidi,
baso simmes, ba laggetanne guta asata issi bolla xeygidi ‘Dhayida ta dorsayo demmadis; tanara issife ufayettite’ gaana.
Ta intes yootays ‘Hessathoka maaroteth koshshonta uddufun tammanne uddufun xillotappe maaretethan geliza issi nagaranchan salon ufays gidana.’
“Woykko issi tammu bira santimey diza macasaya he tammafe issineya dhaykko xompe oythada demmana gakkanaas keeththa gars pittada lo7etha koyonta macas oonee?
Izakka demmida wode ba laggetanne ba gutata issife xeeygada ‘Taappe dhayda bira santimeyo demmida gish tanara issife ufayettite’ gaandus.
Ta intes yootays ‘Hessathoka maarotan geliza issi nagarancha asan Xoossa kiitanchata achchan ufays gidana.’
“Issides nam7u nayti deettes.
Istafekka kaalo naazi ba aawa ‘Aabo! Nees diza miishafe ta gisha taas imma’ gides. Aawaykka baas diza miisha ba naytas gishides.
“Daro wode gam7onta dishe kaalo naazi ba miisha wursi shiishshi ekkidi haaho biitta bides. Heenka baas diza miisha go7ay baynda coo mela dhayssides.
Izikka baas dizayssa wursi dhayssidappe guyen he biittan iita koshay dendin daro waayettides.
Hessa gish he deren diza asappe issaadekko shiiqides. Izaadeyka ba guddunth heemmana mala gudduntha heemizaso yeddides.
Naazikka guddunthati miza harqozappe maanas amottides shin hessaka immizadey beettibenna.
“Gido attin iza woznay simmida wode ‘Ta aawa ashkarata aappunatappe kathi tirpize shin tani hayssan gafan hayqqana matadinaa?
Dendada ta aawa so baada, aabo! Salon Xoossa, sa7an ta nena qohadis.’
Hayssafe guye ‘Tani ne naa geetettada xeeygettanas taas bessenna; ne ashkaratappe issa mala tana qooda’ gides.
Hessa gish dendidi ba aawakko bides. Gido attin buro izi hahora yishin aaway beyidi mishettidinne izakko woxxi biidi idimmi oykkidi yeerides.
“Naazikka ‘Aabo! Salon Xoossa, sa7an ta nena qohadis; hayssafe guye ta ne naa geetettada xeeygettanas taas bessenna’ gides.
“Gido attin aaway ashkaratas ‘Eesottidi ubbafe doorettida may7o ehidi mayzite; iza biradhen migda, iza tohonka caamma aaththite.
Modho mirgo boora ehidi shukite; miidi ufayetoos.
Hayssi ta naazi hayqqides shin paxides; dhayides shin beettides’ gides; hessafe guyen ufayeteth oykkida.
“Hessi haniza wode bayra naazi goshshason dees; heeppeka simmidi so matida wode diiththa duris siydes.
Izikka ashkaratappe issa xeygidi ‘Hessi aazee?’ gi oychides.
Ashkarazikka ‘Ne ishay yides; izi saroninne lo7on simmida gish ne aaway modho mirgo boora shukides’ gides.
“Bayra ishazikka hanqettidi so gelanaska koybenna. Aawaykka kare kezidi izi so gelana mala woossides.
Gido attin izikka zaaridi aawas ‘Hekko tani hayssa gakkanaas nees aylle mala ooththadis; ne azazoppe issinokka paccisabeekke; gido attin tani ta laggetara ufayettana mala ne taas issi deysha laaqakka immabeekka.
Gido attin hayssi ne naazi nees dizayssa wursi laymatizaytara wursidi yishin modho mirgo boora izas shukadasa’ gides.
“Aawaykka ‘Ta naazo ne ubba wode tanara daasa; taas gididay wurikka neessa.
Hayssi ne ishay hayqqides shin paxides; dhayides shin beettides; hessa gish nuni ufayetanas bessees’ ” gides.
Yesusi bana kaallizaytas “Issi dure adde dayssas iza keeththa ayssiza issi asi dees; izi he dure addeza miisha ogey baynda laallizayssa worey ha dure addeza haythan wodhdhides.
Dure addezi he addeza xeygidi ‘Haysso ta siyzayssi hessi aazee? Hayssafe doommada ne ta keeththas ayssizadde gidanas dandayonta gish ne alafetetha giddon diza miisha oykkida mazgaba taas zaara’ gides.
“Keeththa ayssiza addezi ba woznara ‘Ta goday tana ta alafetethafe gooddana gees; goya maanas taas wolqay baawa; woossanas yeellatays; hessa gidida gish ay ooththoo?’ giidi,
tani alafetethafe kezikko asay tana mokki ekkana mala ooththana oge ta erays.
“Hessa gish iza goda accoy ista bolla diza asata issa issa xeygides. Koyro yidayssa ‘Ne bolla goda acoy aapunee?’ gides.
“ ‘Issi xeetu xaaro kumeththa zaytey ta bolla dees’ gides. Alafezi zaaridi kase ne faramida waraqata heyi ekka uttada elle ichashu tammu xaaro gaada xaafa gides.
“Kaallidi hankoyssa ‘Nech ne bolla aappun dizee?’ gides. ‘Xeetu ogoro gistey dees’ gides. Alafezi zaaridi ‘Kase ne tal7ashe faramida waraqata hey osupun tammu ogoro gaada xaafa’ gides.
“Godazikka shocechiza alafezi ooththida cincateththa gish iza nashshides. Ha alame nayti bana misatizaytara diza gaaggoteththan poo7o naytappe aadhdhida cincata.
“Hessa gish tani intena gizay ha biitta miishay wurida wode merna keeththan inte ekettana mala ha7i intes diza miishara intes lagge medhite gays.
Guutha miishan ammanettizadey daro miishanka ammanettana; guutha miishan ammanettontadey daro miishanka ammanettenna.
Histikko inte ha biitta miishan ammanettonta ixikko tuma miisha hadara oykkite giidi ooni intes immanee?
Asa miishan inte ammanettonta ixikko intes buzo gidana miish ooni immanee?
“Nam7u godas issito issi bolla azazettana dandayizadey oonikka deenna; woykko issa dosidi issa ixees woykko issakko shiiqidi hankoyssa leqqees. Xoossasinne miishas issife gaththi haarettanas dandayekketa” gides.
Miish darsi siiqiza Farsaaweeti hessa wursi siydi Yesusa qidhida.
Yesusikka istas “Inte intena asa achchan xilliseta; gido attin Xoossi inte wozna erees. Asa achchan bonchettidadey Xoossa sinthan tuna” giidi istas yootides.
“Muse wogaynne nabeti Yohannisi yaana gakkanaas yootishe gam7ida. Hessa kaallidi qasse Xoossa Kawoteththa Mishiraachcho qaalay sabakettides. Asi wurikka hee gelanas wadhettes.
Gido attin Muse wogappe issi qeerina kunda attanayssafe saloynne sa7ay aadhdhanayssi kawushsha gidana.
“Ba macho anji yeddidi hara macho ekkiza asi wurikka laymattes; ba azinappe anjetta bidaro ekkidayssikka laymattes.
“Qasseka Yesusi istas ‘Lo7o may7o may7idi gallas gallas lo7o duussa ufayssan diza issi dure asi dees’ gides.
He addeza pengen kumeththa bollay madunth xalla gidida issi Alazaare geetettiza manqo adde dizayssi ichchidi dees.
Izikka he dure addeza keeththan asay kath mishin maaddafe gaden wodhdhiza suupa maxi maanas amottes. Kanatikka iza maduntha laacettes.
“Ha manqo addezi hayqqin Salo Kiitanchati Abrahaame ki7o ekki bida; qasse dure addezikka hayqqidi moogettides.
Izi Si7oolen waayettishe dhoqu giidi haahon Abrahaame xeellides; Alazaarekka ba ki7on oykki dishin beydes.
“Dure addezi ‘Aawa Abrahaame! Hayssan waayettiza taas michettarkii! Gi Alazaarey ba biradhe xeera irxa haaththan bochchidi ta inxars irxisana mala ha yeddarki!’ giidi waassides.
“Gido attin Abrahaamey ‘Ta naazo neni biitta bolla dashe lo7o duus de7idayssa mala Alazaarey kase waaye beyidayssa ne qoppa; gido attin ha7i izi ufayettishin neni waayetasa’ gides.
Hessi wuri hanishin haan diza asi haappe hee inteko aadhdhonta mala qasseka intekon dizay haa nuukko aadhdhana koyizadey haa aadhdhonta mala intessinne nuus giddon gita aafoy giigettides gides.
“Dure addezi qasse ‘Aabo! Hessi hessa gidikko neni Alazaare duge ta aawaso yeddana mala ta nena woossays; taas ichashu ishati deettes; hayti hayssa ha waayeso yoonta mala biidi istas lo7ethi yootana mala Alazaare yeddarkii?’ gides.
<range>
“Abrahaamey izas zaaridi ‘Museynne nabeti heen ista achchan diza gish istafe siyeto’ gides.
“Izikka zaaridi ‘Aawa Abrahaame hessa mala gidenna; hayqida asappe issidey hayqoppe dendi biikko isti Xoossa maarotethan gelana’ gides.
“Abrahaameyka zaaridi ‘Museynne nabeti gizayssa siyonta ixikko hayqqida asappe issadey dendidakkokka isti amanettenna’ ” gides.
Yesusi bana kaallizayta “Asa dhuphidi nagaran yeggiza miishi yoonta aggenna; gido attin yaana dhuphezas gaaso gidizaddes aayye-ana!
He addezi ha guuthatappe issas dhuphe gidanappe woxa shuchchi iza qoodhen qashetin abba gido izi yegetizakko izas lo7o gidana.
Hessa gish inte hu7es naagetite. ‘Ne ishay nena qohikko hanqeta; izi ba mooro eridi simmikko maara.’
Issi gallassan laapunto zaari zaari qohidi laapun tokka zaari zaari ‘Maara giikko maara’ ” gides.
Hawaaretikka “Godo! Nuus ammano gujja” gida.
Godaykka “Gaashe ayfe lagge ammanoy intes diikko hayssa ‘Eththa dhoqalleta baada abban gela tokketa’ inte giikko izi intes azazettana” gides.
Qasseka Yesusi “Inte giddofe issi asas goshshanchay woykko dorsa heemiza ashkaray diikko izi goshshasoppe simmishin ‘Taas maana kawo giigissa; ta maada uyana gakkanaas gixetada taas ooththa; hessafe guye baggan maandassanne uyandassa’ gees attin ha7i quma maana ha aadhdha gizee?
<range>
Histikko he ashkara goday izi iza azazo polida gish iza galati erizee?
Hessa gish intenikka inte azazettidayssa wursi polida wode ‘Nuni go7ay baynda oosanchata nuus ooththanas bessizayssa poli ooththidos’ gite” gides.
Hessafe guye Yesusi Yerusalame bishe Samaariyaranne Galila achchara aadhdhides.
Issi guta gelida wode inchiracha hargiza tammu asati iza demmida. Istika haahon eqqidi;
ba qaala dhoqu histidi “Yesusa! Godo! Nuus mishetarki!” gida.
Izikka ista beyidi “Biite! Intena Qeesetas bessite” gides. Istika buro bishe oge bolla paxida.
Istafe issoy ba paxidayssa beyidi ba qaala dhoqu histidi Xoossa bonchishe simmides.
Izaadeyka Yesusa toho bolla kundidi galattides; izikka Samaariya biitta asa.
Yesusikka addeza “Paxidayti tamm as deettenee? Histin uddufunati awa bidoo?
Hayssa dumma dere addezappe attin Xoossa galatizay baawa guussee?” giidi oychides.
Addezakka zaaridi “Dendada ba! Nena ne ammanoy pathides” gides.
“Xoossa Kawotethi ayde yaanee?” giidi Farsaaweeti Yesusa oychida wode Yesusi “Xoossa kawotethi beettiza malatatan yuukku.
Asay Xoossa kawotethi haan dawus woykko heen dawus gaanas dandayettenna; Xoossa kawotethi inte giddon dawus” giidi zaarides.
Bana kaallizaytaska “Asa Naa gallassatappe issi gallassayo beyanas inte amottana wodey yaana; gido attin inte beyekketa.
Asay intes ‘Haan dawus’ woykko ‘Heen dawus’ gaana shin inte ista kaallidi booppite.
Gaasoyka wolqanthi wolqamidi ha gaxappe he gaxa gakkanaas poo7isiza mala Asa Nay yiza gallas iza mala hanana.
Gido attin hayssi wuri hananappe koyro Asa Nay daro meto ekkanasinne hayssa ha yeletethan kadhettanas bessees.
“Nohe wode hanidayssa mala Asa Naa wodenka hessatho hanana.
Nohey markaben gelana gallas gakkanaas asay mishininne uyishin; ekkishininne gelishin dhaysiza haaththi yiidi wursikka dhayssides.
“Looxe wodekka iza mala hanides; asay meessinne uyees; bayizessinne shamees; tokkizaz tokkees; keeththika keexetes.
Gido attin Looxey Soddomeppe kezida gallas shuchinne mith qoronta diine tamay saloppe bukkidi wursi dhayssides.
“Asa Nay qonciza gallas hessatho hanana.
He wode ba keeththa bolla dizaddey oonikka keeththa giddon diza miish ekkana giidi duge wodhdhofo; hessathoka goshsha soon diza asi guye so simmofo.
Looxe macho qoppite.
Ba de7o gam7isana koyizay wuri dhayssana; ba shempo aaththi immizaddey gam7isana.
Ta intes gizay he wode omars nam7u asi issi hiixan ichchana; issoneya ekettana; issoy attana.
Nam7u macasati issife gaaccishin issineya ekettana; hankoora attana.
Nam7u asi issife goshshason daana; issoy ekettana; issoy attana.
“Istika zaaridi ‘Godo! Isti awa ekettanee?’ gida. Izikka ahay dizason ankoti shiiqana” gides.
Bana kaallizayti azallonta ubba wode woossanas bessizaysa erisanas Yesusi ha leemisoza istas yootides.
“Issi kataman Xoossas yayonta asinne bonchonta issi daannay dees.
He katamanka issi am7e macassi dawus. Izakka “Ta balgarara taas mootoy diza gish pirdarkii?” gashe izakko simeretadus.
Daannazikka daro wode gakkanaas izis pirdibenna; gido attin guyeppe ba woznan “Xoossas yayonta asekka bonchonta aggikko,
hanna am7e macasaya tana waayssiza gish ta izis pirdana Hessa histonta aggikko ubba wode simeretada iza tana daabbursana” gides.
“Godayka “Makalancha daannay gidayssa siyite;
Xoossi qamma, gallasinne omars izakko waassiza doorettidaytas pirdeneyee? Tana ay metide! giidi ba maado gam7issandee?
Ta intes gays; istas elle pirdana; gido attin Asa Nay yiza wode biitta bolla ammano demmandeshaa?” gides.
Bana xillo asa mala qoodidi ceeqettizaytassinne harata leqo ayfen xeellizaytas leemisora,
“Nam7u asati woossanas Xoossa Keeththe bida; issoy Farsaawe, hinkoyssi qaraxa shiishshizade.
Farsaaweezikka eqqidi ba gish ‘Xoosso! Tani hara asa mala bonqizadde, makalizade, laymatizade harappeka hayssa qaraxa shiishshizadde mala gidonta aggida gish ta nena galatays.
Saamintan nam7a xoomays; taas diza tammafe issa immays’ giidi woossides.
“Gido attin qaraxa shiishshizaddezi haahon eqqidi pude salo dhoqu giidi xeellanas koybenna; gido attin ba tira iccishe ‘Xoosso! Tana nagaranchaza maararki!’ gides.
“Ta intes yootays; Xoossa sinthan Farsaawezi xillotethi demmibenna shin hayssi qaraxizayssi xillidi baso simmides. Bana dhoqusizay wuri ziqqi gaana; bana ziqqisizay gidikko dhoqu gaana” gides.
Yesusi bosherethana mala asay guutha nayta izakko ehides. Iza kaallizaytikka hessa beyidi hanqettida.
Gido attin Yesusi guutha nayta baako xeygidi “Guutha nayti taakko yaanayssa diggofte; Xoossa kawotethi haytanta malatassa.
Ta intes tumu gays; Xoossa kawotethi guutha naa mala ekkontay wuri izin gelenna” gides.
Ayhudata halaqatappe issoy “Kiya astamare! Merna de7o laattanas ta ay ooththoo?” giidi oychides.
Yesusikka “Aazas tana kiya gay? Issi Xoossafe attin hara kiyay deenna.
‘Laymatoppa; wodhoppa; kaysotoppa; wordo markattofa; ne aawa boncha’ giza azazozata ne eraasa” gi zaarides.
Addezikka “Hayta gidikko guutha natetethafe doomada naagadis” gides.
Yesusikka hessa siydi “Histikko nees issi miishi paccees; nees dizazi wursa bayizada manqotas imma; salo mazgaban demmandasa; izappe guye yaada tana kaalla” gides.
Gido attin addezi hessa siyida wode daro haaroy izas diza gish keehi mishettides.
Yesusikka addeza xeelidi “Daro miishi diza asati Xoossa kawotethi gelanayssi ay mala meto!
Durey Xoossa kawoteth gelanayssafe Gaammelay narpe lukkora aadhdhanayssi matana” gides.
Hessa siyida asay “Histin ooni attana dandayizee?” gides.
Yesusikka asa achchan dandayetontay Xoossa achchan dandayettes gides.
Phexroosikka “Hekko nuni nuus dizaz ubba aggidi nena kaallidos” gides.
Yesusikka istas “Ta intes tumu gays; Xoossa Kawoteththa gish giidi ba keeththe, ba macho, ba ishanta woykko bana yelidayta woykko ba nayta aggidadey,
ha7i wode daro dakko kushe ekkontaynne yiza wode qasse merna de7o ekkontay oonikka deenna” gides.
Yesusikka bana kaalliza tammanne nam7ata dumma efidi “Ha7i nuni Yerusalame kezana goos; nabeti asa naa gish xaafidayssi wuri polettana.
Dere asas aaththi immana; istika iza qidhi ka7ananne waayssana; iza bolla cuttana.
garafana; hessafekka zaaridi wodhana; Izikka heedzdzantho gallas hayqoppe dendana” gides.
Iza kaallizayti gidikko hessa ubbafe issinoka eribeyttenna. Iza gizayssikka istas gelibenna. Izi aaza gish haasayidakkonne eribeyttenna.
Yesusi Iyarko geetettizaso matida wode issi qooqe addey oge duunan uttidi woosses.
He qooqe addezikka daro asay ogera aadhdhizayssa siydi “Hessi aazee?” gi oychides.
Istika izas “Naazirete Yesusi hayssara aadhdhees” giidi yootida.
Izikka “Dawute naa Yesusa taas qadheta” gi waassides.
Yesusappe sintheti bizayti “Co7u ga!” giidi hanqettida. Gido attin izi “Dawute nawu! Taas qadheta” giidi darsi waassides.
Yesusikka eqqidi addeza izakko ehanna mala azazides; izikka izakko shiiqida wode
“Ta nees ay ooththana mala koyay?” giidi oychides. Qooqezikka “Godo xeellanas koyays” gides.
Yesusikka “Nena ne ammanoy pathides xeella” gides.
Addezi heerakka xeellides; Xoossakka bonchishe Yesusa kaallides. Hessa beyida derey wuri Xoossa galattides.
Yesusi Iyarko geetettizasora aadhdhi bishin,
Zekkiyoosa geetettiza issi asi heen Yesusi biza oge bolla dees. Izikka dere qaraxa qanxisizaytas halaqanne keehi dure asa.
Izi Yesusa geetettizayssi awayssakkonne beyanas koyishin qaantha asa gidida gishshinne daro derey Yesusa kaalliza gish Yesusa beyanas dandaybenna.
Yesusi he ogera aadhdhishin sinthe aadhdhidi oge bolla diza issi eththa mitha bolla kezides.
Yesusi eththa gars gakkidi dhoqu histi xeelidi “Zekkiyoosa! Hach ta ne keeththan pe7anas bessees. Elela wodhdha” gides.
Izikka elle wodhdhidi ufayssan mokki ekkides.
He wode heen izara diza asay hessa beyidi “Nagarancha asa keeththan imato maana gees” giidi wurikka ba giddon zuuzumettida.
Gido attin Zekkiyoossi eqqidi “Godo! Tani taas diza miishe ubbafe bagga shaakada manqotas immana; tani oonappekka wordora bonqa ekkidazi diikko oyddu kushe gujjada izaades immana” gides.
Yesusikka “Ha addezi Abrahaame naa gidida gish hach ha keeththas paxatethi yides” gides.
Hayssas gaasoyka Asa Nay haa yiday dhayidayssa koyanassinne ashshanassa.
Asay hayssa siyishin leemisora haasaya oykkides; gaasoyka izi Yerusalame gakkanaas matida gishshinne asatas Xoossa Kawoteth qoncana haniza misatida gishassa.
Hessa gish “Issi kawo nay ba kawoteththa shuumeteth ekki yaanas haaho biitta bides.
Ba ashkarata giddofe tammata xeygidi tammu minane istas immidi ‘Ta simmada yaana gakkanaas hayssa miishan zal7ite’ gides.
“He dere asati qasse iza ixida gish ‘Hayssi addezi nu bolla kawotana mala koyokko’ giidi as iza geedora kiita aaththi yeddida.
“Gido attin ha kawo naazi kawo gididi guye ba dere simmides. Kase bishe tammu minane immida tammu ashkarati izi immida biran zal7idi ay keena tirfisidakkonne eranas ista xeygides.
“Istafe koyroy shiiqidi ‘Godo! Ne taas immida tammu minaney hara tammu yelides’ gides.
“Godazikka iza ‘Ne ammanettida ashkara; lo7o ooththadasa. Ne guutha miishan amanettida gish tammu katamata ne haarana mala nees immadis’ gides.
“Nam7anthozikka izakko shiiqidi ‘Godo! Ne taas immida minaneppe hara ichashu minaney wodhdhides’ gides.
“Iza godazi izas zaaridi ‘Neni ayssana mala tammu katamati nees imettida’ gides.
“Qasseka hanko oosanchay shiiqidi ‘Godo! Neni woothontasoppe ekkizadde; zerontasoppe maxizadenne menxe iita as gidida gish ta nees babbada curqan xaaxa woththida ne minaneyo hey ekka’ gides.
<range>
“Iza godazi zaaridi izas ‘Haysso iita oosanchazo! Ta ne qaalan nena zaara pirdays. Tani wothontasoppe ekkizaddenne zerontasoppe maxiza menxe iita as gididayssa eraasashin tani ta miisha yelora ekkana mala he miishan ooththana asatas aazas immabeekii?’ gides.
<range>
Iza “Godazikka heen eqqida asata ‘Iza kusheppe minaneza ekkidinne tammu minaney dizayssas immite’ gides.
“Istika zaaridi ‘Godo! Izas tammu minaney deessikko’ gida.
“Izikka zaaridi ‘Dizades ubbas haray gujjettana; bayndades kase dizayssi izappe ekettichana. Gido attin tani ista bolla kawotonta mala koydayta hayta ta morketa taakko haa ehidi ta sinthan shukite’ ” gides.
<range>
Hessa haasayi simmidi Yesusi Yerusalame kezanas istafe sinthati bides.
Dabrazayte geetettiza zuma bolla diza Betefaagenne Bitaaniya geetettiza katamatako matida wode bana kaallizaytappe nam7ata “Heeni inte sinthan diza qeeri katamayo biite; biidi katamayo inte gelishin oonikka togi eronta issi qasheti diza Hare gutte inte demmenna; iza birshidi haa taas ekki yiite; intena oonikka ‘Aazas birshetii?’ giidi oychikko ‘Godas koshshees gite’ ” gi kiittides.
<range>
<range>
Kiitetidaytikka biidi izi istas yootida mala hare gutteza demmida.
Isti gutteza birshin gutteza godati beyidi “Aazas birshettii?” giidi oychida.
Istika “Godas koshshees” gida.
Hare gutteza Yesusakko ehidi ba may7o wursi gutteza bolla yeggidi Yesusa Hare gutteza togisida.
Asay wurikka ba afala Yesusi biza oge bolla micides.
Dabrazayte zuma bollara duge woththiza ogezakko matida wode qooday baynda derey ba beyida malata gish wurikka ufayssara ba qaala dhoqu histidi “Goda sunthan yiza kawoy anjettidayssa; saroy salon bonchoy saloppe bolla salon gido” gides.
<range>
Deretappe issi issi Farsaaweeti Yesusa “Astamaare! Ha nena kaalliza asay gizayssa goonta mala hanqa” gides.
Izikka istas zaaridi “Hayti co7u gidakkonne shuchchatikka waassana” gides.
Yesusi Yerusalame matishe katamayo beyidi izis yeekkides. “Nees saro gidizaz hachchi ne eridakko aaze dizay? Ha7i ne ayfeppe qotettida gish ne morketi heera haara nena giddoththidi un7ethana wodey yaana.
<range>
<range>
Nenanne ne gibbe giddon nenara diza ne nayta wursi biitta kessana. Shuchchakka shuchcha bollafe laalonta aggettenna. Hessi wurikka Xoossi nena koyishin neni eronta aggida gishassa” gides.
Hessafe kaallidi Yesusi Xoossa Keeththe gelidi Xoossa Keeththa giddon zal7izayta kessides.
Qasseka “Ta keeththay Woosa Keeththa gidana geetettidi xaafettides; inten gidikko pangay diza gongolo histideta” gides.
Wontin wontin Xoossa Keeththan izi tamarisishin Xaafetinne dere halaqati iza wodhanas koyda.
Gido attin derey wurikka izara oyketidi izi tamarsizayssa kaalliza gish ooththanazi istas kirqi gides.
Issi gallas Yesusi asaa Xoossa Keeththan tamarsishinne Mishiraachcho qaala sabakishin Qeese halaqati Xaafetinne dere Cimati shiiqettidi izakko yida.
“Hayssa ne ooththizay oona shenenee? Nees shene immiday oonee?” giidi iza oychida.
Izikka istas “Takka intena issi oysho oychays; ane taas zaarite.
Yohannisa xinqatay saloppeyee? Asappee?” gides.
Istika ba giddon issoy issara “Nu ‘Yohannisa xinqatay saloppe’ giikko izi nuna ‘Histin aazas ammanibeekketii?’ gaana.
‘Asappe’ giikko asay wuri Yohannisi nabe gididayssa ammaniza gish nuna shuchchara caddana” gi zorettida.
Hessa gish “Izi awappekkonne nu erokko” giidi zaarida.
Yesusikka histikko “Takka aaza wolqan ooththizakkonne intes yootikke” gides.
Qasseka Yesusi asaas leemisora “Issadey woyne mith tokkides; gade goyizaytas kira immidinne hara dere biidi heen gam7ides.
Kaxiza bone wode kathafe ekki yaana mala ba ashkaratappe issade gadeza goyda asatakko yeddin gadaa goyizayti kiita bidayssa qoxidi mela kushe yeddida.
Kaalethidikka hara ashkara yeddin goshshanchati ha7ikka oykki qoxidinne kawushshidi mela yeddida.
Ha7ikka kaaleththidi heedzdzantho ashkara yeddin goshshanchati izakka qoxerethi madunthidi gede kare kessi yeggida.
“Woyne mitha goday ‘Ha7i ay ooththoo? Oone erizay ta keeha siiqiza ta naaza yeddidakko iza bonchandettoshaa?’ gides.
“Gido attin biitta goyizayti naaza beyida mala ba giddon ‘Hayssi iza laattana naaza gidennee? Haa yiite iza wodhidi biitta laattoos’ giidi zoretida.
Woyine mitha tokkidasoppe gede kare kessidi naaza wodhida. Histikko ha7i woyne mitha goday ha asata wostanee?
Yiidinne he goshshanchata dhayssana; woyne mitha tokkizasoza haratas immana” gides. Dereyka hessa izi gidayssa siydi “Hayssa malay hanoppo” gides.
Yesusikka “Istako xeelidi ‘Histin shuchchan keeththe keexiza asati leqqi aggida shuchchay keeththas waanna hu7e gidana” geetettidi xaafettida leemisozas birsheththay aazee?’ gides.
Ha shuchcha bolla kundiday wuri shuchchan qoxettana; shuchchaykka iza bolla wodhdhidadey wurikka liiqana” gides.
Xaafetinne Qeeseta halaqati hessi leemisozi ista bolla haasayettidayssa eridi heerakka iza oykkanas koyda shin derezas babbida.
Yesusa wolqara haarizaytas aaththi immanas iza duunappe keziza bala qaala demmidi oykkanas kaalli kaalli naagidanne xillo asa misatidi iza kaalli iza duunappe yo7o naagiza asata izakko yeddida.
Iza duunappe yo7o koyiza asati Yesusa “Astamare! Neni tuma haasayizayssanne tuma tamarsizayssa qasseka Xoossa oge ne tumu tamarsizayssanne oonakka shaaka maadontayssa nu eroos.
Gido attin Qeesares giira giiranas bessizee? Bessennee?” giidi oychida.
Izikka istas diza gene qofa eridi,
“Ane issi dinare tana bessite, hayssi iza bolla diza medhazinne Xaafetoyssi oonayssee?” gides. Istika “Qeesareyssa” gida.
Izikka zaaridi istas “Qeesareyssa Qeesares, Xoossayssa Xoossas immite” gides.
Hessa gish izi haasayida qaalappe ekkidi asa sinthan iza qaxanas dandaybeetenna; izi immida qaalan malalettidi co7u gida.
Hayqqidayta denthi baawa giza Saduqaawetappe issi issi asati Yesusakko yiidi oysho shiishida.
“Godo! ‘Issadey macho ekkidi naa yelonta hayqqikko he hayqqidayssa macheyo iza ishay ekkidi ba isha laattana naa izas yelo’ giidi Musey nuus xaafides.
Histin laapun ishati deettes shin istafe bayray machidi naa yelonta hayqqides.
Iza kaalozikka izatho hayqqides;
heedzdzanthozikka izo ekkidees; laapunati wurikka he macasayo ekkidi wurikka naa yelonta hayqqida.
Wursethan macasaya hayqqadus.
Laapunatikka ha macasayo ekkida shin ha macasaya wursethan hayqqidayti dendiza wode iza awayssa macho gidanee?”
Yesusi istas “Ha dere nayti geleettessinne ekkettes.
Buro yaana alamen hayqqidayta dentha demmanas bessizayti gidikko gelettenanne ekkettenna.
Isti Kiitanchata mala gidana gish hessafe guye hayqqettenanne hayqoppe dentha nayta gidida gish isti Xoossa nayta.
Musey qeeri wora gish xaafettida taarikezan Goda ‘Abrahaame Xoossa, Yisaaqa Xoossa Yaqoobe Xoossa’ guussan hayqqidayti dendanayssa bessees.
Wurikka izas de7oy diza gish izi paxata Xoossafe attin hayqqethata Xoosse gidenna” gides.
Issi issi xaafeti “Astamare! Lo7o gadasa” gida.
Hessafe guye ay asikka iza oychanas xaalibeenna.
Hessafe guye Yesusi “Asay Masihe waanidi izi Dawute naa gizee?
Gaasoyka Dawutey ba xaafida mazamure maxaafatan ‘Ta ne morketa ne toho gars aaththana gakkanaas Goday ta Goda ne ta ushachan utta’ waanidi gidee?
<range>
Histikko Dawutey iza ‘Goda’ gi xeygishe waani izas naa gidanee?” gides.
Derey wuri siyishin bana kaallizaytas
“Gooshettiza aduussa qamse may7idi yuushshe dosizaytappenne giyay dizason saroketeth koyizaytappenne Ayhuda Woosa Keeththan dhoqa oydenne diggisason bonchoso koyizaytappe xaafetappe naagettite.
Haytanti am7eta keeththa kallosizayta. Asi ista beyana mala woossa aduussetes; heytanta iita pirday naages” gides.
Yesusi dhoqu gi xeellishin dure asati Xoossa Keeththen muxuwata izan shiishshizayssa giddon muxuwata yeggishin beydes.
Qasseka issi am7o dizaara nam7u sikina gidiza nam7u xarqimala he muxuwata izan shiishshizayssan yegishin xeelidi,
“Ta intes tumu gays; hanna am7eya ubba asappe bollara aadhdheth immadus gides.
Hayti asati immiday baas diza tirpafe gidishin iza gidikko baas baynda wolqafe baas dizaronne ba duussas koshshizaro wursa yeggadus” gides.
Iza kaallizaytappe issi issi asati Xoossa Keeththay lo7o shuchchaninne asay immida imotan ay mala lo7i keexettidakko giidi ba giddon haasayettishin Yesusi siydi “Hayssi inte beyizayssi wuri laalettonta shuchchi shuchcha bolla keelettida mala attonta wodey yaana” gides.
<range>
Istika iza “Astamaare! Hayssi wuri ayde hananee? Qasse hayssi hananayssas malatay aazee?” giidi oychida.
Izikka istas “Inte balettonta mala naagettite; daroti bana ‘Ta Kirstoosakko! Wodeykka matides’ gishe ta sunthara yaana shin inte ista kaallofte.
Ola gishshinne dere makalatetha gish siyiza wode daggamofte. Hessi wuri kasetidi hananas bessees; wursethi gakkides; gido attin heerakka hanenna” gides.
Qasse “Derey dere bolla, kawoy kawo bolla dendana.
Biittay wolqama qaath qaaxana; koshaynne boshay dumma dummason hanana; daro babissizazinne saloppe gita malatay beettanna.
“Hessi wuri hananappe kasetidi asay intena oykkananne gooddana; Ayhuda Woosa Keeththinne qasho keeththe gelthana; kawota sinthinne daannata sinth shiishana. Hessi wuri ta suntha gish inte bolla gakkana.
Hessi wurikka markattanas lo7o qaada gidana.
Hessa gish nuna oychizaytas nu ay zaarinoo? giidi kasetidi hirgonta mala hayssa woznan woththite.
Inte morketappe oonikka intenara eqettanassinne baleththanas dandayonta qaalanne cincateth ta intes immana.
Intena yelidaytinne inte ishati, inte dabbotinne inte laggeti wuri intena aaththi immana; intefe baggata wodhana.
Ta suntha gish ubba asa achchan inte ixettana.
Gido attin inte hu7e binanatappe issinaka dhayukku.
Inte minni eqqikko inte shempo inte ashshana.
“Ola asay Yerusalame giddoththishin beykko izis dhayiza wodey matidayssa erite.
He wode Yuhudan dizayti pude zuma bolla gangetto; kataman dizaytikka katamappe kezite; dere giddon dizaytikka he katamayo geloppetto.
Xaafettidays wuri polettanas hanna halo kessiza wode.
Biitta bolla gita metoy hanana; hayssa dereza bolla hanqoy yaana; hessa gish he wode qanthara diza macasatassinne dhanthiza aayetas aayye ana!
Bagga asay mashshan hayqqana; ba dereppe hara dere di7ettana; Yerusalameykka Xoosse eronta dereta wodey polettana gakkanaas, Xoosse eronta asatan yedhetidaro gidana.
“Awa arshe bolla, agina bollanne xoolinte bolla malatay beettana; Abbafenne abba dambala giirissafe dendidayssan biitta bolla diza derey hirgananne metottettana.
Salo wolqamati qaaxiza gish asay biitta bolla aaze hananesha guussaninne naagon xalla daaburana.
He wode Asa Nay wolqara, gita bonchoranne shaarara yishin beyana.
Inteka hayti ha ta gidayti poleteth oykkishin intes atetha wodey matida gish siti gi eqqite; inte ayfe pude dhoqu histite” gides.
Kaalethidi “Balase mithinne hara mithata wursi xeellite; he mithati haythe kessishin inte beyiza wode boney matidayssa inte ereeta.
<range>
Hessathokka haytanti geetettidayti polettishin inte beyiza wode Xoossa Kawotethi inteko matidayssa erite.
“Ta intes tumu gays; hayssi wuri polettana gakkanaas ha yelettay aadhdhenna.
Saloynne sa7ay aadhdhana shin ta qaalay aadhdhenna.
“Histikko wogay baynda duussan, daro ushshaninne duussas hirgan inte woznay daaburopo; hessa ooththonta ixikko he gallassay inte qopponta narxa mala inte bolla gakkonta mala naagettite.
Hayssi biitta bollan diza asa ubba bolla gakkana.
Hessa gish buro yaanayssafe inte kessi ekkana malanne Asa Naa sinthan eqqanas dandayana mala ubba gallas minnidi woossite” gides.
Yesusi gallas gallas Xoossa Keeththan tamarsi tamarsidi omars omars Dabrazayte geetettiza zuma bolla kezi kezi aqqees.
Asay wurikka izappe siyanas maalado wontara Yesusakko Xoossa Keeththe yees.
He wode Paaziga geetettiza ukethara bonchettiza ba7aaley mati uttides.
Qeeseta halaqatinne Xaafeti hanko dere asaas babbiza gish Yesusa dhayssana oge koyda.
Yesusa kaalliza tammanne nam7atappe Asqoroonto dere asa Yuhuda geetettizayssan Xala7ey gelides.
Yuhudaykka Qeeseta halaqatakkonne Xoossa Keeththa alafetakko biidi istas Yesusa wost aaththi immanakkonne istara haasayettides.
Istika hessan ufayettidi miishe immanas izara giigida.
Yuhudaykka ista qofa dossides; Yesusa istas asi beyonta aaththi immanas inje wode naagishin Paaziga dorsa shukidi ukethara bonchiza ba7aale gallas gakkides.
<range>
Yesusikka bana kaallizayta “Paaziga kawo maanas biidi nuus giigissite” giidi Phexroosanne Yohannisa kiittides.
Istika “Nu awan giigissana mala koyay?” gida.
Izikka zaaridi “Inte gede Yerusalame katama gelishin haaththa oto tookkida asi intena demmenna; inteka izi biidi geliza keeththe gakkanaas iza kaallite.
Keeththadezas ‘Astamarey tana kaallizaytara Paaziga kawo maanas imatha keeththi awan dizee?’ gees giite.
Izikka imathas giigettida aahoso intena bessana; izi bessiza soon giigissite” gides.
Istika biidi Yesusi gida mala keeththa demmidi Paaziga heen giigissida.
Wodey gakkida mala Yesusi Hawaaretara quma maaddan uttidi “Ta waaye beyanappe kasetada hayssa Paaziga intenara issife maanas keehi amottadis.
<range>
Ta intes tumu gays; Xoossa Kawoteththan hayssa birsheththi polettana gakkanaas hayssa Paaziga nam7antho ta intenara miikke” gides.
Woyneppe oosettida ushsha xu7ara ekkidinne Xoossa galati simmidi “Heyte; wurikka izappe uyte” giidi istas immides.
“Ta intes tumu gays; hayssafe guye Xoossa Kawotethi yaana gakkanaas nam7antho ha woyne ushshafe uyikke” gides.
Uketha ekkidi Xoossa galatides. Izappe istas menthi immidi “Hayssi inte gish imettana ta asho leemiso gidiza gish hayssa ubba wode tana qoppanas ooththite” gides.
Izathoka kawoppe guye ushsha xu7a denthidi “Hayssi ushshay inte gish ta suuthan hanana oorath caaqo woga.
“Gido attin tana aaththi immanade kushey ta kushera issife maaddan dees.
Asa Nay kasetidi iza gish hananayssi wuri uttida mala izi baana; gido attin iza aaththi immizades aayye-ana” gides.
Istika hessa ooththanay oonee? giidi ba giddon issoy issa oysherethida.
Qasseka “Ooni oonappe aadhdhizakkonne” giidi ba giddon issoy issara palamettida.
Yesusikka ista “Dere haariza kawoti ba dere asa wolqara haarettessinne istika lo7o kawota geetettidi xeygettetes.
“Inte gidikko hessatho hanoppite; intefe gita gididadey woykko ta ooppekka aadhdhays giza asi ubbafe qeeri naa mala gido; haarizaddey haarettizade mala gido.
Quma eqqidi mizidadefenne uttidi mizadefe ooni aadhdhizee? Uttidi mizade gidennee? Tani qasse inte giddon ashkara mala days.
“Inten gidikko taappe shaaketonta ta waayishin ta matan eqqidayta.
Ta Aaway tana kawothidayssa mala tanikka ta kawoteththan intena kawoththana.
Hessika ta kawoteththan ta maaddafe inte maana malanne uyana mala. Qasseka ta kawoteththa algan uttidi tammanne nam7u Isra7eele nayta bolla pirdanassa” gides.
Qasseka Yesusi Simoona xeygidi “Simoona! Xala7ey intena giste mala suraganas woossides.
Gido attin tani neeppe ammanoy dhayonta mala ne gish Xoossa woossadis; nekka simmida wode ne ishata minthetha” gides.
Simoonikka zaaridi “Godo! Ta nenara qashettanassinne hayqqanas giiga uttadis” gides.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Phexroosa hach kuttoy issito waassanas ‘Ta iza erikke’ gaada heedzdzuto ne tana kaadana” gides.
Qasseka Yesusi ista “Ta intena kase caammay, korojoynne qaraxite baynda kiittida wode intes aazi paccidee?” giidi oychides. Istika “Aykkoykka paccibenna” gida.
Izikka zaaridi “Ha7i gidikko korojokka qaraxiteyka dizadey oykko; giththa mashshay bayndadey ba may7o bayzidi shamo.
Ta intes tuma gays ‘Makalatara izi issife taybettides’ geetetti kase xaafettida qaalay ta bolla polettana bessees; ta gish xaafettidayssas poloy tumappe gakkides” gides.
Iza kaallizayti qasse “Godo! Hekko nam7u giththa mashshati hayssan deettes” gida. Izikka iza gish “Hayssi gidana” gides.
Kase izas lose gidida mala pude Dabrazayte geetettiza zuma bolla kezi bides. Iza kaallizaytikka iza kaalli bida.
Hee gakkida mala “Inte paacen gelonta mala woossite” gides.
Yesusi bana kaallizaytappe asi shuch olidi gaththanaso mala haakki biidi gulbati woossides.
“Ta Aawawu! Ne shene gidikko hanno metoyo taappe digga; gido attin ne sheney hanoppe attin ta sheney hanoppo” giidi woossides.
Saloppe Kiitanchay qoncidi Yesusa minthethides.
Izikka keehi xuugettidi woossishin iza asatethafe caway suutha mala gukkides.
Woosappe dendidi bana kaallizaytakko bides. Istika izas mishetidi qoppishin dhiskoy efidashe Yesusi istako yiidi,
“Ays dhisikeetii? Inte paacen gelonta mala ha7i dendidi woossite” gides.
Izi buro haasayan dishin Yesusa kaallizaytappe issoy Yuhuda geetettizayssi banara daro asa kaalethi ekki yiidi Yesusa yeeranas izakko shiiqides.
Gido attin Yesusi iza “Yuhuda! Tana Asa Naa yeeron aaththa immay?” gides.
Yesusa yuuyi aadhdhi diza asay hanoza lo7ethi xeelidi “Godo! Haytanta mashshara buththinoo?” gida.
Istafe issoy Qeeseta alafe ashkara ushacha haythe mashshara qanxides.
Yesusi ista “Inte ha7i taas aggite!” giidi ashkara haytha bochchidi pathides.
Qasseka iza oykkana yida Qeeseta halaqata Xoossa Keeththa alafetanne cimata “Panga oykkiza asa mala giththa mashshanne durqa ekkidi yidetii?
Gallas gallas ta intenara Xoossa Keeththan dishin ta bolla kushe woththibeekketa; hayssi dhumay kawotida inte wode” gides.
Hessafe guye Yesusa oykki ekkidi Qeeseta halaqaso gelida; Phexroosikka Yesusa hahora kaallides.
Asay Qeeseta halaqa gaathan tama eethidi ho7ishe issi bolla uttidashe Phexroosikka istara issife uttides.
Issi garadeya Phexroosi tama ho7izaytara uttidayssa beyadanne tishshi ooththa xeellada “Hayssi addezikka Yesusara dees!” gadus.
Phexroosikka “Hanne macasaye! Ta iza erikke” giidi kadides.
Guuth gam7ishin hara issadey iza beyidi “Nekka izara dizaytappe issa gidikii?” gides. Phexroosikka “Haysso tani istara diikke!” gides.
Issi saate mala gam7ishin hara asi qasseka “Galila as gidiza gish sidhey baynda hayssi izara dees” gides.
Phexroosikka qasse “Haysso ne gizadde ta erikke!” gides. Hinno gi kessonta dishin kuttoy waassides.
Godayka Phexroosakko yishe xeellin Phexroosi “Hach kuttoy waassanas ne tana heedzdzuto kaadana” giidi Goday kase yooto qaalay iza woznan karp gides.
Phexroosikka kare kezidi hiqqimidi yeekkides.
Yesusa qachchidi naagiza asatikka iza bolla qidhi qidhi kaa7ishe shocerethida.
Iza ayfe goozidi “Ne nabe gidikko nena shociday oonakkone ane era!” giidi oychida.
Hara daro cashsha qaalara kawushshida.
Gadey wontin dere Cimati, Qeeseta halaqatinne Muse woga tamarsizayti duulata shiiqidi Yesusa duulatakko shiishida.
Istika Yesusa “Ne Kirstoosee? Ane nuus yoota” gida. Yesusikka “Ta intes yootidakkokka tana ammanekketa.
Ta intena oychidakko taas zaarekketa.
Gido attin ha7ippe doommidi Asa Nay wolqama Xoossa ushachan uttana” gides.
He wode wurikka “Histin ne Xoossa Naa?” giidi oychida. Izikka “Ta Xoossa Naa gididayssa inteka geeta” gides.
Istika “Hekko izi ba duunara markatishin nu haythara siydos; hayssafe hara marka aazas koshshizee?” gida.
Heen shiiqida asay wuri dendidi Yesusa Philaxoosakko ekki bides.
“Ays nu asay Qeesares giira giironta mala baleththishenne bana ‘Tani Kirstoosi kawo’ giidi baleththishin hayssa addeza demmidos” giidi mootida.
Philaxoosikka Yesusa “Neni Ayhudata kawoo?” giidi oychides. Yesusikka zaaridi “Ne gida mala” gides.
Philaxoosikka Qeeseta halaqatassinne shiiqida asas “Hayssa addeza bolla iza mootisiza iita yo7o demmabekke” gides.
Isti zaaridi “Hayssi addezi Galilappe hayssa gakkanaas kumeththa Yuhuda waayiso bolla dees” giidi minthi yootida.
Philaxoosi asay gizayssa siydi “Yesusi Galila asakkone giidi lo7ethi eranas” oychides.
Yesusi Herdoosa Kawoteththa giddon dizayssa shaakki eridi he wode Herdoossi Yerusalamen diza gish izakko Yesusa yeddides.
Herdoossika kase Yesusa beyanas daro koyishe diza gish Yesusa beyidi keehi ufaydes. Iza gish kase siydi izi ooththishin beyanas koydi ufayettides.
Daro oyshataka iza oysherechides shin Yesusi iza oysha zaaribenna.
Qeese halaqatinne Xaafeti heen iza matan eqqidi keehi wordo mooto mootida.
Herdoosikka ba wotadaratara issife iza kadhida; kawo may7o mayzidi gede Philaxoosakko zaari yeddides.
Herdoossinne Philaxoosi kase ba giddon issoy issara oosha shin he gallas giigida.
Philaxoosi Qeeseta halaqatara, dere daannataranne dere asa shiishshidi,
“Hayssi addezi asay wuri makalana mala dentheththes giidi inte taakko ehin ta qorn iza oythiza issi iita miishikka demmabekke.
Qasseka Herdoossi issi iita miishikka iza bolla demmonta aggida gish ha nuukko zaari yeddides. Ha7i inte beyiza mala iza hayqos gaththiza issi iita miishikka ooththibenna.
Hessa gish qaxayada ta iza yeddana” gides.
Izi hessa giday ista ba7aale gallas qashettida asappe issade birshiza wogay diza gishassa.
Derey wurikka issi bolla “Barbaane birshada hayssa addeza digga!” giidi waassides.
Barbaaney katama giddon asa makala yo7on dentheththidi as wodhi qashettida asa.
Philaxoosikka Yesusa birshanas koyda gish qasseka zaaridi oychides.
Asay zaaridi iza “Kaqqa! Kaqqa!” giidi waassides.
Philaxoosi heedzdzanthokka “Aazas kaqqoo? Hayssi addezi ay iita ooththidee? Tani iza hayqos gaththiza iita ooso iza bolla beyabeekke; hessa gish qaxayada ta iza birsha yeddana” gides.
Asaykka qaala dhoqu histidi Yesusi kaqqettana mala Philaxoosa keehi woossishe waassida.
Hessa gish Philaxoosi ista oyshoy polettana mala azazides.
Asa makalisidi shempo wodhdhida gish qashettidayssa birshana mala isti woossidade birshidi qasseka Yesusa isti dossida mala ooththeto giidi deraas aaththi immides.
Istika Yesusa oykkidi ekki bishin Qareena geetettiza katamappe issi Simoona geetettiza addey hahoppe yizayssa demmida Yesusi kaqqettana masqale koca izi tookkidi Yesusa kaallana mala wolqathida.
Daro derey ba tira icci icci yeekkiza macasati,
Yesusappe guyera iza kaallida. Yesusi istako simmi xeelidi “Inte Yerusalame macasay intessinne inte naytas yeekkite attin taas yeekkofte.
‘Sinthafe inte hekko makkara gidida macasati, yelonta ulotinne nay dhammonta dhanthati anjettidayta!’ gaana wodey sinthara yees.
He wode asay ‘Zumato! Nu bolla woddite; qeeri zumatikka nuna qottite!’ gaana.
Histin qaye mitha bolla hayssatho ooththidayti mela mitha bolla wostaneshaa?” gides.
Izara issife hayqqana mala hara nam7u iita ooththida asata izara efida.
Qaaraaniyo geetettizaso gaththidi kaqqida. Iita ooththidaytappe issa ushacha baggara issa hadirsa baggara kaqqida.
Yesusikka “Ta Aawawu! Hayti ba ooththizayssa eridi ooththonta gish istas atto ga!” gides. Istika iza may7oza saama yeggidi ba giddon gishetti ekkida.
Hessi hanishin asay wuri eqqi xeellides; daannatikka “Izi hara asa ashshides shin Xoossafe doorettida Kirstoosi iza gidikko ane ha7i bana asho” giidi qidhida.
Wotadaratikka shiiqidi woyneppe aggettida caala ushsha ushshidi iza qidhida.
“Neni Ayhuda kawo gidikkii? Ane ha7i nena ashsha” gida.
Iza hu7eppe bolla baggara masqale koca bolla “Hayssi Ayhudata kawo” giza qaala xaafi qaaphida.
Iita ooththidi kaqqettida asatappe issoy cashsha qaala Yesusa bolla qoqofides. “Ne Kirstoosa gidikii? Ane nenakka nunakka ashsha” gides.
Iita oosidaytappe issoy “Neni nees bessiza pirda ekkashe Xoossas babbikkii?
Nuni nu ooththida iita oosos bessizayssa ekkoos; hayssi addezi gidikko issi iitakka ooththibenna” gides.
Yesusa “Neni ne kawoteththara yiza wode tana qoppa!” gides.
Yesusikka zaaridi “Ta nees tumu gays; hach ne tanara Gannaten daana” gides.
Hessa wode gadey seeta gallas shin biidi uddufun saate gakkanaas kumeththa biitta bolla dhumay dhumides.
Awa arshe poo7oy diggettides. Xoossa Keeththa magalashaykka dakkettidi nam7u kezides.
Yesusikka keehi waassidi “Ta aawawu! Tani ta shempo ne kushen immays” gida mala shempo kezides.
Mato halaqay hessa beyidi “Hayssi addezi tumappe xillo asakkoshin” giidi Xoossa galatides.
Hessa beyanas heen shiiqidi derey wuri he hanidayssa beyidi tira icci icidi simmides.
Gido attin Yesusa kase lo7ethi erizayti wuri qasseka Galilappera iza kaalliza macasati hessa xeellishe haakki eqqida.
Ayhudata duulata asappe issoy izikka Yoosefe geetettizayssi issi daro kiyanne xillo asa.
Izikka kase asay Yesusa bolla duulatishin he duulatan deenna; izikka issi Armatiyasa geetettiza Ayhudata katama asa shin Xoossa Kawotethi yaanayssa naagishe gam7ides.
Izikka Philaxoosakko biidi Yesusa aha baas immana mala Philaxoosa woossides.
Philaxoosi izas ero gin Yoosefey aha masqale kocappe woththida mala xaaxidi shuchchafe woocettida kase hara asi moogettonta duufon efidi woththides.
He gallassay asay Sambatas giigettiza gallas gidida gish Sambatay gelana hanees.
Galilappe dendidi Yesusara yida macasatikka Yoosefe kaalli biidi duufoza beyida. Yesusa aha wost woththidakkone beyida.
Heeppe simmidi shittonne tiyiza miish giigissida. Wogay giza mala Sambata gallas shempida.
Wogga wonta maaladora macasati ba giigissida shittoza ekkidi Yesusa woththida duufozakko bida.
Shuchchaykka duufoza duunappe genderidi dizayssa beyida.
Gido attin giddo gelidi Yesusa aha demmonta aggida gish,
istas hanzaazi dhayin isti tollu gidashe qopponta xoliqettiza may7o may7ida nam7u asati ista achchan eqqida.
Macasatikka keehi babbidi duge biitta xeellishin “He asati paxidi dendidayssa hayqqethata giddon ays koyetii?
Izi dendides! Haan baawa. Qasseka izi Galilan dishe intes kase ay gidakkonne ane qopite.
Asa Nay nagaranchata kushen aadhdhi imettanassinne kaqettanas, hayqoppeka heedzdzantho gallas dendanas bessees” giidi yooti woththides.
Macasatikka he wode kase izi gida qaala haasayida.
Macasati duufosoppe simmidi hessa wursi Yesusa kaalliza tammanne issinetassinne haratas yootida.
Hessaka Hawaaretas yootiday Magdale gizasoppe yida Maaramonne Yohaano geetettizarira Yaqoobe Maaramonne istara issife diza hara macasata.
Gido attin istas macasati yootidayssi agumo misatin ammanibeetenna.
Gido attin Phexroosi wothan Yesusa duufokko gakkidinne hokkidi duufo giddo xeellishin iza aha xaaxida may7oy xalla dizayssa beyidi keehi malalettishe baso simmides.
He gallas iza kaallizaytappe nam7ati Yerusalameppe tammanne issi kilometire haakkiza Emahoose geetettiza katama beettes.
Bishe isti he wode hanida Yesusa hayqo gish ba giddon haasayetettes.
Isti haasayettishin Yesusi istako shiiqidi istara issife bishin,
isti iza eronta mala ista ayfey oykettides.
Yesusi ista “Hayssi oge hamuttishe inte inte giddon haasayettizayssi aazee?” gides. Istika dagamara modhettishe siti gi eqqagida.
Ista giddofe issoy Qaliyoopha geetettizayssi zaaridi “Ha mata gallassatan Yerusalamen hanidayssa eronta imatha asi nena xallaa?” gides.
Izikka istas zaaridi “Aazi hanidee?” giin isti qasse zaaridi “Xoossa sinthaninne ubba asa sinthan oosoninne qaalan mino nabe gidida Naazirete Yesusa gish” gida.
Izakka Qeeseta halaqatinne daannati hayqo pirdas aaththi immidanne kaqqida.
Nuni gidikko “Isra7eele woznay iza giidi ufayettidosishin harappeka hessi hanin qasse hach heedzdzantho gallassa.
Qasse nu giddofe issi issi macasati nuna keehi malalisida; istika maalado wontara gede iza duufokko biidi,
iza ahay beettonta ixin yiidi izi paxa dizayssa istas yootin Kiitanchata beyidayssa nuus yootida.
Nuupekka issi issi asi iza duufokko biidi macasati gida mala beyida attin Yesusa demmibeetenna” gida.
Izikka istas “Inte woznan wothontayto! Inte woznay kase nabeti yootidayssa ammananappe takkidayto!
Xoossafe kiitettidayssi ha metoza ekkanassinne gede ba bonchoso gelanas bessennee?” gides.
Museppenne nabetappe doommidi Geeshsha Maxaafatan iza gish xaafettidayssa istas lo7eth yootides.
Isti ba bizaso matida wode Yesusi aadhdhi biza misatides.
Istika qasse “Gadey qammiza gish nunara aqa” giidi iza keehi woossin istara aqanas gelides.
Istara issife maaddan uttidi uketh ba kushen oykkidi istas menthi menthi immides.
Hessa wode ista ayfey doyettin iza gididayssa erida; izikka ista ayfeppe geemides.
Istika “Nu yishe oge bolla dishin nuna haasayisidi Geeshsha Maxaafataka qoncisidi nuus gelanashe yootin nu woznay tama mala xuugettibenee?” giidi issoy issara haasayettida
Heerakka dendidi Yerusalame simmi bida. Tammanne issinetinne istara issife dizaytikka issi bolla shiiqi dizayta demmida.
Istika ba giddon issoy issas “Goday tumu dendides! Simoonaska beettides” gida.
Iza kaallizaytappe nam7ati oge bolla hanidayssanne Yesusi uketha menthi menthi immida wode isti wost eridakko istas yootida.
Hessa gish isti ba giddon haasayettishin Yesusi ista giddon eqqidi “Saroy intes gido!” gides.
Gido attin isti moytile beyida misatin keehi daggamida.
Izikka istas “Aazas daro qoppetii? Aazas inte woznara sidheetii?
Ta kushetanne ta tohota haa xeellite tanakko; qasseka tana oykki beyite; tana inte beyizayssa mala moytiles ashoynne meqethi deenna” gides.
Hessa gi simmidi ba tohotanne ba kusheta ista bessides.
Istika ufayssa daroppenne malaletethafe dendidayssan buro ammanonta dishin Yesusi “Hessan aykko mizazi dizee?” giidi ista oychides.
Istika mole xiixa issi bars izas immida.
Izikka ekkidi ista sinthan mides.
Izikka “Intenara ta diza wode ‘Muse wogan nabetaninne Mazamure Maxaafatan ta gish xaafettidayssi wurikka polettanas bessees’ gaada ta intes yootida ta qaalay hayssakko” gides.
He wode Geeshsha Maxaafata isti erana mala wozna istas doyides.
Istaska “Kirstoosi waaye beyana; heedzdzantho gallas hayqoppe dendana geetettidi xaafettides.
Yerusalameppe doommidi ubba deres nagarappe simoynne maarotethi iza sunthan yootettana.
Inteka hayssas markata.
Takka ta Aaway immida ufayssa intes yeddana; inte qasse wolqa bollafe may7ana gakkanaas Yerusalame kataman takkite” gides.
Hessafe guye ista ekkidi Bitaaniya geetettizaso kezides. Ba kushetaka denthidi ista anjides.
Ista anjishe istafe shaakattidi pude salo bides.
Istika izas hokki goynnida; keehi ufayettishe Yerusalame simmida.
Ubba wode Xoossa Keeththan Xoossa galatishe gam7ida.
Qaalay kase koyro dees. Qaalaykka Xoossa achchan dees. He qaalaykka Xoossa.
Izi koyro Xoossa achchan dees.
Medhetethi wuri izan medhettides. Medhettidazan izi baynda medhettiday issinaka duukku.
De7oy izan dawus. Hanna de7oya asas poo7o.
Poo7oy dhuman poo7ises. Dhumay poo7o mulekka xoonenna.
Xoossafe kiitettida Yohannisa geetettiza issadey dees.
Iza markatethan asi wuri ammanana mala Poo7os marka gidi yides.
Izi poo7o gish markattana yides attin izi ba hu7es poo7o gidenna.
Asa ubbas poo7o immiza tumu poo7oy hayssa ha alamezan Yesusan dees.
Qaalaykka kase alamen dees. Alameyka medhettiday izanna. Gido attin alamey iza eribenna.
Izi ba baggatakko yiin iza baggati iza ekkibeetenna.
Gido attin iza ekkidayti iza sunthan ammanidayti isti Xoossa nayta gidana mala maata istas immides.
Istika Xoossa nayta gididay Xoossafe yelettida gish attin asa zerethafe hessika asa wogan woykko asho shenen gidenna.
Qaalaykka as gidides. Xoossa kiyatethaninne tuman kumidi nunan aqides; issi naas aawa matan diza boncho misatiza iza boncho nu beydos.
Yohannisikka “Taappe guyera yizayssi taappe aadhdhees. Gaasoyka izi taappe kasekka dees gaada ta intes yootidayssi hekko hayssi izakko!” gi markattides.
Iza kumeththa kiyatethan nu wuri kiyatetha bolla kiyateth ekkidos.
Wogay Muse baggara imettides; kiyatethinne tumay gidikko Yesus Kirstoosa baggara nuus yides.
Xoosse beyiday oonikka baawa. Gido attin Xoossa Aawa matan diza Xoossa Naa issoy xalala iza qoncisides.
Ayhudata daannati Yerusalameppe Qeesetanne Lewe nayta Yohannisakko kiittidi “Ne oonee?” giidi oychishin,
Yohannisi “Tani Kirstoosa gidikke” giidi geeshshi markattides attin markattanas ixibenna.
Istika “Histin ne oonee? Ne Elaasaa?” giidi oychida. Izikka “Gidikke” giidi istas zaarides. Istika “Izi yaana geetettida nabey nenee?” gida. Izikka “Akay tana gidikke” gides.
Isti qas “Histin ne oonee? Nuna kiittida asas nu yootana mala ne nena oona gay?” gida.
Izikka “Nabe Isayaassi yootida mala tani ‘Xoossa oge suurisite’ gishe bazzo biittan waassizade qaala giirisa” gides
Farsaaweetappe kiitettida issi issi asati
Hessa gish “Ne Xoossi kiittidade woykko buro yaana geetettida nabey nena gidonta gidikko histin aazas nuna xammaqay?” giidi iza oychida.
Yohannisikka istas “Ta haaththan xammaqays; gido attin inte erontaddey inte giddon eqqides.
Taappe guyera yaanayssi iza. Ta iza caamma qasho birshanas bessizade gidikke” gides.
Hayssi wuri haniday Yohannisi xammaqiza Yordanoose shaafappe he pinthan diza Bitaaniya geetettiza katamanna.
Wontetha gallas Yohannisi Yesusi baako yishin beyidi “Dere nagara biittafe diggana Xoossa dorsi hekko hayssich!
‘Taappe guyera yaanayssi izi taappe kasekka diza gish taappe aadhdhees’ gaada ta intes yootizay hayssich!
Takka ta baggara iza erabeekke shin gidikkokka izi Isra7eele deres qoncana mala ta haaththan xammaqashe yadis” gides.
Kaalethidikka Yohannisi hizgi markattides “Xillo Ayanay haraphe kafo misatdi saloppe wodhdhishininne iza bolla uttishin beyadis.
Ta ta baggara iza erike shin ta haaththan xammaqana mala tana kiittidadey ‘Xillo Ayanay iza bolla wodhdhi shempishin ne beyanaddey Xillo Ayanan meecanay iza’ giidi taas yootides.
Takka hessa beyadis. Hessa gish izi Xoossa naa gididayssa ta markatays” gides.
Wontetha gallas Yohannisi bana kaalliza nam7atara heen eqqides.
Yesusi iza achchara aadhdhishin Yohannisi beyidi “Xoossa dorsi hekko hayssich!” gides.
Yohannisa kaalliza nam7ati hessa siydi Yesusa kaallida.
Isti iza kaallishin Yesusi guye yuuy xeelidi “Ay kooyetii?” gides. Istika “Astamare! Ne duussasoy awaa?” gida.
Izikka ista “Ha yiidi beyte” gides. Hessa gish biidi izi awan dizaakko beyidanne he gallas izara issife pe7ida. Wodeykka gede tammu saateso bides.
Yohannisi yootida qaala siydi Yesusa kaallida nam7atappe issoy Simoona Phexroosa isha Indiraasa.
Indiraassi koyro ba isha Simoonakko biidinne “Xoossi kiittida Kirstoosa nu demmidos!” gides.
