Izakko shiiqi shiiqidi “Ayhuda kawo saro! saro!” gi giidi iza shagalan baqqida.
Philaxoosi qasseka kare kessidi “Hekko ta iza bolla aykko mooroka demmontayssa inte erana mala ta iza intes haa kare kessana” gides.
Hessa gish Yesusi aguntha zawude hu7en woththi ekkidinne zo7o kaaba may7idi kare kezides. Philaxoosika istas “Hekko addezi hayssich!” gides.
Qeeseta halaqatinne ista ashkarati Yesusa beyidi “Ne iza kaqqa! Kaqqa!” gishe waassida. Philaxoosi qasse “Ta ta baggara iza bolla issi mooroka demmabekke; koykko inte efidi kaqqite” gides.
Ayhuda asati qasse “Nuus wogay dees; hayssi addezi bana Xoossa naa giza gish nu woga mala izas hayqoy bessees” gida.
Philaxoosi hessa isti gizayssa siydi daro babbides.
Gede gibbe gelidi Yesusa “Ne awappe yadii?” giidi oychides. Yesusi qasse izas ay zaaroka immibenna.
Hessa gish Philaxoosi “Ne taas yootikii? Ta nena kaqqanas woykko birsha yeddanas godateththi taas dizayssa erikii?” gides.
Yesusikka izas zaaridi “Sheney nees Xoossafe imettontako nees ta bolla ay godateththika deennashin; gido attin tana nees aaththi immidade bolla gita nagaray dees” gides.
Philaxoosi hessa Yesusa haasaya siyidappe guye iza birshi yeddana koyides shin Ayhudatas babbida gish isti “Ne hayssa addeza birshikko Oroome Kawo Qeesare bagga gidakka; gaasoykka bana barka kawothizadey wuri Qeesares morke” gishe wurikka waassida.
Philaxoosi hessa siyida mala Yesusa gede kare kessidi “Lochcha shuch” geetettiza soon pirda womboran uttides. He pirdasoy Ayhudata qaalara “Gabata” geetettes.
He wode gadey asi Paaziga ba7aales giigettiza gallassa. Wodeykka gallassafe usuppun saate mala gidides. He wode Philaxoosi Ayhudata “Hekko inte kawoy hayssich!” gides.
Gido attin isti qas “Gede digga! Gede digga! Kaqqa!” gishe waassida. Philaxoosika “Ta inte kawo kaqqoo?” gides. Qeeseta halaqati zaaridi “Nuus Qeesareppe hara kawoy deenna” gida.
Hessafe simmidi Philaxoosi Yesusa kaqqana mala istas aaththi immides. Istika Yesusa oykki ekki efida.
Hessafe guye Yesusi ba kaqqettana masqaleza tookkidi “Asa hu7e guuge” geetettizaso kezides. Hesoy Ayhudata qaalara “Golgota” geettettes.
Iza heen kaqqida. Yesusa giddo gelthidi hara nam7u asata izatho hadirisaranne ushachara kaqqida.
Philaxoosi “Naazirete Yesusi Ayhudata kawo” giza qaala xaafidi iza masqale bolla izas hu7esora qaaphides.
Yesusi kaqqettidasoy katamas mata gidida gish daro Ayhuda asay Philaxoosi xaafidayssa nabebides. Xaafetidaysikka Ayhudata qaalara, Laatine geetettiza qaalaranne Girike qaalara.
Ayhudata Qeeseta halaqati Philaxoosa “Ne iza Ayhudata kawo” gaada xaafoppa. Gido attin “ ‘Hayssi addezi bana ta Ayhudata kawo gides’ gaada xaafa” gida.
Philaxoosi qas “Ta xaafidayssa xaafadis” gides.
Wotadarati Yesusa kaqqidappe guye iza may7oza ekkidi wotadarata issa issa gakkana mala oyddu kessi shaakerethida. Garsara may7iza may7ozakka hessatho shaakerethida. Gido attin giddora may7iza may7ozi siketonta pudeppe duge gakkanaas coo yeda dees.
Hessa gish wotadarati ba giddon “Gishan oona gakkanakkonne erana mala iza bolla saama yeggana attin daakkokko” gida. Hessika haniday kase “Ta may7o isti gishetti ekkida, ta bollara may7iza may7oza bolla saama yeggida” geetettida Geeshsha maxaafa qaalay polettana malassa. Wotadaratikka hessa ooththida.
Yesusa masqale achchan iza aayeyanne aayeyi micheya Qaliyoopha macha Maaramanne Meg dale geetettizasoppe yida Maarama heen eqqida.
Yesusi ba aayeyonne izi siiqiza iza kaallizayssi ba achchan eqqidayta beyidi, ba aayeyo “Aayee! Ne naaza hessa beya” gides.
Hessafe kaaleththidi bana kaallizayssa “Ne aayo hinno beya” gides. Hinno he saateyppe simmin he iza kaallizayssi aayeyo baso efides.
Hessafe guye Yesusi ha7i wurikka poletidayssa eridi Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafetidayssi polettana mala “Tana saamees” gides.
Heen gadaan caala phanqida ushshi kumi uttida issi xaaro malay dees. Hessa gish heen gadaan dizayti he caala ushsha zandza misatiza safnage geetettizayssara hisophe geetettiza mitha xeeran qaaphidi iza duunakko shiishida.
Yesusi he caala ushsha xunxi xeelidi “Polettides!” gides. Ba hu7e duge ziqqisidi shempo kezides.
Hessafe guye Ayhudata daannati kaqettida asata meqeth wodirappe menthidi isti iza masqale bollafe wothana mala Philaxoosa woossida. Isti hessa ooththiday Ayhudati sambatas giigettiza gallas gidida gishshinne he sambataykka daro gita ba7aale gidida gish Sambata gallas ahay masqale bolla gam7onta mala koyda gishassa.
Hessa gish wotadarati biidi Yesusara kaqettida asata meqeth wodirappe wodirappe menthida.
Isti Yesusakko biin izi kasetidinne hayqqidayssa beyidi iza wodira meqeth menthibeetenna.
Gido attin wotadarata giddofe issadey toorara iza millen caddin heerakka suuthinne haaththi gukkides.
Hessa beyidaddey inte izan ammanana mala markattides. Iza markaykka tuma. Izi yootizaykka tumu gididayssa izi erees.
Hessika haniday “Iza meqethafe issinaka meqquku” geetettida Geeshsha maxaafa qaalay poletanassa.
Qasseka Geeshsha Maxaafan harason “Isti ba cadidade beyana” gees.
Ayhudata daannata babbidi qotan Yesusa kaalliza Armatiyasa geetettizasoppe yida Yoosefey Yesusa aha ekkanas Philaxoosa woossin Philaxoosikka izas ero gides. Hessa gish Yoosefey biidi Yesusa aha ekkides.
Kase Yesusakko qamara yida Niqodimoosikka bagga kilo gidiza karbenne godare uuthara walaketida shitto ekki yides.
He nam7u asati Yesusa aha ekkidi Ayhudati aha xaaxiza mala shiito puukkidi lee7e may7ora xaaxida.
Yesusi kaqqettidason issi atakiltesoy dees. He atakiltezason oonikka moogetonta ooratha duufoy dees.
Ayhudata sambatas giigetiza gallas gidida gishshinne duufoykka matan diza gish Yesusa aha heen moogida.
Wogga gallas wonta malado buro bazzoy zo7ishin Magdale Maarama Yesusa duufokko badus. Iza he gakkishin kase Yesusa duufo izara gordida shuchchay duufoza duunappe dendidi genderidayssa beyadus.
Hessa gish iza Yesusa kaallizaytappe Simoona geetettiza Phexroosakko Yesusi dosiza hanko iza kaallizayssako woxxa baada “Goda duufoppe kessi ekkidi awan woththidakkone nu erokko” gadus.
Heerakka Phexroosinne Yesusa kaalliza hinko issoy kezidi gede duufoy dizaso bida.
Nam7aykka issife woxxida. Gido attin Yesusa kaalliza hinkoyssi Phexroosappe pilati woxxidi kaseti duufoy dizaso gakkides.
Duufoza hokki xeelidi ahay izan xaaxettida may7oy xalla dizayssa beyides; gido attin gede duufoza giddo gellibeenna.
Simoona geetettiza Phexroosikka iza kaalli gakkidi duufoza giddo gelides; ahay izan xaaxettida carqay heen dizayssa beyides.
Yesusa hu7ey xaaxettida carqay hanko xaaththa carqatara gidonta dumma harason xaaxetti dizayssa beyides.
Koyrotti gakkida Yesusa kaallizayssika duufoza giddo geli beyidi ammanides.
Gaasoyka “Izi hayqoppe dendana bessees” giza maxaafa qaala isti buro haasayibeetenna.
Hessafe guye nam7atikka simmidi baso baso bida.
Magdale Maarama yeekkashe Yesusa duufoppe karera eqqada hokka duufoza giddo xeelladus.
Yesusa ahay dizason bootha may7o may7ida nam7u kiitanchatappe issoy hu7eson issoy tohoson uttidayta beyadus.
Istika Maaramo “Hanne macasaye! Aazas yeekkay?” gida. Izakka “Isti ta Goda efidi awan woththidakkone ta erike” gadus.
Iza hinno gaada guye yuuyishin Yesusi eqqidayssa demmadus shin izi Yesusa gididayssa erabeyku.
Yesusi izo “Hanne macasayee! Aazas yeekkay? Qasse oona kooyay?” gides; izikka izis atakilte naagizade misatin “Godo! Ne ekkida gidikko ne woththidaso taas yootarki; Ta iza taas ekkana” gadus.
Yesusi izo “Maarame!” gides; izakka gede izakko simmada Ayhudata qaalara “Rebuune!” gadus; Hessa birsheththi “Astamaree!” guussa.
Yesusi qas “Ta buro pude ta Aawakko kezabeekke; tana bochofa; gido attin ne ha7i ta ishataako baada ‘Tani ta Aawakkone inte Aawakko, ta Xoossakkonne inte Xoossako kezana gides’ gaada istas yoota” gides.
Hessa gish Magdale Maarama Yesusa kaallizaytakko baada iza Yesusa beyidayssanne izi izis yootidayssa istas yootadus.
He gallas wogga omars Yesusa kaallizayti Ayhudata daannatas babbidi kare ba bolla goordidi keeththa giddon shiiqon dishin karey doyettonta Yesusi iza kaallizayti shiiqi diza keeththa gelides; ista giddon eqqidi “Saroy intes gido!” gides.
Hessa gi simmidi ba kushetanne ba mille ista bessides; iza kaallizaytikka Goda beyidi keehi ufayetida.
Hessafe guye qasseka Yesusi ista “Intes saroy gido! Ta Aaway tana kiittida mala takka intena kiittays” gides.
Hessa gi simmidi ista bolla ufu giidi “Inte Xillo Ayana ekkite.
Inte asa nagara atto giikko istas atto geetettana; inte asa nagara atto goonta ixikko qas intes atto geetettenna” gides.
Yesusi bana kaallizaytakko yida wode tammanne nam7atappe issoy Didimoosa geetettiza Toomaassi istara deenna.
Hessa gish hanko Yesusa kaallizayti Toomaasa “Nu Goda beydos” gida. Toomaassi qas “Misimaaren cadettida iza kusheta tani ta ayfera beyonta dashe, qasseka ta biradhdhe misimaarey gelidason geltha xeellonta dashenne ta kushe iza mille madunthan geltha xeellonta dashe ammanikke” gides.
Hessafe kaallin osupun gallassafe guye iza kaallizayti qasseka keeththa giddon dishin; Toomaaska istara issife dishin; kareykka gordan dishin Yesusi yiidi ista giddon eqqidi “Saroy intes gido!” gides.
Hessafe guye Toomaasa “Ne biradhdhe ha ehada ta kusheta beya. Ne kushe ha ehada ta millen geltha ammana attin ammanontade gidoppa” gides.
Toomaassi “Ta Godo! Ta Xoosso!” gides.
Yesusikka Toomaasa “Neni tana beyida gish ammanadasa; tana beyonta ammanizayti gidikko isti anjettidayta” gides.
Hayssa maxaafan xaafetonta daro malatata bana kaallizayta sinthan Yesusi ooththides.
Gido attin Yesusi izi Masihe, Xoossa naa gididayssa inte erana malanne inte iza sunthan ammanidi de7o demmana mala hayssi xaafetides.
Hessafe guye Yesusi Xibiraadoose Abba achchan bana kaallizaytas qasseka beettides.
Simoona geetettiza Phexroosi, Didimoosa geetettiza Toomaassi, Galila Qaana as gidida Natina7eeley, Zabidoosa naytikka Yesusa kaallizaytappe hara nam7atikka wuri issife dishin
Simoona geetettiza Phexroosi istas “Ta mole oykkana bays” gides; istika izas “Nukka nenara baana” gida. Izara kezi biidi wogolon gelida shin he gallas omars issi molekka oykkibetenna.
Gadey wontishin Yesusi abba achchan eqqides; iza kaallizayti qas izi Yesusa gididayssa eribeetenna.
Yesusi ista “Nayto moley dizee?” gides; istika “Aykkoyka baawa” gida.
Izikka “Giteza wogolozappe ushacha baggara abban yeggite; inte demmana” gida gish giteza abba giddo yeggidanne daro moley oyketida gish giteza molezara goochana dandaybeetenna.
Hessa wode Yesusa kaallizaytappe izi siiqiza issoy Phexroosas “Hessi Godakko!” gides. Simoona geetettiza Phexroosi “Hessi Godakko!” giza qaala siyida mala kase ooso diggofo giidi may7o qaari woththidi kallo diza gish heerakka may7o ekki may7idi abba giddo guppi gelides.
Yesusa kaalliza hankoyti qas biittafe xeetu metre mala haakki diza gish moley kumi diza giteza goochchi ekkidi wogolora gakkida.
Isti wogolozappe wodhdhishin moley iza bolla diza bonqo tammanne ukethi beyida.
Yesusi ista “Ha7i inte oykkida molezappe ane ha ekki yiite” gides.
Hessa gish Simoona geetettiza Phexroosi wogoloza giddo gelidi xeetanne ichashu tammanne heedzdzu wogga gita moleti kumida giteza abbafe gede gade bolla goochchides. Hessa mala daro molera diinka gitezi daakkettibenna.
Hessafe guye Yesusi ista “Ha yiidi miite” gides. Izi Goda Yesusa gididayssa wuri erida gish iza kaallizaytappe issadeykka “Ne oonnee?” gi oychanas xalidadey baawa.
Yesusi yiidi ukethanne moleza ekkidi istas immides.
Yesusi hayqoppe dendin iza kaallizayti iza beyishin hayssi heedzdzantho.
Isti mi giigishin Yesusi Simoona Phexroosa “Yoona naa Simoona! Haytantafe ne tana aaththa tana dosay?” gides. Izikka “Ee ta Godo! Ta nena dosizayssa nekka eraasa” gides.
Yesusi iza “Ta dhammizayta heemma” gides; nam7anthokka “Yoona naa Simoona! Ne tana dosay?” gides; Izikka zaaridi “Ee Godo! Ta nena dosizayssa nekka eraasa” gides; Yesusi qasseka “Laaqqata naaga” gides.
Heedzdzantho “Yoona naa Simoona! Ne tana dosay?” gides. Izi heedzdzantho “Ne tana dosay?” gida gish Phexroosi michetidinne “Godo! Ne wursa eraasa ta nena dosizayssakka ne eraasa” gides; Yesusikka qasseka “Ta dorsata heemma.
Ta nees tumu gays; ne naatethan dashe ne giththe nerka gixxada ne koyidaso baasashin; ne cimmiza wode gidikko neni ne kusheta piddisin hara asi nena gixxisananne ne dosontaso nena efana” gides.
Yesusi iza hessatho giday Phexroosi ay mala hayqon Xoosse bonchanakkone izas erisanassa; hessafe guye Phexroosa “Ne tana kaalla” gides.
Phexroosi yuushi xeelidi Yesusi dosizayssi iza kaallishin beyides; hessadey kase isti kawo miishin Yesusa haythako shiiqidi “Godo! Nena aaththi immanadey izi oonnee?” gi oychides.
Phexroosi iza beyidi “Godo! Hayssadey waanandee?” giidi Yesusa oychides.
Yesusikka izas “Ta ha simma yaana gakkanawu ta iza paxa woththikko nena aazi gaththidee? Ne tana kaalla” gides.
Hessa gaason ishata giddon “Izi hayqo hayqqenna” giza worey laalettides. Gido attin Yesusi “Ta yaana gakkanaas paxa daana mala ta koykko nena aaze gaththiday?” gides attin “Hayqqaka” gibenna.
He yo7ota gish markattidaynne xaafiday ha Yesusa kaallizayssa; iza markatethikka tumu gididayssa nuni eroos.
Yesusi ooththida hara daroti deettes. Taas misatiza mala izi ooththida miishata wursi issi bolla xaafizakko xaafetiza maxaafata hayssi alamey tookkana dandayenna.
Tofiloosa, Yesusi ooththanassinne tamarsanas oykkidayssa wursa ta nees koyro maxaafan xaafadis.
Hessika izi pude dentha gallas gakkanaas ba doori kiittidaytas Xillo Ayana baggara izi istas immida azazokko.
Izi daro waaye beyidappe guye Istako shiiqidi hayqoppe dendanayssa istas daro markara qoncisishe oyddu tammu gallas gakkanaas istas gallas gallas beettishe Xoossa Kawoteththa gish yootides.
Istara issife maaddan utti dishe ista “Yerusalameppe kezoppite; gido attin ta intes yootishin inte siyidayssa ta Aaway immida ufayssa naagite.
Yohannisi haaththan xammaqides shin inte qas guuththa wodeppe guye Xillo Ayanan xammaqettana” giidi azazides.
Istika issi bolla shiiqeti dishe “Godo! Ne Isra7eeleta kawoteth zaarada ha7i essanee?” gi oychida.
Izikka istas “Aaway ba shenen woththida wode eroy intes imettibenna.
Gido attin Xillo Ayanay inte bolla wodhdhida wode inte wolqa ekkana. Yerusalamenka, Yuhudanikka, Samaariyanka ubbason biitta gaxa gakkanaas inte taas markata gidana” gides.
Hessa gi yootidappe guye isti xeellishin pude salo dendides. Salo shaaraykka ista ayfeppe iza geenthides.
Izi bishin isti iza tishshi histi pude salo xeellishin booththa may7o may7ida nam7u asati qopponta ista achchan eqqidi;
“Inteno Galila asato! Inte pude salo xeellishe hayssan aazas eqqidetii? Hayssi inte matappe pude salo dendishin inte beyiza Yesusi salo kezishin inte beyida mala hessathoka izi ha simmi yaana” gida.
Hessafe guye Dabrazayte geetettiza zuma bollafe wodhdhidi Yerusalame simmida. He zumaykka Yerusalameppe issi kilo metre mala haakkees.
Gede katamayo gelida wode kase ba diza keeththa Pooqe bolla kezida; heytikka Phexroosa, Yohannisa, Yaqoobe, Indiraasa, Piliphoosa, Toomaasa, Bartelemoosa, Matoosa, Ilfiyoosa naa Yaqoobe, ba bagga maaddizade geetettiza Simoonanne Yaqoobe naa Yuhuda.
Heyti wurikka macasatappe Yesusa aayo Maaramira hessathoka iza ishatara issi woznan issi bolla qanxonta minni woossida.
He gallasatan Phexroosi xeetanne nam7u tammu ammaniza asa giddon eqqidi,
“Ta ishato! Yesusa oykkida asata kaalethi ehida. Yuhuda gish Xillo Ayanay kasetidi Dawute duunan haasayida Geeshsha maxaafa qaalay polettana koshshees.
Izikka nuuppe issade mala taybettidi hayssa ha oosozan gellanas qaada demmides” gides.
Gidikkoka hayssadey ba iita ooson demmida miishan gade shamides; henka ba liiphen gufanni kundin iza asatethay giddofe phalqeti wodhdhides; iza maracey biitta bolla zaazetides.
Hessika Yerusalamen diza asas ubbas siyettides. Biittaykka ista qaalara “Akeldama” geetettides; hessas birsheththayka suutha biitta guussa.
Gujjidikka Phexroosi “Mazamure maxaafan ‘Iza gadey mela atto, izan ay asikka dooppo; qasseka iza daannateth hara asi ekko’ geetetti xaafettides.
“Hessa gish Goda Yesusi nunara diza wode ubban nunara issife dizayta giddofe nu issade dooranas koshshees.
Hessika Yohannisa xinqateppe haa simmin Yesusi nuuppe shaaketi dendi baana gakkanaas nunara dizadde gidanas bessees. Gaasoyka ha asatappe issadey nunara Yesusa denthas marka gidana koshshees” gides.
Hessa gish Barsabaasa woykko Yosxoosa geetettiza Yoosefenne Maatiyaasa nam7ata shiishshidi,
“Godo! Ne asa ubba wozna eraasa; hayta nam7ata giddofe ne oona dooridakko issade nuna bessa.
Yuhuday yeggi bidason ha oosa ooththanadenne Hawaare gidanadde ne doora” gi woossida.
Hessafe saama yeggin saamay Maatiyaasas kezides. Izikka tammanne issi Hawaaretara issife tayibettides.
Phenxaqoste geetettiza ba7aale gallassi gakkida wode asay wurikka issi soon shiiqi dishin;
qofay baynda daro mino gote carko mala giirissi yides; asay diza keeththakka kumides.
Tama laco inxarsa malay asas beettidi shaaketi shaaketi issi issi asa bolla uttides.
Ammanizayti wuri Xillo Ayanan kumidi Ayanay istas haasayanas immidayssa keena hara qaalara haasaya oykkida.
He wode salo gufanthon diza dereppe yida Xoossas babbiza Ayhudati Yerusalamen deettes.
He giirissa siydi derey shiiqides. Issi issi asay ba qaalara haasayizayssa siydi malalettida.
Malaletidinne gaanazi dhayin “Hayti haasayizayti wurikka Galila as deettenee?
Histin nuni nu yeletida nu dere qaalara isti haasayishin wosti siyizonii?
Nuni Pharteena asay, Meede asay, Eelaame asay, Mesopotoomiyan, Yuhudan, Qophodooqiyan, Phanxoosan, Iisiyan,
Firgiyan, Phinfiliyan, Gibxen, Qareena achchan diza Liibiyappenne Oroomeppe yidayti
Ayhudatinne gede Ayhudatethan gelida Qarxeese asanne Araabe asata gidishin Xoossa wolqama oosoza hayti nu qaalara haasayishin nu siyoos” gida.
Wurikka keehi malalettidinne gaanazi dhayin ba giddon “Hayssi aazeshaa?” geetettida.
Bagga asay “Hayti daro woyne cajje uyida” giidi ista qidhida.
He wode Phexroosi tammanne issinetara eqqidinne ba qaala dhoqu histidi deraas hizgides “Inteno Yuhuda asato! Yerusalamen dizayto! Inte wurikka hayssa issi miish eritenne ta gizayssa siyite.
Ha7i gadey wontin buro heedzdzu saate gidida gish inte qoppiza mala hayti asati mathotibeetenna.
Gido attin hayssi kase nabe Iyu7eelen hizgi yootetida qaalay poletanassa,
‘Xoossi Wursetha gallas ta Ayana asho may7ida ubba bolla ta gussana; inte maca naytinne inte attuma nayti tinbite haasayana; yelaga nayti ajjuta beyana; Cimati agumo agumettana.
He wode ta maca ashkarata bollanne ta attuma ashkarata bolla ta Ayanappe ta gussana. Istika tinbite haasayana.
Bolla Salon malalisiza hanota ta bessana, garsa sa7an malatata ta bessana; suuthi, tamaynne tulalay hanana.
Gitanne boncho gidida Goda gallassi yaanappe kasetidi awa arshey dhumana; Aginaykka suuth misatana.
Goda sunth xeygizay wuri attana’ gides.
“Isra7eele nayto! Hayssa qaala siyite; inte inte baggara erizayssa mala inte giddon malatanne asi siyi eronta miishata iza kushen ooththidi Xoossi Naazirete Yesusas markatides.
Xoossi kase ba qachidayssa izas beni eratetha mala hayssade inte kushen aaththi immides. Inteka iita asata kushen kaqeti hayqqana mala ooththideta.
Gido attin Xoossi iza bollafe hayqo wolqa diggidi hayqoppe denthides. Hayqoyka iza oykki ashshanas dandaybenna.
Dawuteykka iza gish ‘Tani Goda ubba wode ta sinthan beyays; izi ta ushachan dees; mulekka hirgike.
Hessa gish ta woznay ufayetees; ta duunaykka galatees; ta ashoy ufayssan daana.
Ne ta shempoyo Duufon aggaka; ne naa geeshshaza wooqana mala aggaggakka.
Ne de7o oge ta erana mala ooththadasa. Ne tanara diza gish ta ufayssay kumeththa’
“Ta ishato! Beni aawatappe Dawutey hayqqi moogetiddayssanne iza duufoy hach gakkanaas nu achchan dizayssa babbonta ta intes yootana danda7ays.
Izi nabe gidida gish Xoossi iza zerethafe issade iza kawoteththa alga bolla wothanayssa kase caaqo qaalan yootidayssa erides.
Hessa kasetidi erida gishshinne iza ashoy wooqi Duufon attonta doorettida Kirstoosa dentha gish haasayides.
He Yesusa Xoossi hayqoppe denthides. Nukka wuri hayssas markata.
Hessa gish izi Xoossa ushachchan dhoqu dhoqu gidappe guye Xillo Ayana ufaysa ba aawappe ekkidi ha7i inte beyizayssanne siyizayssa duge gussides.
Dawutey pude salo kezibenna; izi ba duunan ‘Goday ta Godas “Ta ne morketa ne toho garsan yedhissana gakkanaas ta ushachchan utta” gides.’
<range>
“Hessa gish Xoossi inte kaqqida Yesusa Godanne Kirstoosa histidayssa Isra7eele asay wuri lo7ethi ero” gides.
Derey hessa siyida mala woznay boshettides. Phexroosanne hanko Yesusi kiittidayta “Nu ishato! Histin nu ay ooththinoo?” gida.
Phexroosikka “Maarotethan gelite; inte nagaray maarettana mala intefe issi issi asi Yesus Kirstoosa sunthan xammaqettite; izi immiza Xillo Ayana inte ekkana.
Ufayssa qaalay intessinne inte naytassa; qasseka Goda Xoossi baako xeygiza haahon dizaytassara ubbassa” gides.
Hara daro qaalara istas markatishe “Hayssa geella yeletethafe intena ashshite” giidi ista qofisides.
He gallas qaala ekkidaytinne xammaqetidayti heedzdzu shi mala asay kaseyta bolla gujettides.
Istika Hawaareta timirten, issife quma muussaninne woossan minnida.
Hawaareta kushen daro malatati oosettida gish asi ubbay istas babbides.
Ammanidayti wurikka issife de7ida; baas dizazikka ubba issi bolla go7ettida.
Baas diza miishenne mehe bayzi bayzi ba giddon koshshida mala gishechchida.
Gallas gallas Xoossa Keeththan issife shiiqetes. Ba keeththanka quma issife ufayssaninne suure woznara meetes.
Isti Xoossa galatishe dere sinthan bonchettida. Godayka ista bolla gallas gallas oorath ammanizayta gujjides.
Issi wode gallassafe uddufun saate bolla Phexroosinne Yohannisi woossa saaten Xoossa Keeththe baana kezida.
Issi yeletosappe doommidi tohoy silidade Xoossa Keeththe geliza asappe miishe woossana mala asay gallas gallas tookki efidi woththin issi “Lo7o” geetettiza Xoossa Keeththa pengen woossizadey dees.
Izikka Phexroosinne Yohannisi Xoossa Keeththe gelishin beyida istafe miishe woossides.
Phexroosinne Yohannisi iza tishshi histi xeellida. Phexroosikka iza “Ane haa nuna xeella” gides.
Addezikka istafe aykko demmana giidi ista tishshi histi xeellides.
Gido attin Phexroosi izas zaaridi “Taas biraynne worqay deenna; gidikkokka taas dizaz ta nees immays; Naazirete Yesus Kirstoosa sunthan dendada ne tohora hamuta” gides.
Izas ushachcha kushe oykkidi denthides. Heerakka addeza tohoynne toho qirphey minnides.
Guppi dendi eqqidi hamuth oykkides. Yaanne haanne hamutishenne guppishe Xoossaka galatishe istara issife Xoossa Keeththa gibbe gelides.
Izi Xoossa galatishe yaanne haane simerettishin asay beyides.
Hayssadey hannife kase “Lo7o” geetettiza Xoossa Keeththa pengen uttidi miishe woossizay iza gididayssa erides. Iza bolla hanidayssafe dendidayssan asay keehi malaletides.
Ha paxida woossanchay Phexroosakonne Yohannisakko shiph giidi istara oykketi dishin derey wuri malaletidi istako “Solomoone simeretethaso” geetettizaso wothan yides.
Phexroosi he asa beyidi “Inteno Isra7eele dereto! Hayssan aazas malaletetii? Qasseka hayssa addeza nuni nu wolqan woykko nuni nu xillotethan pathidi hamutissida mala qoodidi nuna aazas tishshi histi xeelletii?
Nu aawanta Abrahaamenta, Yisaaqanta, Yaqoobenta Xoossi ba naaza Yesusa bonchides. Inte qas iza hayqos aaththi immideta; Philaxoosi izi birshana koynka inte ‘Koyokko’ gideta.
Geeshshanne xilloza inte kadidi shempo wodhizayssi birshettana mala woossideta.
De7o immizade inte wodhideta; gido attin Xoossi iza hayqoppe denthides; hessas nuni marka.
Hayssi inte beyizayssinne inte erizayssi minni eqqiday Yesusa sunthan ammanida gishassa. Inte wurikka beyiza mala izi kumeththa paxa demmiday Yesusa sunthaninne iza sunthan beettiza ammanona.
“Ha7ikka ta ishato! Inte hessa ooththiday inte halaqata mala eronta gididayssa ta erays.
Gidikkoka Kirstoosi waaye ekkanayssa Xoossi kase nabeta duunan haasayidayssa polides.
Hessa gish inte nagaray qucceti dhayana mala maarotethan gelite. Inte biza ogeppe simmite; Goda matappe inte ooraxana wodey intes yaana.
Qasseka Xoossi kase intes doori woththida Yesus Kirstoosa izi intes yeddana.
Xoossi kase geeshsha nabeta duunan haasayidayssa mala hanizayssa wursi ooraxissana wodey gakkanaas izi salon gam7anas koshshees.
Museykka ‘Inte Goda Xoossay inte giddofe ta mala nabe intes denthana. Izi intes yootizayssa siyite.
He nabeza siyonta ixida shempoy wuri dere giddofe shaaketi dhayo’
“Tumappe Sameelappe ha simmin dendida nabeti wuri hayta wodeta gish haasayida.
Inteka nabeta nayta. Qasseka Xoossi Abrahaames ‘Ne zerethan biitta asi wuri anjettana’ giidi izi caaqida caaqoza inte laattana.
Xoossi naaza denthida wode intena issa issa inte iitatethafe zaaridi anjana mala kasetidi inteko kiittides” gides.
Phexroosinne Yohannisi asas haasayan dishin Qeeseta Halaqatinne Xoossa Keeththa naagizayta halaqay qasseka Saduqaaweti akekonta istako yida.
Yiidinne Hawaareti asa tamarsizayssassinne Yesusa baggara bettida hayqqidayta dentha gish sabakizayssas keehi hanqettida.
Phexroosanne Yohannisa gadey qammishin oykidi wontana gakkanaas qasho keeththan ayssida.
Gido attin qaala siyida asappe dariza baggay ammanides. Ammaniza attuma asata qooday gede ichashu shi gakkanaas dhoqu gides.
Wontetha gallas ista halaqatinne cimati qasseka Muse woga tamarsizayti Yerusalamen shiiqida.
Ista Qeeseta halaqa Haanaynne Qayaafay, Yohannisi, Iskindirosinne Qeeseta halaqaso asay wuri he gadaan bettida.
Istika Phexroosanne Yohannisa ba giddon aaththi essidi “Hayssa inte ooththizay aaza wolqanee? Woykko oona sunthanee?” giidi oychida.
He wode Phexroosi Xillo Ayanan kumidi “Inteno dere halaqato! Dere cimato!
Inte hach ha toho sila addezas oosettida lo7o oosoy waani izi paxidakko inte nuna oychiza gidikko,
inte kaqqin Xoossi hayqoppe denthida Naazirete Yesus Kirstoosa sunthan izi paxidayssanne inte sinthan izi eqidayssa inteka Isra7eele dere asay wuri hayssa erite.
Izikka inte keeththa hiillati leqqi aggida shuchchay ginbe keeththas gula bolla bollara woththiza shuch gidides.
Atotethi hara oonanka ba; saloppe garsa baggara nu asa nayti attana mala nuus imettiday hayssafe hara sunthi deenna” gides.
Ayhudata duulata asaykka Phexroosinne Yohannisi hessatho xali haasayizayssa beyidi isti tamaronta as gididayssa eridi malaletidanne isti kase Yesusara dizayta gididayssa akeekida.
He paxida addezi istara eqqidishin beyida gish istas hara ooththanas gaasoy dhayides.
Hessa gish ista duulatappe kessana mala azazida. Hessafe qasseka shiiqetidi ba giddon zoretida.
Ba giddon “Hayta asata wostinoo? Yerusalamen diza asay wuri ista kushen hanida gita malata erides. Hessa gish nu ha yo7oza asa baleththanas dandayokko.
Gido attin hayssi yo7ozi dere giddon keehi aakkonta malanne hayti asati nam7antho hayssa ha sunthan hara oonaska yootonta mala istas lo7ethi yootana” gida.
Ista xeygidinne mulekka Yesusa sunthan haasayonta malanne tamarsonta mala azazida.
Phexroosinne Yohannisi qasse zaaridi “Nuni Xoossafe bollara intes azazettanas bessizakonne ane inte Xoossa sinthan pirdite.
Nuni nu beyidayssanne nu siyidayssa haasayanappe guye gookko” gida.
Qasseka ista bolla mandidi yeddida. Gaasoyka hanko derey wuri hanida yo7oza gaason wurikka Xoosse galatiza gish ista qaxayanas dandaybetenna.
He gita malatan paxida addezas laythi oyddu tammafe bolla.
Phexroosinne Yohannisi qashoppe birshettidi gede ba asatakko simmidi Qeeseta Halaqatinne Dere cimati ista gidayssa wursika yootida.
Istika hessa siyida mala ba qaala dhoqu histidi issife Xoossakko “Wogga Godawu! Neni salonne sa7a, abbanne abba giddon dizayta wursa medhadassa.
Ne ashkara nuus aawa Dawute duunara Xillo Ayanan ‘Dere asay aazas hanqetti dendidee? Derey aazas mela maqetizee?
Biitta kawoti issife gaaggidi biitta haarizayti issi bolla shiiqettidi Goda bollan ne dooretti tiyettidayssa bolla duulatida’ giidi waassida.
“Tumappe Herdoossinne Phanxoosa Philaxoosi Isra7eelataranne hara dere asara hanno katamayn ne doora tiyida geeshsha naaza Yesusa bolla yo7o qachanas shiiqetida.
Hayssanka ne wolqaninne ne shenen kase ne qoppidayssa isti polida.
Godo! Ha7ikka ista mandeza ne beya; nuni ne aylleti ne qaala babbonta kumeththa xalatethara yootana mala dandayissa.
Pathanas ne kushe micca. Ne naa geeshshaza sunthan gita malata ooththa” gida.
Isti woossidappe guye isti dizasoy qaaxides. Wurikka Xillo Ayanan kumidi Xoossa qaala xalatethan yootida.
Ammanizayti wurikka issi woznaninne issi qofan gaaggi deettes. Istas dizay wuri issi bolla dees attin baas dizaz “Hayssi taas buzo miisha” gizaddey deenna.
Hawaaretikka Goda Yesusa dentha gita wolqan markateth oykkida. Ubba bolla gita Xoossa kiyatethi dees.
Ista giddon metotanchay issadeykka baawa. Gaasoyka gade gidin keeththe gidin baas diza wursi bayzi bayzi shiishida miish
Hawaareta kushen woththidi issi issades izas koshshiza mala gisheettes.
Qophiroose geetettizason diza Yoosefe geetettizadey issi Lewe bagga asi dees. Izikka Hawaaretan “Barnabaasa” geetetti summides. Hessas birsheththay “Minthetho naa” guussa.
Izikka ba gade bayzida miisha ehidi Hawaareta kushen woththides.
Issi Hananiya geetettiza asi Saphphira geetettiza ba macheyra ba gade bayzides.
Macheya Saphphiray lo7etha erishin gadeza bayzida miishafe bagga shaakki ashshidi bagga ehidi Hawaareta kushen immides.
Qasse Phexroosi “Haysso Hananiya! Neni Xillo Ayana bolla wordotanassinne gade miishafe ashshana mala Xala7ey ays ne woznan gelidee? Bayzanappe kase gadezi neyssa gidenee? Ne bayzidappe guye qasse miishay ne kushen deenee? Histin ne hayssa mala wosta ne woznan qoppadii? Ne Xoossa bolla wordotadassa attin asa bolla gidenna” gides.
<range>
Hessa siyida mala Hananiyay kundi hayqqides. Hessa siyida asay wuri daro babbides.
Attumasay dendidi aha xaaxidinne heerakka efidi moogides.
Heedzdzu saateppe guye macheya izi waanidakkonne eronta dashe yadus.
Phexroosikka “Ane taas yoota; inte gadeza bayzida waagay hanno xallaa?” gides. Izakka “Ee hanno ha waagayn bayzidos” gadus.
Phexroosikka “Inte Xoossa Ayana paacanas aysi issi duuna gididetii? Hekko ne azina moogida asati moogi simmidi karen penge bolla deettes. Isti nenakka kessi ekki efana” gides.
Iza siyida mala heerakka iza toho bolla kundada hayqqadus. Attumasaykka soo gelida mala hayqqidaro beyidi kessi efidi izi azina achchan moogida.
Kumeththa Woosa Keeththa asaynne hessa siyida asay wuri daro babbides.
Hawaaretikka dere giddon daro malatanne malalisiza miish ooththida. Ammanizayti wuri “Solomoone simeretethaso” geetettiza pengen shiiqeetes.
Istas babbida gish oonnikka istara walakketanas koyibenna. Gido attin derey ista keehi bonches.
Daro macasattinne addeti wodeppe woden Godan ammani ammani ista bolla gujettida.
Hessa gaason Phexroosi aadhdhishin haray attin iza eeshoy harganchatappe bagga harganchata bolla wodhdhana mala hargizayti ichchiza alga bollanne hala bolla karen ishiseetes.
Yerusalame yuushon diza katamatappe hargizaytanne tuna ayanay waayssizayta ehin wuri paxida.
Hessa wode Qeeseta Halaqaynne izara diza Saduqaaweta baggati wurikka qanate qanatizayta xalla gidida.
Hawaareta oykkidi qasho keeththe gelthida.
Gido attin Goda kiitanchay qamara qasho keeththa kare doyidi ista kessidi,
“Biidi Xoossa Keeththa gibbe giddon eqqidi hayssa de7o qaala ubba deres yootite” gides.
Gadey wontida mala istas yootidayssa Xoossa Keeththa gibbe gelidi dereza tamarso oykkida; Qeeseta halaqaynne izara dizayti yiidi Ayhudata duulatanne Isra7eele dere cimata kumeth issi bolla shiishida. Hawaareta qasho keeththafe ekki yaana mala as yeddida.
Kiiteti bida asati biidi ista qasho keeththan demmibeetenna; simmidinne
“Qasho keeththay lo7ethi qulfeti dees; naagizaytikka penge bolla eqqi dishin beyidos; gido attin nu doy gelishin qas keeththan oonikka ba” gida.
Xoossa Keeththi naagizayta halaqaynne Qeeseta Halaqatika hessa siyida mala hanozan daro malaletidanne istas hanoy wuri tikki gides.
Heerakka issi asi yiidi “Hekko inte qasho keeththe gelthida asati Xoossa Keeththa gibbe giddon eqqidi dere tamarson deettes” gides.
Xoossa Keeththe naagizayta halaqay ba oosanchatara biidi ista oykki ekki yides. Oykki ehidaytti asay bana shuchchara caddonta mala babbidi wolqathonta loddara ehida.
Hawaareta ehidi Ayhuda duulata sinthan essida. Qeeseta halaqaykka ista “Hayssa ha sunthan inte tamarsonta mala intes lo7ethi yootidoskoshin inte inte timirteza Yerusalame ubban kuntheta. Qasse nunakka ha addeza suuthas oyshetizayta histanas gixxi dendideta” gides.
<range>
Phexroosinne hanko Hawaaretikka zaaridi “Nuni asappe aaththidi Xoossas azazettanas bessees.
“Inte iza mitha bolla kaqqi wodhida Yesusa nu aawanta Xoossay iza hayqoppe denthides.
Izikka Isra7eele naytas nagarappe simmidi maarettana mala Xoossi iza ubbafe bollanne ashshizade histidi ba ushachchan dhoqu dhoqu histides.
Nunikka hayssas markata. Qasseka Xoossi baas azazettiza oonaska immida Xillo Ayanaykka marka” gida.
Asati hessa siydi iita hanqo hanqettida. Wodhanakka koyda.
Gido attin dere achchan keehi bonchettida issi woga astamare, izikka Gamalyaale geetettiza Farsaaweeta baggay dere cimata giddon dendi eqqidi Hawaareti guuththa wode karen gam7ana mala azazides.
Dere cimatas hizgides “Isra7eele asato! Inte hayta asata bolla ooththanayssa daro akeekkara ooththanas bessees.
Hayssafe kase issi Tewoodaasa geetettizadey bana gita as histi qoodi dendin oyddu xeetu derey iza kaallides. Gido attin izi asa kushen hayqqides. Iza kaallizaytikka coo laalettin iza hanoy coo mela attides.
Izappe guyekka derey taybetiza wode Galila Yuhuday dendidi daro dere banara kaalethides. Bana kaallizaytaka demmides shin izikka dhayides. Iza kaallizaytikka wuri dhayida.
“Hessa gish ta ha7i intena gizay hayta asata aggite, bochchofte. Ista qofay woykko ista oosoy asappe gidikko dhayana.
Xoossafe gidikko qas inte ista teqanas dandayekketa. Oone erizay inte Xoossara oyeetishe beettanakkonne” gides.
Istika iza zoreza ekkidi Hawaareta xeygidi garafissida. Nam7antho Yesusa sunthan haasayonta mala azazidi yeddida.
Hawaaretikka iza suntha gish kawuyanas bessiza gish daro ufayetishe dere cimata achchafe kezi bida.
Gallas gallas Xoossa Keeththaninne issa issa keeththan Yesusi izi Xoossi dooridade gididayssa tamarsofenne sabakoppe mulekka guye gibeetenna.
Ammanizayta qooday dari dari biza wode Girike biittafe yida Ayhuda asati Yuhudan diza Ayhuda asa guyera zigirettida. Gaasoyka ubba wode miza kath gishishe am7eta wudetonta aggida gishassa.
Hessa gish nu tammanne nam7u Hawaareti ammaniza harata issi bolla shiishshidi “Nuni kaththa gishon gelidi Xoossa qaala tamarso agganas bessenna.
Hessa gish nu ishato! Inte giddofe eranchata, Xillo Ayanan kumidaytanne lo7o markateth diza laapun asata doorite; hayssa alafeteth nu istas immana.
Nuni gidikko woossaninne qaala yooton minnana” gida.
Isti gida yo7oy siyidayta ufaysides; Ammanoninne Xillo Ayanan kumidayti Istifanoose, Piliphoosa, Phirosqoroosa, Niqaroona, Ximoona, Pharmenanne Yuhudatethan gelida Anxokiya dere as Niqoloosa doorida.
Heyta ehidi Hawaareta sinth shiishida. Istika ba kushe ista bolla woththidi istas woossida.
Xoossa qaalay akki akki bides. Ammanizayta qooday Yerusalamen dari dari bides. Qeesetappe daroti ammanida.
He wode Istifanoossi Xoossa immotethaninne wolqan kumidi dereza giddon gita malalisiza malatata ooththides.
Wozeti kezida geetetti xeeygetizasoppe Ayhudata Woosa Keeththafe yida as gidida Qareenappenne Iskindiriyappe; qasseka Kilqiyappenne Iisiya awurajjatappe yida asatikka wuri Istifanoosera marshetida.
Gido attin eratethan izi haasayiza haasayanne izan diza Ayana eqqetanas dandayibeetenna.
Hessa gish “Istifanoossi Musenne Xoosse cayishin nu siyidos” giza asata guyera giigissida.
He wode dereza, dere cimatanne woga tamarsizayta dentheththidine Istifanoose oythidi dere duulatakko shiishida.
Iza bolla “Hayssi addezi hayssa Xoossa Keeththa bollanne woga bolla cashsha qaala haasaya mulekka aggibenna.
Gaasoyka hayssi addezi ‘Naazirete Yesusi hayssa Xoossa Keeththa dhayssana’ gishininne ‘Nu Museppe ekkida woga laammana’ gi haasayishin nu siyidos” gi wordora markattiza asata shiishshidi markasida.
Duulata uttida asay wuri Istifanoose tishshi histi xeellishin iza ayfesoy istas kiitancha ayfeso misati beettides.
Qeeseta halaqay Istifanoose “Hayssi ne bolla shiiqida yo7ozi tumee?” gi oychides.
Istifanoossika hizgides “Ta ishato! Ta aawato! Ta gizayssa siyite! Nu aawa Abrahaamey Kaarane geetettizaso yaanappe kase buro Mesopotoomiyan dishin boncho Goday izas qoncidi,
‘Ne dereppenne ne dabbofe shaaketada ta nena bessizaso ba’ gides.
Izikka Kaldaweta biittafe kezidi Kaarane geetettiza biittan uttides. Iza aaway hayqqidappe guye inte ha7i dizaso ha dere iza ehides.
Haray attoshin issi tohoy eqqiza gadey izas hayssafe immetibenna. Gido attin he wode izas issi naykka baynda dishin izinne izappe guyen iza zerethi Biittayo laattana mala Xoossi izas caqqides.
Qasseka Xoossi izas hizgi yootides ‘Ne zerethi allaga biittan bete as gidana. Oyddu xeetu layth aylletetha qambara giddon waayettana.
Gido attin ista aylle mala haariza dere ta qaxayana. Hessafe guye isti he biittafe kezidi hanno ha soyn taas goynnana’ gides.
Hessafe guye qaxxara woga caaqo izas immides. Abrahaameyka Yisaaqa yelidi iza ospuntha gallas qaxxarides. Yisaaqaykka Yaqoobe yelides. Yaqoobeykka tammanne nam7u qommota yelides.
“He qommota aawati Yoosefe bolla qanatidi iza aylletethas duge Gibxe bayzida. Gido attin Xoossi izara dees;
meto ubbafe iza ashshides. Gibxe kawo Paaroone sinthan boncho immides. Paarooney iza Gibxe biittaninne ba keeththa asa ubba bolla alafetethan shuumides.
“He wode Kanaaneninne Gibxen daro meto ehida gita koshay dendides. Nu aawataska miza kaththi dhayides.
Yaqoobey Gibxe deren kaththi dizayssa siydi nu aawata koyro Gibxe yeddides.
Isti nam7antho biza wode Yoosefey izi oonakkonne bana ba ishatas qoncisides. Paarooneykka Yoosefe ishata erides.
Hessafe guye Yoosefey kiittidi ba aawa Yaqoobenne laapun tammanne ichashu gidiza ba dabbota kumeth ehisides.
Yaqoobey duge Gibxe wodhdhides. Izikka nu aawatikka wuri heen hayqqida.
Ista ahaykka Seekeme geetettizaso efin Abrahaamey Eemoore naytappe ba miishan shammida duufon moogetides.
“Xoossi Abrahaames caaqida qaalay poletiza wodey matishin Gibxen diza nu asa qooday dari dari bides.
Hessafe guye Gibxe biittan Yoosefe eronta hara kawoy kawotides.
Izikka nu asa ba gene ooson metothides. Buro yelettida guutha nayti hayqqana malanne yelida nayta kare kessi wora yeggana mala wolqathides.
He wode Musey yeletides. Izikka Xoossa achchan dosettida mala lo7o naa gidides. Ba aawa keeththan heedzdzu agina al7isson diccides.
Izi gede wora yegetida wode kawo Paaroone maca naya demmada baas ekkadus. Ba naa mala ooththada dichchadus.
Museykka Gibxeta aadhdho eratetha wursi tamarides. Yo7on era; oosonka mino gidides.
“Muse laythi oyddu tammu gidida wode Musey ba ishata Isra7eele nayta beyanas ba woznan qoppides.
Izikka issi Gibxe asi Muse bagga asappe issade bolla qoho gaththishin beyidi ba bagga addeza maadides; he Gibxe addeza wodhidi he qohetidayssa halo kessides.
Muses Xoossi iza kushen ista wozanayssa iza asay akeekkiza misatides. Gido attin isti hessa yuushi qoppibetenna.
Wontetha gallas qasseka Isra7eele naytappe nam7ati ba giddon oyeetishin gakkidi oyeetizayta giigissanas koydi ‘Hayto! Asato inte inte giddon ishantakko; inte waanidi issoy issa qoheetii?’ gides.
“Ba laggeza bolla qoho gaththidayssi Muse sugi yeggidi ‘Nena nu bolla nuna haarizadenne nu bolla pirdizade ooththi shuumiday oonee? Woykko qamma Gibxe addeza wodhoyssatho tanakka wodhana koyay?’ gides.
<range>
Musey hessa siyida mala Midiyaame biitta beettidi heen bete as gidi de7ides; Yaanka nam7u attuma naa yelides.
“Hessafe oyddu tammu laythafe guye Siina zuma achchan diza bazzo biittan qeeri wora giddon eexiza tama lacon kiitanchay izas beettides.
Museykka iza beyida mala malaletides. Azakkonne shaakki eranas izi heen izakko shiiqishin Goda qaalay ‘Tani ne aawanta Xoossa Abrahaame, Yisaaqanne Yaqoobe Xoossa’ gishin siydes. Museykka daro daggamides; xeellanaska xalibenna.
<range>
“Godayka izas ‘Hayssi ne eqqidasoy geeshshaso gidida gish ne tohoppe caamma shodda. Gibxen diza ta dereta waaye ta tumappe beyadis; isti waassiza waaye waasoza ta siyada ista ashshanas wodhdhadis. Ne ha7ikka haaya; ta nena duge Gibxe zaarada kiitana’ gides.
<range>
“Histin heyti ‘Nu bolla nena haarizadenne pirdizade histi ooni shuumidee?’ giidi asay kase kadhida Muse Xoossi qeeri wora giddon izas bettida kiitancha baggara ista haarizadenne ashshizade histidi istako zaari yeddides.
Izikka ista kaalethidi Gibxeppe kessides. Gibxen, Zo7o Abbaninne bazzo biittan oyddu tammu laythi daro malalisiza miishatanne gita malatata istas ooththides.
“Isra7eele naytas ‘Ta mala nabe Xoossi inte giddofe denthana’ gidayssi hayssa Musekko!
Izikka Siina zuma bolla haasayida kiitancharanne bazzo biittan nu aawatara dere duulata giddon dees. De7o qaalakka ha nuus aaththanas ekkides.
“Nu Aawati gidikko izara eqqetida attin izas azazettanas koyonta gish ba woznara guye Gibxe simmida.
Aaroneska ‘Nu sinthara biza eeqa nuus giigissa! Nuna Gibxeppe kaalethi kessida Musey waanidakko nu erokko’ gida.
He wode mara misile medhidi eeqas yarsho shiishida. Barka medhdhida ba kushe ooson ufayetidi guppida.
“Gido attin Xoossi istas zokko zaarides. Isti salo xoolintetas goynnana mala aaththi immides. Hessika nabeta maxaafan ‘Inteno Isra7eele nayto! Inte bazzo biittan oyddu tammu layth diza wode intefe yarshonne muxuwata taas shiishshi eretii?
Harappeka inte goynnanaso ooththida eeqa Molooke dunkananne inte eeqa Rafaanne xoolinte misileza dhoqu dhoqu histi oykkideta. Hessa gish ta intena inte dizasoppe denthada Babiloonera aaththa yeddana’ geetettidi xaafettides.
“Xoossi Muse bessida leemisoza malanne azazidayssa mala oosettida Xoossi asara gaaggiza dunkaneya nu aawatara bazzo biittan de7adus.
Nu Aawati dunkaneyo ekkidayssafe guye Xoossi Iyaaso kaaleththin kase ista gooddida dereta laattida wode dunkaneyo ekki geellida. Dawute wode gakkanaas dunkaneya he biittan de7adus.
Dawuteykka Xoossa sinthan boncho demmidi Yaqoobe Godas aqoso giigissanas woossides.
Gido attin Solomooney izas aqqoso keexxides.
“Gido attin wogga Goday asa kushey keexida keeththan deenna. Hessika nabey kase Geeshsha maxaafan xaafetida mala ‘Saloy ta uttiza alga; biittaykka ta tohon yedhdhizaso; histin inte taas ay mala keeththe keexxetii? woykko ta shempanasoy awayssee? Hayssa wursi ta kushey ooththibenee?’ gees Goday Xoossay.
<range>
<range>
“Inteno wozna muumeto! Haytha tulleto! Inteka inte aawata mala ubba wode Xillo Ayanara eqetteta.
Nabetappe inte Aawati gooddonta nabey oonee? Xilloza Yohannisa kaseti yootida nabetaka wodhida; inteka ha7i iza aaththi immidetanne wodhideta.
Kiitancha baggara intes imettida woga ekkideta attin naagibeekketa” gides.
Duulatan diza asay hessa siyida mala daro hanqettidi, iza bolla ba achchi garcides.
Gidinka Istifanoosi Xillo Ayanan kumidinne pude salo tishshi histi xeellishin Xoossa bonchon Yesusi Xoossa ushachchan eqqidayssa beyidi “Hekko ta saloy doyettidayssanne Asa Nay Xoossa ushachchan eqqidayssa beyays” gides.
<range>
Hessa wode asay qaala dhoqu histi waassishe ba haythe tucci oykidi izakko issife woxxides.
Istifanoose oykkidi katamappe gede kare olida. Shuchchan cach oykkida. Hessi wuri hanishin markatikka ba may7o Sawule geetettiza paantha achchan woththida.
Isti shuchchara iza caddishin Istifanoossi “Ta Goda Yesusaa ta shempoyo neekko ekka” giidi woossides.
Qasseka gulbatidi dhoqa qaalan “Godo! Haytanta nagara qoodoppa” giidi waassides. Hessa gidappe guye hayqqides.
Sawuleykka Istifanoose hayqon istara qofan gaaggides. He wode Yerusalamen diza ammanizayta bolla gita goodeteththi dendides. Hawaareti attaafe ammanizayti wuri Yuhuda awurajjaninne Samaariya awurajjan ubban laalettida.
Ayana ooson minni eqqida asati Istifanoose moogidi, izas daro yeekkida.
Sawuley qasse Woosa Keeththa dhayssanas gixxi dendides. Ammaniza asa issa issa keeththe gelidi macatanne addeta goochchi goochchi kessidi qasho keeththan gelthides.
Laalettidayti wuri ba bidason bidason Xoossa qaala yootida.
Piliphoosikka Samaariya geetettiza katama wodhdhidi asas Kirstoosa sabakides.
Daro derey Piliphoosi ooththiza malata beyidi izi yootiza qaala woznappe lo7ethi siydes.
Tuna ayanatikka daro asappe waassi waassi kezida. Daro toho silatinne wobetikka paxida.
Hessa gish he katama asay daro ufayetides.
Gido attin hessafe kase he katamayin maro marotidi Samaariya asa daro malalisizaz ooththiza issi Simoona geetettiza maroy dees. Izikka bana gita asa mala qoodizade.
Asay wuri guuthatappe gitata gakkanaas wurikka “Hayssi addezi gita wolqama geetettiza Xoossa wolqa” gishe izi gizayssa wursi woznappe siyees.
Daro wode ba marotetha ooson asa malalisida gish asay iza woznappe kaallishe gam7ides.
Gido attin Piliphoosi Xoossa Kawoteththa gishshinne Yesus Kirstoosa gish sabakidayssa siydi ammanida macasaynne attumasay xammaqetides.
Simoonikka ammanidi xammaqetides. Piliphoosakka kaalli biidi haniza gita malata beyidi malalettides.
Yerusalamen diza Hawaareti Samaariya asay Xoossa qaala ekkidi ammanidayssa siydi Phexroosanne Yohannisa Istako kiittida.
Istika Samaariya gakkidi ammanida asay Xillo Ayana ekkana mala asas woossida.
Gaasoyka he wode isti coo Yesusa sunthan xammaqetida attin buro Xillo Ayanay istafe issade bollakka wodhdhibenna.
Hessa gish Phexroosinne Yohannisi ba kushe asa bolla woththin asay Xillo Ayana ekkides.
Simoonikka Hawaareti kushe woththi woossin Xillo Ayanay imettizayssa beyidi Phexroosasinne Yohannisas miishe ekki yiidi,
“Ta iza bolla ta kushe woththizadey wuri Xillo Ayana ekkana mala hayssa mala godateth taaska immite” giin,
Phexroosi izas zaaridi “Xoossa imota ne miishan shammana qoppida gish neni ne miishara issife dhaya.
Ne woznay Xoossa sinthan suure gidonta gish nees hayssa ha oosozan gishay woykko qaaday deenna.
Hayssa ne iitatetha gish ha7i elle maarotethan gela; ne wozna qofa nees atto gaanakkonne nees Goda woossa.
Gaasoyka neni iitatethan kumidayssinne makalan qasheta uttidayssi taas beettees” gides.
Simoonikka zaaridi “Inte gida yo7otappe aykkoykka ta bolla gakkonta mala taas Goda woossite” gides.
Phexroosinne Yohannisi Goda qaala markattidayssafenne qoncisi yootidayssafe guye daro Samaariya gutatan mishiraachcho qaala sabakishe Yerusalame simmida.
Goda kiitanchay Piliphoosa “Denda! Yerusalameppe duge baggara gede Gaaza efiza bazzo ogara ba” gides.
Izikka dendi bides. Hindeko geetettiza Tophiyappe gidida kawoya ba keeththaninne ba kawoteththan diza ubba miisha bolla alafetethan woththida issi Tophiya gundula asi izara gaaggides. He addezi Xoossas goynnana Yerusalame bides.
Izi heeppe simmishe para-gaaren uttidi nabe Isayaasa maxaafa nababes.
Ayanay Piliphoosa “Ba! Gede para-gaarezakko shiiqa” gides.
Piliphoosikka eesotidi para-gaarezakko biidi addezi nabe Isayaasa maxaafa nababishin siydi “Hessi ne nababizayssi nees gelizee?” gides.
Gundula addezikka “Tana erisiza asi baynda ta wosta eroo?” gides. Izikka gede iza gaarezan geldi iza achchan uttana mala woossides.
Izi nababiza maxaafay “Izi dorsa mala shukettana laagettides; dorsa laaqay isike qanxizayssa sinthan co7u giza mala hessathoka izi ba duuna pogibenna.
Bana kawushshidi pirday bayndade gidides. Iza shempoy biitta bollafe diggettides. Iza yeletetha gish haasayana dandayizay oonee?” gees.
Gundula addezikka zaaridi Piliphoosa “Nabezi hayssa oona gish gizee? Ba gish gizeyee? Woykko hara asa gish gizee? Hayana, taas yootarki!” gides.
Piliphoosikka ba duuna doydi he maxaafappe doommidi Yesusa Mishiraachcho qaala gish markattides.
Isti issife bishe haaththi dizaso gakkida. Addezikka “Hekko haaththi hayssan dees; histin ta xammaqetonta mala diggizay aazee?” gides.
Piliphoosikka “Ne kumeththa woznappe ammanikko xammaqettana dandayassa” gides. Addezikka “Yesus Kirstoosi Xoossa Naa gididayssa ammanays” gides.
Addezi para gaarezi eqqana mala azazin nam7ay issife haaththan wodhdhin Piliphoosi addeza xammaqides.
Isti haaththafe kezishin Xoossa Ayanay Piliphoosa denthi efides. Addezi hessafe guye iza beybenna. Gido attin ufayssan ba oge bides.
Hessafe guye Piliphoosi Azaxoone geetettizason beettides. Qisaariya geetettizaso gakkanaas izi biza oge bolla kataman ubban mishiraachcho qaala sabakides.
Sawuley Goda ammaniza asa wodhanas ceeqqettishe Qeeseta halaqakko bides.
Goda oge kaallizayta macasatanne addeta demmi qachidi Yerusalame ekki yaanas Damasqo geetettizason diza Ayhudata Woosa Keeththas babdaabe xaafana mala Qeeseta halaqa woossides.
Damasqo gakkana matishin qopponta saloppe poo7oy iza yuushon pol7u gides.
Izikka heerakka biitta bolla kundidi saloppe “Sawule, Sawule, tana aazas goodday?” giza qaala siydes.
Sawuleyka “Godo! Ne oonee?” gides. Izikka izas “Tani ne goodeththiza Yesusakko!”
“Ne ha7i dendada gede katama gela; ne ooththanas bessizaz nees ta yootana” gides.
Sawulera issife biza asati qaala giiris sissafe attin oonakka beyonta gish ba duuna oykki eqqida.
Sawuley ba kundidasoppe dendidi ayfe doyi xeelliza wode aykkokka demmanas dandaybenna. Hessa gish izara diza asati iza kushe oykkidi kaalethi ekkidi Damasqo efida.
Heedzdzu gallas gakkanaas qooqidinne kath haaththe beybenna.
Damasqon issi Hananiya geetettiza ammanizadey dees. Izas Goday ajjutan “Hananiya” giidi xeygides; izikka “Yee Godo!” gides.
Godayka iza “Denda! Suure geetettiza ogeyra Yuhuda geetettizaso ba. Heen Sawule geetettiza issi Xarseese asi woossishe dees; ne iza koya demma.
Gaasoyka Hananiya geetettizayssi Sawuley dizaso yiidi izi xeellana mala iza bolla ba kushe woththishin ajjutan beyides.”
Hananiyaykka zaaridi “Godo! Hayssadey Yerusalamen diza geeshshata bolla ay mala iita meto gaththidakkonne ta daro asappe siyadis.
Izi haa yiday ne suntha xeygizayta wursi qachanas Qeeseta halaqatappe godateth ekkidikko” gides.
Godayka izas “Ne ba! Hayssi addezi Ayzaabeta sinthaninne kawota sinthan hessathoka Isra7eele dere sinthan ta sunth tookkana mala izi taas doorettidayssa.
Izi ta suntha gish ay mala waaye beyanakko ta iza bessana” gides.
Hananiyay biidi izas yootetidaso gelides. Sawule bolla ba kushe woththidi “Ta isha Sawule ne ha yishin nees oge bolla qoncida Goda Yesusi ne ayfey xeellana malanne neni Xillo Ayanan kumana mala tana neekko kiittides” gides.
Heerakka Sawule ayfeppe poqo malay poqeti wodhdhin izi xeellana dandayidessinne dendidi xammaqetides.
Kaththikka miidi minnides. Undena wode ammanizaytara Damasqon gam7ides.
Heerakka Yesusi Xoossa Naa gididayssa Ayhudata Woosa Keeththatan tamarso oykkides.
Siyida asay wuri “Hayssi Yerusalamen ha suntha xeygizayta dhayissiza addeza gidenee? Qasse izi ha yiday he asata qachi ekki Qeeseta Halaqatakko efanas deenee?” gishe malaletida.
Sawuley kaseppe minni minni bides. Damasqon diza Ayhudatas Yesusi izi Xoossi kiittidade gididayssa ammanthishe asa duuna oythides.
Daro gallassatappe guye Ayhudati Sawule wodhanas duulatida.
Izikka ista qofa erides. Istika iza wodhanas katama gelthiza ogen gallassinne qamma naagida.
Ammanizayti gidikko iza gidoth katama yuushon diza maskotezara keeshen duge woththida.
Sawuley Yerusalame yiidi ammanizaytara walakkettana koyin izi tumu ammanizade gididayssa isti ammanetonta gish izas babbida.
Gido attin Barnabaassi iza Hawaaretakko efin Sawuley izi Damasqo oge bolla Goda wosti beyidakko, Godayka izas ay yootidakkonne qasseka Damasqon dishe izi ay mala xalateththara Yesusa sunthan sabakidakko istas yootides.
Hessa gish Sawuley istara dides. Yerusalamen yuuyi yuuyi as babbonta Goda sunthan tamarsides.
Girike dereppe yida Ayhudatara haasayshe palametides; gido attin asaykka iza wodhanas koyides.
Ammanizayti hessa eridi duge Qisaariya geetettizaso woththidi Xarseese yeddida.
Hessa wode Yuhudaninne Galilan, Samaariyanka diza ammanizayti saron diidi kaseppe minnida. Qasseka Xoossa yashshatethan simeretishe Xillo Ayanan minetidanne kaseppe qoodan dari dari bida.
Phexroosi dereppe deren yuuyishe Liida kataman diza ammanizayta beyanas duge wodhdhides.
Heen Eniya geetettizayssa osupun layth hiixan qasheti uttida issi gunda as demmides.
Phexroosikka “Haysso Eniya! Yesus Kirstoosi nena pathana; denda ne hiixa dentha!” gides. Eniyay heerakka pusuku gi dendides.
Liidaninne Saroonan diza asay wuri iza beyidi Godan ammanides.
Iyophphe geetettizason Xaabita geetettiza issi ammanizara dawus. Izi suntha birsheththi Girike qaalara “Dorqa” geetettes. Iza ubba wode lo7o ooso minna ooththashenne manqota maaddashe dawus.
He wode iza hargada hayqqin asay aha meeci pude pooqen kessi woththides.
Liiday Iyophphes mata gidida gish ammanizayti Phexroosi Liidan dizayssa siydi nam7u asata kiittidi “Elle ha yarki!” gi woossida.
Phexroosikka dendidi kiitettida asatara gakkida wode iza pude he pooqe bolla kessida. Am7etikka wuri iza yuuyi aadhdhi eqqidi Dorqay paxa dashe istara ooththida qamisetanne may7ota bessishe yeekkida.
Phexroosikka asa wursi kiflezappe kessidi gulbati woossides. Ahakko simmidi “Hanne Xaabita denda!” gides. Izakka ba ayfe doyada xeelladus. Phexroosakka beyada denda uttadus.
Izikka izi kushe oykki denthides. Ammanizaytanne am7eta xeygidi izo istas pathidi immides.
He hanoy kumeththa Iyophphen eretidesinne daro asayka Goda ammanides.
Phexroosikka issi Simoona geetettiza galba qaacizadera Iyophphen daro wode de7ides.
Qisaariya geetettiza deren “Xaalane wotadarata” issi butte giddon mato halaqa gidida issi Qornoloosa geetettizayssi dees.
Izikka ba keeththa asa kumeththara Ayana hanon minonne Xoosse babbizadde; manqotaska daro muxuwata immizadenne daro wode Xoosse woossiza asa.
Issi gallas gallassafe uddufun saate bolla Xoossa kiitanchay izas ajjutan beettidi izakko yiidi “Qornoloosa” gi xeygishin qoncen beyides.
Qornoloosikka dagamara tishshi histi xeellishe “Godo hayssi aazee?” gides. Kiitanchaykka zaaridi “Ne woossaynne ne muxuwatay qofetanas pude Xoossa sinth gakkides.
Ne ha7i as Iyophphe yedada Phexroosa geetettiza Simoona xeygisa.
Izikka abba matan diza galba qaaciza Simoona soon imathateth dees” gides.
Qornoloosa haasayssida kiitanchay izappe shaaketidi bidappe guye ba ashkaratappe nam7ata qasse Ayana yo7os minone izas daro ammanettiza wotadaratappe issa xeygisidi,
izi beyidayssa wursi istas yootidi Iyophphe kiittides.
Kiitettida asati wontetha gallas gede katamaykko matishin Phexroosi usuppun saate bolla woossana pude Pooqe bolla kezides.
Hessa wode izi gafida gish qumay buro kaxxishin dhisko mala liphiphi histin ajjutara saloy doyettin issi gita xaaxettida may7o malay oyddu baggara oyketidi duge biittan wodhdhishin beyides.
<range>
He may7oza bolla oyddu tohoy diza dumma dumma do7ati biittara gooshettiza medhetethatinne salo bolla piradhiza kafoti deettes.
Hessa wode “Phexroosa denda hayta shukada ma” giza qaalay izas siyetides.
Phexroosi qasse “Godo hayssi hanenna! Geesh gidontayssa woykko tuna miisha ta mulerakka ma erikke” gides.
He kase qaalay qasseka nam7antho izakko yiidi “Xoossi geeshshidayssa ne tuna mala qoodoppa” gides.
Hessika heedzdzuto shireti shireti izakko yidappe guye may7o misatizayssi heerakka pude salo bides.
Phexroosikka ba beyida ajjutaza birsheththa eranas daro metotidi keehi qofo bolla dishin Qornoloosi kiittida asati Simoona keeththe koyishe demmidi pengen eqqida.
Qaala dhoqu histidi “Phexroosa geetettiza Simooni dizasoy hayssan awanee?” gi oychida.
Phexroosi ba beyidayssa keehi qoppishin Xillo Ayanay iza “Hekko heedzdzu asati nena koyeetes. Denda! Duge wodhdhada ista yeddiday tana gidida gish sidhey baynda istara ba” gides.
<range>
Phexroosikka duge wodhdhidi “Hekko inte koyizadey tanakko! Inte yiday aazasee?” gides.
Istika izas “Nuni mato halaqa Qornoloosa matappe yidos. Izikka Xoossas babbiza xillo asanne Ayhuda asa ubba matan daro bonchettida asa. Nekka iza keeththe baana malanne ne gizayssa izi siyana mala geeshsha kiitanchay izas yootides” gida.
Phexroosikka asata ba dizason mokki ekkidi ayssides. Phexroosikka wontetha gallas dendidi istara bides. Iyophphefe yida issi issi ammaniza asati izara issife bida.
Qornoloosikka ba dabbotanne mata laggeta ba soon shiishshidi naago bolla dishin izi nam7antho gallas Qisaariya gakkides.
Phexroosikka gede Qornoloosa keeththe gelin Qornoloossi iza mokki ekkidi iza toho bolla hokki goynnides.
Gido attin Phexroosi “Takka ne mala asakko! Denda” giidi denthides.
Phexroosikka iza haasayssishe izara so gelishin daro derey shiiqi uttidayssa beyides.
Izikka istas “Ayhuda asi hara dere asara gaaggonta mala woykko hara dere as gididayta mata shiiqonta mala nu wogay diggizayssa inte ereeta. Gido attin ta oonakka tuna woykko izi geesh deenna goonta mala Xoossi taas qoncisides.
Hessa gish ta xeeygetida wode hekko sidhonta yadis. Histin inte tana aazas xeygidakkone erana koyays” gides.
Qornoloosikka “Oyddu gallassafe kase likke hanni wode gallassafe uddufun saaten tani ta soon woossishin qopponta booththa may7o may7ida asi yiidi ta sinthan eqqidi
tana ‘Qornoloosa! Ne woossay siyetides; ne manqotas immiza muxuwatay Xoossa sinthi gakkides.
Hessa gish Iyophphe katama as kiittada Phexroosa geetettiza Simoona ehissa. Izi abba achchan galba qaaciza Simoona keeththan imathateth dees’ gides.
Takka heerakka neekko as kiittadis. Ne yuussaykka lo7o. Histikko Goday nena azazidayssa ne nuus yootikko Xoossi yootidayssa neeppe siyanas nu wurikka hayssan Xoossa sinthan doos” gides.
Phexroosikka “Xoossi oonaka shaakki maadontayssa ta tumappe eradis.
Gido attin Xoossas babbizaytanne xillo ooththizayta wursi oona baggafe gidinka izi ekkees.
Xoossi ubbas Goda gidida Yesus Kirstoosa baggara Isra7eele asas kiittida sarotetha Mishiraachcho kiitay hayssa.
Yohannisi xinqata gish sabakidappe guyen Galilappe doommidi kumeththa Yuhudan hanidayssa inte ereeta.
Xoossi Naazirete Yesusa Xillo Ayananinne wolqan tiyides. Izikka Xoossi izara diza gish ba gakkidason ubban lo7o ooththishe Xala7e godateththa giddon dizayta wursi pathides.
“Izi Ayhudata dereninne Yerusalame kataman ooththidayssa ubbas nu marka. Qasseka asay iza mitha bolla kaqqi wodhides.
Gido attin Xoossi iza heedzdzantho gallas heyqoppe denthidessinne asi iza beyana mala ooththides.
Izi qonciday asa ubbas gidonta hayqoppe dendin izara midaytassinne izara uyidaytas Xoossi koyro doorida nuus iza markatassa.
Izi nu derezas sabakana malanne hayqqidayta bollanne paxa dizayta bolla pirdanas Xoossi shuumiday iza gididayssa nu markattana mala nuna azazides.
Iza ammanidadey wuri iza sunthan nagara maaretidi geeyanayssa nabeti izas markatettes” gi yooto doommides.
Phexroosi hessa haasayishin qaala siyizayta ubba bolla Xillo Ayanay wodhdhides.
Qaxxaretidayta baggafe Phexroosara yida ammanizayti Xillo Ayana imotethi Ayzaabeta bolla wodhdhishin beyidi malaletida.
Hessika isti dumma qaalan haasayishininne Xoossa galatishin siyida gishassa. He wode Phexroosi,
“Hayti asati nu mala Xillo Ayana ekkida gish isti haaththan xammaqetonta mala ista digganay oonnee?” gides.
Hessa gish Yesus Kirstoosa sunthan xammaqettana mala azazides. Hessafe guye Phexroosi guuththa wode istara daana mala woossida.
Hawaaretinne Yuhudan diza ammanizayti Ayzaabeti Xoossa qaala ekkidayssa siyida.
Hessa gish Phexroosi pude Yerusalame kezin qaxxaretida Ayhudappe ammanizayti Phexroosa,
“Ne qaxxaretonta asata keeth gelada istara kath madasa” giidi walassida.
Phexroosi qasse istas gelana mala maarara hizgi yootides.
“Tani Iyophphe kataman woossishin dhisikko mala tana liphiphi histidi ajjutan gita may7o misatiza miishi oyddu baggara oyketidi saloppe ta dizaso wodhdhishin beyadis.
Ta tishshi hista xeellishin oyddu tohora diza meheta, wora do7ata, biitta bolla gooshettiza medhetethatanne salo bolla piradhiza kafota beyadis.
Heerakka tana ‘Phexroosa denda! Hayssa shukada ma’ giza qaala siyadis.
“Takka ‘Godo hessi hanenna; tani tuna woykko geesh gidontayssa mulekka ta duunakko shiisha erikke’ gadis.
“He kase qaalay qasseka ‘Xoossi geeshidayssa ne tunisoppa’ giidi saloppe taas yootides.
Hessika heedzdzuto shireti shireti yootetidappe guye wurikka simmidi pude salo bides.
“Qisaariyappe taakko kiitettida heedzdzu asati heerakka he saateyn yi gakkidi ta diza keeththa karen eqqida.
Ta aynne sidhonta istara baana mala Xillo Ayanay taas yootides. He usuppun ishati tanara issife biidi addeza keeththe geldos.
Izikka Xoossa kiitanchay iza keeththan eqqidi izas beettidayssanne ‘Iyophphe geetettizaso as yeddada Phexroosa geetettiza Simoona xeygisa.
Izi yiidi nenanne neso asa wursi ashshana qaala yootana’ gidayssa nuus yootides.
“Takka baada buro yooto oykkishin koyro Xillo Ayanay kase nu bolla wodhdhoyssatho ista bollaka wodhdhides.
Kase Goday nuus yootishe ‘Yohannisi haaththan xammaqides shin inte Xillo Ayanan xammaqettana’ gida qaalay heerakka taas qofetides.
Hessa gish nuni Goda Yesus Kirstoosa ammanishin nuus immida Xillo Ayana Xoossi istas immikko histin Xoossara eqqetanas tani oonee?” gides.
Isti hessa siyida wode istas gizazi dhayin co7u gi simmidi “Hayssa mala gidikko Ayzaabetikka ha ooratha de7okko yaana mala Xoossi asas maaroteth immides guussa” giidi Xoossa galatida.
Istifanoose bolla dendida goodeteththa gaason laalettida ammaniza asay qaala Ayhudatas xalala yootishe Pinqe, Qophiroosenne Anxokiya geetettizaso gakkanaas kanthi bida.
Qophirooseppenne Qareenappe yida issi issi asati Anxokiya biidi Giriketasikka Goda Yesusa Mishiraachcho qaala yootida.
Goda maadoykka istara dees; Qoodan keehi daro asay ammanidi Godakko simmides.
Hessa woreykka Yerusalamen diza Woosa Keeththa asa haythan wodhdhin Woosa Keeththaya Barnabaasa Anxokiya yeddadus.
Izikka he bi gakkidi Xoossi ba aadho kiyateth deraas immidayssa beyidi ufayetidessinne asay wurikka kumeththa woznappe Goda ammanon minnana mala zorides.
Izikka Xillo Ayananinne ammanon kumida lo7o asa. Daro derey Goda ammanon gujettides.
Hessafe kaallidi Barnabaassi Sawule koyana Xarseese bides.
Iza demmidi Anxokiya ekki yides. Nam7aykka heen diza Woosa Keeththa asara gididi layth kumeth daro dere tamarsida. Heen Anxokiyan ammanizayti koyro “Kirsaane” geetetti xeeygetida.
He wode issi issi nabeti Yerusalameppe duge Anxokiya wodhdhida.
Ista giddofe issoy Agaboossa geetettizayssi dendi eqqidi Xillo Ayanay iza bessin alame ubban gita koshay dendanayssa yootides. Hessika Oroome kawo Qalawodosa Qeesare geetettizayssa kawoteththa wode poletides.
Ammanizayti wuri issoy issoy ba wolqa keena miishe kesettidi Yuhudan diza ammaniza ishata maaddanas qachida.
Maado miisha kesettidi Barnabaasanne Sawule kushen cimatas gaththana mala yeddida.
He wode kawo Herdoossi issi issi ammaniza asa gooddi gooddi metothides.
Yohannisa isha Yaqoobe mashshan wodhisides.
Izikka hessa ooththiday Ayhudata ufaysidayssa beyidi Phexroosakka oythides. Hessika haniday Ayhudatas uketha ba7aale geetettiza ba7aale gallassa.
Phexroosakka qasho keeththe gelsidappe guye oyddu oyddu wotadarati taran taran naagana mala giigettida wotadaratas immides. Izi hessatho ooththiday Paaziga ba7aaley aadhdhida mala kessidi derey pirdana mala shiishanaasa.
Hessa gish Phexroosa qasho keeththe gelsidi naagetes. Gido attin Woosa Keeththa asay izas keehi mino woossa woossides.
Herdoossi Phexroosa dereza sinth shiishana qoppi utti dishin he qamma gidoth nam7u sansalatan qashetidi nam7u wotadarata giddon ichchides. Qasho keeththa naagizayti keeththa penge bolla eqqi naagishin,
Goda kiitanchay ezigonta istas beettides. Isti diza kifilen poo7oy poo7ides. Kiitanchazikka Phexroosa mille bochchi beeggoththidi “Elle denda!” gides. Heerakka sansalatay iza kusheppe gaden wodhdhides.
Kiitanchazi iza “Ne may7o may7a! Caammakka aaththa!” giin Phexroosikka azazettida mala ooththides; qasseka kiitanchay “Ne gaabe may7ada tana kaalla” gides.
Phexroosikka qasho keeththafe iza kaalli kezides. Gido attin izas agumo beyiza misatides attin kiitanchazi ooththizayssi tumu gididayssa eribenna.
Koyro zabetappenne nam7antho zabetappe aadhdhidi gede katama kessiza oge bolla diza birata pengako gakkida. Pengeykka barka doyetti wodhdhides. Isti kezi bida. Isti qeeri oge dizaaro aadhdhida mala kiitanchazi izappe shaaketides.
Phexroosas kahay simmishin “Goday ba kiitancha kiittidi iza Herdoosa kusheppenne Ayhudati ta bolla qoppida ubbafe tana kessidayssa ta ha7i tumappe eradis” gides.
Hessa akeekki eridappe guye daro asay issi bolla shiiqetidi woossiza Marqoosa geetettiza Yohannisa aayo Maaramiso bides.
Izi he biidi kare penge qooxin issi Roodo geetettiza garadeya kare ooni qoxxizakkonne eranas kare mata badus.
Qaalay Phexroosayssa gididayssa erada keeha ufayetida gish kare doyonta wothan guye simmada “Phexroosi Karen penge bolla eqqides” gadus.
Asaykka izo “Hanne gooyay!” gida. Iza qas zaara zaara istas yootin “Histikko hessi iza naagiza kiitancha gidonta aggenna” gida.
Phexroosi qas penge qoth gujjides. Istika penga doydi iza beyida mala malalettida.
Izikka isti co7u gaana mala ba kushen malati bessidi Goday iza qashosoppe wosti kessidakkonne lo7ethi yootides. “Hayssa wursi Yaqoobesinne hanko ammanizaytas yootite” gides. Hessafekka gede haraso bides.
Wontetha gallas wontara wotadarati “Phexroosi waanidee?” gishe ba giddon bul7akettida.
Herdoossi Phexroosa as yeddi koysidi izi dhayida gish naagizayta lo7ethi oychidappe guye ista wodhana mala azazides. Hessafe guye Herdoossi Yuhudappe duge Qisaariya wodhdhidi heen uttides.
Herdoosikka Xiroose asaranne Sidoona asara oosha. He dere asay kath demmizay Herodossa dereppe gidida gish he dere kawo xeellizade Bilasxoosappe maado qaala demmida mala issi bolla gididi Herdoosara maqaynthanas oychida.
Giigana barettida gallas Herdoossi kawoteththa may7o may7idi kawoteththa algan uttidi deraas haasayides.
Derezikka “Hayssi Xoossa qaalappe attin asa qaala deenna!” gi waassides.
Herdoosikka Xoossas boncho immoonta aggida gish Goda kiitanchay heerakka Herdoosa shoci yeggin guxuni hayqqides.
Xoossa qaalay gidikko diccidi akki akki bides.
Barnabaassinne Sawuley ba ekki bida kiita polidi Yerusalame simmidi Marqoosa geetettiza Yohannisaka banara ekki simmida.
Anxokiyan diza Woosa Keeththan nabetinne astamareti deettes. Heytikka Barnabaassinne Negeere geetettiza Simoonara, Qareena dere as Luqiyoosara, Herdoosara issife dicida Minaheranne Sawulera wuri issife deettes.
Heyti wuri Godas goynnishenne xoomishe dishin Xillo Ayanay “Barnabaasanne Sawule ta ista xeygida oosos taas shaakki kessite” gides.
Istika xoomi woossidi ba kushe ista bolla woththidappe guye moyzida.
Barnabassinne Sawuley Xillo Ayana kiitan duge Selawuqiya wodhdhida; heeppeka markaben geellidi Qophiroose bida.
Salmeena geetettizaso gakkidi Ayhudata Woosa Keeththatan Xoossa qaala sabakida; Marqoosa geetettiza Yohannisikka istara biidi ista maaddides.
Abba giddon diza biitta Qophiroose geetettiza dereyo ha gaxappe he gaxa gakkanaas kanthi kezidi Phaafa geetettizaso gakkishin issi Ayhuda asa shin maronne wordo nabe Bar-Yesusa geetettiza as demmida.
Izikka issi Sargoosa Phawuloosa geetettiza woznama dere ayssizayssara issife dees. Ha dere ayssiza addezi Xoossa qaala siyana koydi Barnabaasanne Sawule xeygisides.
Marozi Ellimaassi ba suntha birsheththa mala dere ayssizayssi ammanonta mala dhuphanas koydi istara eqqetides.
Phawuloosa geetettida Sawuley Xillo Ayanay izan kumin maroza tishshi histi xeelidi,
“Neno xillotetha ubbas morkezo! Geneynne iitatethi nenan kumidaysso haysso dabuloosa nawu! Goda suure oge geellaseththafe shempikii?
Hekko ha7i Goda kushey ne bolla dees. Ne qooqana; hannife guye awa arshe poo7o Issinokka beyakka” gides. Heerakka shaarumaynne dhumay iza bolla wodhdhides. Kushe oykki bana kaalethanade koshshi yaanne haanne gides.
Dere ayssizayssi ha hanida yo7oza beyidi goda gish siyida timirten malaletidi ammanides.
Phawuloosinne izara dizayti Phaafappe dendidi Phinfiliya geetettizason diza Phergene geetettizaso markaben geli bida; Yohannisi istafe shaaketidi guye Yerusalame simmides.
Isti gidikko Phergeneppe dendidi Phissidiya giddon diza gede Anxokiya bida; Sambata gallas Ayhudata woossa keeth geli uttida.
Muse woga maxaafatinne nabeta maxaafati nababetidappe guye Ayhudata Woosa Keeththa halaqati “Nu ishato! Intes hayssa asa zorana qaalay diikko haasayte” giidi istako ase yeddida.
Phawuloosika dendi eqqidi ba kushera malatidi “Inteno Isra7eele asato! Qasseka inteno Xoossas yayyiza Ayzaabeto! siyite.
Ha Isra7eele dere Xoossay kase nu aawata doorides; isti Gibxe deren dishin ista dhoqu dhoqu histides. Ba wolqama qesera heeppe ista kessides.
Oyddu tammu layth kumeth ista bazzo biittan dandayides.
Kanaane biittan dizayta laapun kawota dhayssidi ista biitta ba deretas gade histi laattissides.
Hessi wuri poletiday oyddu xeetanne ichashu tammu laythata giddonna. Hessafe guye nabe Sameela wode gakkanaas ista pirdiza daannata immides.
“Hessafe guye derey ba bolla kawo kawoththana mala Sameela woossides; Xoossayka Biniyaame baggafe Qiise naa Sa7oole istas immides. Izikka ista oyddu tammu layth haarides.
Sa7oole shaaridappe guye Dawute kawothides; iza gish ‘Ta wozna mala hanizayssanne ta koyidayssa wursi ooththiza Iseeye naa Dawute ta demmadis’ giidi Dawute gish Xoossi markattides.
Xoossika ba caaqo qaalatho ha addeza zerethafe as ashshizayssa Yesusa Isra7eeles ehides.
Yesusi yaanappe kase Yohannisi Isra7eele derey wuri maarotethan gelidi xammaqettana mala sabakides.
Yohannisi ba kiitettidayssa polo bolla dishe ‘Ta intes oona misatazinaa? Ta kiitettidayssa gidikke haray attoshin ta izas toho caamma kire birshanas bessontayssi taappe guyera yaana’ gides.
“Inteno Abrahaame zerethafe yeletida nu ishato! Qasseka inte giddonka Xoossas yayyizayti wuri hayssi atotetha kiitay kiitettiday nuus ubbatassa!
Yerusalame asatinne ista halaqati Yesusa eribetenna; gido attin isti iza bolla pirdida; hessanka sambatan sambatan nababetiza kase nabeta qaalay iza bolla polettides.
Iza hayqos gaththiza issi gaasokka isti demmoonta aggikkokka Philaxoosi iza bolla hayqo pirda pirdana mala woossida.
Iza gish xaafetidayssa isti wursi polidappe guye iza kaqqettida mitha bollafe gaden woththidi duufon moogida.
Gido attin Xoossi iza hayqoppe denthides.
Galilappe Yerusalame gakkanaas banara dizaytas daro wode beettides; heytikka ha7i iza gish deretas markata.
“Nukka kase Xoossi nu Aawatas caaqida Mishiraachcho qaala intes sabakoos.
Yesusa kiittidi istas caaqida qaala nuus ista naytas polides; hessika mazamure maxaafan nam7antho shempon ‘Ne ta naaza; ta nena hach yeladis’ geetetti xaafetides.
Qasseka izi wooqontayssanne Xoossi iza hayqoppe denthidayssa shaakki erana mala ‘Anjettidayssanne ammanettida Dawute anjo ta intes immana’ gides.
Hessa gish harasonka ‘Ne geeshshay hayqqi wooqana mala ne koyakka’ gees.
“Dawutey ba woden Xoossa shene mala ooththidappe guye hayqides; kase ba aawatara moogetin iza ashoy wooqides.
Xoossi iza hayqoppe denthidayssi izi gidikko wooqibenna.
Hessa gish ta ishato! Nagaras maarotethi beettizay Yesusa baggara gididayssi intes sabaketidayssa erite.
Iza ammanizadey wuri kase Muse woga baggara demmoonta xilloteth demmana.
Hessa gish kase nabeti ‘Inteno qidhizayto xeellite, malaletitenne, dhayite, intes oonikka yootin ammananas intena metiza miish ta inte woden ooththana’ gida qaalay inte bolla gakkonta mala naagetite” gides.
<range>
Phawuloosinne Barnabaassi Ayhudata Woosa Keeththafe kezishin asay ista hessa isti yootida qaala kaalliza Sambata gallas zaari yootana mala woossides.
Shiiqoy laalettidappe guye daro Ayhudatinne Ayhudata ammanon gelidi Xoosse goynniza asati Phawuloosanne Barnabaasa kaallida. Phawuloosantika ista qofsishe isti Xoossa kiyatethan minni daana mala zorida.
Kaalliza Sambata gallas katama asappe guuththati xalala attin dariza baggay wuri Goda qaala siyana shiiqides.
Ayhudatikka daro dere beyidi qanatetethan kumida. Phawuloosa haasaya eqqetishe iza cayida.
Phawuloosinne Barnabaassi babbonta xalateththan “Xoossa qaalay koyro intes yootetanas bessees. Gido attin inte qaala leqqideta. Intes merna de7oy bessontayssa interka inte bolla pirdida gish ha7i nuni gede Ayzaabetakko baana koyoos. Qasseka Goday nuna ‘Asas atotetha qaala biitta gaxa gaththana mala ta nena Ayzaabetas poo7o hista kiittadis’ gi azazides” gida.
<range>
Ayzaabeti hessa siydi daro ufayetida. Goda qaalasikka boncho immida. Merna de7os giigettida derey wuri ammanides.
Goda qaalay heeran diza dere ubbaso gakkides.
Ayhudati qas Ayana hanon kaseppe minnizaytanne duussan bonchettida macasata hessathoka kataman diza gita asata dentheththidi Phawuloosa bollanne Barnabaasa bolla goodeteththi denthidi ba dereppe kessi gooddida.
Phawuloosinne Barnabaasi asay ista ixidayssa bessanas ba toho bolla diza gudulla pittidi Iqoniyoone geetettizaso bida.
Ammaniizayti ufayssaninne Xillo Ayanan kumida.
Iqoniyoonen Phawuloosinne Barnabaassi issife Ayhudata Woosa Keeththe gelida. Henka isti asa lo7eth tamarsida gish Girike asappenne Ayhuda asappe daroy ammanides.
Hinko ammanonta Ayhuda asay Ayzaabeta ista bolla dentheththidi asay ammanizayta ixana mala ooththides.
Phawuloosinne barnabaassi Goda gish xalatethara asas yootishe heen daro wode gam7ida. Godayka isti yootiza iza qaala gita malataranne wolqama ooson qoncisi markattides.
Katama asay ba giddon nam7u kezi shaaketidi baggay Ayhudata bagga baggay Phawuloosanta bagga gidides.
He wode Ayhudatinne Ayzaabeti bana kaaleththizaytara issife gididi ista waayssanassinne shuchchan caddanas koyda.
Istika hessa erida mala Listiranne Derbeene geetettizaso gede Liqa7ooniya katamatanne he heeran diza dere baqatida.
Henka mishiraachcho qaala sabako doommida.
Listiran yeeletosappe ba tohora hamuti eronta issi toho sila addey dees.
Hessadey Phawuloosi sabakishin utti siyees; Phawuloosikka izakko tishshi histi xeelidi addeza pathana ammanoy iza bolla dizayssa beyidinne qaala dhoqu histidi “Sitti gaada ne tohon eqqa!” gides. Addezi heerakka guppi dendidi hamuth oykkides.
<range>
Asay Phawuloosi ooththidayssa beyidi Liqa7ooniya qaalara “Eeqa Xoossati as misatidi ha nuukko wodhdhida” giidi waassides.
Barnabaasa “Diya” gida Phawuloosakka haasayiza waannay iza gidida gish “Hermeene” gida.
Katamappe asi bayndason diza Diya geetettiza eeqa keeththa Qeesey kormatanne xaaxeti giigida ciish gede katama geliza oge bolla efidi derezara issife gididi Phawuloosasinne Barnabaasas yarshana koyides.
Hawaareti Barnabaassinne Phawuloosi hessa siyida mala ba may7o daakkidi gede dereza giddo woxxida; ba qaala dhoqu histidi hizgida;
“Hayto asato! Hayssa aazas ooththetii? Nukka inte mala assako! Inteka qasse hayssa mela hada yo7oppe haakkidi salonne sa7a, abbaka, abbata giddon dizayta wursi medhdhida de7o Xoossakko inte simmana mala intes mishiraachcho qaala sabakoos.
Izi kase aadhdhida yeletethaynne derey wurikka ba koyda mala hananas yeddi bessides.
Gido attin Xoossi saloppe iranne hessaththokka kaththi kaxxiza wodeta immidi inte wozna kaththaninne ufayssa kunthides; ufayssaka intena kalthidi lo7o ooson bana markay baynda aggibenna” gida.
Hessa wursi haasayidi asay istas yarshonta mala waaydi diggida.
Ayhudati qas Anxokiyappenne Iqoniyooneppe yida asay asa zoridi Phawuloosa shuchchan caddana mala ammanthida. Phawuloosakka shuchchan caddidinne hayqqides gi goochchidi katamappe gede kare kessida.
Gido attin ammanizayti iza yuuyi aadhdhi naagishin Phawuloosi dendidi gede katama gelides. Wontetha gallas Barnabaasara issife Derbeene geetettizaso bida.
Phawuloosinne Barnabaasi Darbeen mishiraachcho qaala sabakida daro asa ammanthidappe guye gede Listira, Iqoniyoonenne Anxokiya simmida.
Ammanzayta wozna minthethishe isti ammanon minni daana mala zorishe “Nu Xoossa kawoteth gelanas daro meto giddora aadhdhanaas koshshees” gida.
Hessafe guye dumma dumma Woosa Keeththatan cimata dooridappe guye xoomaninne woossan ammanettida Godas hadara aaththi immida.
Phissidiyara aadhdhidi Phinfiliya simmida.
Phergenen qaala sabakidi duge Axaaliya geetettizaso wodhdhida.
Axaaliyappekka ha7i gakkanaas isti ooththida oosoza hadara istas imettida katama Sooriyan diza Anxokiya markaben gelidi simmida.
He gakkida mala Woosa Keeththa asa wursi shiishshidi Xoossi istara ooththidayssa qasseka Ayzaabetas ammano pengey waani doyettidakkonne wursi yootida.
Heen ammanizaytara daro wode gam7ida.
Issi issi asati Yuhudappe duge Anxokiya wodhdhidi “Inte Muse woga mala qaxxaretonta aggikko oonikka attanas dandayekketa” giidi ammanizayta tamarso doommida.
Hessika Phawuloosanne Barnabaasa gita palamaninne oosha giddo gelthides; hessa gish Phawuloosinne Barnabaassi hara issi issi ammaniza asatara Yerusalame kezidi ha yo7oza gish cimatanne Hawaareta oychana mala geetettides.
Hessa gish Woosa Keeththaya ista Yerusalame baana mala kiittin isti Pinqeranne Samaariyara aadhdhi bishe heen diza asa Ayzaabeti ammanon simmidayssa yootida; he wode ammanizayti hessa siydi keehi ufayettida.
Isti Yerusalame gakkin Woosa Keeththa asay Hawaaretinne cimati ista mokki ekkida; kiitetti bidaytikka Xoossi istara gididi ooththidayssa wursi istas yootida.
Farsaaweeta bagga asatappe ammanida issi issi asati dendidi “Ayzaabeti qaxxaretanassinne Muse woga naagana mala istas yootanas bessees” gida.
Hawaaretinne cimati he yo7oza giddo lo7eth xeellanas shiiqida.
Daro palamappe guye Phexroosi dendi eqqidi, “Ta ishato! Guuththa wodeppe kase Xoossi tana inte giddofe dooridi Ayzaabeti ta duunappe mishiraachcho qaala siydi ammanana mala ooththidayssa inte ereeta.
Asa wozna eriza Xoossi nuus immidayssa mala istaska Xillo Ayana immidi ista baas ekkidayssa markatides.
Ista woznakka ammanon geeshshidi nu giddoninne ista giddon aykko shaakkokka ooththibenna.
Hessa gish nu aawatinne nukka tookkanaas dandayonta qambara ammanizayta toossanas inte aazas Xoosse paacetii?
Nu attiday likke istaththokka Goda Yesusa aadho kiyatethan gididayssa ammanoos” gides.
Shiiqida asay wurikka co7u giin Barnabaassinne Phawuloosi Xoossi ista baggara Ayzaabeta giddon ooththida gita malatata gish yootishin malaletidi lo7ethi siyides.
Isti yooti wursishin Yaqoobey dendi eqqidi hizgides “Ta ishato! Ta gizayssa siyite;
Xoossi Ayzaabetappe baas gidana dere kasetidi izi wosti xeygi woththidako Simooni nuus lo7ethi yootides.
Kase nabetan hizgi xaafetida qaalay hayssara gaggees.
‘Hayssafe guye ta simmada laaletida Dawute keeththe keexana; laalettidayssa zaara essana; zaaradakka keexana.
Hessika attida asay Goda koyana malanne ta sunthan xeeygettida Ayzaabeti tana koyana mala gees wursi ooththida Xoossi;
Hayssa koyroppekka ersida Xoossi tana’ gides.
“Hessa gish ha Xoossako simmida Ayzaabeta nu metothonta mala hayssi ta baggara taas qasho.
Gido attin eeqas yarshettidi tunida kath mooppite; laymappe haakkite; bawuti hayqqida mehe asho mooppite; suuth uyoppite giidi nu istas xaafana bessees.
Muse wogay gidikko benisofe Sambata Sambata gallas Ayhudata Woosa Keeththan nabebetishenne katamay dizason sabaketishe dees” gides.
He wode Hawaaretinne cimati kumeththa Woosa Keeththa asara gididi ba giddofe issi issi asata dooridi Phawuloosaranne Barnabaasara gaththi Anxokiya yeddanas qachida. Ammaniza asa giddofe waannatizayta Barsabaasa geetettiza Yuhudanne Sillase doorida.
Ista kushen immi yeddida dabdaabezi “Inte ishatappe, Hawaaretappe, cimatappe, Ayzaabetappe ammanida Anxokiyaninne Sooriyan, Kilqiyanka diza ammanizaytas nu sarokay intena gakko.
“Issi issi asati nuuppe gidonta ba baggara nu achchafe biidi ba haasayan inte wozna yaanne haanne qaathidayssanne intena bul7akkidayssa nu siyidos.
Hessa gish guutha asata dooridi dosettida Barnabaasaranne Phawuloosara inteko yeddanas nu wurikka qaala gaaggidos.
Isti Goda Yesus Kirstoosa gish ba shempo aaththi immidayta.
Hessa gish nu intes xaafidayssa isti intes ba duunara lo7ethi yootana mala Yuhudanne Sillase inteko yeddidos.
Hayta intes koshshiza yo7otappe hara deexo tooho nu inte bolla wothonta mala nussinne Xillo Ayanas lo7o misati beettides.
Hessika inte eeqas shukettida ashoppe, suuthafe, bawuti hayqqida mehe ashoppenne laymappe inte hakkana mala; inte hayta misatizaytappe haakkikko intes lo7o; saron diite” gees.
Kiitettida asati moyzetidi duge Anxokiya wodhdhida; heen ammanizayta wursi shiishshidi ehida dabdaabeza istas immida.
Dereyka nababidi minthethiza qaalan ufayetides.
Yuhudaynne Sillassi nabeta gidida gish daro zoridi ammanizayta minthethida.
Heen guutha wode gam7idi ammaniza asay moyzin guye bana kiittidaytakko simmida.
Sillassi qas heen attanas koyides.
Phawuloosinne Barnabaassi hara daro asatara gididi Goda qaala tamarsishenne sabakishe Anxokiyan gam7ida.
Phawuloosi guutha wode gam7idi Barnabaasa “Nu kase Goda qaala yootida ubba katamata biidi ammanzayti ay mala dizaakkonne ane yuuyi beyoos, denda” gides.
Barnabaasikka Marqoosa geetettiza Yohannisi istara baana mala koyides.
Phawuloosi qas iza ekki baanas koybenna; gaasoyka kase Marqoossi istafe shaaketidi Phinfiliya gizason guye attidi istara oosos sinth kezonta aggida gishassa.
Histin daro palamay ista giddon medhetida gish ba giddon shaaketi wodhdhida; hessa gish Barnabaassi Marqoosa ekkidi markaben gelidi Qophiroose bides.
