Inte Xoossa kiyatetha garsan deeta attin woga garsan doonta gish intena nagaray haarenna.
Histin ay ooththinoo? Woga garsan gidonta nuni Xoossa kiyatetha garsan diza gish nagara ooththinoo? Mule ooththanas bessenna.
Inte intena aylle mala shiishshiza wode inte azazettizades aylle gididayssa ereeta. Hessathoka gede hayqokko efiza nagaras woykko xillotethako gaththiza azazetethas inte aylle gididayssa ereketii?
Inte kase nagaras aylleta gidikko intes imettida timirtezas inte woznappe azazetida gish Xoossi galatetto.
Inte nagarappe wozetidi xillotethas aylle gidideta.
Hayssa ta asa qaalan intes qonccen yootizay inte yeletethan daburancha gidida gishassa. Inte kase wode inte asatetha aylletethasinne kaseppe aadhdhi iitana mala ooththi immeta shin ha7i qasse gede geeshshatethakko efiza xillotethas aylle histi haariste.
Inte kase nagaras aylletidi diza wode inte xillotethafe mela attideta shin;
ha7i qasse inte yellatiza miishatappe he wode ay go7a demmidetii? Hessa he hanoza go7ay hayqo.
Ha7i qasse inte nagarappe wozetidi Xoossa aylleta gidideta. Hessika intena gede geeshshatethakko kaalethees. Wursethaykka merna de7o.
Nagara waagay hayqo; gido attin Xoossa imotay gidikko Goda Yesus Kirstoosa baggara merna de7o.
Ta ishato! Tani woga eriza asatas yootays. Wogay shempora paxa diza asa xalala haarizayssa inte ereketii?
Issi macassi azina gelikko ba azinara iza wogan qashetizay azinay paxa diza wode gakkanaassa. Azinay hayqqikko iza macho gidiza wogappe anjettawus.
Gido attin azinay paxa dishin iza hara azina gelikko layma geetettawus. Azinay hayqqikko qasse hara asi gelikko kase azina wogappe anjettadus attin “Layma” geetetuku.
Hessa gish ta ishato! Inteka Yesus Kirstoosa asatetha baggara wogas hayqqideta. Inte hayqoppe dendida Kirstoosa bagga gidin nuni Xoossas ayfe ayfanassa.
Nagarancha medhetetha shenen nu diza wode hayqos gathiza ayfe nu ayfana mala wogay dentheththida nagara amoy nu bolla ooththides.
Ha7i gidikko kase nuna waaxi qachida wogas hayqqida gish he wogappe wozetidos. Hessika kase ceega wogan xaafettidayssan gidonta dishe ooratha Ayana ogen nuni ooththanassa.
Histin nu ay giinoo? Ba hu7es wogay nagaraa? Mulekka gidenna. Woga baggara gidontakko nagaray azakkonne nu erokkokko shin; wogay “Amottofa!” goontakko amoy azakkonne tumappe ta erikke.
Nagaray qasse wogappe kezida azazoy bessida ogen go7ettidi ta giddon dumma dumma iita amo dentheththides. Wogay yaanappe kase nagaray hayqqidaza.
Wogay baynda kase tani paxa dayssishin wogay yiin qasse nagaray paxa gidides. Ta gidikko hayqqadis.
As ashshana qofetida azazoykka hayqo ekii yidayssa eradis.
Nagaray woga baggara beettida gaason go7ettidi tana baleththidesinne azazon wodhides.
Hessa gish wogay ba baggara geeshsha. Azazoykka geeshsha; xillonne lo7o.
Gido attin lo7os hanidayssi taas hayqos gididee? Mulekka gidenna. Gido attin nagaray ba nagaratethan erettana mala lo7o gidida hano baggara ta bolla hayqo ehides. Hessika nagaray azazo baggara kaseppe aaththi nagara darsides.
Wogay Ayana yo7o gididayssa nu eroos. Ta qasse nagaras aylle mala bayzettida asa.
Tani ta ooththizayssa erike. Ta ooththana koyizayssa ooththa erike shin ta ixiza miish ooththays.
Ta ooththana koyonta miish ooththiza gidikko wogay lo7o gididayssa ta markatays.
Hessa ooththizay tana gidonta ta gaaththan diza nagaray ooththes.
Tanan hessikka nagarancha gidida ta medhetetha giddon aykko lo7o miish bayndayssa ta erays. Lo7o ooththanas taas amoteth dees shin pola ooththa erikke.
Ta ooththizay ooththana gaada koyiza lo7o ooso gidenna. Gido attin ta ooththana koyonta iita ooso ooththays.
Tani ooththanas koyontayssa ooththiza gidikko hessa ooththizay tana gidonta ta giddon diza nagara.
Hessa gish hayssi wogay ooson dizayssi taas gelides. Hessika tani lo7o ooththana koyaysishin iita ooththays.
Tani ta gaaththara Xoossa wogan ufayetays.
Gido attin ta asatetha giddon ooththiza nagara wogay tana qachi oykidi ta qofa wogara olettiza hara wogay ta asatetha giddon ooththishin beyays.
Ta ay mala laafa asee! Hayssa hayqos imettida asatethafe tana ashshanay oonee?
Nu Goda Yesus Kirstoosa baggara galatay Xoossas gido. Histikko tani ta baggara ta qofan Xoossa wogas aylle gidashe tani ta medhetetha wogan nagara wogas aylle.
Hessa gish Yesus Kirstoosa ammanizayta bolla pirday deenna.
Gaasoyka de7o Ayana wogay Yesus Kirstoosa baggara nagarappe ista geeshida gishassa.
Nagarancha ashoppe dendidayssan wogay polanas dandayontayssa Xoossi ba naaza nagarancha asa leemison nagaras yarshettana mala yeddidi polides. Histidi nagara iza ashon pirdides.
Hessika nuni ashon gidonta Ayanan simeretiza nuuppe wogay koyiza xillotetha polanassa.
Asho shene mala daana koyiza asata woznay ashoy koyiza miishan shempees. Ayana shene mala dizayti qasse ba wozna Ayanay koyiza miisha bolla wothetes.
Ashos xalala qofay hayqo gidishin Ayana yo7os qofay gidikko de7onne sarotetha.
Nagaras haarettiza woznay Xoossara oosha. Gaasoyka izi Xoossa wogas haarettennanne haarettanas dandayenna.
Asho shene mala diza asatikka Xoosse ufayssas dandayettenna.
Inte qasse Xoossa Ayanay intenan diza gidikko ashon gidonta Ayanan deeta. Kirstoosa Ayanay iza bolla bayndadey Kirstoosas gidenna.
Kirstoosi inte giddon diikko qasse inte asatethay nagara geedon hayqeth gidikkoka inte Ayanay qasse xillotetha gaason de7on dees.
Yesusa hayqoppe denthida iza Ayanay inte bolla diza gidikko Kirstoosa hayqoppe denthidayssi inte giddon diza iza ayanay hayqqanas diza inte asatethas de7o immana.
Hessa gish ta ishato! Hessika hananay dosan gidenna shin nu asho shene mala daanas ashos gidokko.
Asho shene mala diza gidikko inte hayqqana; asho ooso iitaza inte Ayanan wodhikko inte de7on daana.
Xoossa Ayanan kaallizayti isti Xoossa nayta.
Inte ekkida Ayanay zaaridi intena aylletethan haariza ayana gidonta “Nu Aawawu” gi xeygisiza natetha Ayana ekideta.
Nuni Xoossa nayta gididayssa; he Ayanay ba baggara nu ayanara issife nuus markatees.
Nuni Xoossa nayta gidikko iza laattizayta. Nu Kirstoosa bonchoza laattizayta gidana mala addafekka izara iza metoza gishettizayta gidikko nu Xoosse laattizayta; Kirstoosarakka issife laattizayta.
Ha7i nu ekiza waayey buro nuus sinthan giigi uttida bonchozara gaththi xeellishin aykkokka gidenna gays.
Medhetethay wurikka Xoossa nayti qoncanayssa laamotethan naagon dees.
Medhetethi wurikka mela hada gidana mala pirdetides. Hessika ba dooron gidonta sinthafes haarettana mala izi ba shene mala haarisida gishassa.
Hessika medheteth wurikka dhayssa aylletethafe wozetidi Xoossa naytas gidida gede bonchettida shene mala dizaso gakkanaassa.
Ha7i gakkanaas medhetethi wurikka daro waayen miixatishe dizayssa nu eroos.
Iza xalala gidonta koyro Xillo Ayana imota demmida nunikka nu asatethay attana; nu iza naa gidanayssakka laamotishenne woznara miixattishe doos.
Hayssa ha hidotan xalala attidos. Hidotay qasse ayfen beettiza miish gidikko buroppe naagiza miish gidenna; ha7i ba ayfen beyiza miishi buroppes naagiizay oonee?
Gido attin nuni buro nu ayfen beyonta miish hidotan naagizaz gidikko saletay baynda naagoos.
Hessathoka qasse nu daaburishin Ayanay nuna maaddes. Nuni woossa wosti woossanakkone eronta gish Ayanay nuni qaalan qoncisanas dandayettonta qaalara nuus woosses.
Nu wozna paaci eriza Ayanay izi Ayana qofa eres. Gaasoyka Ayanay Xoossa shene mala ammaniza asas nuus woosses.
Xoossi bana dosizaytassinne iza shene mala xeeygetidaytas ubbas ooththiza miish wursikka lo7os ooththizayssa nu eroos.
Xoossi kaseppe ba erizayta isti iza naaza misatana mala kasekka doori woththides. Hessika daro ba ishata giddofe izi bayra gidanassa.
Kase koyroppe ba dooridayta ista xeygides. Qasseka xeygidayta xillisides. Ba xillisidaytakka bonchides.
Histin hessa nu ay giinoo? Xoossi nunara gidikko nunara eqetanas dandayizay oonee?
Ba naazas mishetonta nu gish aaththi immiday iza. Histin ubba miish nuus izara kiyatethan wursi aazas imenee?
Xoossi dooridayta mootizay oonee? Xillisizay Xoossa.
Histin pirdizay oonee? Hayqqidi hayqoppe dendidi Xoossa ushachchan uttida Yesus Kirstoosi nu gish gaannates.
Nuna Kirstoosa siiqoppe shaakanay oonee? Metoyee? Waayee? Woykko goodeteththee? Woykko gafaa? Woykko kallotethee? Woykko qopponta gakkiza metoyee? Mashshaa?
Hessika kase “Ne gish nu shukettiza dorsa mala qoodetidos. Gallas kumeth ne gish nuni hayqora baaxettana” geetetti xaafettidayssa mala.
Nuna aazika izappe shaakenna. Hayssa ubban nuna siiqidayssan xoonizaytappekka nu aadhdhos.
Hessa gish hayqo gidin, de7o gidin, kiitanchata gidin, woykko ha7i diza miish gidin, buro yaana miish gidin, woykko ay wolqama gidin,
dhoqa gidin woykko ziqa gidin, woykko ay medheteth gidin Goda Yesus Kirstoosa baggara nuus diza Xoossa siiqoppe nuna shaakana dandayiza miishi bayndayssa ta shaaka eradis.
Ta Yesusa sunthan tumu gays; wordotikke; ta woznaykka Xillo Ayana baggara taas markatees.
Taas woznappe kichchonta gita qofaynne miishay dees.
Ta dabbota gish ta qangetadanne Kirstoosappe shaaketada wora wodhdhidakko dosays.
Istika Isra7eele nayta; isti Xoossa naa gidana mala Xoossa bonchoynne caaqo qaalay, wogaynne Xoossa Keeththa woga hidotay istas imettides.
Kase Aawatikka ista bagga Kirstoosi ista zeretha zarken qoodetes. Izikka ubbafe bolla gidida mernas galattettida Xoossa. Amiin.
Gido attin hessa guussi Xoossa qaalay attides gussi gidenna. Isra7eeleppe yeletiday wuri Isra7eele as gidenna.
Abrahaameppe yeletidayti izappe yeletida gish wurikka iza nayta gidettennashin “Ne zereth Yisaaqa baggara xeeygettana” geetettida mala hanides.
Hessa guussikka Xoossa naa geetettidayti isti ashon yelidayta gidettenna; gido attin naa gidanayti hidota qaalan yooteti uttidayta.
“Yiza layth hanni wode ta ha simmana; Saaraykka nees attuma naa yelana” geetetidi izas hidota qaalay imettides.
Hessa xalalaka gidenna. Irbiqa nayti issade naakko! Izikka nu aawa Yisaaqa.
Menteti yeletidi buro iita woykko lo7o ooththonta dishin Xoossa qofay minnana mala,
ooson gidonta xeygidayssafe gidida gish “Bayray kaalozas haarettana” geetettidi Irbiqas yootetides.
Hessika “Ta Yaqoobe dosadis; Eesawe ixadis” geetetti kase xaafettida mala hanides.
Histin nu ha7i ay giinoo? Xoossi bessonta ogera maaddi erizee? Mulekka maaddi erenna.
Xoossi Muses “Ta maarana koyidade maarana; ta mishettana koyizadeska mishettana” gees.
Hessa gish asi koyda mala gidonta woykko asa daburan gidonta Xoossi maarida mala hanees.
Geeshsha Maxaafay Faaroone “Ta wolqay ne bolla bettana malanne ta sunthi biitta ubba bolla yootettana mala ta nena hayssas denthadis” gees.
Hessa gish Xoossi maarana koyizade maarees. Iza wozna muumisana koyizade wozna muumises.
Intefe issadey “Histin hanoy hessa mala gidikko nuna hanno gakkanaas aazas waayssizee? Gaasoyka iza shene diggana dandayizay oonee?” gaada ne oychonta aggaka.
Gido attin Xoossas zaaro zaara immizay ne oonee? “Oosetida miish zaaridi ooththidayssa ne tana aazas hayssatho ooththadii?” gi erizee?
Urqa medhizadey he urqafe bagga bonchos bagga qasse coo hiraaysso oosos medhanas iza shene gidenee?
Xoossika ba hanqo besanasinne ba wolqa erisanas koydi iza hanqo qoncisizayta, dhayanas giigettidayta dhayssonta aggagikkochi!
Koyro bonchos giigissida iza maaroteth bessizaytaas iza boncho duretethay erettana mala izi ooththanassa.
Xeeygidadey Ayhudata baggafe xalala gidonta Ayzaabeta baggafe gidida nunakka ashshonta xeygides.
Hose7e maxaafan “Ta dere gidontayta tani ‘Ta dereta’ ga xeeygana; dosettontayta ista ta ‘Dosettidayta’ gaada xeeygana.
Qasseka ‘Inte ta dere deekketa’ geetetti yootetidason heenka ‘Isti de7o Xoossa nayta’ geetetti xeeygettana.”
Isayaassikka Isra7eele nayta gish “Isra7eele nayta qooday abba ace mala darikkoka guuthati xalala attana.
Goday ba pirda biitta bolla elle pirdana” gi yootides.
Hessika “Wogga Goday nuus zereth ashshontakko nukka soddome katama malanne Gamoora katama mala dhayanashin” geetettidi kase Isayaasa duunan yootidayssa mala hanides.
Histin nu ay giinoo? Ammanon beettida xilloteth demmanas Ayzaabey daaburonta demmides.
Gido attin xillotetha woga kaalliza Isra7eele nayti demmibettenna.
Hessi aazas hessatho hanidee? Isti ammanon gidonta ooson demmana kaallida gishassa. Istika dhuphe shuchchan dhuphetida.
Hessika “Hekko asa dhuphiza shuch ista kundisiza zaalla Xiyoone bolla ta wothana; izan ammanizadey yeellatenna” geetettidi kase Geeeshsha Maxaafan xaafettidayssa mala hanides.
Ta ishato! Isra7eele nayta gish ta amoynne ta Xoosse woossizay isti dhayonta attanassa.
Isti Xoossa yo7os mishetizayta gididayssa ta ista gish markattana dandayays; ista mishetethi gidikko eratethan gidenna.
Xoossi as xillisiza oge eronta aggidi ba xillotethas oge kaallida attin Xoossa xillotetha oge kaallibettenna.
Ammaniza asa ubba xillisanas Kirstoosi woga ubba polides.
Musey woga baggara beettiza xillotetha gish erisishe “Hayta wogata poli ooththizadey ha wogatan daana” gizayssa.
Ammanon beettiza xillotethi qasse hizgees “Ne woznara pude salo oonee kezanay? gooppa” hessatho guussi Kirstoosa saloppe duge ha wothana guussa.
Woykko “ ‘Duge ciimman oonee wodhdhanay?’ Gooppa!” hessikka Kirstoosa hayqoppe buro denthana guussa.
Gido attin qaalay ay gizee? “Qaalay ne achchan dees.” Ne duunaninne ne woznan dees. Nuni ammano gish sabakiza qaalay hayssa.
Neni ne duunara “Yesusi Goda” gaada markattikko Xoossi iza hayqoppe denthidayssa ne woznan ne ammanikko attana.
Neni xillanay woznan ammanikkonne attanay ne duunara markatiinna.
Geeshsha Maxaafay giza mala “Izan ammanizay wurikka yeellatenna.”
Ayhudata giddoninne Ayzaabeta giddon dummateththi deenna; issi Goday ubbaska Goda; iza woossizayta gujji anjees.
“Goda sunth xeygizayti wurikka attana” geetetti Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafetides.
Histin iza ammanontayti iza wozgi xeeyganee? Qasse iza gish siyonta dishe wosti ammananee? Saabakey baynda dishin wosti siyanee?
Kiitetonta wosti sabakandetoo? Hessika “Mishiraachcho qaala ekkii yizayta yuussi ay mala lo7o” geetetti Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettida mala hanides.
Gido attin siyidayti wurikka Mishiraachcho qaala ekibettenna; Isayaassi “Godo nu yootidayssa ooni ammanidee?” gida mala hanides.
Hessa gish ammanoy beettizay yootiza qaala siyethanna. Yootetiza qaalaykka Kirstoosa gish yootiza qaalappe.
Gido attin asay siybeneshaa? gaada ta oychays; tumappe asay siydes; Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettida mala “Ista qaalay biitta ubbaninne alame gaxa gakkanaas siyetides.”
Ta qasseka oychays; Isra7eele nayti qaala eribeteneshaa? Koyro Musey istas “Ta dere gidontaytan ta ista amosisana; yuushi qopponta deretan ta ista yiillochana” gides.
Isayaassikka xalatethan “Tana koyontaytas ta bettadis; tana oychontaytas tana qoncisadis” gides.
Isra7eele gish qasse “Taas azazetonta derekkonne taas eeno goonta derekko kumeththa gallas ta kushe micadis” gees.
Histin Xoossi ba dereta yeggi aggidee? Gaada ta oychays; mulekka aggibenna; takka ta baggara Biniyaame zarike, Abrahaame zereth gidida Isra7eele asa.
Xoossi koyroppe ba erida dereza yeggibenna. Elaassi Isra7eele nayta bolla mooto Xoossakko wosti shiishshidakkonne Geeshsha Maxaafay iza gish ay gizakko inte ereketii?
“Godo! Isti ne nabeta wodhida. Nees yarshizasotakka laallida. Qasse tani tarka attadis. Tanaka wodhana geetes” gides.
Xoossi izas “Ba7aale geetettiza Eeqas goynontayta laapun shi as tani taas ashshadis” gi zaarides
Hessa malaka ha7i ha wodezanka Xoossa kiyatethan Isra7eele asappe dooretti attida guuthati deettes.
Histin hessi Xoossa kiyatethan gidikko asa ooson gidenna. Asa ooson gididakko Xoossa kiyatethi kiyateth gidenna.
Histin ay gaanee? Isra7eele nayti lo7ethi koyidayssa demmibettenna. Xoossan doorettidayti gidikko demmida. Hanko attidayta woznay muumides.
Kase “Ista ayfey xeellonta mala, ista haythayka siyonta mala Xoossi hanno gakkanaas istas doccissiza Ayana immides” geetetti Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettida mala.
Dawuteykka “Ista maadday ista oykiza narxanne yarde; istas dhuphizazinne qixaate gido.
Ista ayfey xeellofo; goozzetto; ista zokkoy mernas kuunno” gides.
Ane qasse ta zaara oychays; Isra7eele asay nam7antho kundethafe dendennee? Dendana. Harappeka Isra7eele nayta qanatissana gish ista mooro gaason atotethi Ayzaabetas gakkides.
Gido attin qasse ista mooroy Ayzaabetas anjo gidides. Ista kundethikka qasse Ayzaabetas anjo gidikko isti simmi attidakko ay mala gita anjo gidandeshin!
Ayzaabeto! Ta intes yootays, ta Ayzaabetas kiitettidade gidida gish ta oosoza minnada polana.
Hessika ta bagga asati amozana mala denthethada istafe guutha asata ashshanas ufayssa ooththays.
Xoossi ista aggida Ayzaabeti Xoossara giigikko Xoossi Isra7eele nayta zaaridi ekkiza wode intes aazi hanana misatizee? Hessa guussi “Hayqoppe dendides” guussa mala.
Koyro bukeesoy lo7o gidikko hanko izappe oosettizays wurikka lo7o gides. Hessathoka issi mitha xaphoy lo7o gidikko hanko iza bolla diza haggatikka lo7o gidettes.
Keeththa matan diza wogara mitha haggata malati inte meqqi wodhdhin hanko woran diza wogara mithata misatiza Ayzaabeti inte kichchosan gididi inte haaronne inte anjo shaakki ekkizadenta gidikko;
heyta he meqqi wodhdhida haggata bolla otoretofa. Inte ista bolla otoretikko qasse hanno woznan woththite. He mitha tookkiday nena gidakka. Mithay nena tookkides attin.
Histikko “He haggati meqqi wodhdhiday nuni isti kichchosan gelana malassa” goonta aggeketa.
Tumu gideta shin isti meqiday ammano paceppe dendidayssanna. Inte qas ammanon eqideta. Babbite attin otoretofte.
Xoossi koyroppe diza haggatas mishetontade gidikko inteska mishetenna.
Hessa gish Xoossa kiyatethinne iza menxe iitatetha ane xeella. Iza menxe iitatethay kundidayta bolla. Iza kiyatethay qasse inte iza qadhetetha garsan diza wode gakkanaas xalala. Hessi baynda aggikko inteka qanxettana.
Isti ammanonta minni eqidasoppe simmikko kase baso simmi gelana. Xoossika ista zarsi gelthana dandayes.
Inte bazzo wogara mithafe qanxetidayti kase inte medhetethafe gidonta lo7o mithan inte gelana dandayikko koyroppe ba medhetetha haggata gididayti heyti kase iza bolla diza wogara mithan simmi geloy istas waani hannenee?
Ta ishato! Inte cinca as gididayssa intes misatonta mala hayssa gido xuura yo7oza inte eronta attana mala ta koyikke. Hessika Ayzaabetappe xeeygetidayti wuri ammanana gakkanaas Isra7eele nayta woznay muumides.
Hessa gish Isra7eele nayti wurikka attana. “Ashshizaddey Xiyooneppe yaana; Yaqoobeppeka iitateth diggana.
Tani ista nagara wursa dhayssidappe guye ta istara caaqon geliza qaalay hessa” geetettidi kase Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettida mala hanides.
Intes Ayzaabetas Mishiraachcho qaalay gakkana mala Isra7eele nayti Xoossan ixettida as gidida. Gidikkoka kase dooro mala gidikko ba aawata baggara isti dosettidayta.
Xoossi dooridappenne ba kiyateth immidappe guye ba ooththida miishan simmidi modhetenna.
Inteka kase azazettontaytakko! Isti azazettonta ixin ha7i intena maaridayssatho;
Xoossi intena maarida geedon istika maarettana mala ha7i azazettontayta gidida.
Xoossi wursikka maaranas asi wurikka azazettonta mala gordides.
Xoossa duretethay, aadho eratethaynne iza eratethay ay mala ciimma! Iza pirday ay malakkonne paacetenna. Izi aadhdhida geedoyka eretenna.
“Goda wozna eriday oonee? Izas zore immiday oonee?
Xoossi zaari immana mala izas tal7e immiday oonee?” geetetti xaafettida mala.
Wurikka izappe, izan, izassa; izas bonchoy mernappe mernas gido! Amiin.
Hessa gish ta ishato! Inte asatetha geeshshinne Xoosse ufayssiza de7o yarsho ooththidi inte shiishana mala ta intena Xoossa qadhetan woossays. Hessika woznama asa mala inte Xoossas ooththiza ooso.
Lo7o, ufaysizazinne kumeth gidida Xoossa sheney aazakkonne inte paaci erana mala inte qofan oraxidi laametite attin hayssa alame asa misatoppite.
Intes Xoossi immida ammano mala interka intena paaci xeellite attin ha7i dizayssafe bollara intena dhoqisi xeellonta mala tani taas imettida Xoossa kiyatethan intena issa issa zorays.
Nuuppe issi issi asas issi asatetha bolla daro billiteti diza mala heytikka he billiteti issi mala ooso ooththontayssatho;
hessathoka nuni darota gidi uttidi Kirstoosan issi asho; nuni issoy issas asho.
Nuus imettida imota mala dumma dumma imotethi dees. Issades buroppe hananaz yooto gidikko izaades imettida ammano mala yooto.
Ooththi maaddizadey ooththi maaddo; tamarsizadeykka tamarso.
Zorizadey gidikko zoro; bayndaytas immizadey gujji immo. Ayssizaddey minni aysso. Maarizadeykka ufayssan maaro.
Inte siiqotethi qoodheppe qommon gidoppo. Iita gididayssa wursikka ixite. Lo7o gididayssara issife oyketite.
Inte inte garsan issoy issara ishata mala lo7ethi siiqetite. Issoy issa bappe aaththi bonchizayta gidite.
Godas ooththana Ayanan xuugetizayta gidite attin hessa he minotethafe guye gooppite.
Hidotan ufayetizayta gidite; meto dandayite; woossan minnite.
Ammanishe waayetizaytas intes dizayssafe shaakki immite. Imath mokkite.
Intena qangizayta anjite attin qangofte.
Ufayetizaytara ufayetite; muuzotizaytara muuzotite.
Inte inte garsan doseteththan diite. Manqotara issifetethan daanas koyite attin otoretofitenne ceeqqettofte.
Oonaska iita gish iita zaaroppite. Asa ubba achchan lo7o miish ooththanas minnite.
Intes dandayettikko inte inte baggara asa ubbara saron diite.
Ta siiqoto! Inte halo Xoossi kesso attin interka halo kessofte “Halo kessanay tana gees Goday” geetetti Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettides.
Halo kessanappe “Neni ne morkey gafikko miza; izi saamotikko ushsha; ne hessatho ooththikko tama bonqo iza bolla koraasa” geetettidi Geeeshsha Maxaafan xaafetides.
Iita lo7o ooson xoona attin iitan xoonetofa.
Ay assikka bana ayssiza daannatas haarettanas bessees. Xoossafe imettonta dishin daannatethi deenna. Ha7i diza daannati Xoossafe daannattidayta.
Hessa gish daanna bolla makaliday Xoossa woga bolla makalees. He makalizaytikka ba bolla pirda eheetes.
Dere ayssizayti iita ooththizayta babisettes attin lo7o ooththizayta babisettenna. Ne dere aysizades babbonta aggana koyay? Histikko lo7o ooththa; izikka nena galatana.
Izi nees lo7o ooththanas Xoossa oosancha. Gido attin ne iita ooththida gidikko izas babba. Gaasoyka izi mashsha coo mela gixxibenna; izi iita ooththizade qaxayanas Xoossa oosancha.
Hessa gish iza qixaates babo xalala gidonta ne qofanka daannattizades azazettanas bessees.
Inte giira immizay hessassa. Ayssizayta hessa he oosoza bolla Xoossi ista woththides.
Istafe issas issas bessizayssa immite. Giira immana bessizaytas giira immite; qaraxa qanxanas bessizaytas qaraxa qanxite; babbanas bessizaytas babbite; bonchanas bessizayta bonchite.
Inte garsan issoy issara siiqetethafe attin oona bollaka accoy dooppo. As siiqiza asi izi woga polides.
“Laymatoppa, wodhoppa, amottofa” gizaytinne hara azazoti diikkokka “As ubbakka ne mala siiqa” giza hanno issi wogan wurikka kuuyettides.
Siiqoy asa bolla iita ooththenna; hessa gish siiqoy woga ubbas kuushsha.
Hayssa wodeza caddi xeelidi hessa ooththite. Ha7i hanna inte dhiskofe dendiza wode. Nu kase ammanosappe haa simmin ha7i nuus attiza wodey matides.
Qamay aadhdhin wontana gees. Hessa gish ane nu dhuma ooso wora yeggidi poo7o ola miishi may7os.
Gallassara hammuttiza mala ane wogara hammuttos. Magulthaninne mathon gidoppo; layma amoninne layman gidoppo; qanatetethaninne palaman gidoppo.
Hessa aggidi Yesus Kirstoosa may7ite. Asho amo polanas qoppofte.
Inte garsan ammanon buro minnontade shiishshi ekkite attin iza qofa bolla pirdofte.
Issi issi asi beettidayssa wursi maanas ammanoy dees. Qasse ammanon minnontadey atakilte xalala mees.
Bettidayssa wursi mizadey wursi moontade kadhoppa. Moontadey qasse mizade bolla pirdofo. Xoossi ubbakka ekides.
Hanko ooththizade bolla pirdizadey ne oonee? Izaadey kundikko woykko eqikkoka Godassa. Goday iza essanas dandayiza gish izi eqandes.
Issadey “Gallassatappe issi gallas hara gallassafe aaththidi baasi dumma gallas” gi qoppees. Hara asi qasse “Gallassati wurikka issi gina” gi qoppees. Issi issi asi ba woznan ammanida mala ooththo.
Issi gallassi hara gallassafe dummassi qoppizadey izi hessa ooththizay Goda bonchos gidikko mizadeyka Goda bonchos giidi mees. Miidi Xoosse galattees. Montadeyka Goda bonchos giidi muus aggessinne Xoossas galata imees.
Nuuppe oonikka baasi dizaddeynne bappe baasi hayqqizaddey deenna.
Nu diikkoka Godas doos. Hayqqikkoka Godas hayqos. Hessa gish diikkoka woykko hayqqikko nu Godassa.
Hessa gish hayqqidaytassinne paxa dizaytas Goda gidanas Kirstoosi hayqqidi hayqoppe paxi dendides.
Histin ne aazas ne isha bolla pirday? Aazas ne isha leqqay? Nu wurikka Xoossa pirda wombora sinth shiiqos doos.
“Ta paxa days. Gulbatey wurikka taas gulbatana. Inxarsi wuri Xoossas markattana” geetetti kase Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettides.
Hessa gish nuni issi issi asi Xoossa sinth shiiqidi nu ooso gish izas zaaro immana.
Hessa gish nuni nu garsan issoy issa bolla pirdanappe ane naagetos. Hessa aggidi nu ishas dhuphe gidizayssa woykko iza oykiza narxa wothonta mala ane nu naagetos.
Tani Goda Yesusan ammanada miza kaththan tunay bayndayssa eradis. Gido attin issadey issi miish tuna gi qoppikko he miishay izaadesi tuna.
Neni ne isha miza kaththa geedon dhuphe gidikko siiqon simeretabakka. Kirstoosi iza gish hayqqida ne isha ne miza kaththa gaason wodhoppa.
Inte lo7o giidi qoppiza miish iita getettana mala ooththofte.
Xoossa kawotethi Xillo Ayanan beettida xilloteth, sarotethinne ufayssafe attin muussa yo7onne ushsha yo7o gidenna.
Hayssatho Kirstoosas ooththizadey Xoosse ufayssessinne asa achchanka galattettes.
Hessa gish sarotethi beettiza ogenne nuni nu garsan lo7onas bessiza oge ane koyoos.
Nuni miza kaththa gish giidi Xoossa ooso ane laallokko. Kaththi wurikka geeshsha. Gido attin hara asas dhuphe gidiza kath muussi bala ooso.
Ne ishas dhuphe gidizazi gidikko ashokka maanappenne woyne cajje uyanappe woykko ay miishikka ne ooththonta aggikko lo7o.
Hessa gish, haytanta misatiza miishatas nees diza ammanoy ne giddoninne Xoossa giddon de7o. “Hayssi likkeko” giidi ammanon ekkida miishan barka ba bolla pirdontadey izaadey anjettidade.
Gido attin woznara sidhishe miikko izi ammanon moonta gish iza bolla pirdetides. Ammanon ooththontazi wurikka nagara.
Nuni ammanon minnidayti hanko ammanon minnotayta meto tookkanas bessees attin nu xalla ufayetizayta gidanas bessenna.
Nuni wurikka hara asi ba ammanon minnana mala iza go7izazinne ufaysiza miish ane ooththoos.
Kirstoosi bana ufaysibenna; harappeka “Asay nena cayida cashshay tana gakkides” geetetti kase Geeshsha Maxaafan xafetidaysi poletides.
Nuni Geeshsha Maxaafatappe demmiza dandayaynne minotethi nuus daana mala koyroppe xaafettidayssi wurikka nu izappe nuus timirte demmana mala xaafettides.
Minotethinne dandaya immiza Xoossi inte Yesus Kirstoosa kaallishin intes inte giddon Ayana issifeteth immo.
Hessika inte issi woznaninne issi duuna gididi nu Goda Yesus Kirstoosa Aawa Xoossa bonchanassa.
Hessa gish Xoossi intena Xoossa bonchon mokki ekkida mala inteka issoy issa ufayssan mokki ekkite.
Kase aawatas imettida hidota qaala polanas Xoossa tumatethi erettana mala Kirstoosi Ayhudatas ooththizade gididayssa ta intes yootays.
Hessathoka Ayzaabeti iza maarotetha gish Xoosse galatana mala; hessikka “Ta nena dere giddon galatana; ne sunthaska galata yeth yexana” geetetti Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettida mala.
Qasseka “Ayzaabeto! Inteka Xoossa deretara ufayetite” geetetti Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafetides.
Nam7anthokka “Ayzaabeti inte wurikka Goda galattite; derey wuri iza sabbite” geetetti Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettides.
Hessatho Isayaasan “Ba dere asa bolla kawotiza Iseeye nay yaana. Alame asa ayssizaddey dendana; istika izan ufayettana” gees.
Inte izan ammaniza gish hidota Xoossi intenan ufaysinne saroteth kuntho. Hessika Xillo Ayana wolqa hidota intes daranassa.
Ta ishato! Inte lo7etethan; erateth ubban kumidaytanne harata zoranas eray dizayta gididayssa ta addafe shaaka eradis.
Ta Xoossafe ekkida imotetha gina qasseka intena qofisanas issi issi yo7ota xalatethan intes xaafadis.
Hessa he kiyatethay imettiday tani Xoossa Mishiraachcho qaala hanko deretas yootana mala; qasseka Qeese mala gidida Yesus Kirstoosas ooththanassa; hessa gish hanko dere asay Xillo Ayanan dummatidi Xoosse ufaysiza yarsho gididi shiiqana mala ooththays.
Hessa tani Xoossas ooththiza gish Yesus Kirstoosan ceeqqettays.
Ta yootidayssaninne ta ooththidayssan hanko dere asay Xoossas azazettana mala Kirstoosi tanan gididi ooththidazappe attin hara haasayana xalikke.
Hessika haniday Xillo Ayana wolqan malatata baggara hanides. Hessa malanka Yerusalameppe Ilwaqoore gakkanaas ta Kirstoosa Mishiraachcho qaala sabakadis.
Hara asi kase ooththidason ta gelonta mala gaada kase Kirstoosa sunthi xeeygeti erontason Mishiraachcho qaala sabakanayssi taas amo.
Harappeka “Iza gish istas yootetontayti iza beyana; siyi erontayti haasa7ana” geetetti kase Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettida mala hanides.
Hessa geedon ta inteko boonta mala daro wode diggettadis.
Ha7i qas taas haan oosoy baynda gish daro laythatappe haa simmin intena beyanas ta daro laamotadis.
Hayssa ta qofa tani Ispene biza wode polanas qoppays. Heera aadhdhashe intena beyanassinne intenara guutha wode gam7ada laamota aaththida mala inte tana maaddana gaada hidota ooththays.
Ha7i qas ammanizaytas imettiza maado gish ekkada Yerusalame bays.
Gaasoyka Maqidooniyaninne Akaayan diza manqota maaddana dendides.
Hayssa ha maadoza isti ba dosan immiday isti ooththanas bessiza gishassa; Ayzaabeti Ayhudatara issife Ayana anjo ekkizayta gidikko istika baasi diza biitta anjon Ayhudata maaddanas bessees.
Hessa gish hayssa shiiqida maado miisha Yerusalame immidappe guye inte achchan ta Ispene baana.
Ta he inteko bashe intes Kirstoosa anjo kuntha eka baanayssa ta erays.
Ta ishato! Tani Xoossa woossan baaxetiza mala inteka tanara baaxettana mala ta intena Goda Yesus Kirstoosaninne Xillo Ayana siiqon woossays.
Tani Yuhudan diza ammanonta asa kusheppe attana malanne Yerusalamen diza ta ooththoykka heen ammanizayta achchan ekettana mala taas woossite.
Hessika Xoossa shene mala he inteko ta ufayssara baana malanne intenara issife shempana mala.
Sarotetha Goday intenara ubbatara gido. Amiin.
Kinkira7oose Woosa Keeththan ooththiza ammanettida micheyo Pebeeno intes hadara gays.
Ammaniza asas bessiza mokko inte izo Goda sunthan mokki ekkana malanne iza intefe koyiza ay miishanka inte izo maaddana mala ta intena qofisays.
Kase tanara Goda Yesus Kirstoosas issife ooththida Phirsiqillassinne Aqilas ta sarokka gaththite.
Isti ta gish hayqqana gakkanaas bana aaththi immida; tana xalala gidonta Ayzaabetappe ammanidaytikka ista galatetes.
Ista keeththan diza ammaniza asaaka saro giite. Iisiyappe koyro Kirstoosan ammanida ta siiqoza Ephenexoose saro giite.
Intes daro daaburidaro Maaramo saro giite.
Tanara issife qashetida Andiraqonenne Yuniyase saro giite. Heytanti Hawaareta garsan lo7o sunthara dizaytanne Kirstoosa taappe kase ammanidayta.
Tani Goda baggara daro siiqiza Philyaxone saro giite.
Kirstoosa ooso tanara issife ooththiza Irobanoonenne ta siiqiza Senxakekka saro giite.
Kirstoosan iza ammanoy paacetidi galattettida Exessenesses ta sarokka gaththite. Arsixabaloso asaska ta sarokka gaththite.
Ta dabbo Herodiyaana saro giite. Godan diza Niriqaasoso asa saro giite.
Godan gididi minotethan ooththiza macasata Tirofimoononne Xirofimoono saro giite. Godas ooson daro daaburidaris Kirstoosan tani izo siiqiza Xarsidis ta sarokka gaththite.
Godan doorettida Ruufoones, taassinne izas aayo gididaris ta sarokka yootite.
Asqeroonessi, Afilasoonessi, Heromeenessi, Phaxirobaanessi, Hermaanessinne istara diza ishata ubbatas ta sarokka gaththite.
Filegoones, Yuuliyaas, Neeriyassinne iza micheys hessathoka Alxoones, istara diza ammanizaytaska ta sarokka gaththite.
Issoy issa yeeri yeer ekkidi saroketite. Kirstoosan ammaniza Woosa Keeththa asay wurikka intena saro gees.
Ta ishato! Asa garsan shaaketethi medhizaytappenne inte tamarida timirta ekkonta ixon intes dhuphe gidiza asatappe inte naagetite.
Heytanta mala asati Yesus Kirstoosas ooththizayta gidonta ba qantha kaththa gish ooththizayta. Shugo qaalara haasayaninne wozna kiya asata baleththetes.
Inte mishiraachcho qaalas azazettizayta gididayssa asi wuri siydes. Hessika tana daro ufaysides. Gidikkoka inte lo7o hanos cincata qasse iita oosos eeyata gidana mala ta koyays.
Sarotetha Goday Xala7e eeson inte toho gars aaththi dincereththana. Goda Yesus Kirstoosa kiyatethi intenara gido.
Tanara issife ooththiza Ximtoossi qasseka ta dabbo Luqiyoossi, Iyaasooneynne Susiphexiroossi intena saro saro geetes.
Hayssa kiita xaafiday tani Xerixiyoossi intena Goda sunthan saro gays.
Taninne hayssan diza kumeththa Woosa Keeththa asay mokki ekkiza Gayiyoossikka intena saro gees; katama miishsha oykkiza Erisxoossinne nu isha Qo7axiroossi intena saro geettes.
Goda Yesus Kirstoosa kiyateth intenara ubbatara gido. Amiin.
Tani yootiza Mishiraachcho qaalay Yesus Kirstoosa gish yootetiza kiitaynne beni wodeppe doommidi qotan gam7idi ha7i qasse qoncida tuma xuura baggara izi intena ammanon essanas dandayees.
Ha7i qasse hayssi tumay qoncides. Merna Xoossa azazon wurikka ammanidi azazettana mala nabeta maxaafa baggara dereti wurikka iza erana mala hanides.
Izi xalala era gidida Godas Yesus Kirstoosa baggara merna bonchoy izas gido. Amiin.
Xoossa shenen Yesus Kirstoosas kiitetanas xeeygetida Phawuloosappenne nu isha Sostineeseppe;
Qorontoosen diza Xoossa Woosa Keeththas; Goda Yesus Kirstoosas dummatidaytasinne istassara nuussara Goda gidida Goda Yesus Kirstoosa suntha awan awanka xeygiza ammanizaytara gidanas xeeygetida asa ubbas.
Nu Aawa Xoossafenne Goda Yesus Kirstoosappe kiyatethinne saroy intes gido.
Goda Yesus Kirstoosa baggara intes imettida Xoossa kiyatetha gish ubba wode inte gishikka tani Xoossa galatays.
Gaasoy ay yo7onka; hessikka haasayan gidin eratetha inte ubban duretideta.
Kirstoosa gish nu intes markattidayssi inte achchan minnides.
Hessa gish inte Yesus Kirstoosi qoncana gallas naagishin Ayana imotethatappe aykkoykka intes paccenna.
Goda Yesus Kirstoosi nam7antho yaana gallassan inte inte bolla boroy baynda bettana mala wurseth gakkanaas izi intena lo7eth naagana.
Izi ba naaza nu Goda Yesus Kirstoosa issifetethako intena xeygida Xoossi izi ammanettida Xoossa.
Ta ishato! Inte garsan shaaketethi doonta mala intes issi woznaynne issi qofay daana mala inte inte garsan issino gidana mala Goda Yesus Kirstoosa sunthan ta intena woossays.
Ta ishato! Inte garsan palamay dizayssa ta Qaalo7e so asappe siyadis.
Yo7ozikka hayssa mala; inte garsan issi issi asay “Ta Phawuloosa bagga” gees; baggay qasse “Ta Aphilosa bagga” gees; baggay qasse “Ta Keefa bagga” gishin haray qasse “Ta Kirstoosa bagga” gees.
Histikko Kirstoosi shaaketi wodhdhidee? Inte gish Phawuloosi kaqettidee? Woykko Phawuloosa sunthan xammaqetidetii?
Inte giddofe Qerisphoosappenne Gayiyoosappe attin hara oonakka ta xammaqonta gish Xoossa galatays.
Hessa gish oonikka “Ta Phawuloosa sunthan xammaqetadis” gaana asi deenna.
Tumukka Istifanoose so asa xammaqadis. Heytappe hara ta xammaqidakkone ta erizadey deenna.
Kirstoosi tana kiittiday Mishiraachcho qaala yootanas attin xammaqanas gidenna. Kirstoosa masqaley hada gidonta mala ta asappe gidida cincateththan sabakikke.
Masqaleza kiitay dhayana dizaytas eeyateththa. Gido attin attana diza nuus gidikko Xoossa wolqa.
“Cincata cincatethi ta istafe dhayssana; eranchata eratetha ta hada ooththana” geetetti Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettides.
Cincay awan dizee? Tamarida eray awan dizee? Hayssa wodeza pilgi erizay awan dizee? Xoossi ha alameza erateth, eeyateth ooththibenee?
Xoossa eratethafe dendidayssan alamey ba eratetha gaason Xoossa eroy xoonin sabako eeyateththan ammanizayta ashshanas Xoossa shene gidides.
Ay wodekka Ayhudati dumma malata koyettes. Girike asati qasse erateth koyettes;
Nuni gidikko kaqettida Kirstoosa sabakoos. Hessika Ayhudatas dhuphe; Ayzaabetas qasse eeyateththa.
Xoossi xeygidaytas isti Ayhudata gidin woykko Girike dere asa gidikkoka Kirstoosi Xoossa wolqanne Xoossa eratetha.
Gaasoyka asa erappe Xoossa eeyateththi aadhdhida eratetha; asa minotethafe Xoossa laafatethi aadhdhees;
Ta ishato! Kase inte xeeygetiza wode inte ay mala asakkonne ane qoppite. Asa qofa mala gidikko intefe darizayti erata gidekketa. Intefe daroti wolqay bayndayta; darotikka gita keeththa asappe yeletibekketa.
Gido attin Xoossi erata yeelachanas deraappe eeyata doorides; Xoossi minota yeelachanas alamezappe daburanchata doorides.
Xoossi hanko ammanonta asa achchan deettes geetetti erettiza miishata baynda miisha mala ooththana hayssa alamezan leqettidaytanne kawuyidayta laafata doorides.
Hessakka izi ooththiday oonikka iza sinthan ceeqqettonta mala.
Intena qasse Xoossi Yesus Kirstoosara issifetethi daana mala ooththides. Hessa gish Xoossi Yesus Kirstoosa nu erateth, nu xilloteth, nu geeshshatethinne nuna ashshizade gidana mala ooththides.
Hessa gish kase “Ceeqqiza asi Godan ceeqo” geetetti Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettida mala.
Ta ishato! Ta inteko Xoossa xuura qoncisana biday taas duuna qaratethi woykko era daroy diza gish gidenna.
Ta inte giddon diza wode kaqettida Yesus Kirstoosappe attin hara eronta mala ta baggara murtadis.
Ta inteko daro daaburan, yashshatethaninne daro kokkorashe badis.
Ta qaalaynne sabakoykka Ayana wolqa qoncisethanppe attin cimoninne era daron gidenna.
Hessika inte ammanoy Xoossa wolqanppe attin asa cincateththa bolla xaphonta mala hanides.
Nu kaha kunthida asata achchan era haasaya hasayos; gido attin hayssa ha alameza erateth gidenna; woykko dhayana diza ha alameza haarizayta erateth gidenna.
Gido attin nu haasayizay kase qoteti diza Xoossa xuura eratetha; he eratethay Xoossi daro wodeppe kase nuna bonchos kasetidi wursi woththidayssa.
Ha alameza haarizaytappe oonikka ha eratetha eribenna; eridako isti boncho Goda kaqettenna.
Gido attin Geeshsha Maxaafan “Asa ayfey beyontaz, asa haythi siyontaz, asa woznaykka qoppontaz Xoossi ba dosizaytas giigissides” gees.
Xoossi gidikko hessa ba Ayana baggara nuus qoncisides. Ayanaykka Xoossas diza ciimma yo7o ashshonta wursi pilgi xeelles.
Asa garsan izaades diza ayanappe attin izaade wozna erizay oonee? Hessathoka Xoossa Ayanappe attin Xoossa qofa erizay oonikka deenna.
Xoossafe nuus imettidayssa nuni erana mala Xoossa Ayanay nuus imettides attin nuni hayssa ha alameza ayana ekibeekko.
Nu yootizay hayssa; nu asappe tamarida qaala gidonta Ayanappe tamarida qaala hasayos. Ayana tumatethakka nu qoncisizay Ayana qaalanna.
Xoossa Ayanay izan baynda asi Xoossa Ayanappe gididaz ekkanas dandayenna; Gaasoyka hessa mala yo7oy izas eeyateththa; izi baasi Ayanan paacetizade gidida gish izi eranas dandayenna.
Xoossa Ayanay izan dizadey qas wursikka paaces attin baasi oonanka paacettenna.
Hessika “Goda qofa eranas dandayizay oonee? Iza zoranas dandayizay oonee?” geetetti kase Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettida mala; nuus gidikko Kirstoosa woznay dees.
Ta ishato! Ta intena inte Kirstoosan buro guutha nayta malanne buro ammanoy gelonta asa malappe attin Ayanan kumida asa mala gaada intes haasayanas dandayabekke.
Inte buro minnonta gish ta intena maath paahadis attin buro mino kath mizabekke; ha7ikka gidikko inte burokko!
Inte ha7ikka buro ammanon minnontayta gidida gish inte giddon qanatetethinne palamay dees; histin inte buro ammanon minnonta asa mala gidekketii? Inte oosoy coo mela asi ooththizayssa mala gidenee?
Gaasoyka inte garsafe issoy “Ta Phawuloosassa” hankoys qas “Ta Aphiloosassa” giikko inte coo asho qofan xalala diza asa mala gidekketii?
Ero! Gido attin Aphiloossi aazee? Phawuloosikka aazee? Isti Goday istas issas issas immida mala ooththiza ooththanchata; inteka ista baggara ammanideta.
Ta tokkadis; Aphiloossi haaththe ushshides; dichchiday gidikko Xoossa.
Hessa gish dichchizay Xoosse attin tokkizadeykka, haaththe ushshizadeykka aykkokka gidettenna.
Tokkizade gidin woykko ushshizade gidin isti issino; istafe issadey issadey ba ooso mala woyto ekkana.
Gaasoyka nu Xoossara issife ooththizayta. Inteka Xoossa goshsha gadenne Xoossa Keeththata.
Xoossafe taas imettida imotetha gina Keeththe keexxiza hiilla mala keeththay eqqanas lo7etha giigissadis; iza bolla hara asi keeththa keexana. Gido attin keeththa keexxizadey wosti keexanakone naagetanas bessees.
Gaasoyka keeththay keexeteth oyketidappe guye hara woththi qasse keexana dandayizadey oonikka baawa; hessikka keeththas koyroy Yesus Kirstoosa.
Oonikka keeththay koyro keexettidayssa bolla worqan woykko biran bonchettida shuchchan woykko mithaninne maatan woykko maqan keexxikko,
izaade oosoy ay mala pirda gallas qoncana. Gaasoyka he gallassay iza ha poo7oy dizaso kessana. He oosoy taman paacettana gish issade issade oosoy ay mala buro taman paacettana.
Oonikka keexxida keeththi minni eqqiza gidikko hessadey ba woyto ekkana.
Iza oosoy xuugetidadey gidikko woytoy izas deenna shin izaadey ba hu7es attana. Gido attin izaade atethi tamappe asi waaydi attiza atetha mala gidana.
Inte inte hu7es Xoossa Keeththe gididayssanne Xoossa Ayanay inte giddon dizayssa ereketii?
Oonikka Xoossa Keeththe laallikko Xoossi izaade laallana. Xoossa Keeththi geeshsha. Hessika intenakko!
Oonikka barka bana baleththofo; intefe oonikka hayssa ha alamezan bana erancha mala qoppikko izaadey erancha gidana mala bana barka eeya mala qoodo.
Hayssa ha dereza eratethi Xoossa achchan eeyateththa. Kase Geeshsha Maxaafan “Izi eranchata ista gene ooso geedon zaaridi oykkana” geetetti xaafettides.
Qasseka harason “Eranchata qofay mela hada gididayssa Goday erees” geetetti xaafettides.
Hessa gish wurikka intes gidida gish oonikka asan ceeqqettofo.
Phawuloosa gidin, Aphlossa gidin, woykko Keefa gidin, alame gidin, de7o gidin, woykko hayqo gidin, ha7i dizaz gidin, woykko buro yaana miish gidin, wurikka intessa.
Inteka Kirstoosayta; Kirstoosikka Xoossayssa.
Hessa gidida gish asi wurikka nuna Kirstoosa oosanchata malanne Xoossa xuura qoncisanas hadara ekkida asa mala qoodanas bessees.
Hadara ekidaytika ammanettidayta gidanas bessees.
Ta bolla inte pirdinka woykko duulata asay pirdinka ta baggara taas aykkoy baawa. Haray attoshin tarka ta bolla pirdikke.
“Ta eriza mala tani ta woznara sidhiza miishi baawa; gido attin hessa guus ta bolla mooroy baawa” guus gidenna. Buro ta bolla pirdanay Goda.
Hessa gish pirdana wodey gakkonta haara ay yo7okka pirdofte. Goday yaana gakkanaas naagite; izi dhuma giddon qotetidayssa buro qonce kessana. Asa wozna giddon diza qofakka qonce kessana. He wode issi issi asi baasi bessiza galata Xoossa achchafe ekkana.
Hessa gish ta ishato! Ta intena go7ana mala ha yo7ozan tananne Aphiloosa intes leemiso shiishadis; ta hayssa ooththiday “Xaafetidayssafe aadhdhofa” gizayssa inte nuuppe tamarana mala gaada. Hessa gish inte issade sabbidi hara as kadhanas bessenna.
Neni aazan aadhdhay? Neni harappe ekkonta attida miishi aazee? Histin ne wursaka ekkiday hara asappe gidikko, hara asappe ekkonta asa mala aazas ceeqqetay?
Ha7i gidikko intes koshizaz inte wursi demmidetanne duretideta; nuupekka shaaketidi kawotideta. Inte tumukka kawotidakko nuka intenara kawotanakko shin.
Gaasoyka Xoossi nuna Hawaareta nu bolla hayqo pirday pirdetida asata mala asa ubbafe wursethi ooththidaz taas misatees. Hessa gish alames kiitanchatassinne asa ubbas kaassa miish gididos.
Nu Kirstoosa gish eeyata gididos. Inte qas Kirstoosan eranchata; nuni daburanchata; inte gidikko minota; inte bonchettidayta; nuni gidikko kawushshata.
Hanno gakkanaas nu gafoos; saamettoos; kallottoos; bukettoos; aqizaasoy dhayin waayetoos.
Nu kushera ooththi daaburi aqoos. Nuna qangishin nu qas anjos; nuna goodishin nu dandayoos.
Nu sunth isti moorishin nu qas lo7o zaaros; hanno gakkanaas nu biittafe pitetida buura gididos.
Ta hayssa intes xaafizay intena ta dosiza ta nayta mala zoranas gaada attin intena yeelachanas gidenna.
Intena Kirstoosan dichchiza daro asati diikkokka intes daro Aawati deettenna. Tani qas Yesus Kirstoosa Mishiraachcho qaalan intena yeladis.
Hessa gish inte tana misatana mala ta intena woossays.
Godan daro dosettidayssanne ammanettida ta naa Ximtoosa ta inteko kiittiday hessa gaasonna. Izikka dumma dumma soon diza Woosa Keeththa asa wursi ta tamarsida timirtezara gaggizayssa Yesus Kirstoosan diza de7o oge gish intena izi qofisana.
Intefe issi issi asati ta nam7antho intena beyanas boontaz istas misatin otoretida.
Gido attin Goda shene gidikko matara ta inteko baana. Hee baada he otoranchati hasayizaz xalala gidonta istas aaza wolqay dizaakkonne beyana koyays.
Gaasoyka Xoossa kawotethi coo duuna xalala gidonta duunappe bollara Xoossa wolqa.
Ero! Inte koyizay awayssee? Durqa ekka boyee? Woykko siiqoranne ashketetha Ayanara boo?
Inte garsan yeellachiza laymay dizayssi woretees. Hessa mala tunatethi ammanonta dereta achchanka deenna. Ba aawa macho ekkida asi intekon dees.
Histin hessa mala yeelachiza miishi inte giddon dishin aazas otoretetii? Hessafe he yo7ozan inte muuzotanas intena bessenee? Hessa mala ooththidade inte garsafe diggite.
Ta intenara ashon issife doonta aggikkokka ayanan qas intenara days; ta ha7i intenara diza mala hessa ooththidade bolla pirdadis.
Inte shiiqizason ta intenara diza gish Goda Yesusa sunthaninne inte giddon diza nu Goda Yesusa wolqan he mooranchaza ashoy dhayin iza shempoy Goda gallassan attana mala hessa mala asi Xala7es aadhi imetto.
<range>
Inte ceeqqettizayssi lo7os gidenna. Guutha irshoy daro bukeeso dentheththiza erekketii?
Inte ha7i irshoy baynda ooratha bukeeso gidana mala kase caala irshoza inte giddofe diggite. Nu Paaziga dors gidida Kirstoosi nuus yarshetides.
Hessa gish ane nuni Paaziga ba7aaleza qohoynne iitatethi izan kumida kase caala irsho bolla gidonta irshoy baynda ukethan suuretethaninne tuman bonchos.
Intes laymatiza asatara issifetethi doonta mala ta intes kase dabdaabe xaafadiskoshin.
Inte mela ammanonta laymatiza asara gidonta woykko coo gaphigaphizaytara, kaysotizaytara, eeqas goynnizaytara gaaggofte guus gidonta dishin ha7i ta xaafiday ammanays gishe laymatizaytara woykko mathotizaytara, gaphigaphizaytara, eeqas goynnizaytara, asa sunth moorizaytara woykko cayzaytara, asa miish bonqizadentara intes issifeteth dooppo. Heytanta malara haray atto shin kaththika issife moopte.
<range>
Hanko ammanonta asa bolla pirdanas tana aazi gaththizee? Woosa keeththan dizayta bolla inte pirdeketii?
Woosa keeththafe karera dizayta bolla gidikko Xoossi pirdana “Inte inte giddofe iita as diggite” geetetti Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettides.
Inte garsafe issades hara ammanizadera yo7oy diikko he yo7oza ammanizayta ach shiishanayssa wosti ammanonta asa sinthan pirdettana shiishshizee?
Ammaniza asay ammanonta asa bolla pirdanayssa inte ereketii? Inte buro alame bolla pirdandeta. Gidikkoka hessa guutha yo7o bolla pirdanas dandayekketii?
Hayssa biitta bolla diza pirday attoshin inte buro kiitanchata bolla pirdanayssa ereketii?
Inte inte garsan oyeetikko ammanizayta maabarappe karen dizaytaninne kadhettida asata sinthan wosti inte yo7o shiisheetii?
Ta hessa intes gizay intena yeelachanassa. Inte garsan ammanizayta giigissanas dandayiza waznama asi dennee?
Gido attin ammanizadey hara ammanizade mootanas alame pirda keeththe baanas bessizee?
Inte garsan issoy issa mootoy inte kundethas malata bessees. Inte qohanappe qohetikko lo7enee? Qasseka inte as baleththanappe intena asi baleththikko lo7enee?
Inte haa qohetanappe gede qoheetanne baleththeta. Hessika inte ishata.
Makalanchati Xoossa kawoteth gelontayssa ereketii? Hessa mala yo7on balettofte. Laymatana qaqatizayti, eeqa eqqizaytinne addey addera laymatizayti,
woykko kaysoti, gaphigaphizayti, mathotizayti, as cayzaytinne bonqizayti Xoossa kawoteth laatetenna.
Intefe issi issi asati heytanta mala shin ha7i qas Goda Yesus Kirstoosa sunthaninne nu Xoossa Ayanan mecettideta; dummatidetanne xillideta.
Haray wurikka taas imettides; Gido attin wurikka go7izaz gidenna. Wurikka taas imettides gido attin ay miishikka tana haarenna.
Qasse Kaththi ulossa; uloykka kathassa; gido attin Xoossi nam7aakka dhayssana; asatethi Godasfe attin laymas gidenna. Godayka asaatethassa.
Xoossi Goda hayqoppe denthida mala nunakka qasse izi ba wolqan hayqoppe denthana.
Inte asatethay Kirstoosa asateth billite gididayssa inte ereketii? Histin ta Kirstoosa asatethafe issa layman aqqiza asatara issino histoo? Mulekka bessenna.
Woykko laymatizaarira aqizadey izira issi asho gidizayssa inte ereketii? “Nam7ay issi asho gidettes” geetettides.
Gido attin Godara issino gidizadey izara issi Ayana gides.
Laymappe haakkite; asi ooththiza hara nagaray wuri izaade ashoppe karera hanees. Layma laymatizadey gidikko barka ba asateth bolla nagara ooththes.
Inte asatethay inte gaaththan diza Xillo Ayanas duussaso gididayssa inte erekketii? He Ayanaykka inte Xoossafe ekidayssa. Inteka intes gidekketa.
Inte miishan shametideta. Hessa gish inte inte asatethan Xoosse bonchite.
Inte taas xaafida mala asi macasakko gakkonta aggizakko lo7okko! Gido attin laymappe naagetanas attumasas issas issas macha du. Macasaska issineys issineys azinay do.
<range>
Azinay ba macheys koshshizaz wursi ooththo. Machaka ba azinas koshizaz wursa ooththu.
Machi asatethi izis xalala gidonta azinassara koththa. Hessathoka azina asatethi izas xalala gidonta macheyssara koththa.
Nam7ay dosan woossas giidi zoren gido giidi qachida gallassatappe attin hara gallas issoy issas akay gooppite. Hessa gaason intes intena haaroy xoonin Xala7ey intena paaconta mala nam7ay issife aqite.
Ta hessa gizay coo azazo mala gidonta zore zorays.
Asi wuri ta mala macho ekkonta dizaakko ta dosays. Gido attin issi issi asas Xoossafe imettida dumma imotay dees. Issas dumma issi imotay dees. Hankoyssas qas hara imotay dees.
Buro ekontaytanne gelontayta gish qasseka azinay hayqqida macasata gish ta gizay isti gelontanne ekkonta ta mala dizaakko istas lo7o gays.
Gido attin isti bana naaganas dandayontayta gidikko geletonne eketo; coo amon xuugetanappe ekoynne geloy lo7o.
Ekidaytasinne gelidaytas ta immiza azazoy hayssa. Hessika Goda azazoppe attin ta azazo gidenna. Azina gelida macasaya ba azinappe shaaketufu.
Shaaketiza gidikko hara azina gelonta uttu. Akay giikko ba azinara giigu. Azinaykka ba macho anji yeddofo.
Hanko asas qas ta hizgays. Hessa gizayka tana attin Goda gidenna. Ammanonta macha diza ammanizadey macheya izara daana dosikko izi izo anjanas bessenna.
Ammanonta azinay diza ammaniza macasiya he ammanonta azinay izira daanas koykko iza izappe anjeta baanas bessenna.
Gaasoyka ammanonta azinay ammaniza ba macheyin anjetes. Ammanonta macasayaka ammaniza ba azinan anjetawus. Hessatho hanonta aggikko inte yelida nayti tunata gidana shin ha7i qas anjettidayta.
Gido attin nam7afe issoy ammanontadey shaakettana koykko shaaketo. Adde gidin maca gidin ammanizadey hessa mala wogan qashetenna. Xoossi nuna saron daana mala xeygides.
Hanne neni ne azina ashshanakkonne ay eray? Woykko haysso ne ne macho ashshanakkonne ay eray?
Coo issi issi asi Xoossi xeygida malanne Goday woththida mala de7o. Woosa keeththatas ta woththiza wogay hessa.
Issadey ammananappe kase qaxaretidaz gidikko qaxaretonta asa mala hanoppo. Qas qaxaretonta dishe ammanidadeyka qaxaretofo.
Qaxxaretin qaxxaretonta aggin nam7aanka go7ay baawa. Waanna ayfe yo7oy Xoossa azazo polo.
Issi issi asi ba xeeygetida xeeygetethan minni de7o.
Ammaniza wode ne ayllee? Ne hessas daro metotoppa; wozettana dandayikko wozeta. Gaasoyka aylle gidi dishe Goda ammanidadey izi Goda goqa. Hessathoka ammaniza wode goqa gidontaddey izi Kirstoosas aylle.
<range>
Inte miishan shametideta. Hessa gish asa aylle gidoppite.
Ta ishato! Intefe issi issi asi ba xeeygetida mala Xoossara minni de7o.
Geela7otanne paanthata gish taas godappe imettida azazoy deenna. Gido attin Goda maarotethafe dendidayssan ta intes ammanettidade gidada intena zorays.
Hayssa ha7i wode meto gaason inte ha7i diza mala dizaakko taas lo7o misatees.
Ne machidade gidikko anjanas koyoppa. Machontade gidikko macho ekkanas koyoppa.
Macho ekikkoka nagara gidenna. Geela7oyaka gelikko nagara gidenna. Gido attin ekkiza asatanne gelizayta bolla hayssa alamezan ista daro metoy gakkana. Ta qas hessi inte bolla gakkonta agganayssa dosays.
Ta ishato! Ta qofay hayssa mala; wodezi qaanth gidida gish macha dizaddey macha bayndade mala de7o.
Yeekkizayti yeekkonta asa mala, ufayetizayti ufayetonta asa mala gidetto. Miishe shamidadenti shametida miisha baas gi qoppofeto.
Hayssa alameza miishan go7ettizayti wursi go7etonta asa mala gidi deetto. Gaasoyka Hayssa alameza hanoy aadhdhanas dees.
Inte hirgay baynda daana mala ta koyays. Machontadey Goda ufayssanas Goda gish qoppees.
Machidadey qas ba machiyo ufayssanas hayssa alameza miish qoppees.
Hayssan iza qofay nam7u kezi shaaketes. Gelonta macasaya woykko gela7oya Godaz xalala qoppawus. Izis gita qofaykka ashonikka, ayananka Godas dummateththa. Gelidara gidikko ba azina ufayssanas hayssa alameza hano xalala qoppawus.
Ta hessa gizay intes lo7anaz qoppadappe attin intena daro qofan yegganas gidenna. Taas gita qofay inte woznay shaaketi nam7u kezonta inte Godan minnidi wogara de7yanassa.
Issadey ba oychida gela7oyo wogara oykkonta aggikko izi wodeykka cimmi cimmi biikko ekkana koykko ba koyda mala ekko. Ekikkone gelikko lo7o. Nagara gidenna.
Gido attin hayssa ha yo7ozan iza woznay qaaxonta bana haaridi geela7oyo ekkike giidi murtida asi lo7o ooththides.
Hessa gish geela7oyo ekidadey lo7o ooththides. Ekontadeyka aadhdhetha lo7o ooththides.
Issi macassi azinay paxa diza wode kumeththan ba azinara qashetadus. Azinay hayqqikko ba koyda as gelana dandayawus. Iza gelanadey ammanizade gido attin gelu.
Ta qofa mala gidikko iza gelonta dizaakko daro ufayssan de7andus. Taaska tanan Xoossa Ayanay diza misatees.
Eeqas shukettida asho gish inte taas xaafidayssa mala gidikko tumukka nu wurikka eriza miishi dees. Eroy otorises; siiqoy qas go7ees.
Ta erays giza asi eranas bessiza mala buro eribenna.
Xoosse siiqizadey gidikko izi Xoossa achchan eretidade.
Hessa gish eeqas yarshetida asho muussa gish ta intes gizay hayssa alamezan eeqay hada gididayssanne issi Xoossafe attin hara Xoossi bayndayssa nu eroos.
Aydekka gidikko daro eeqatinne daro godati deettes shin salon gidin sa7a bolla Xoosse geetettiza daro eeqati diikkokka nuus gidikko haniday wurikka izan hanides. Nukka izas gidida issi Xoossi Aaway dees. Qasseka hanidazi wurikka izan haniday nuka izan hanida issi Goday Yesus Kirstoosi xalala nuus dees.
<range>
Gido attin hessa asi wuri erenna. Issi issi asati hanno gakkanaas eeqa goynno dosida gish hessa mala asho miishe addaka Eeqas shukettidayssa qoppeetes. Istas qofay laafa gidida gish isti tuneetes.
Gido attin kathi nuna Xoossa ach gaththenna. Nu moonta agikkoka nuus paccizay deenna. Nu mikkokka nuus wodhey deenna.
Gido attin inte metoy baawa guussan ooththizays ammanon minnonta asas dhuphe gidonta mala naagetite.
Nees hessa misatiza erateth diza gish hinko ammanon minnontadey eeqa keeththan ne mizayssa beyidi eeqas shukettidayssa maanas xalenee?
Hessa gish Kirstoosi iza gish hayqqida he ammanon minnonta ishay ne eratetha gaason dhayees guussa.
Hessathoka inte inte ishata qohoninne ista laafa qofa madunthon Kirstoosa qoheeta.
Hessa gish ta miza miishi ta isha dhuphizaz gidikko ta isha ta dhuphethonta mala mulekka asho miikke.
Tani goqa as gidikinaa? Ta Hawaare gidikinaa? Nu Goda Yesusa tani ta ayfera beyabekkinaa? Inteka Godan ta ooson bettida ayfe gidekketii?
Haratas ta Hawaare gidonta agikkokka ta intes tumappe Hawaare. Gaasoyka Godan ta Hawaaretetha bessiza maatamey intena.
Tana paacizaytas ta immiza malthey hessa.
Ero! Maanassinne uyanas nuus bessenee?
Hara Hawaareta mala Goda ishata malanne keefanta mala nuka ammaniza nu macheta ekki yuuyana dandayokkonii?
Woykko waayeti daaburidi daanas bessizay tananne Barnabaasa xalalaa?
Ero! Ba miishara wotadarateth ooththizay oonee? Woyne mithi tokkidi, he tokkida mitha ayfe moontay oonee? Mehe heemmishe ba heemmiza meheza maath uyontay oonee?
Ta hayssa gizay coo asa qofa mala xalalaa? Muse wogay hessatho genee?
Muse woga garsan “Kath bukkiza mehe duuna qachofa” geetetti xaafettides. Histin Xoosse metiday he meheza qanthee?
Izi hessa giday tumappe nu gish gidenee? Heessi xaafettiday addafe nu gishassa. Goshshanchaynne qasseka bukkizayssi ba ooso ayfeppe bana gakkizayssa ekkanas ufays ooththes.
Nu inte giddon Ayana zerethi zeridayti ashos gidizaz maxikko hessi gita miishee?
Hara asati intefe hessa mala go7a ekanas dandayikko nu qas hessafe daro demmanas bessennee? Gido attin nuni nuus bessiza mala go7ettibeekko. Harappeka nu Kirstoosa Mishiraachcho qaalas dhuphe gidonta mala hanizaz wursikka dandayoos.
Xoossa Keeththan ooththizayti ba maanayssa Xoossa keeththafe ekkizayssa mala yarshoson ooththizaytikka he ba ooththiza yarshizayssafe mizayssa inte ereketii?
Hessathoka Mishiraachcho qaala sabakizayti baasi koshshizayssa Mishiraachcho qaala ooththizasoppe ekkana mala Goday woga woththides.
Tani gidikko hessa ubbafekka aykkokka go7etabekke. Ha7ikka ta intes hayssa xaafizay heytanta mala miish taas ooththeto gaada gidenna. Ayssi giikko oonikka tani ta Godan ceeqqettizaro taappe woththi ekanappe taas hayqoy lo7o.
Mishiraachcho qaala sabakidayssi tana ceeqqissenna. Ta sabakizay dosan gidida gish gidonta wolqara tana gakkida gishassa. Ta Mishiraachcho qaala sabakonta aggikko tana aayye-ana!
Mishiraachcho qaala ta dosan ta sabakikko taas woytoy dees. Tani ta dosan gidonta wolqara ooththizayssa gidikko hadara polana mala ooso xalala gidana.
Histin taas aaza woytoy dizee? Taas woytoy daanay Mishiraachcho qaala sabakashe taas bessizayta ta go7etonta aggikkokko.
Ta goqappe attin oonaska aylle gidikke. Gido attin darota Godakko zaarana gish asa ubbas aylle mala gidadis.
Ayhudata ashshanas Ayhudatara ista misatadis. Tani ta baggara Muse wogappe garasara gidonta dashe Muse wogappe garsara dizayta ashshanas ista misatadis.
Tani ta baggara Xoossa wogay dizaddenne Kirstoosa wogas haarettizade gidikkoka wogay bayndayta ashshanas ista mala wogay bayndade gidadis.
Daburanchata ashshanas gaada takka daburanchatara ista mala daburancha gidadis. Taas dandayettida mala ubban issi issi asata ashshanas asa ubbara isti hanizaz hanadis.
Ta hayssa wursa ooththizay Mishiraachcho qaala anjo istara gishettanas Mishiraachcho qaala gish ooththadis.
Gaadde woththi woxxizayti daro shin xoonidi shilmate demmizay issade xalala gididayssa inte ereketii? Hessa gish shilmate ekkanas woxxizade mala inteka woxite.
Gaadden wooxxi aadhdhanas giigettizaddey oonikka hano barka bana naagees. Heytanti aadhdhananne dhayana aklile ekanas daaburettes shin nu qas mernas dhayonta aklile demmanas daaburoos.
Hessa gish ta qas poloy baynda coo mela woxxizade mala woxxike. Qasseka carkora baaxetizadde mala coo mela gaden baaxetike.
Ta qas haratas sabaka pe7ada taas kunda attonta mala ta asateth shiisha oykkada haarays.
Ta ishato! Kase nu Aawati shaaray istafe bollara gididi kaalethidayssa malanne isti wurikka zo7o abba pinnidayssa ta intena qoppisanas koyays.
Isti Musera gidanas giidi shaaraninne abban xammaqetida.
Wurikka issi ayana quma mida.
Wurikka issi ayana ushshi uyida. Isti uyidaykka bana kaalliza ayana zaallafe pultidayssafe. He zaallayka Kirstoosa.
Gido attin Xoossi darotan ufayetibenna. Hessa gish ista ahay bazzon kundi attides.
Isti iita miish amottidayssatho nuka amottonta mala he ista hanoy nu naagettana mala nuus leemiso gidides.
“Derey maanassinne uyanas uttides; yexanaska dendides” geetetti kase Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettida mala ista garsafe issi issi asati ooththoyssatho inteka eeqa goynnizayata gidoppite.
Ista garsafe issi issi asati laymatidi issi gallas nam7u tammanne heedzdzu shi asay dippi gi wuroyssatho wuronta mala nuka ane laymatokko.
Ista garsafe issi issi asati Goda paacidi shooshan duketti hayqqi dhayidayssa mala nuka ane Goda paacokko.
Ista garsafe issi issi asati zuuzumetidi dhaysiza bosha kiitanchan dhayidayssatho inteka dhayonta mala zuuzumoppite.
Hessi wuri nuus leemiso gidana mala ista bolla gakkides. Wode wursethan diza nuus timirte gidana mala nuus xaafettides.
Hessa gish ta minna eqqa days gizaddey diikko kundonta mala baasi naageto.
Asa bolla gakkida paaceppe hara aadhdhiza paacey inte bolla gakkibeenna. Xoossi ammanettiza Xoosse gidida gish inte dandayonta inte wolqafe bollara inte paacetenna mala izi intena aggaggenna. Gido attin inte paacetiza wode he paaceza inte dandayana mala wolqa immidi paaceppe inte kessi ekkana oge izi intes giigissana.
Hessa gish ta siiqoto! Eeqas goynnoppite; izappe hakkite.
Ta intes hayssa gizay woznama gidida gishassa. Hessa gish ta yootizayssa ane inte interka pirdite.
Nuni Xoossa galatidi ekkiza ushshay Kirstoosa suuthara gaggoteththi dizayssa gidenee? Hessathoka nu baththi baththi gishetti miza ukethay Kirstoosa ashora gaggoteththi dizayssa gidenee?
Ukethay issino gidida mala nunikka daro gidi uttidikka wurikka issi asho. Nu wurikka issi ukethaza gishetti moos.
Ane inte Isra7eele nayti ooththidayssa qoppite. Shiiqza yarshozappe mizaytas yarshoy shiiqzasora gagoteththi denee?
Histin eeqas yarshetida yarsho gidin woykko eeqay ba baggara go7ara dees gazinaa?
Gidenna! Ammanonta asay shiishshiza yarshoy Xoossas gidonta Xala7esa. Intes Xala7era issifetethi daana mala ta koyikke.
Xala7e ushshinne Goda ushshi inte issife gaththi uyana dandayekketa. Goda maaddafenne Xala7e maaddafe gaththi maana dandayekketa.
Nuni Goda hanqethinoo? Nu izappe minnizonii?
Wurikka taas imettides shin wurikka tana go7izaz gidenna. Wurikka taassa shin wurikka tana maaddenna.
Asi wurikka ba lagge go7anaz gaaththi xeello attin bana go7anaz xalala koyoppo.
Giyan bayzettiza asho wursi sidhey baynda miite.
Biittaynne biitta bolla dizay wurikka Godayssa.
Ammanonta asi intena baso xeygidi shiishida kath wursi aykkokka sidhonta miite.
Gido attin issadey “Hayssi eeqas yarshetida kaththa” giikko he kaththaa he addeza qofa gishshinne intena sidhisikko mooppite.
Ta intes hessa gizay he yootidade qofa gish gadis attin inte qofa gish gabeyke. Ta xillo gida dishin aazas hara asa qofa geedon ta bolla pirdetizee?
Ta Xoosse galatada mizade gida uttada aazas hara asan pirdetoo?
Histikko inte ay miikkoka, ay uyikkoka woykko aykko ooththikko wursikka Xoossa bonchos ooththite.
Ayhuda asas gidin Ayzaabetas gidin woykko Xoossa Woosa Keeththas oonaska dhuphe gidoppite.
Ta as wursaka ay ogerakka ufayssana koyiza mala inteka hessatho ooththite. Daroti attana mala ta tana go7izaz gidonta ista go7izaz koyays.
Tani Kirstoosa misatada iza kaallizayssatho inteka tana misatidi kaallite.
Inte taas wursi qoppiza gishshinne taappe ekkida timirteza lo7ethi oykkida gish ta intena galatays.
Gido attin ta inte erana mala koyizay attumasas ubbas hu7ey Kirstoosa gididayssa mala attumasay macasas ubbas hu7e. Qasse Xoossi Kirstoosas hu7e.
Ba hu7e gulluntidi Xoosse woossizadey woykko qaala yootizadey oonikka barka bana kawushshees.
Ba hu7e goozonta woossiza macasiya woykko tinbite qaala yootiza ay macaska barka bana kawushshawus. Hessi iza ba hu7e bulissiddadera gina.
Macassi ba hu7e goozonta aggikko meedetu woykko qanxisu. Izis ba hu7e meedetethi woykko qanxisethi yeelachizaz gidikko goozu.
Addey ba hu7e gulluntanas bessenna. Attumasi Xoossa leemisonne Xoossa boncho. Macassi gidikko addes boncho.
Gaasoyka macassi addefe medhetadus attin attumasi macasappe medhetibenna.
Qasseka macassi addes medhetadus attin addey macasas medhetibenna.
Hessa gish kiitanchati beyanas naagiza macasas imettida maata bessiza goosse ba hu7en goozu.
Goda achchan gidikko macassi addey baynda, addeyka macassi baynda deyettenna.
Macasi addefe bettidayssatho addeyka macasappe yelettes. Gido attin nam7aykka Xoossafe bettida.
Macassi ba hu7e goozonta Xoosse woossanas bessizakone ane inte pirdite.
Attumasi ba hu7e adussi dichchikko borso gididayssa intena medhetetha hanotethi erisuwee?
Macay gidikko ba hu7e binana dichchikko hessi izis boncho gidenee? Izis adusa hu7e binanay imettiday seelo gidanassa.
Hessa gish oonikka hayssa ha yo7ozan palamettana koykko nuus gidinka Xoossa Woosa Keeththatas hayssafe hara wogay deenna.
Inte issi so shiiqetiza wode qohos attin go7as gidonta gish ta hayssa azazoza intes aaththizay intena galatashe gidenna.
Inte Woosa Keeththan shiiqiza wode inte garsan shaakotethi dizayssa ta kaseta siyadis. Ta siyoyssafe baggay tumu gidanayssa ta ammanays.
Inte giddofe tumanchati shaaketi erettana mala hessa mala shaakoy inte giddon daanayssi dosa gidenna.
Inte issife shiiqetidi mizay Goda kawo gidenna.
Inte shiiqetidi issoy issa naagonta dishe kath meeta. Intefe issadey gafan dishin hankoyssi qas mathottes.
Histin intes uyanasoynne maanasoy baawee? Woykko Xoossa Keeththe leqqidi aykkoykka bayndayta yeelachetii? Histin ta intena ay goo? Hayssa ha hanozas intena galatoo? Mulekka galatikke.
Ta Godappe ekkidayssa intes aaththadis. Hessika Goda Yesusi aadhdhi imettida omars uketh denthidinne Xoosse galati baththidi “Heyite! Miite! Hayssi intes gidiza ta asho. Tana qoppanas inte hayssa ooththite” gides.
<range>
Hessathoka kawoppe guye ushsha denthidi “Hayssi ushshay ta suuthan haniza ooratha caaqo. Hessa gish ushshafe inte uyiza wode hayssa tana qoppana mala ooththite” gides.
Hayssa uketha inte miza wodenne hayssa ushshakka uyiza ubba wode Goday yaana gakkanaas inte iza hayqo yootana.
Hessa gish oonikka bessonta dishin hayssa uketha miikko woykko Goda ushsha uyikko izaadey Goda ashonne iza suutha kawushshida gish izi oyshettana.
Oonikka hayssa ha uketha mannappenne ushshafe uyanappe kaseti barka bana paaco.
Gaasoyka oonikka Goda asho baasi gelonta dishin miikkonne Goda ushsha uyikko izaadey barka ba bolla pirda ehees.
Inte garsan daro asay daaburidaynne saketiday qasseka baggay hayqqiday hessa gaasonna.
Nu nurka nuna paacizakko nu bolla pirdana.
Gido attin Goday pirdiza wode nu hanko ammanonta asara pirdetonta mala izi nuna kaseti murees.
Hessa gish ta ishato! Inte maana shiiqiza wode issoy issara naagetite.
Inte shiiqiza shiiqoy pirdas gidonta mala intefe oonikka gafiddaddey diikko kasetidi ba soon mo. Hanko attidayssa tani hara wode he inteko baada woga wothana.
Ta ishato! Ayanay immiza imotetha gish inte issi miish erana mala ta koyays.
Inte ammananappe kase coo mela yaanne haanne guussan inte eronta kaalethettidi duuna duude gidida eeqatakko bidayssa inteka ereeta.
Hessa gish oonikka Xoossa Ayanan haasayishe “Yesusi qangetidade” geenna. Hessathoka Xillo Ayanan gididi attin oonikka “Yesusi Goda” gaana asi doontayssa ta intes yootays.
Asas imotethi dumma dumma gidishin Ayanay gidikko issino.
Oosoykka dumma dumma gidishin Goday gidikko issino.
Dumma dumma ooso ogeti diikkokka wursikka ooththizay issi Xoossa.
Gido attin Xillo Ayana qonciso imotay issades imettizay issife go7ettanassa.
Issades hiillan haasayana eratethi imetees. Hara asas qas he Ayananka eratetha qaalan haasayana qaalay imetees.
Issades he Ayanan ammanoy imetees. Hara asas qas he Ayananikka hargizayta pathiza imotay imetees.
Issades malalisiza ooso ooththiza imotay; qasseka hara asa buro tinbite qaala haasaya imotay; hara asa qasseka ayanata shaakki eroy; hara asas dumma dumma qaalan hasayay; qasseka hara asas hara dumma dumma qaalan haasayettidayssa birshana imotay imetees.
Heyti wurikka he issi Ayanay immiza imota gidishin issi issi asas ba koyda mala immees.
Issi asatetha bolla daro billiteti diikkokka asatethay issino. Gido attin billiteti daro gidikkoka asatethay issino xalala. Kirstoosikka hessa mala.
Ayhuda asata gidinka Girike asata gidinka, aylle gidinka woykko goqa asata gidinka nu wurikka issino gidanas issi Ayanan xammaqetidos. Nu wurikka ha issi Ayanappe uyidos.
Asatethi medhetiday daro billitetappe attin issi billiteppe xalala gidenna.
Tohoy “Ta kushe gidonta gish asatetha giddon diikke” giikko izi hizgida gish izas asatethan duussi attanee?
Haythi “Ta ayfe gidonta gish asatetha giddon diikke” giikko hessa gish asateth giddon duussi izas attanee?
Asatethi wurikka ayfe xalala gididakko aazan siyanee? Asatethi wurikka haythe xalala gididakko aazan singanee?
Gido attin Xoossi issa issa ba koyda mala asatetha giddon daanas bessizason woththides.
Billitey wurikka issino gididakko kumeththa asatethi awappe betanee?
Hessa gish billiteti daro shin asatethi gidikko issino xalala.
Ayfey kushe “Nena ta koyikke” gaanas dandayenna. Hu7ey toho “Nena taas koshshenna” gaana dandayenna.
Haray attoshin ubbafe laafa misatiza billiteti daro koshshizayta.
Nuni laafa gi leqqiza billiteta hankoytaappe aaththi bonchos. Qasseka nu istan yeelatiza billiteta harappe aaththi naagos.
Nu istan yeelatonta billitetas gidikko hessa mala boncho koshshenna. Xoossi gidikko asateth billiteta issi bolla oythethidi bonchoy paacizaytas aadhdhetha boncho immides.
Izi hessa ooththiday asatetha billiteta garsan shaakotethi doonta isti ba garsan issoy issa banara gina gi qoppanassa.
Issi billitey saketikko hanko billiteti wurikka izara issife saketetes. Issi billitey bonchettikko biilliteti wurikka issife ufayetetes.
Histikko inte wurikka Kirstoosa asateth; inte issoy issoy iza asatetha billiteta.
Xoossi Woosa Keeththa giddon koyro Hawaareta, nam7antho qasse nabeta, heedzdzantho astamareta, kaalethidi malata ooththizayta, paathiza imotethi dizayta, harataka as maaddiza imotay dizayta, dere ayso eratethi dizaytanne dumma dumma qaala haasayana imotethi diza asata woththides.
Wurikka hawaratee? Wurikka nabetee? Wurikka astamaretee? Wurikka malalisiza miishe ooththizoo?
Ubbaska hargizayta paathiza imotay dizee? Asi wurikka dumma qaalan hasayizee? Dumma qaalan hasayettoyssa asi wuri birshizee?
Gido attin inte wurikka ubbafe aadhdhiza imoteth lo7ethi koyite. Qasseka hara ubbafe aadhdhiza oge ta intena bessana.
Ta asa qaalaninne salo kiitanchata qaalan hasayikkoka taas siiqoy baynda aggikko coo mela birata giirissa mala woykko daala giiretha mala.
Tinbite haasayiza imotay taas diikkokka, woykko xuura yo7otanne erateth wursa ta erikkoka, zumay izi dizasoppe dhooqada haraso diggiza ammanoy taas diikkokka hessa wursaka siiqoy baynda ta ooththikko hessi mela hada.
Taas dizaz wursa manqotas ta immikkoka, ta asateth ta taman xuugikkokka, siiqoy baynda aggikko tana hessi aykkokka maaddenna.
Siiqoy dandaya, qasseka kiya; siiqoy miqaynenna; ceeqqettenna; otoretenna;
bessontaz ooththenna, barka ba go7a xalala xeellenna. Qoho qoodan yeggenna.
Siiqoy tumanppe attin makalan ufayetenna.
Siiqoy ubba wode dandayees. Ubba wodekka ammanees. Ufays ooththessinne minni eqees.
Siiqoy mulekka kundenna. Tinbitey gidikko attana. Hara qaalan haasayayka attana. Eratethika shaarettana.
Gaasoyka nu erizay wursi gidonta shaakki eroos. Tinbite haasaya gidikkoka bagga hasayos.
Gido attin wursethi gakkiza wode kumeth gidonta imotay he wode shaarettana.
Ta guutha naatetethan dashe naa mala haasayayssinne naa mala qoppays. Naa malaka yuusha qoppays. Kaha kunthidappe guye kase naatethan hanizayssa wursaka yegga aggadis.
Nuni ha7i beyzayssi haaththan xeelliza mala coo bozhi bozhes shin he wode gidikko nu iza ayfeso lo7ethi beyana. Ta ha7i kumeth gidonta bagga xalala erays. He wode gidikko tani ta hu7es eretidayssa mala erana.
Hessa gish ammanoy, hidotaynne siiqoy hayti heedzdzati eqi daana. Hayta ubbafe aadhdhizay siiqo.
Siiqo kaallite; ayana imotethata harappeka tinbite haasayiza imotata lo7ethi koyite.
Hara qaalan hasayizaddey Xoossas attin asas hasayenna. Xuura gidida yo7o Ayanan haasayiza gish izi gizay asas gelenna.
Tinbite hasayizaddey asa minthethanas, dentheththanassinne go7anas haasayees.
Hara qaalan hasayizaddey qas barka bana minthethes. Tinbite hasayizaddey gidikko Woosa Keeththa go7ees.
Inte wurikka hara qaalan hasayizakko ta dosays shin hessafeka bollara inte tinbite qaalan hasayizakko ta dosays. Woosa keeththay minnana mala hara qaalara hasayizaddey ba haasayizayssa birshonta izi hara qaalara hasayizayssafe tinbite hasayizaddey aadhdhees.
Hessa gish ta ishato! Ta inteko biza wode ta intes qoncisethan woykko eratethan woykko tinbiten, woykko timirten yootonta hara qaalara yootikko hessi intena ay go7anee?
Hessi coo susul7e malanne diiththa mala shempoy baynda ista giirissas dummateththi shaaketi eretonta aggikko iza wosti eranee?
Qasseka xurumbay aazas punetizakko woykko zayey aazas zayettizakonne shaakki eretonta ogera punetikko ooni olas giigetanee?
Inteka hessa mala. Inte duunappe erettiza qaalay kezonta aggikko inte gizayssa ooni eranee? Coo mela carkon dhayana.
Alame bolla daro dumma dumma qaalay dees shin birsheththi baynda qaalay baawa.
Hessa gish issadey haasayiza qaala birsheththi ta eronta aggikko hasayizades ta imathe gidays. Izaadeyka taas imath gides.
Inteka hessa mala Ayanan imotethata demmanas koyiza gish Woosa Keeththa go7iza imoteth demmanas lo7ethi koyite.
Hessa gish hara qaalan haasayiza asi ba haasayidayssa birsheththi erana mala baasi woosso.
Tani hara qaalara woossiza wode ta Ayanan woossays attin ta izappe aykkokka erike.
Histin ta ay ooththana mala taas bessizee? Tani ta Ayananka woossana. Woznan wothadakka woossana. Ta Ayananka yexana. Woznarakka yexana.
Hessatho gidonta aggikko ne Xoosse Ayanan galatiza wode hessa eronta issi imatha asi ne galata woossa wosti “Amiin” gaanas dandayizee?
Ne bessiza mala galatanas dandayassa. Hankoyssi gidikko izan go7ettenna.
Tani intefe bollara hara qaalan haasayiza gish Xoosse galatays.
Gido attin Woosa Keeththan eretonta daro shi qaalata haasayanappe hara asata tamarsanas asay eriza ichash qaala haasayana dosays.
Ta ishato! Inte inte qofan guutha nayta mala gidoppite. Iita oosos gidikko guutha nayta mala gidite. Qofan gidikko kaha kunthida asata gidite.
Kase woganka “ ‘Ista qaalay imath gidida alaga asata qaalara ta hayssa asas yootana. Hessatho yootinka ta gizaz isti siyettenna’ gees Goday” geetetti kase Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettides.
Hessa gish hara qaalan haasayay ammanonta asas malata gides attin ammanizaytas malata gidenna. Tinbitey gidikko ammanizaytas attin ammanontays gidenna.
Histikko Woosa Keeththan ammaniza asay issife shiiqidason wurikka eronta hara qaalan hasayishin imatha asati woykko ammanonta asay shiiqidi hasayizaso gelikko “Hayti goyeettes” geettenee?
Gido attin asay wuri tinbite qaala haasayettishin imaththi woykko ammanontadey gelikko ba siyidayssa ubba erananne he qaalan pirdettana.
Izaadey ba woznan qotti woththidazi wuri qoncananne izikka ba baggara “Tumappe Xoossi intenara dees” giidi gufannidi Xoossas goynnana.
Hessa gish ta ishato! Histin ay giinoo? Inte issife shiiqiza wode intefe issi issi asas yeth qasse issi issi asas timirtey dees. Issi issi asas qonconta xuura miishata qoncisiza imotay dees. Hara asas dumma qaalan haasayana imotay dees. Haras qasse he qaala birsheththa imotay dees. Hessi he imotay wurikka ammanizayta go7anas bessees.
Hara qaalara haasayizay diikko nam7u as woykko dari darikko heedzdzu gididi taran taran yooteto. Hara asi qasse birsho.
Birshizaddey baynda aggikko shiiqida asa giddon co7u giidi baasi xalalanne Xoossas xalala yooto.
Tinbite haasaya imotay dizayti nabeti nam7ati woykko heedzdzati tinbite hasayetto. Hanko asay yootetidayssa lo7ethi paaco.
Uttida asa garsafe issadey issi miishi qoncikko koyro hasayizayssi co7u go.
Inte garsafe issi issi asi tamarana malanne minettana mala inte wurikka taran taran tinbite yootanas dandayeeta.
Nabeta ayanay nabetas azazetes. Gaasoyka Xoossi sarotetha Xoossafe attin wocama Xoosse gidenna. Ammanizayta Woosa Keeththe ubbasonka hessa mala.
<range>
Ammaniza asay goynnos shiiqizason macasati co7u getto. Muse wogay kase gida mala isti azazetteto attin shiiqoson isti haasayana mala istas imettibenna.
Macassati eranas koyiza issi issi yo7oti diikko ba keeththan ba azinata oycheto. Gaasoyka macassi shiiqoson haasayay yeelachizaza.
Xoossa qaalay intefe kezidee? Woykko inteko xalala gakkidee?
Oonikka bana “Nabe” giikko woykko “Taas Xillo Ayanappe imotethi dees” gizaddey diikko hayssi ta intes xaafidayssi Goda azazo gididayssa ero.
Hayssa eronta asi diikko izi ba hu7es eretenna.
Hessa gish ta ishato! Buro tinbite haasayanas lo7eth koyite. Dumma dumma qaalan haasayaka diggofte.
Gidikkoka wurikka maararanne wogara gido.
Ha7ikka ta ishato! Ta intena sabakin inte ekkidinne izan minni eqqida Mishiraachcho qaala ha7i qofisana koyays.
Ta intes sabakida qaala inte lo7ethi oykkikko he Mishiraachcho qaalan inte attana. Hessa mala gidonta aggikko inte ammanoy coo mela hada.
Tani taas ekkidayssanne ubbafe aadhdhizayssa intes aaththa immadis. Geeshsha Maxaafati gizayssa mala Kirstoosi nu nagara gish hayqqides.
Moogetides; Geeshsha Maxaafatan xaafettidayssa mala heedzdzantho gallas hayqoppe dendides.
Hessafe kaallidi Phexroosas beettides. Qasseka Yesusa kaalliza tammanne nam7atas beettides.
Hessafe guye ichashu xeetuppe bollara diza ammanizaytas issito beettides. He iza beyda asappe dariza baggay paxa dees. Baggay qasse hayqqides.
Hessafe guye Yaqoobes beettides. Kaallidika kumeththa Hawaaretas beettides.
Tani Hawaareta ubbafe laafanne kase Xoossa Woosa Keeththe goodida gish Hawaare geetetanas tani bessontadekko shin asa wursofe awucaya misatiza taaska beettides.
<range>
Gido attin Xoossa kiyatethan ha7i ta hananayssa hanadis. Taaska imettida Xoossa kiyatethi mela hada gidibenna. Tani oonappekka bollara daro minna ooththadis. Gido attin hessa ooththiday tana gidonta Xoossa aadhdho kiyatethi ooththides.
Hessa gish tana gidin istaka gidin nu wurikka sabakizay hessa. Inteka ammaniday hessa.
Kirstoosi hayqoppe dendidayssa nu tamarsikko histin inte garsafe issi issi asati waanidi hayqoppe dendoy baawa gizoo?
Hayqqida asas denthi doontaz gidikko Kirstoosikka dendibenna guussakaa?
Kirstoosikka hayqoppe dendontaz gidikko nu sabakos go7ay baawa. Inte ammanoyka coo mela hada.
Hessafekka bollara “Xoossi Kirstoosa hayqoppe denthides” giidi nu markattida markaykka nuna wordo Xoossa markata kessideskaa? Hayqqida asay hayqoppe dendontaz gidikko Xoossi Kirstoosakka denthibenna guussa.
Gaasoyka hayqqidayti dendontaz gidikko Kirstoosikka hayqoppe dendibenna.
Kirstoosi hayqoppe dendontaz gidikko inte ammanoy coo mela. Inteka hanno gakkanaas inte nagarara deeta guussa.
Hanoy hessa mala gidikko Kirstoosa ammanidi hayqqidayti wurikka dhayida guussa.
Nuni Kirstoosan ufays ooththizay hanno biittay bolla duussas xalala gidikko nu asa ubbafe laafata.
Gido attin Kirstoosi hayqqidaytas ubbas bayra gididi hayqoppe tumu dendides.
Hayqoy issi asa Addame baggara yida mala hayqqidayta denthi Kirstoosa baggara.
Asi wurikka Addame baggara hayqqida mala hessathoka asi wurikka Kirstoosa baggara hayqoppe dendana.
Gido attin wurikka ba tarara tarara dendana. Koyro bayra gidida Kirstoosi dendides. Izappe kaallidi izi yiza wode Kirstoosas gidizayti dendana.
Hessafe guye haarettiza dereta godateththinne wolqamata wursi dhayssidappe guye kawota Xoossa Aawas aaththi immiza wode he wode wurseth gidana.
Izi ba morke wursikka ba toho gars aaththana gakkanaas izi kawotanas bessees.
Buro wursethan xooneti dhayana morkey hayqo.
“Xoossi wursikka iza godateththafe garsan woththides” gizazi Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettides. Gido attin “Wurikka iza Godateththa garsan gidides” gishin wurikka iza godateththa garsan ooththida Xoossa Aawa gujjenna.
Wurikka izas haarettidayssafe guye Xoossi wursofe bolla gidana mala Xoossa nay qasse ubba baasi haarisidayssas Xoossa Aawas haarettana.
Hayqoppe denthi doonta aggikko histin hayqqida asa gish giidi xammaqetiza ubbas go7ay aazee? Hayqqidayti mulekka dendontaz gidikko histin asay ista gish aazas xammaqetizee?
Nu qas ubba wode iita metos aadhi imettizay aazasee?
Ta ishato! Hach hach hayqoy tanara gaaggees. Hessaka nu Goda Yesus Kirstoosa geedon inte bolla diza ammaneteth ta intes qoncisays.
Tani Efesoonen do7a misatiza asatara baaxetidayssi asi beyana mala xalala gidikko taas izan aaza wodhey dizee? Hayqqidaytas denthi doonta aggikko “Nu wonto hayqqana gish ane moos, ane uyoos” gizayta mala nuka ista mala gidoos.
Inte balettofte! Iita laggetethi lo7o amalera dizayta moores.
Woznama gidite; nagara ooththofte; Xoosse erontayta issi issi asati inte garsan diza gish ta hessa intena yeelachanas gays.
“Hayqqidayti waani dendanee? Ay mala ashora dendanee?” gizadey daana dandayees.
Neno eeyazo! Ne zeriza zerethay hayqqonta dishe caarenna.
Neni zeriza kaththa modheya giste woykko hara kaththa ayfe gidikkoka guyeppe ne ekkanara ha7i ne zeroro gidukku.
Xoossi qasse ba koyda mala he zerethas iza mala medho immees. Zeretha qommotas issas issas iza misatiza asateth immees.
Ashoy wurikka issi mala gidenna. Asa ashoy issa gidishin mehe ashoy qasse hara; kafo ashoy hara; mole ashoykka hara qommo.
Hessa malaka salon dizaytassikka ista misatiza medhoy dees. Biitta bolla dizaytassikka ista misatiza medhoy dees. Gido attin saloyta bonchoy issi mala. Biitta bolla dizayta medho bonchoyka dumma.
Awa arshe bonchoy issino. Gido attin agina bonchoy qasse dumma. Xoolinteta bonchoyka hara. Issi xoolinte bonchoy hara xoolinte bonchofe dummates.
Hayqqida asa denthikka hessa mala. Wooqiza medhoy zeretin wooqonta medhoy dendana.
